	public enum CaseType {
	    WEAPON_CASE_ONE("Weapon Case One", 75.0, 1.0),
	    BRAVO("Bravo Case", 50.0, 1.0),
	    BREAKOUT("Breakout Case", 10.0, 1.0),
	    SPECTRUM("Spectrum Case", 5.0, 1.0);
	    
	    final String name;
	    final double price;
	    final double rarityBonus;
	    int timesOpened;
	    double totalSpent;
	    double totalReceived;
	    
	    CaseType(String name, double price, double rarityBonus) {
	        this.name = name;
	        this.price = price;
	        this.rarityBonus = rarityBonus;
	        this.timesOpened = 0;
	        this.totalSpent = 0.0;
	        this.totalReceived = 0.0;
	    }
	    
	    public double getROI() {
	        if (totalSpent == 0) return 0.0;
	        return ((totalReceived - totalSpent) / totalSpent) * 100.0;
	    }
	    
	    public double getAverageProfit() {
	        if (timesOpened == 0) return 0.0;
	        return (totalReceived - totalSpent) / timesOpened;
	    }
	}

	private static final Image[] NPC_AVATAR_POOL;
	static {
	    NPC_AVATAR_POOL = new Image[64];
	    Color[] avatarColors = {
	        new Color(255, 100, 100), new Color(100, 150, 255), new Color(100, 255, 150),
	        new Color(255, 200, 100), new Color(200, 100, 255), new Color(255, 150, 200),
	        new Color(150, 255, 255), new Color(255, 255, 100), new Color(255, 150, 100),
	        new Color(150, 100, 255), new Color(100, 255, 200), new Color(255, 100, 150)
	    };
	    for (int i = 0; i < NPC_AVATAR_POOL.length; i++) {
	        java.awt.image.BufferedImage img = new java.awt.image.BufferedImage(48, 48, java.awt.image.BufferedImage.TYPE_INT_ARGB);
	        java.awt.Graphics2D g2 = img.createGraphics();
	        g2.setRenderingHint(java.awt.RenderingHints.KEY_ANTIALIASING, java.awt.RenderingHints.VALUE_ANTIALIAS_ON);
	        g2.setColor(avatarColors[i % avatarColors.length]);
	        g2.fillOval(4, 4, 40, 40);
	        g2.setColor(java.awt.Color.WHITE);
	        g2.setFont(new java.awt.Font("Arial", java.awt.Font.BOLD, 20));
	        String initial = "" + (char)('A' + (i % 26));
	        java.awt.FontMetrics fm = g2.getFontMetrics();
	        int x = (48 - fm.stringWidth(initial)) / 2;
	        int y = ((48 - fm.getHeight()) / 2) + fm.getAscent();
	        g2.drawString(initial, x, y);
	        g2.dispose();
	        NPC_AVATAR_POOL[i] = img;
	    }
	}

	        this.inventoryValue = value;
	        this.avatar = avatar;
	        this.isPlayer = isPlayer;
	    }
	}
	static class ScrollablePanel extends JPanel implements Scrollable {
	    public boolean getScrollableTracksViewportWidth() { return true; }
	    public Dimension getPreferredScrollableViewportSize() { return getPreferredSize(); }
	    public int getScrollableUnitIncrement(java.awt.Rectangle r, int o, int d) { return 16; }
	    public int getScrollableBlockIncrement(java.awt.Rectangle r, int o, int d) { return 100; }
	    public boolean getScrollableTracksViewportHeight() { return false; }
	}
	
	public static class SaleRecord {
	    double price;
	    long timestamp;
	    String condition;
	    double itemFloat;
	    String skinName;
	    String specialVariant;
	    String buyerName;
	    Image buyerAvatar;
	    
	    public SaleRecord(double price, long timestamp, String condition, double itemFloat) {
	        this.price = price;
	        this.timestamp = timestamp;
	        this.condition = condition;
	        this.itemFloat = itemFloat;
	    }
	    
	    public SaleRecord(String skinName, double price, String condition, double itemFloat, String specialVariant) {
	        this.skinName = skinName;
	        this.price = price;
	        this.condition = condition;
	        this.itemFloat = itemFloat;
	        this.specialVariant = specialVariant;
	        this.timestamp = System.currentTimeMillis();
	        this.buyerName = generateRandomUsername();
	        this.buyerAvatar = generateRandomAvatar();
	    }
	    
	    private static String generateRandomUsername() {
	        return NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	    }
	    
	    private static Image generateRandomAvatar() {
	        return NPC_AVATAR_POOL[random.nextInt(NPC_AVATAR_POOL.length)];
	    }
	}
	
	public static class MarketListing {
	    InventoryItem item;
	    double listPrice;
	    int timeRemaining;
	    boolean isPlayerListing;
	    String sellerName;
	    Image sellerAvatar;
	    
	    public MarketListing(InventoryItem item, double listPrice, int timeRemaining, boolean isPlayerListing) {
	        this.item = item;
	        this.listPrice = listPrice;
	        this.timeRemaining = timeRemaining;
	        this.isPlayerListing = isPlayerListing;
	        this.sellerName = isPlayerListing ? "YOU" : generateRandomUsername();
	        this.sellerAvatar = isPlayerListing ? null : generateRandomAvatar();
	    }
	    
	    private static String generateRandomUsername() {
	        return NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	    }
	    
	    private static Image generateRandomAvatar() {
	        return NPC_AVATAR_POOL[random.nextInt(NPC_AVATAR_POOL.length)];
	    }
	}
	
	public static class BuyOrder {
	    String skinName;
	    double maxPrice;
	    String rarity;
	    String desiredCondition;
	    int quantity;
	    int filled;
	    long placedTime;
	    boolean notified;
	    long lastFillTime;

	    public BuyOrder(String skinName, double maxPrice, String rarity, String desiredCondition, int quantity) {
	        this.skinName         = skinName;
	        this.maxPrice         = maxPrice;
	        this.rarity           = rarity;
	        this.desiredCondition = desiredCondition;
	        this.quantity         = quantity;
	        this.filled           = 0;
	        this.placedTime       = System.currentTimeMillis();
	        this.notified         = false;
	        this.lastFillTime     = System.currentTimeMillis();
	    }
	    boolean isComplete() { return filled >= quantity; }
	    int remaining() { return quantity - filled; }
	}

	public static class NpcBuyOrder implements java.io.Serializable {
	    private static final long serialVersionUID = 2L;
	    String marketKey;
	    String condition;
	    double price;
	    int    quantity;
	    int    filled;
	    long   lastFillTime;
	    String buyerName;

	    NpcBuyOrder(String marketKey, String condition, double price, int quantity, String buyerName) {
	        this.marketKey    = marketKey;
	        this.condition    = condition;
	        this.price        = price;
	        this.quantity     = quantity;
	        this.filled       = 0;
	        this.lastFillTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
	        this.buyerName    = buyerName;
	    }

	    int remaining() { return quantity - filled; }
	}

	private class AnimationPanel extends JPanel {

	    private int scrollOffset = 0;
	    private ArrayList<AnimatedSkin> skinStrip = new ArrayList<>();
	    private int finalIndex = 50;
	    private int previousScrollOffset = 0;
	    private boolean isGoldReveal = false;

	    private Set<Image> gloveSet  = null;
	    private Set<Image> knifeSet  = null;
	    private Set<Image> redSet    = null;
	    private Set<Image> pinkSet   = null;
	    private Set<Image> purpleSet = null;

	    private void initRaritySetsIfNeeded() {
	        if (gloveSet == null) {
	            gloveSet  = new HashSet<>(java.util.Arrays.asList(gloveSkins));
	            knifeSet  = new HashSet<>(java.util.Arrays.asList(knifeSkins));
	            redSet    = new HashSet<>(java.util.Arrays.asList(redSkins));
	            pinkSet   = new HashSet<>(java.util.Arrays.asList(pinkSkins));
	            purpleSet = new HashSet<>(java.util.Arrays.asList(purpleSkins));
	        }
	    }

	    private class AnimatedSkin {
	        Image image;
	        boolean isStatTrak;

	        AnimatedSkin(Image image, boolean isStatTrak) {
	            this.image = image;
	            this.isStatTrak = isStatTrak;
	        }
	    }

	    public AnimationPanel() {
	        skinStrip.clear();

	        initRaritySetsIfNeeded();
	        boolean finalIsGold = (gloveSet != null && gloveSet.contains(finalSkin))
	                           || (knifeSet != null && knifeSet.contains(finalSkin))
	                           || finalSkinName.contains("Knife")
	                           || finalSkinName.contains("Gloves")
	                           || finalSkinName.contains("Doppler");
	        isGoldReveal = finalIsGold;

	        // Build collection-specific image pools for the animation strip
	        TradeUpCollection animCol = getCurrentCaseCollection();

	        // Build image lists for each rarity from this collection
	        java.util.List<Image> animBlue   = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	        java.util.List<Image> animPurple = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	        java.util.List<Image> animPink   = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	        java.util.List<Image> animRed    = new java.util.ArrayList<>();

	        if (animCol != null && !skinImageMap.isEmpty()) {
	            for (String s : animCol.milspecSkins)    { Image img = skinImageMap.get(s); if (img != null) animBlue.add(img); }
	            for (String s : animCol.restrictedSkins) { Image img = skinImageMap.get(s); if (img != null) animPurple.add(img); }
	            for (String s : animCol.classifiedSkins) { Image img = skinImageMap.get(s); if (img != null) animPink.add(img); }
	            for (String s : animCol.covertSkins)     { Image img = skinImageMap.get(s); if (img != null) animRed.add(img); }
	        }
	        // Fallback to global arrays if collection pools are empty
	        if (animBlue.isEmpty())   for (Image img : blueSkins)   animBlue.add(img);
	        if (animPurple.isEmpty()) for (Image img : purpleSkins) animPurple.add(img);
	        if (animPink.isEmpty())   for (Image img : pinkSkins)   animPink.add(img);
	        if (animRed.isEmpty())    for (Image img : redSkins)    animRed.add(img);

	        Image[] animBlueArr   = animBlue.toArray(new Image[0]);
	        Image[] animPurpleArr = animPurple.toArray(new Image[0]);
	        Image[] animPinkArr   = animPink.toArray(new Image[0]);
	        Image[] animRedArr    = animRed.toArray(new Image[0]);

	        for (int i = 0; i < 60; i++) {
	            Image skinToAdd;
	            boolean stattrakRoll = random.nextDouble() < 0.10;

	            if (i == finalIndex) {
	                skinToAdd = finalIsGold ? goldIconImage : finalSkin;
	                stattrakRoll = (isStattrak == 1);
	            } else {
	                double roll = random.nextDouble();
	                if (roll < 0.80) {
	                    skinToAdd = animBlueArr[random.nextInt(animBlueArr.length)];
	                } else if (roll < 0.96) {
	                    skinToAdd = animPurpleArr[random.nextInt(animPurpleArr.length)];
	                } else if (roll < 0.992) {
	                    skinToAdd = animPinkArr[random.nextInt(animPinkArr.length)];
	                } else {
	                    skinToAdd = animRedArr[random.nextInt(animRedArr.length)];
	                }
	            }

	            skinStrip.add(new AnimatedSkin(skinToAdd, stattrakRoll));
	        }
	    }
	    
	    @Override
	    protected void paintComponent(Graphics g) {
	        super.paintComponent(g);
	        Graphics2D g2d = (Graphics2D) g;

	        g2d.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_ANTIALIASING, RenderingHints.VALUE_ANTIALIAS_ON);
	        g2d.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_RENDERING, RenderingHints.VALUE_RENDER_QUALITY);

	        java.awt.GradientPaint bgGrad = new java.awt.GradientPaint(
	            0, 0, new Color(18, 18, 28),
	            0, getHeight(), new Color(28, 28, 42));
	        g2d.setPaint(bgGrad);
	        g2d.fillRect(0, 0, getWidth(), getHeight());

	        int centerX = getWidth() / 2;
	        int centerY = getHeight() / 2;

	        int circleRadius = Math.min(getWidth(), getHeight()) / 2 - 10;

	        for (int r = circleRadius + 60; r >= circleRadius; r -= 2) {
	            float alpha = 0.05f * ((circleRadius + 60 - r) / 60.0f);
	            g2d.setColor(new Color(0f, 0f, 0f, Math.min(alpha * 4, 0.55f)));
	            g2d.fillOval(centerX - r, centerY - r, r * 2, r * 2);
	        }

	        g2d.setColor(new Color(0, 0, 0, 140));
	        java.awt.geom.Area outside = new java.awt.geom.Area(new java.awt.Rectangle(0, 0, getWidth(), getHeight()));
	        outside.subtract(new java.awt.geom.Area(new java.awt.geom.Ellipse2D.Float(
	            centerX - circleRadius, centerY - circleRadius, circleRadius * 2, circleRadius * 2)));
	        g2d.fill(outside);

	        g2d.setColor(new Color(200, 200, 200, 60));
	        g2d.setStroke(new BasicStroke(2));
	        g2d.drawOval(centerX - circleRadius, centerY - circleRadius, circleRadius * 2, circleRadius * 2);

	        int skinWidth  = 210;
	        int skinHeight = 155;
	        int cardGap    = 6;
	        int rarityBarH = 8;
	        int startX     = -scrollOffset;

	        for (int i = 0; i < skinStrip.size(); i++) {
	            int x = startX + (i * (skinWidth + cardGap));
	            int y = (getHeight() - skinHeight) / 2;

	            if (x + skinWidth < 0 || x > getWidth()) continue;

	            AnimatedSkin anim = skinStrip.get(i);
	            Image skin = anim.image;

	            Color rarityColor = getAnimationRarityColor(skin);

	            g2d.setColor(new Color(55, 55, 65));
	            g2d.fillRoundRect(x, y, skinWidth, skinHeight, 8, 8);

	            g2d.setColor(new Color(80, 80, 95, 55));
	            g2d.fillRoundRect(x + 1, y + 1, skinWidth - 2, skinHeight / 3, 8, 8);

	            boolean isGoldIcon = (isGoldReveal && i == finalIndex && skin == goldIconImage);
	            int imgPad = isGoldIcon ? 16 : 10;
	            int imgW = skinWidth - imgPad * 2;
	            int imgH = skinHeight - rarityBarH - imgPad * 2;
	            int imgX = x + imgPad;
	            int imgY = y + imgPad;
	            g2d.drawImage(skin, imgX, imgY, imgW, imgH, null);

	            java.awt.GradientPaint barGrad = new java.awt.GradientPaint(
	                x, 0, rarityColor.darker(),
	                x + skinWidth, 0, rarityColor.brighter());
	            g2d.setPaint(barGrad);
	            g2d.fillRoundRect(x, y + skinHeight - rarityBarH, skinWidth, rarityBarH, 4, 4);
	            g2d.fillRect(x, y + skinHeight - rarityBarH, skinWidth, rarityBarH / 2);
	            g2d.setPaint(null);

	            if (anim.isStatTrak && !isGoldIcon) {
	                g2d.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 13));
	                String text = "StatTrak";
	                FontMetrics fm = g2d.getFontMetrics();
	                int tx = x + (skinWidth - fm.stringWidth(text)) / 2;
	                int ty = y + skinHeight - rarityBarH - 6;
	                g2d.setColor(new Color(0, 0, 0, 180));
	                g2d.drawString(text, tx + 1, ty + 1);
	                g2d.setColor(new Color(255, 140, 0));
	                g2d.drawString(text, tx, ty);
	            }
	        }

	        g2d.setColor(new Color(255, 215, 0));
	        g2d.setStroke(new BasicStroke(2));
	        g2d.drawLine(centerX, 0, centerX, getHeight());
	    }

	    private Color getAnimationRarityColor(Image skin) {
	        initRaritySetsIfNeeded();
	        if (skin == goldIconImage)                                  return new Color(228, 174,  57);
	        if (skin == finalSkin && finalSkinName.contains("Doppler")) return new Color(228, 174,  57);
	        if (gloveSet.contains(skin) || knifeSet.contains(skin))    return new Color(228, 174,  57);
	        if (redSet.contains(skin))                                  return new Color(235,  75,  75);
	        if (pinkSet.contains(skin))                                 return new Color(211,  44, 230);
	        if (purpleSet.contains(skin))                               return new Color(136,  71, 255);
	        return new Color(75, 105, 255);
	    }

	    public void setScrollOffset(int offset) {
	        int skinSpacing = 216;
	        
	        int currentCenterSkinIndex = (offset + 400) / skinSpacing;
	        int previousCenterSkinIndex = (previousScrollOffset + 400) / skinSpacing;
	        
	        if (currentCenterSkinIndex != previousCenterSkinIndex && 
	            currentCenterSkinIndex >= 0 && currentCenterSkinIndex < skinStrip.size()) {
	            playSoundFile("case_open.wav");
	        }
	        
	        previousScrollOffset = offset;
	        this.scrollOffset = offset;
	        repaint();
	    }

	    public int getFinalSkinPosition() {
	        return finalIndex * 216;
	    }
	}

	private void initializeMarketQueue() {
	    marketProcessQueue.clear();
	    marketProcessQueue.addAll(globalMarketListings.keySet());
	}
	
	private void loadAvatars() {
	    npcAvatars = new Image[20];
	    for (int i = 0; i < npcAvatars.length; i++) {
	        npcAvatars[i] = createNPCAvatar(i);
	    }
	    playerAvatar = createPlayerAvatar();
	}
	
	private Image createPlayerAvatar() {
	    BufferedImage img = new BufferedImage(64, 64, BufferedImage.TYPE_INT_ARGB);
	    Graphics2D g2 = img.createGraphics();
	    g2.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_ANTIALIASING, RenderingHints.VALUE_ANTIALIAS_ON);
	    
	    g2.setColor(new Color(50, 150, 255));
	    g2.fillOval(2, 2, 60, 60);
	    
	    g2.setColor(Color.WHITE);
	    g2.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 24));
	    String initial = "YOU";
	    g2.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    FontMetrics fm = g2.getFontMetrics();
	    int x = (64 - fm.stringWidth(initial)) / 2;
	    int y = ((64 - fm.getHeight()) / 2) + fm.getAscent();
	    g2.drawString(initial, x, y);
	    
	    g2.dispose();
	    return img;
	}

	private Image createNPCAvatar(int id) {
	    BufferedImage img = new BufferedImage(64, 64, BufferedImage.TYPE_INT_ARGB);
	    Graphics2D g2 = img.createGraphics();
	    g2.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_ANTIALIASING, RenderingHints.VALUE_ANTIALIAS_ON);
	    
	    Color[] colors = {
	        new Color(255, 100, 100),
	        new Color(100, 150, 255), 
	        new Color(100, 255, 150), 
	        new Color(255, 200, 100), 
	        new Color(200, 100, 255), 
	        new Color(255, 150, 200),
	        new Color(150, 255, 255), 
	        new Color(255, 255, 100), 
	        new Color(255, 150, 100),
	        new Color(150, 100, 255), 
	        new Color(100, 255, 200), 
	        new Color(255, 100, 150), 
	        new Color(200, 200, 100), 
	        new Color(100, 200, 255), 
	        new Color(255, 180, 200), 
	        new Color(180, 255, 180), 
	        new Color(200, 150, 255), 
	        new Color(255, 200, 150),
	        new Color(150, 200, 255),
	        new Color(255, 220, 150) 
	    };
	    
	    g2.setColor(colors[id % colors.length]);
	    g2.fillOval(2, 2, 60, 60);
	    
	    g2.setColor(Color.WHITE);
	    g2.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 24));
	    String initial = "" + (char)('A' + (id % 26));
	    FontMetrics fm = g2.getFontMetrics();
	    int x = (64 - fm.stringWidth(initial)) / 2;
	    int y = ((64 - fm.getHeight()) / 2) + fm.getAscent();
	    g2.drawString(initial, x, y);
	    
	    g2.dispose();
	    return img;
	}
	
	private void updateBalanceLabel() {
	    balanceLabel.setText(String.format("Balance: $%.2f", balance));
	    if (openCrateButton != null) {
	        openCrateButton.setEnabled(balance >= currentCase.price);
	        openCrateButton.setText(String.format("OPEN CASE  $%.2f", currentCase.price));
	    }
	}

	public JLabel makeLabel(int x, int y, int w, int h, int size) {
		JLabel lbl = new JLabel("", SwingConstants.CENTER);
		lbl.setBounds(x, y, w, h);
		lbl.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, size));
		return lbl;
	}

	public JLabel makeStatLabel(int x, int y, int w, int h, int size) {
		JLabel lbl = new JLabel("");
		lbl.setBounds(x, y, w, h);
		lbl.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, size));
		return lbl;
	}
	
	private JButton makeHeaderButton(String text, Color bg, Color fg) {
	    JButton btn = new JButton(text);
	    btn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    btn.setBackground(bg);
	    btn.setForeground(fg);
	    btn.setFocusPainted(false);
	    btn.setOpaque(true);
	    btn.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(65, 65, 85), 1),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(5, 12, 5, 12)));
	    btn.setCursor(new Cursor(Cursor.HAND_CURSOR));
	    Color hover = bg.brighter();
	    btn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) { btn.setBackground(hover); }
	        public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e)  { btn.setBackground(bg); }
	        public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) { btn.setBackground(hover.darker()); }
	        public void mouseReleased(MouseEvent e){ btn.setBackground(hover); }
	    });
	    return btn;
	}

	private void styleButton(JButton btn, Color bg, Color fg, Color border) {
	    btn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));
	    btn.setBackground(bg);
	    btn.setForeground(fg);
	    btn.setFocusPainted(false);
	    btn.setOpaque(true);
	    btn.setBorderPainted(true);
	    btn.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(border, 1),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(6, 14, 6, 14)));
	    btn.setCursor(new Cursor(Cursor.HAND_CURSOR));
	    Color hover = bg.brighter();
	    btn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) { btn.setBackground(hover); }
	        public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e)  { btn.setBackground(bg); }
	        public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) { btn.setBackground(hover.darker()); }
	        public void mouseReleased(MouseEvent e){ btn.setBackground(hover); }
	    });
	}

	private JButton makeIconButton(String text, Color bg, Color fg, Color border) {
	    JButton btn = new JButton(text);
	    styleButton(btn, bg, fg, border);
	    btn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    return btn;
	}
	private void styleComboBox(JComboBox<String> box) {
	    box.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    box.setBackground(Color.WHITE);
	    box.setForeground(Color.BLACK);
	    box.setUI(new javax.swing.plaf.basic.BasicComboBoxUI() {
	        @Override
	        protected JButton createArrowButton() {
	            JButton btn = super.createArrowButton();
	            btn.setBackground(Color.WHITE);
	            btn.setContentAreaFilled(false);
	            btn.setBorderPainted(false);
	            return btn;
	        }
	        @Override
	        public void installUI(javax.swing.JComponent c) {
	            super.installUI(c);
	            // Remove any extra padding that causes the white box artifact
	            comboBox.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(100, 100, 110), 1));
	        }
	    });
	    box.setBackground(Color.WHITE);
	    box.setForeground(Color.BLACK);
	    box.setRenderer(new DefaultListCellRenderer() {
	        @Override
	        public Component getListCellRendererComponent(
	                JList<?> list, Object value, int index,
	                boolean isSelected, boolean cellHasFocus) {
	            super.getListCellRendererComponent(list, value, index, isSelected, cellHasFocus);
	            setBackground(isSelected ? new Color(200, 220, 255) : Color.WHITE);
	            setForeground(Color.BLACK);
	            setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(2, 6, 2, 6));
	            return this;
	        }
	    });
	}

	private JLabel makeModernLabel(int x, int y, int w, int h, int size, Color color) {
	    JLabel lbl = new JLabel("", SwingConstants.LEFT);
	    lbl.setBounds(x, y, w, h);
	    lbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, size));
	    lbl.setForeground(color);
	    return lbl;
	}

	private static final Map<String, String> DOPPLER_FILES = new HashMap<>();
	static {
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("Karambit | Doppler (Phase 1)", "karamp1.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("Karambit | Doppler (Phase 2)", "karamp2.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("Karambit | Doppler (Phase 3)", "karamp3.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("Karambit | Doppler (Phase 4)", "karamp4.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("Karambit | Doppler (Sapphire)", "sapphirekaram.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("Karambit | Doppler (Ruby)", "rubykaram.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("Karambit | Doppler (Black Pearl)", "blackpearlkaram.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Phase 1)", "mninep1.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Phase 2)", "mninep2.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Phase 3)", "mninep3.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Phase 4)", "mninep4.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Sapphire)", "sapphiremnine.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Ruby)", "rubymnine.png");
	    DOPPLER_FILES.put("M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Black Pearl)", "blackpearlmnine.png");
	}

	private Image getKnifeImage(String skinName) {
	    if (imageCache.containsKey(skinName)) return imageCache.get(skinName);
	    for (Map.Entry<String, String> e : DOPPLER_FILES.entrySet()) {
	        if (skinName.contains(e.getKey())) {
	            Image img = new ImageIcon(e.getValue()).getImage();
	            imageCache.put(skinName, img);
	            return img;
	        }
	    }
	    return null;
	}
	
	private void refreshMainUI() {
	    revalidate();
	    repaint();
	}

	@Override
	public void paint(Graphics g) {
	    super.paint(g);
	}

	private void updateCrateImageDisplay() {
	    if (casesTabPanel == null) return;
	    if (crateImageLabel == null) {
	        crateImageLabel = new JLabel();

	        crateImageLabel.setBounds(240, 370, 280, 180);
	        crateImageLabel.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        casesTabPanel.add(crateImageLabel);
	        casesTabPanel.setComponentZOrder(crateImageLabel, 0);
	    }
	    if (crateImage != null) {
	        crateImageLabel.setIcon(new ImageIcon(crateImage.getScaledInstance(280, 200, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH)));
	    } else if (skinImage != null) {
	        crateImageLabel.setIcon(new ImageIcon(skinImage));
	    } else {
	        crateImageLabel.setIcon(null);
	    }
	    casesTabPanel.repaint();
	}
	
	private void stopAutoOpen() {
	    if (autoTimer != null) {
	        autoTimer.stop();
	        autoTimer = null;
	    }
	    autoStateOpen = false;
	    autoOpenButton.setText("AUTO OPEN");
	}

	private void selectCase(CaseType ct) {
	    playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
	    currentCase = ct;
	    currentCaseLabel.setText(ct.name);
	    openCrateButton.setText(String.format("OPEN CASE  $%.2f", ct.price));
	    updateBalanceLabel();

	    rebuildCaseBoxes();
	}

	private void rebuildCaseBoxes() {
	    Color BG_DARK   = new Color(15, 15, 20);
	    Color BG_CARD   = new Color(30, 30, 40);
	    Color ACCENT2   = new Color(95, 200, 255);
	    Color TEXT_DIM  = new Color(140, 140, 155);
	    Color BORDER    = new Color(45, 45, 60);
	    int boxW = 130, boxH = 80, boxY = 5, boxGap = 8;
	    CaseType[] orderedTypes = new CaseType[]{
	        CaseType.WEAPON_CASE_ONE, CaseType.BRAVO, CaseType.BREAKOUT, CaseType.SPECTRUM
	    };
	    int totalBoxRowWidth = orderedTypes.length * boxW + (orderedTypes.length - 1) * boxGap;
	    int boxStartX = Math.max(10, (760 - totalBoxRowWidth) / 2);

	    for (Component comp : casesTabPanel.getComponents()) {
	        if (comp instanceof JPanel && comp.getBounds().y == boxY && comp.getBounds().height == boxH) {
	            JPanel box = (JPanel) comp;
	            int idx = Math.round((float)(comp.getBounds().x - boxStartX) / (boxW + boxGap));
	            if (idx >= 0 && idx < orderedTypes.length) {
	                CaseType ct = orderedTypes[idx];
	                boolean selected = ct == currentCase;
	                box.setBackground(selected ? new Color(50, 80, 50) : BG_CARD);
	                box.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	                    BorderFactory.createLineBorder(selected ? new Color(80, 200, 80) : BORDER, selected ? 2 : 1),
	                    BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 6, 4, 6)));
	                for (Component inner : box.getComponents()) {
	                    if (inner instanceof JPanel) {
	                        inner.setBackground(selected ? new Color(50, 80, 50) : BG_CARD);
	                        for (Component lbl : ((JPanel)inner).getComponents()) {
	                            if (lbl instanceof JLabel) {
	                                ((JLabel)lbl).setForeground(
	                                    lbl == ((JPanel)inner).getComponent(0) ? 
	                                        (selected ? new Color(80, 220, 80) : ACCENT2) :
	                                        lbl == ((JPanel)inner).getComponent(1) ?
	                                        new Color(255, 210, 80) : TEXT_DIM
	                                );
	                            }
	                        }
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    casesTabPanel.repaint();
	}

	private void showCaseInfoWindow() {
	    JFrame infoFrame = new JFrame("Case Info");
	    infoFrame.setSize(820, 520);
	    infoFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    infoFrame.getContentPane().setBackground(new Color(15, 15, 20));
	    infoFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());

	    JTabbedPane caseTabs = new JTabbedPane(JTabbedPane.TOP);
	    caseTabs.setBackground(new Color(22, 22, 30));
	    caseTabs.setForeground(new Color(230, 230, 235));
	    caseTabs.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));

	    CaseType[] infoTypes = { CaseType.WEAPON_CASE_ONE, CaseType.BRAVO, CaseType.BREAKOUT, CaseType.SPECTRUM };
	    String[] colNames    = { "Weapon Case One", "Bravo Collection", "Breakout Collection", "Spectrum Collection" };

	    for (int ti = 0; ti < infoTypes.length; ti++) {
	        CaseType ct = infoTypes[ti];
	        String colName = colNames[ti];
	        boolean knivesCase = (ct == CaseType.WEAPON_CASE_ONE || ct == CaseType.BRAVO);

	        TradeUpCollection col = null;
	        for (TradeUpCollection c : TRADE_UP_COLLECTIONS)
	            if (c.collectionName.equals(colName)) { col = c; break; }

	        java.util.List<String[]> skins = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	        if (col != null) {
	            for (String s : col.milspecSkins)    skins.add(new String[]{s, "Mil-Spec"});
	            for (String s : col.restrictedSkins) skins.add(new String[]{s, "Restricted"});
	            for (String s : col.classifiedSkins) skins.add(new String[]{s, "Classified"});
	            for (String s : col.covertSkins)     skins.add(new String[]{s, "Covert"});
	        }
	        skins.add(new String[]{knivesCase ? "Rare Special Item (Knife)" : "Rare Special Item (Gloves)", "Gold"});

	        final boolean kc = knivesCase;
	        JPanel gridPanel = new JPanel(null);
	        gridPanel.setBackground(new Color(15, 15, 20));

	        int cardW = 115, cardH = 105, gap = 6, startX = 10, startY = 10;
	        int numCols = 6;
	        int numRows = (int) Math.ceil((double) skins.size() / numCols);
	        gridPanel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(790, startY + numRows * (cardH + gap) + 10));

	        for (int i = 0; i < skins.size(); i++) {
	            String skinName = skins.get(i)[0];
	            String rarity   = skins.get(i)[1];
	            int col2 = i % numCols;
	            int row  = i / numCols;
	            int x = startX + col2 * (cardW + gap);
	            int y = startY + row * (cardH + gap);

	            Color rarityCol;
	            switch (rarity) {
	                case "Restricted":  rarityCol = new Color(136, 71, 255); break;
	                case "Classified":  rarityCol = new Color(211, 44, 230); break;
	                case "Covert":      rarityCol = new Color(235, 75, 75);  break;
	                case "Gold":        rarityCol = new Color(228, 174, 57); break;
	                default:            rarityCol = new Color(75, 105, 255); break;
	            }

	            final Image skinImg;
	            if (rarity.equals("Gold")) {
	                skinImg = kc ? (knifeSkins != null && knifeSkins.length > 0 ? knifeSkins[0] : null)
	                             : (gloveSkins != null && gloveSkins.length > 0 ? gloveSkins[0] : null);
	            } else {
	                skinImg = skinImageMap.get(skinName);
	            }
	            final Color fRarityCol = rarityCol;
	            final Color CARD_BG = new Color(30, 30, 40);

	            JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(0, 0));
	            card.setBounds(x, y, cardW, cardH);
	            card.setBackground(CARD_BG);
	            card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(rarityCol, 2));

	            JPanel imgPanel = new JPanel() {
	                @Override protected void paintComponent(java.awt.Graphics g) {
	                    g.setColor(CARD_BG);
	                    g.fillRect(0, 0, getWidth(), getHeight());
	                    if (skinImg != null) {
	                        int pad = 5;
	                        g.drawImage(skinImg, pad, pad, getWidth() - pad * 2, getHeight() - pad * 2, null);
	                    }
	                }
	            };
	            imgPanel.setOpaque(false);

	            JPanel rarityBar = new JPanel() {
	                @Override protected void paintComponent(java.awt.Graphics g) {
	                    g.setColor(fRarityCol);
	                    g.fillRect(0, 0, getWidth(), getHeight());
	                }
	            };
	            rarityBar.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(cardW, 4));
	            rarityBar.setOpaque(false);

	            JLabel nameLabel2 = new JLabel("<html><div style=\'text-align:center\'>" + skinName + "</div></html>", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	            nameLabel2.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9));
	            nameLabel2.setForeground(rarity.equals("Gold") ? new Color(228, 174, 57) : new Color(220, 220, 230));
	            nameLabel2.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(cardW, 22));

	            card.add(rarityBar, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	            card.add(imgPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	            card.add(nameLabel2, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	            gridPanel.add(card);
	        }

	        JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(gridPanel);
	        scroll.setHorizontalScrollBarPolicy(JScrollPane.HORIZONTAL_SCROLLBAR_NEVER);
	        scroll.setVerticalScrollBarPolicy(JScrollPane.VERTICAL_SCROLLBAR_AS_NEEDED);
	        scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	        scroll.setBorder(null);
	        scroll.getViewport().setBackground(new Color(15, 15, 20));

	        caseTabs.addTab("  " + ct.name + "  ", scroll);
	    }

	    infoFrame.add(caseTabs, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    infoFrame.setVisible(true);
	}

	private void refreshInventoryTab() {
	    inventoryTabPanel.removeAll();
	    Color BG_DARK = new Color(15, 15, 20);
	    Color BG_PANEL = new Color(22, 22, 30);
	    Color BG_CARD = new Color(30, 30, 40);
	    Color ACCENT = new Color(247, 147, 30);
	    Color ACCENT2 = new Color(95, 200, 255);
	    Color TEXT_MAIN = new Color(230, 230, 235);
	    Color TEXT_DIM = new Color(140, 140, 155);
	    Color BORDER = new Color(45, 45, 60);

	    if (inventoryList.isEmpty()) {
	        JLabel empty = new JLabel("Your inventory is empty - open some cases!", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        empty.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 16));
	        empty.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	        inventoryTabPanel.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	        inventoryTabPanel.add(empty, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        inventoryTabPanel.revalidate();
	        inventoryTabPanel.repaint();
	        return;
	    }

	    JPanel controlPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(4, 1));
	    controlPanel.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    controlPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 1, 0, BORDER));

	    // Thumbnails are now cached inside each InventoryItem (getThumb110/getThumb130)
	    // so no local per-refresh cache is needed here.

	    JPanel searchPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 8, 6));
	    searchPanel.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    JLabel searchLabel = new JLabel("Search:");
	    searchLabel.setForeground(TEXT_MAIN);
	    searchLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    JTextField searchField = new JTextField(22);
	    searchField.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	    searchField.setForeground(TEXT_MAIN);
	    searchField.setCaretColor(TEXT_MAIN);
	    searchField.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 13));
	    searchPanel.add(searchLabel);
	    searchPanel.add(searchField);

	    JPanel sortPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 8, 6));
	    sortPanel.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    JLabel sortPriceLabel = new JLabel("Price:");
	    sortPriceLabel.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	    sortPriceLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    JComboBox<String> priceSortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{"Default","Highest Price","Lowest Price"});
	    priceSortBox.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	    styleComboBox(priceSortBox);

	    JLabel sortRarityLabel = new JLabel("Rarity:");
	    sortRarityLabel.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	    sortRarityLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    JComboBox<String> raritySortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{"Default","Knife","Gloves","Covert","Classified","Restricted","Milspec"});
	    raritySortBox.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	    styleComboBox(raritySortBox);

	    JLabel sortFloatLabel = new JLabel("Float:");
	    sortFloatLabel.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	    sortFloatLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    JComboBox<String> floatSortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{"Default","Lowest Float","Highest Float"});
	    floatSortBox.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	    styleComboBox(floatSortBox);

	    sortPanel.add(sortPriceLabel); sortPanel.add(priceSortBox);
	    sortPanel.add(sortRarityLabel); sortPanel.add(raritySortBox);
	    sortPanel.add(sortFloatLabel); sortPanel.add(floatSortBox);

	    JLabel sortSTLabel = new JLabel("StatTrak:");
	    sortSTLabel.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	    sortSTLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    JComboBox<String> stattrakSortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{"All", "StatTrak Only", "Non-StatTrak"});
	    styleComboBox(stattrakSortBox);

	    java.util.Set<String> colSet = new java.util.LinkedHashSet<>();
	    colSet.add("All");
	    for (InventoryItem it : inventoryList) {
	        if (it.collection != null && !it.collection.isEmpty()) colSet.add(it.collection);
	    }
	    JLabel sortColLabel = new JLabel("Collection:");
	    sortColLabel.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	    sortColLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    JComboBox<String> collectionSortBox = new JComboBox<>(colSet.toArray(new String[0]));
	    styleComboBox(collectionSortBox);

	    // StatTrak and Collection go on a second filter row
	    JPanel sortPanel2 = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 8, 6));
	    sortPanel2.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    sortPanel2.add(sortSTLabel); sortPanel2.add(stattrakSortBox);
	    sortPanel2.add(sortColLabel); sortPanel2.add(collectionSortBox);

	    JPanel sellPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 8, 6));
	    sellPanel.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    JLabel sellLabel = new JLabel("Quick Sell:");
	    sellLabel.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	    sellLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    JComboBox<String> sellRarityBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{"Default","Knife","Gloves","Covert","Classified","Restricted","Milspec"});
	    styleComboBox(sellRarityBox);
	    JButton sellRarityButton = new JButton("SELL RARITY");
	    styleButton(sellRarityButton, new Color(140, 80, 20), TEXT_MAIN, new Color(180, 110, 30));
	    JButton sellAllButton = new JButton("SELL ALL INVENTORY");
	    styleButton(sellAllButton, new Color(160, 40, 40), TEXT_MAIN, new Color(200, 60, 60));

	    JLabel invValueLabel = new JLabel();
	    invValueLabel.setForeground(ACCENT2);
	    invValueLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    invValueLabel.setText(String.format("  Inventory: $%.2f (%d items)", inventoryValue, inventoryList.size()));

	    JButton generateSkinBtn = new JButton("✦ GENERATE SKIN");
	    styleButton(generateSkinBtn, new Color(20, 80, 140), TEXT_MAIN, new Color(40, 120, 200));
	    generateSkinBtn.addActionListener(e -> showGenerateSkinDialog());
	    sellPanel.add(sellLabel); sellPanel.add(sellRarityBox); sellPanel.add(sellRarityButton); sellPanel.add(sellAllButton); sellPanel.add(generateSkinBtn); sellPanel.add(invValueLabel);

	    controlPanel.add(searchPanel);
	    controlPanel.add(sortPanel);
	    controlPanel.add(sortPanel2);
	    controlPanel.add(sellPanel);
	    inventoryTabPanel.add(controlPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 2, 8, 8));
	    grid.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 8, 8, 8));
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    scroll.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    scroll.getViewport().setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    optimizeScrollPane(scroll);
	    scroll.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(BORDER, 1));
	    inventoryTabPanel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    inventoryTabPanel.setBackground(BG_DARK);

	    Runnable rebuildGrid = () -> {
	        grid.removeAll();
	        String search = searchField.getText().toLowerCase().trim();
	        String rarityOrder2 = (String) raritySortBox.getSelectedItem();
	        String priceOrder = (String) priceSortBox.getSelectedItem();
	        String floatOrder = (String) floatSortBox.getSelectedItem();

	        String stattrakOrder = (String) stattrakSortBox.getSelectedItem();
	        String collectionOrder = (String) collectionSortBox.getSelectedItem();

	        List<InventoryItem> filtered = new ArrayList<>(inventoryList);
	        if (!search.isEmpty()) {
	            filtered.removeIf(it -> !it.name.toLowerCase().contains(search) &&
	                              !it.condition.toLowerCase().contains(search) &&
	                              !it.rarity.toLowerCase().contains(search));
	        }
	        if (!rarityOrder2.equals("Default")) {
	            filtered.removeIf(it -> !it.rarity.contains(rarityOrder2));
	        }
	        if ("StatTrak Only".equals(stattrakOrder)) filtered.removeIf(it -> !it.isStattrak);
	        if ("Non-StatTrak".equals(stattrakOrder))  filtered.removeIf(it ->  it.isStattrak);
	        if (!"All".equals(collectionOrder))        filtered.removeIf(it -> !collectionOrder.equals(it.collection));
	        if ("Highest Price".equals(priceOrder)) {
	            filtered.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.price.doubleValue(), a.price.doubleValue()));
	        } else if ("Lowest Price".equals(priceOrder)) {
	            filtered.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(a.price.doubleValue(), b.price.doubleValue()));
	        } else {
	            filtered.sort((a, b) -> Integer.compare(
	                RARITY_ORDER.getOrDefault(a.rarity.replace("StatTrak ",""), 99),
	                RARITY_ORDER.getOrDefault(b.rarity.replace("StatTrak ",""), 99)));
	        }
	        if ("Lowest Float".equals(floatOrder)) {
	            filtered.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(a.itemFloat, b.itemFloat));
	        } else if ("Highest Float".equals(floatOrder)) {
	            filtered.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.itemFloat, a.itemFloat));
	        }

	        int maxInitial = 60;
	        int toRender = Math.min(maxInitial, filtered.size());
	        for (int i = 0; i < toRender; i++) {
	            InventoryItem item = filtered.get(i);
	            JPanel card = createInventoryCardFast(item, item.getThumb110());
	            grid.add(card);
	        }
	        if (filtered.size() > maxInitial) {
	            JPanel loadMore = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	            loadMore.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	            JButton btn = new JButton("Load More... (" + (filtered.size() - maxInitial) + " more)");
	            styleButton(btn, BG_CARD, ACCENT2, BORDER);
	            btn.addActionListener(e -> {
	                loadMore.setVisible(false);
	                for (int i = maxInitial; i < filtered.size(); i++) {
	                    grid.add(createInventoryCardFast(filtered.get(i), filtered.get(i).getThumb110()),
	                             grid.getComponentCount() - 1);
	                }
	                grid.revalidate(); grid.repaint();
	            });
	            loadMore.add(btn, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	            grid.add(loadMore);
	        }
	        grid.revalidate(); grid.repaint();
	    };

	    grid.putClientProperty("rebuildGrid", rebuildGrid);
	    javax.swing.Timer searchTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(300, e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    searchTimer.setRepeats(false);
	    searchField.addKeyListener(new KeyAdapter() {
	        public void keyReleased(KeyEvent e) { searchTimer.restart(); }
	    });
	    priceSortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    raritySortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    floatSortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    stattrakSortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    collectionSortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());

	    sellRarityButton.addActionListener(e -> {
	        String rarity = (String) sellRarityBox.getSelectedItem();
	        if ("Default".equals(rarity)) {
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "Please select a rarity from the dropdown first.");
	            return;
	        }
	        int confirm = JOptionPane.showConfirmDialog(this,
	            "Sell all " + rarity + " items?",
	            "Confirm Sell Rarity", JOptionPane.YES_NO_OPTION);
	        if (confirm == JOptionPane.YES_OPTION) {
	            sellItemsByRarity(rarity);
	            refreshInventoryTab();
	        }
	    });

	    sellAllButton.addActionListener(e -> {
	        int confirm = JOptionPane.showConfirmDialog(this,
	            String.format("Sell your ENTIRE inventory (%d items)?%nSold to buy orders where possible. This cannot be undone!",
	                inventoryList.size()),
	            "Confirm Sell All", JOptionPane.YES_NO_OPTION, JOptionPane.WARNING_MESSAGE);
	        if (confirm == JOptionPane.YES_OPTION) {
	            sellItemsByRarity("All");
	            refreshInventoryTab();
	        }
	    });

	    SwingUtilities.invokeLater(rebuildGrid);
	    inventoryTabPanel.revalidate();
	    inventoryTabPanel.repaint();
	}

	private void refreshTradeUpTab() {

	    javax.swing.Timer existingSelTimer = (javax.swing.Timer) tradeUpTabPanel.getClientProperty("selTimer");
	    if (existingSelTimer != null) {
	        existingSelTimer.stop();
	    }
	    tradeUpTabPanel.removeAll();
	    Color BG_DARK = new Color(15, 15, 20);
	    Color BG_PANEL = new Color(22, 22, 30);
	    Color BG_CARD = new Color(30, 30, 40);
	    Color ACCENT = new Color(247, 147, 30);
	    Color ACCENT2 = new Color(95, 200, 255);
	    Color TEXT_MAIN = new Color(230, 230, 235);
	    Color TEXT_DIM = new Color(140, 140, 155);
	    Color BORDER = new Color(45, 45, 60);

	    tradeUpTabPanel.setBackground(BG_DARK);

	    if (inventoryList.size() < 10) {
	        JPanel info = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	        info.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	        JLabel lbl = new JLabel("<html><center>You need at least 10 skins to trade up.<br>Open more cases!</center></html>", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        lbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 16));
	        lbl.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	        info.add(lbl, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        tradeUpTabPanel.add(info, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        tradeUpTabPanel.revalidate();
	        tradeUpTabPanel.repaint();
	        return;
	    }

	    JPanel controlPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1));
	    controlPanel.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    controlPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 1, 0, BORDER));

	    JPanel searchPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 8, 6));
	    searchPanel.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    JLabel searchLabel = new JLabel("Search:");
	    searchLabel.setForeground(TEXT_MAIN);
	    searchLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    JTextField searchField = new JTextField(20);
	    searchField.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	    searchField.setForeground(TEXT_MAIN);
	    searchField.setCaretColor(TEXT_MAIN);
	    searchPanel.add(searchLabel); searchPanel.add(searchField);

	    JPanel filterPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 8, 6));
	    filterPanel.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    JLabel sortRarityLabel = new JLabel("Rarity:");
	    sortRarityLabel.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	    sortRarityLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    JComboBox<String> raritySortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{"Default","Industrial","Milspec","Restricted","Classified"});
	    styleComboBox(raritySortBox);
	    JLabel sortFloatLabel2 = new JLabel("Float:");
	    sortFloatLabel2.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	    sortFloatLabel2.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    JComboBox<String> floatSortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{"Ascending","Descending"});
	    styleComboBox(floatSortBox);
	    filterPanel.add(sortRarityLabel); filterPanel.add(raritySortBox);
	    filterPanel.add(sortFloatLabel2); filterPanel.add(floatSortBox);

	    controlPanel.add(searchPanel);
	    controlPanel.add(filterPanel);
	    tradeUpTabPanel.add(controlPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    ArrayList<InventoryItem> selectedItems = new ArrayList<>();
	    JLabel selectedLabel = new JLabel("Selected: 0/10", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    // Thumbnails cached inside InventoryItem — no local cache needed
	    selectedLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));
	    selectedLabel.setForeground(ACCENT2);

	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 2, 8, 8));
	    grid.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 8, 8, 8));
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    scroll.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    scroll.getViewport().setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    optimizeScrollPane(scroll);

	    JPanel bottomPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(8, 0));
	    bottomPanel.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    bottomPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(1, 0, 0, 0, BORDER),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 12, 8, 12)));

	    JPanel leftBottom = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1, 0, 2));
	    leftBottom.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    leftBottom.add(selectedLabel);
	    JLabel totalPriceLbl = new JLabel("Total value: $0.00", SwingConstants.LEFT);
	    totalPriceLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    totalPriceLbl.setForeground(ACCENT2);
	    leftBottom.add(totalPriceLbl);

	    JPanel rightBottom = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.RIGHT, 8, 0));
	    rightBottom.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    JButton outcomesBtn = new JButton("VIEW OUTCOMES");
	    styleButton(outcomesBtn, new Color(70, 100, 160), BG_DARK, new Color(150, 180, 255));
	    outcomesBtn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    outcomesBtn.setEnabled(false);
	    JButton tradeUpBtn = new JButton("TRADE UP (10 SELECTED)");
	    styleButton(tradeUpBtn, ACCENT, BG_DARK, ACCENT);
	    tradeUpBtn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 14));
	    tradeUpBtn.setEnabled(false);
	    rightBottom.add(outcomesBtn);
	    rightBottom.add(tradeUpBtn);

	    bottomPanel.add(leftBottom, BorderLayout.WEST);
	    bottomPanel.add(rightBottom, BorderLayout.EAST);

	    tradeUpTabPanel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    tradeUpTabPanel.add(bottomPanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    Runnable rebuildGrid = () -> {
	        grid.removeAll();
	        String search = searchField.getText().toLowerCase().trim();
	        String rarityFilter = (String) raritySortBox.getSelectedItem();
	        String floatSort = (String) floatSortBox.getSelectedItem();

	        List<InventoryItem> filtered = new ArrayList<>(inventoryList);
	        filtered.removeIf(it -> it.rarity.contains("Covert") || it.rarity.contains("Knife") || it.rarity.contains("Glove"));
	        if (!search.isEmpty()) {
	            filtered.removeIf(it -> !it.name.toLowerCase().contains(search));
	        }
	        if (!rarityFilter.equals("Default")) {
	            filtered.removeIf(it -> !it.rarity.contains(rarityFilter));
	        }
	        if ("Ascending".equals(floatSort)) {
	            filtered.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(a.itemFloat, b.itemFloat));
	        } else {
	            filtered.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.itemFloat, a.itemFloat));
	        }

	        String lockedRarity = selectedItems.isEmpty() ? null
	            : selectedItems.get(0).rarity;
	        for (InventoryItem item : filtered) {
	            String itemRarity = item.rarity;
	            if (lockedRarity != null && !itemRarity.equals(lockedRarity)
	                    && !selectedItems.contains(item)) {
	                continue;
	            }
	            JPanel card = createTradeUpCardFast(item, item.getThumb110(), selectedItems, grid);
	            grid.add(card);
	        }
	        grid.revalidate(); grid.repaint();
	    };

	    grid.putClientProperty("rebuildGrid", rebuildGrid);
	    javax.swing.Timer searchTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(300, e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    searchTimer.setRepeats(false);
	    searchField.addKeyListener(new KeyAdapter() {
	        public void keyReleased(KeyEvent e) { searchTimer.restart(); }
	    });
	    raritySortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    floatSortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());

	    tradeUpBtn.addActionListener(e -> executeTradeUp(selectedItems, tradeUpTabPanel));
	    outcomesBtn.addActionListener(e -> showTradeUpOutcomes(selectedItems));

	    javax.swing.Timer selTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(200, e -> {
	        selectedLabel.setText("Selected: " + selectedItems.size() + "/10");
	        double totalVal = selectedItems.stream().mapToDouble(it -> it.price.doubleValue()).sum();
	        totalPriceLbl.setText(String.format("Total value: $%.2f", totalVal));
	        boolean ready = selectedItems.size() == 10;
	        tradeUpBtn.setEnabled(ready);
	        outcomesBtn.setEnabled(selectedItems.size() > 0);
	    });
	    selTimer.start();
	    tradeUpTabPanel.putClientProperty("selTimer", selTimer);

	    SwingUtilities.invokeLater(rebuildGrid);
	    tradeUpTabPanel.revalidate();
	    tradeUpTabPanel.repaint();
	}

	private void showTradeUpOutcomes(ArrayList<InventoryItem> selectedItems) {
	    if (selectedItems.isEmpty()) return;
	    String baseRarity = selectedItems.get(0).rarity.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	    boolean isStatTrakInput = selectedItems.get(0).isStattrak;

	    String newRarity;
    if      (baseRarity.equals("Industrial")) newRarity = "Milspec";
    else if (baseRarity.equals("Milspec"))    newRarity = "Restricted";
    else if (baseRarity.equals("Restricted")) newRarity = "Classified";
    else if (baseRarity.equals("Classified")) newRarity = "Covert";
    else { JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "No outcomes for rarity: " + baseRarity); return; }

	    String[] weightedPool = resolveOutcomePool(selectedItems, baseRarity);
	    if (weightedPool.length == 0) { JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "No outcomes found."); return; }

	    java.util.LinkedHashMap<String, Integer> skinWeights = new java.util.LinkedHashMap<>();
	    for (String s : weightedPool) skinWeights.merge(s, 1, Integer::sum);
	    String[] names = skinWeights.keySet().toArray(new String[0]);
	    int totalWeight = weightedPool.length;

	    double totalNormFloat = 0.0;
	    for (InventoryItem item : selectedItems) {
	        FloatRange fr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(item.name);
	        if (fr == null) for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e2 : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet())
	            if (item.name.startsWith(e2.getKey())) { fr = e2.getValue(); break; }
	        double iMin = (fr != null && fr.min != null) ? fr.min : 0.0;
	        double iMax = (fr != null && fr.max != null) ? fr.max : 1.0;
	        totalNormFloat += (item.itemFloat - iMin) / Math.max(0.0001, iMax - iMin);
	    }
	    double avgNorm = totalNormFloat / selectedItems.size();

	    double inputTotal  = selectedItems.stream().mapToDouble(it -> it.price.doubleValue()).sum();
	    double marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(newRarity, 1.0);
	    double stMult      = isStatTrakInput ? 2.0 : 1.0;

	    double[] estPrices     = new double[names.length];
	    double[] estFloats     = new double[names.length];
	    String[] estConditions = new String[names.length];
	    double[] odds          = new double[names.length];

	    for (int idx = 0; idx < names.length; idx++) {
	        String sn = names[idx];
	        odds[idx] = (double) skinWeights.get(sn) / totalWeight;
	        FloatRange fr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(sn);
	        if (fr == null) for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e2 : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet())
	            if (sn.startsWith(e2.getKey())) { fr = e2.getValue(); break; }
	        double oMin = (fr != null && fr.min != null) ? fr.min : 0.0;
	        double oMax = (fr != null && fr.max != null) ? fr.max : 1.0;
	        double pFloat = Math.max(oMin, Math.min(oMax, oMin + avgNorm * (oMax - oMin)));
	        estFloats[idx] = pFloat;
	        String cond;
	        if      (pFloat <= 0.07) cond = "Factory New";
	        else if (pFloat <= 0.15) cond = "Minimal Wear";
	        else if (pFloat <= 0.38) cond = "Field-Tested";
	        else if (pFloat <= 0.45) cond = "Well-Worn";
	        else                     cond = "Battle-Scarred";
	        estConditions[idx] = cond;
	        double cMult = cond.equals("Factory New") ? 2.5 : cond.equals("Minimal Wear") ? 1.7 :
	                       cond.equals("Field-Tested") ? 1.0 : cond.equals("Well-Worn") ? 0.7 : 0.3;
	        estPrices[idx] = getBasePrice(sn) * cMult * marketMulti * stMult;
	    }

	    java.util.List<Integer> order = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	    for (int i = 0; i < names.length; i++) order.add(i);
	    order.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(estPrices[b], estPrices[a]));

	    double totalEV = 0; double profitOdds = 0;
	    for (int idx = 0; idx < names.length; idx++) {
	        totalEV += estPrices[idx] * odds[idx];
	        if (estPrices[idx] > inputTotal) profitOdds += odds[idx];
	    }
	    double avgReturn = totalEV / inputTotal * 100.0;
	    boolean profitable = avgReturn >= 100.0;

	    JFrame frame = new JFrame("Trade-Up Outcomes");
	    frame.setSize(820, 640);
	    frame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    frame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    frame.getContentPane().setBackground(new Color(20, 20, 28));

	    JPanel headerPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1, 0, 2));
	    headerPanel.setBackground(new Color(20, 20, 28));
	    headerPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(12, 12, 8, 12));
	    JLabel returnLbl = new JLabel(String.format("Expected return: %.1f%%", avgReturn), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    returnLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 15));
	    returnLbl.setForeground(profitable ? new Color(60, 220, 60) : new Color(220, 60, 60));
	    JLabel oddsLbl = new JLabel(String.format(
	        "Odds to profit: %.1f%%  (cost $%.2f  ->  avg outcome $%.2f)",
	        profitOdds * 100, inputTotal, totalEV), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    oddsLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));
	    oddsLbl.setForeground(new Color(200, 200, 215));
	    headerPanel.add(returnLbl); headerPanel.add(oddsLbl);
	    frame.add(headerPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 3, 8, 8));
	    grid.setBackground(new Color(20, 20, 28));
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 12, 12, 12));

	    for (int idx : order) {
	        String skinName = names[idx];
	        double estPrice = estPrices[idx];
	        double estFloat = estFloats[idx];
	        String cond     = estConditions[idx];
	        double chance   = odds[idx] * 100;
	        boolean isProfit = estPrice > inputTotal;
	        String colName  = getCollectionName(skinName);

	        JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(4, 2));
	        card.setBackground(isProfit ? new Color(20, 45, 20) : new Color(45, 20, 20));
	        card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(isProfit ? new Color(60, 180, 60) : new Color(180, 60, 60), 2),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 8, 8, 8)));

	        JLabel nameLbl = new JLabel("<html>" + skinName.replace("|", "<br>") + "</html>", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        nameLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11)); nameLbl.setForeground(Color.WHITE);

	        JLabel priceLbl = new JLabel(String.format("~$%.2f (%s)", estPrice, cond), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        priceLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 10));
	        priceLbl.setForeground(isProfit ? new Color(100, 220, 100) : new Color(220, 100, 100));

	        JLabel floatLbl = new JLabel(String.format("Float: %.6f", estFloat), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        floatLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9)); floatLbl.setForeground(new Color(95, 200, 255));

	        JLabel chanceLbl = new JLabel(String.format("%.1f%% chance", chance), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        chanceLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9)); chanceLbl.setForeground(new Color(160, 160, 180));

	        JLabel profitLbl = new JLabel(
	            isProfit ? String.format("+$%.2f PROFIT", estPrice - inputTotal)
	                     : String.format("-$%.2f LOSS",   inputTotal - estPrice), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        profitLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));
	        profitLbl.setForeground(isProfit ? new Color(80, 220, 80) : new Color(220, 80, 80));

	        JLabel colLbl = new JLabel(colName != null ? colName : "", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        colLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.ITALIC, 8)); colLbl.setForeground(new Color(170, 130, 255));

	        JPanel text = new JPanel(new GridLayout(6, 1, 0, 1));
	        text.setOpaque(false);
	        text.add(nameLbl); text.add(priceLbl); text.add(floatLbl);
	        text.add(chanceLbl); text.add(profitLbl); text.add(colLbl);
	        card.add(text, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        grid.add(card);
	    }

	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    scroll.getViewport().setBackground(new Color(20, 20, 28));
	    scroll.setBorder(null);
	    frame.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JPanel legend = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.CENTER, 20, 6));
	    legend.setBackground(new Color(25, 25, 33));
	    JLabel g = new JLabel("[*] Profit"); g.setForeground(new Color(80,200,80)); g.setFont(new Font("Consolas",Font.BOLD,11));
	    JLabel r = new JLabel("[*] Loss");   r.setForeground(new Color(200,80,80)); r.setFont(new Font("Consolas",Font.BOLD,11));
	    legend.add(g); legend.add(r);
	    frame.add(legend, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    frame.setVisible(true);
	}

	private void executeTradeUp(ArrayList<InventoryItem> selectedItems, JPanel parentPanel) {
	    if (selectedItems.size() != 10) {
	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "Please select exactly 10 skins!"); return;
	    }
	    String baseRarity = selectedItems.get(0).rarity.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	    for (InventoryItem item : selectedItems) {
	        if (!item.rarity.replace("StatTrak ", "").equals(baseRarity)) {
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "All selected skins must be of the same rarity!"); return;
	        }
	    }
	    double selectedValue = 0;
	    for (InventoryItem item : selectedItems) selectedValue += item.price.doubleValue();
	    inventoryList.removeAll(selectedItems);
	    inventoryValue = Math.max(0.0, inventoryValue - selectedValue);

	    String newRarity;
	    if      (baseRarity.equals("Industrial")) { newRarity="Milspec"; }
	    else if (baseRarity.equals("Milspec"))    { newRarity="Restricted"; totMil   = Math.max(0, totMil-10);   totRes++;   }
	    else if (baseRarity.equals("Restricted")) { newRarity="Classified"; totRes   = Math.max(0, totRes-10);   totClass++; }
	    else if (baseRarity.equals("Classified")) { newRarity="Covert";     totClass = Math.max(0, totClass-10); totCov++;   }
	    else { JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "Cannot trade up: " + baseRarity); return; }
	    writeStats(); repaint();

	    String[] weightedPool = resolveOutcomePool(selectedItems, baseRarity);
	    if (weightedPool.length == 0) { JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "No outcomes found."); return; }

	    int roll = random.nextInt(weightedPool.length);
	    String skinName = weightedPool[roll];

	    Image skin = getSkinImageFromName(skinName);
	    if (skin == null) {

	        Image[] fallbackSkins = newRarity.equals("Restricted") ? purpleSkins
	                              : newRarity.equals("Classified") ? pinkSkins : redSkins;
	        skin = fallbackSkins[random.nextInt(fallbackSkins.length)];
	    }

	    FloatRange outputFR = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(skinName);
	    if (outputFR == null) for (Map.Entry<String,FloatRange> e2:FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet())
	        if (skinName.startsWith(e2.getKey())) { outputFR=e2.getValue(); break; }
	    double outputMin = (outputFR!=null&&outputFR.min!=null)?outputFR.min:0.0;
	    double outputMax = (outputFR!=null&&outputFR.max!=null)?outputFR.max:1.0;
	    double totalNorm = 0.0;
	    for (InventoryItem item : selectedItems) {
	        FloatRange fr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(item.name);
	        if (fr==null) for (Map.Entry<String,FloatRange> e2:FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet())
	            if (item.name.startsWith(e2.getKey())) { fr=e2.getValue(); break; }
	        double iMin=(fr!=null&&fr.min!=null)?fr.min:0.0;
	        double iMax=(fr!=null&&fr.max!=null)?fr.max:1.0;
	        totalNorm += (item.itemFloat-iMin)/Math.max(0.0001,iMax-iMin);
	    }
	    double avgNorm = totalNorm / selectedItems.size();
	    double outputFloat = Math.max(outputMin, Math.min(outputMax, outputMin + avgNorm*(outputMax-outputMin)));

	    String condition;
	    if      (outputFloat<=0.07) condition="Factory New";
	    else if (outputFloat<=0.15) condition="Minimal Wear";
	    else if (outputFloat<=0.38) condition="Field-Tested";
	    else if (outputFloat<=0.45) condition="Well-Worn";
	    else                        condition="Battle-Scarred";

	    double mMult  = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(newRarity, 1.0);
	    double bp     = getBasePrice(skinName);
	    bp *= condition.equals("Factory New")?2.5:condition.equals("Minimal Wear")?1.7:
	           condition.equals("Field-Tested")?1.0:condition.equals("Well-Worn")?0.7:0.3;
	    bp *= mMult;
	    boolean isST = selectedItems.stream().allMatch(it->it.isStattrak);
	    if (isST) bp *= 2.0;
	    String rarityLabel = isST ? "StatTrak "+newRarity : newRarity;

	    // Store at 130x88 max — enough for all display uses; avoids keeping 280x200 per item
	    double scl = Math.min(130.0/skin.getWidth(null), 88.0/skin.getHeight(null));
	    Image scaledSkin = skin.getScaledInstance((int)(skin.getWidth(null)*scl),(int)(skin.getHeight(null)*scl),Image.SCALE_SMOOTH);

	    int pid = random.nextInt(1000);
	    String bgTier = getBlueGemTier(skinName, pid);
	    if (bgTier!=null) {
	        skinName=skinName+" ("+bgTier+")";
	        bp=applyBlueGemMultiplier(skinName.replace(" ("+bgTier+")",""),pid,bgTier,bp);
	    }

	    String colName = getCollectionName(skinName.replace(bgTier!=null?" ("+bgTier+")":"","").trim());
	    InventoryItem result = new InventoryItem(new ImageIcon(scaledSkin), skinName, condition, rarityLabel,
	        BigDecimal.valueOf(bp).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP), outputFloat, isST, pid, bgTier, bp);
	    result.collection = colName;
	    inventoryList.add(result);
	    inventoryValue += bp;
	    newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	    totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	    newAvgFloat = BigDecimal.valueOf(outputFloat).setScale(6, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	    if (lowestFloat > outputFloat) lowestFloat = outputFloat;

	    String msg = "Trade-Up successful! You received:\n"
	        + (isST?"StatTrak ":"") + skinName + " (" + newRarity + ")"
	        + "\nCondition: " + condition + "\nFloat: " + newAvgFloat
	        + "\nValue: $" + String.format("%.2f", bp)
	        + (colName!=null ? "\nCollection: " + colName : "");
	    missionTradeUps++;
	    checkMissionProgress();
	    selectedItems.clear();
	    JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, msg);
	    refreshTradeUpTab();
	}

	private void refreshMarketTab() {
	    if (marketTabBuilt) return;
	    marketTabBuilt = true;
	    marketTabPanel.removeAll();
	    Color BG_DARK = new Color(15, 15, 20);
	    Color BG_PANEL = new Color(22, 22, 30);
	    Color BG_CARD = new Color(30, 30, 40);
	    Color ACCENT = new Color(247, 147, 30);
	    Color ACCENT2 = new Color(95, 200, 255);
	    Color TEXT_MAIN = new Color(230, 230, 235);
	    Color TEXT_DIM = new Color(140, 140, 155);
	    Color BORDER = new Color(45, 45, 60);

	    marketTabPanel.setBackground(BG_DARK);

	    if (globalMarketListings.isEmpty()) {
	        generateGlobalMarketListings();
	        generateNpcBuyOrders();
	        purgeStaleNpcBuyOrders();
	    }

	    JPanel topPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1));
	    topPanel.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    topPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 1, 0, BORDER));

	    JPanel pricePanel = new JPanel();
	    pricePanel.setLayout(new BoxLayout(pricePanel, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    pricePanel.setBackground(BG_PANEL);

	    JPanel priceRow1 = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 8, 2));
	    priceRow1.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    JLabel priceLbl = new JLabel("Prices: ");
	    priceLbl.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	    priceLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	    priceRow1.add(priceLbl);

	    String[] rarityOrder = {"Knife", "Gloves", "Covert", "Classified", "Restricted", "Milspec", "Industrial"};
	    Map<String, JLabel> rarityPriceLabels = new java.util.LinkedHashMap<>();
	    for (String r : rarityOrder) {
	        if (!marketPriceMultipliers.containsKey(r)) continue;
	        double changeFromBase = (marketPriceMultipliers.get(r) - 1.0) * 100.0;
	        String changeStr = String.format("%+.1f%%", changeFromBase);
	        Color changeColor = changeFromBase > 0 ? new Color(80, 220, 120)
	                          : changeFromBase < 0 ? new Color(220, 80, 80)
	                          : getRarityColor(r);
	        JLabel lbl = new JLabel(r + ": " + changeStr + "  ");
	        lbl.setForeground(changeColor);
	        lbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	        priceRow1.add(lbl);
	        rarityPriceLabels.put(r, lbl);
	    }

	    JPanel priceRow2 = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 8, 2));
	    priceRow2.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    JButton chartBtn = new JButton("PRICE HISTORY");
	    styleButton(chartBtn, BG_CARD, ACCENT2, BORDER);
	    chartBtn.addActionListener(ev -> showPriceHistoryChart());
	    priceRow2.add(chartBtn);

	    pricePanel.add(priceRow1);
	    pricePanel.add(priceRow2);

	    JPanel infoPanel2 = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 8, 5));
	    infoPanel2.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    JLabel listingsInfo = new JLabel("Active Listings: " + activeListings.size() + "  |  Buy Orders: " + buyOrders.size());
	    listingsInfo.setForeground(ACCENT2);
	    listingsInfo.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    infoPanel2.add(listingsInfo);

	    topPanel.add(pricePanel);
	    topPanel.add(infoPanel2);
	    marketTabPanel.add(topPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    
	    javax.swing.Timer headerRefreshTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(MARKET_UPDATE_INTERVAL, ev -> {
	        for (Map.Entry<String, JLabel> e2 : rarityPriceLabels.entrySet()) {
	            String r = e2.getKey();
	            JLabel lbl = e2.getValue();
	            double ch = (marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(r, 1.0) - 1.0) * 100.0;
	            lbl.setText(r + ": " + String.format("%+.1f%%", ch) + "  ");
	            lbl.setForeground(ch > 0 ? new Color(80, 220, 120)
	                            : ch < 0 ? new Color(220, 80, 80)
	                            : getRarityColor(r));
	        }
	        listingsInfo.setText("Active Listings: " + activeListings.size() + "  |  Buy Orders: " + buyOrders.size());
	    });
	    headerRefreshTimer.setRepeats(true);
	    headerRefreshTimer.start();
	    
	    final javax.swing.Timer hrt = headerRefreshTimer;
	    java.awt.event.ActionListener stopListener = ev3 -> {
	        if (mainTabs.getSelectedIndex() != 4) hrt.stop();
	    };
	    mainTabs.addChangeListener(ev3 -> stopListener.actionPerformed(null));

	    JTabbedPane marketTabs = new JTabbedPane();
	    marketTabs.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    marketTabs.setForeground(TEXT_MAIN);

	    JPanel knivesPanel = createMainMarketPanel("knives");
	    marketTabs.addTab("Knives", knivesPanel);
	    JPanel glovesPanel = createMainMarketPanel("gloves");
	    marketTabs.addTab("Gloves", glovesPanel);
	    JPanel regularSkinsPanel = createMainMarketPanel("regular");
	    marketTabs.addTab("Regular Skins", regularSkinsPanel);
	    JPanel armouryPassPanel = createMainMarketPanel("armoury");
	    marketTabs.addTab("Armoury Pass", armouryPassPanel);
	    JPanel myListingsPanel = createMyListingsPanel();
	    marketTabs.addTab("My Listings", myListingsPanel);
	    JPanel buyOrdersPanel2 = createBuyOrdersPanel();
	    marketTabs.addTab("My Buy Orders", buyOrdersPanel2);

	    JPanel recentSalesPanel2 = createRecentSalesPanel();
	    marketTabs.addTab("Market Sales", recentSalesPanel2);
	    JPanel playerPurchasesPanel2 = createPlayerPurchasesPanel();
	    marketTabs.addTab("My Purchases", playerPurchasesPanel2);

	    marketTabPanel.add(marketTabs, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    marketTabPanel.revalidate();
	    marketTabPanel.repaint();
	}


	// Terrorist slots
	private static final String[] T_SLOTS_PISTOL   = {"Glock-18"};
	private static final String[] T_SLOTS_OTHER    = {"Tec-9", "Desert Eagle", "P250", "CZ75-Auto", "Dual Berettas", "R8 Revolver"};
	private static final String[] T_SLOTS_SMG      = {"MAC-10", "P90", "UMP-45", "PP-Bizon", "MP7", "MP5-SD"};
	private static final String[] T_SLOTS_HEAVY    = {"XM1014", "Nova", "Sawed-Off", "Negev", "M249"};
	private static final String[] T_SLOTS_MID      = T_SLOTS_SMG; // kept for compatibility
	private static final String[] T_SLOTS_RIFLE    = {"AK-47", "Galil AR", "SG 553", "AWP", "SSG 08", "G3SG1"};
	// Counter-Terrorist slots
	private static final String[] CT_SLOTS_PISTOL  = {"USP-S", "P2000"};
	private static final String[] CT_SLOTS_OTHER   = {"P250", "Five-SeveN", "CZ75-Auto", "Desert Eagle", "R8 Revolver", "Dual Berettas"};
	private static final String[] CT_SLOTS_SMG     = {"MP9", "MP7", "MP5-SD", "UMP-45", "P90", "PP-Bizon"};
	private static final String[] CT_SLOTS_HEAVY   = {"Nova", "XM1014", "MAG-7", "M249", "Negev"};
	private static final String[] CT_SLOTS_RIFLE   = {"FAMAS", "M4A4", "M4A1-S", "AUG", "SSG 08", "AWP", "SCAR-20"};
	// Knife slot (shared key between both sides — same knife equipped on both)
	private static final String KNIFE_SLOT = "Knife";

	// Track which side sub-tab is selected so refresh restores it
	private int loadoutSelectedSide = 0;
	private int loadoutScrollYT  = 0; // remembered scroll position for T side
	private int loadoutScrollYCT = 0; // remembered scroll position for CT side
	private JScrollPane loadoutScrollPaneT  = null;
	private JScrollPane loadoutScrollPaneCT = null;

	private void refreshLoadoutTab() {
	    // Save current scroll position from the correct pane before tearing down
	    if (loadoutScrollPaneT  != null) loadoutScrollYT  = loadoutScrollPaneT.getVerticalScrollBar().getValue();
	    if (loadoutScrollPaneCT != null) loadoutScrollYCT = loadoutScrollPaneCT.getVerticalScrollBar().getValue();
	    loadoutTabPanel.removeAll();
	    loadoutTabPanel.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    loadoutTabPanel.setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 20));

	    JLabel headerLbl = new JLabel("  LOADOUT", SwingConstants.LEFT);
	    headerLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 20));
	    headerLbl.setForeground(new Color(247, 147, 30));
	    headerLbl.setOpaque(true);
	    headerLbl.setBackground(new Color(18, 18, 30));
	    headerLbl.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 2, 0, new Color(247, 147, 30)),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 18, 10, 18)));
	    loadoutTabPanel.add(headerLbl, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JTabbedPane sides = new JTabbedPane(JTabbedPane.TOP);
	    sides.setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 20));
	    sides.setForeground(new Color(230, 230, 235));
	    sides.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 14));
	    sides.addTab("  TERRORIST  ",         buildLoadoutSidePanel(true));
	    sides.addTab("  COUNTER-TERRORIST  ", buildLoadoutSidePanel(false));
	    sides.setSelectedIndex(loadoutSelectedSide);
	    sides.addChangeListener(ev -> loadoutSelectedSide = sides.getSelectedIndex());
	    loadoutTabPanel.add(sides, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    loadoutTabPanel.revalidate();
	    loadoutTabPanel.repaint();
	}

	private JPanel buildLoadoutSidePanel(boolean isTSide) {
	    Color BG_DARK  = new Color(12, 12, 20);
	    Color BG_PANEL = new Color(20, 20, 32);
	    Color BG_CARD  = new Color(28, 28, 42);
	    Color ACCENT   = isTSide ? new Color(247, 147, 30) : new Color(95, 200, 255);
	    Color TEXT     = new Color(220, 220, 235);

	    JPanel root = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(0, 0));
	    root.setBackground(BG_DARK);

	    // ── Agent panel (left) ──────────────────────────────────────────────
	    JPanel agentPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    agentPanel.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    agentPanel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(220, 0));
	    agentPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 0, 2, new Color(45, 45, 60)),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(16, 12, 16, 12)));

	    JPanel agentInner = new JPanel();
	    agentInner.setLayout(new BoxLayout(agentInner, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    agentInner.setBackground(BG_PANEL);

	    JLabel agentIcon = new JLabel(isTSide ? "T" : "CT", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    agentIcon.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 72));
	    agentIcon.setForeground(new Color(ACCENT.getRed(), ACCENT.getGreen(), ACCENT.getBlue(), 55));
	    agentIcon.setAlignmentX(0.5f);

	    JLabel agentLabel = new JLabel(isTSide ? "Terrorist" : "Counter-Terrorist", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    agentLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));
	    agentLabel.setForeground(ACCENT);
	    agentLabel.setAlignmentX(0.5f);

	    JLabel agentSub = new JLabel("Agent coming soon", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    agentSub.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 10));
	    agentSub.setForeground(new Color(80, 80, 110));
	    agentSub.setAlignmentX(0.5f);

	    agentInner.add(Box.createVerticalGlue());
	    agentInner.add(agentIcon);
	    agentInner.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 6)));
	    agentInner.add(agentLabel);
	    agentInner.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 2)));
	    agentInner.add(agentSub);
	    agentInner.add(Box.createVerticalGlue());
	    agentPanel.add(agentInner, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    root.add(agentPanel, BorderLayout.WEST);

	    // ── Weapon grid (right) — uses WrapLayout so all guns fit without horizontal scroll ──
	    Map<String, InventoryItem> loadout = isTSide ? tLoadout : ctLoadout;

	    // Build section definitions
	    String[][] sectionTitles;
	    String[][][] sectionSlots;
	    if (isTSide) {
	        sectionTitles = new String[][]{
	            {"STARTING PISTOL"},
	            {"PISTOLS"},
	            {"SMGs"},
	            {"HEAVY"},
	            {"RIFLES"}
	        };
	        sectionSlots = new String[][][]{
	            {T_SLOTS_PISTOL},
	            {T_SLOTS_OTHER},
	            {T_SLOTS_SMG},
	            {T_SLOTS_HEAVY},
	            {T_SLOTS_RIFLE}
	        };
	    } else {
	        sectionTitles = new String[][]{
	            {"STARTING PISTOL"},
	            {"PISTOLS"},
	            {"SMGs"},
	            {"HEAVY"},
	            {"RIFLES"}
	        };
	        sectionSlots = new String[][][]{
	            {CT_SLOTS_PISTOL},
