	            {CT_SLOTS_OTHER},
	            {CT_SLOTS_SMG},
	            {CT_SLOTS_HEAVY},
	            {CT_SLOTS_RIFLE}
	        };
	    }

	    // ScrollablePanel: tells the scroll pane to never scroll horizontally,
	    // so WrapLayout always wraps based on the viewport width (fixes last card being cut off).
	    ScrollablePanel weaponArea = new ScrollablePanel();
	    weaponArea.setLayout(new BoxLayout(weaponArea, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    weaponArea.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    // Extra right padding so the vertical scrollbar never clips the last card
	    weaponArea.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 8, 16, 20));

	    // Append KNIFE and GLOVES as final sections in the weapon grid
	    int totalSections = sectionTitles.length + 2; // +1 for knife, +1 for gloves
	    for (int si = 0; si < totalSections; si++) {
	        boolean isKnifeSection  = (si == totalSections - 2);
	        boolean isGlovesSection = (si == totalSections - 1);
	        String sectionTitle = isKnifeSection ? "KNIFE" : isGlovesSection ? "GLOVES" : sectionTitles[si][0];

	        // Section label
	        JPanel secHdr = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 4, 2));
	        secHdr.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	        secHdr.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 26));
	        JLabel secLbl = new JLabel("\u25BC  " + sectionTitle);
	        secLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));
	        secLbl.setForeground(ACCENT);
	        secHdr.add(secLbl);
	        weaponArea.add(secHdr);

	        // Cards in a WrapLayout panel so they wrap to next line automatically
	        JPanel cardsRow = new JPanel(new WrapLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 6, 4));
	        cardsRow.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	        if (isKnifeSection) {
	            // Knife slot — each side has its own knife loadout key
	            String knifeKey = isTSide ? "Knife_T" : "Knife_CT";
	            InventoryItem equippedKnife = loadout.get(knifeKey);
	            JPanel knifeCard = buildWeaponCard(knifeKey, equippedKnife, BG_CARD, ACCENT, TEXT, loadout, isTSide);
	            cardsRow.add(knifeCard);
	        } else if (isGlovesSection) {
	            // Gloves slot — each side has its own gloves loadout key
	            String glovesKey = isTSide ? "Gloves_T" : "Gloves_CT";
	            InventoryItem equippedGloves = loadout.get(glovesKey);
	            JPanel glovesCard = buildWeaponCard(glovesKey, equippedGloves, BG_CARD, ACCENT, TEXT, loadout, isTSide);
	            cardsRow.add(glovesCard);
	        } else {
	            for (String slot : sectionSlots[si][0]) {
	                InventoryItem equipped = loadout.get(slot);
	                JPanel card = buildWeaponCard(slot, equipped, BG_CARD, ACCENT, TEXT, loadout, isTSide);
	                cardsRow.add(card);
	            }
	        }
	        weaponArea.add(cardsRow);
	        weaponArea.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 2)));
	    }

	    JScrollPane scrollPane = new JScrollPane(weaponArea,
	        JScrollPane.VERTICAL_SCROLLBAR_AS_NEEDED,
	        JScrollPane.HORIZONTAL_SCROLLBAR_NEVER);
	    if (isTSide) loadoutScrollPaneT  = scrollPane;
	    else         loadoutScrollPaneCT = scrollPane;
	    scrollPane.setBorder(null);
	    scrollPane.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    scrollPane.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    // Revalidate weaponArea when scroll pane is resized so WrapLayout re-wraps correctly
	    scrollPane.getViewport().addComponentListener(new java.awt.event.ComponentAdapter() {
	        @Override public void componentResized(java.awt.event.ComponentEvent e) {
	            weaponArea.revalidate();
	        }
	    });
	    // Restore scroll: poll until the scrollbar max has stabilised (WrapLayout finishes its pass),
	    // then set the value. This is more reliable than invokeLater or HierarchyListener alone.
	    final int savedY = isTSide ? loadoutScrollYT : loadoutScrollYCT;
	    if (savedY > 0) {
	        final int[] lastMax = {-1};
	        final int[] stable  = {0};
	        javax.swing.Timer t = new javax.swing.Timer(30, null);
	        t.addActionListener(ev -> {
	            int max = scrollPane.getVerticalScrollBar().getMaximum();
	            if (max == lastMax[0]) {
	                stable[0]++;
	            } else {
	                lastMax[0] = max;
	                stable[0]  = 0;
	            }
	            if (stable[0] >= 2 && max > savedY) {   // max settled and big enough
	                t.stop();
	                scrollPane.getVerticalScrollBar().setValue(savedY);
	            } else if (stable[0] >= 10) {            // give up after ~300ms
	                t.stop();
	                scrollPane.getVerticalScrollBar().setValue(savedY);
	            }
	        });
	        t.start();
	    }
	    root.add(scrollPane, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    return root;
	}

	// WrapLayout: FlowLayout that wraps cards to next line when the container is too narrow
	public static class WrapLayout extends FlowLayout {
	    public WrapLayout(int align, int hgap, int vgap) { super(align, hgap, vgap); }
	    @Override
	    public Dimension preferredLayoutSize(java.awt.Container target) {
	        return layoutSize(target, true);
	    }
	    @Override
	    public Dimension minimumLayoutSize(java.awt.Container target) {
	        Dimension min = layoutSize(target, false);
	        min.width -= (getHgap() + 1);
	        return min;
	    }
	    private Dimension layoutSize(java.awt.Container target, boolean preferred) {
	        synchronized (target.getTreeLock()) {
	            int targetWidth = target.getSize().width;
	            if (targetWidth == 0) targetWidth = Integer.MAX_VALUE;
	            int hgap = getHgap(), vgap = getVgap();
	            java.awt.Insets insets = target.getInsets();
	            int maxWidth = targetWidth - insets.left - insets.right - hgap * 2;
	            Dimension dim = new Dimension(0, 0);
	            int rowWidth = 0, rowHeight = 0;
	            int nmembers = target.getComponentCount();
	            for (int i = 0; i < nmembers; i++) {
	                java.awt.Component m = target.getComponent(i);
	                if (m.isVisible()) {
	                    Dimension d = preferred ? m.getPreferredSize() : m.getMinimumSize();
	                    if (rowWidth + d.width > maxWidth && rowWidth > 0) {
	                        dim.width = Math.max(dim.width, rowWidth);
	                        dim.height += rowHeight + vgap;
	                        rowWidth = 0; rowHeight = 0;
	                    }
	                    rowWidth += d.width + hgap;
	                    rowHeight = Math.max(rowHeight, d.height);
	                }
	            }
	            dim.width  = Math.max(dim.width, rowWidth);
	            dim.height += rowHeight + insets.top + insets.bottom + vgap * 2;
	            return dim;
	        }
	    }
	}

	private JPanel buildWeaponCard(String slot, InventoryItem equipped,
	        Color BG_CARD, Color ACCENT, Color TEXT,
	        Map<String, InventoryItem> loadout, boolean isTSide) {
	    boolean hasEquipped = (equipped != null);
	    Color borderCol = hasEquipped ? ACCENT : new Color(45, 45, 60);
	    String slotDisplay = slot.replaceAll("_(T|CT)$", "");

	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(0, 2));
	    card.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(borderCol, 1),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 4, 4, 4)));
	    card.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(116, 110));
	    card.setCursor(java.awt.Cursor.getPredefinedCursor(java.awt.Cursor.HAND_CURSOR));

	    // Image area — scale proportionally to avoid stretching
	    JLabel imgLbl;
	    if (hasEquipped && equipped.image != null) {
	        Image src = equipped.image.getImage();
	        int iw = src.getWidth(null), ih = src.getHeight(null);
	        if (iw <= 0 || ih <= 0) { iw = 90; ih = 52; }
	        double scale = Math.min(90.0 / iw, 52.0 / ih);
	        int sw = (int)(iw * scale), sh = (int)(ih * scale);
	        Image scaled = src.getScaledInstance(sw, sh, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH);
	        imgLbl = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        imgLbl.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(90, 52));
	    } else {
	        // Dark silhouette placeholder with gun name centred (use slotDisplay, not raw slot)
	        String abbrev = slotDisplay.length() > 10 ? slotDisplay.substring(0, 9) + "\u2026" : slotDisplay;
	        imgLbl = new JLabel("<html><center><font color='#3a3a55'>" + abbrev + "</font></center></html>", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        imgLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 8));
	        imgLbl.setOpaque(true);
	        imgLbl.setBackground(new Color(18, 18, 28));
	        imgLbl.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(90, 52));
	    }
	    imgLbl.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    card.add(imgLbl, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    String skinDisplay;
	    if (!hasEquipped) {
	        skinDisplay = "None";
	    } else if (equipped.isStattrak) {
	        skinDisplay = "ST " + equipped.name.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	    } else {
	        skinDisplay = equipped.name;
	    }
	    JPanel bottomPanel = new JPanel();
	    bottomPanel.setLayout(new BoxLayout(bottomPanel, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    bottomPanel.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	    bottomPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(2, 2, 2, 2));
	    JLabel gunLbl = new JLabel("<html><div style='text-align:center;'>" + slotDisplay + "</div></html>", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    gunLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 8));
	    gunLbl.setForeground(new Color(130, 130, 160));
	    gunLbl.setAlignmentX(0.5f);
	    JLabel skinLbl = new JLabel("<html><div style='text-align:center;'>" + skinDisplay + "</div></html>", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    skinLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 8));
	    boolean isSkinST = hasEquipped && equipped.isStattrak;
	    skinLbl.setForeground(isSkinST ? new Color(207, 106, 50) : hasEquipped ? ACCENT : new Color(55, 55, 75));
	    skinLbl.setAlignmentX(0.5f);
	    // No MaximumSize cap — let HTML wrap long skin names to a second line
	    bottomPanel.add(gunLbl);
	    bottomPanel.add(skinLbl);
	    card.add(bottomPanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    card.addMouseListener(new java.awt.event.MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override public void mouseClicked(java.awt.event.MouseEvent e) {
	            showLoadoutPicker(slot, loadout, isTSide);
	        }
	        @Override public void mouseEntered(java.awt.event.MouseEvent e) {
	            card.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 58));
	            card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	                BorderFactory.createLineBorder(ACCENT, 2),
	                BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(3, 3, 3, 3)));
	        }
	        @Override public void mouseExited(java.awt.event.MouseEvent e) {
	            card.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	            card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	                BorderFactory.createLineBorder(borderCol, 1),
	                BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 4, 4, 4)));
	        }
	    });
	    return card;
	}

	private void showLoadoutPicker(String slot, Map<String, InventoryItem> loadout, boolean isTSide) {
	    Color BG_DARK = new Color(12, 12, 20);
	    Color BG_CARD = new Color(28, 28, 42);
	    Color ACCENT  = isTSide ? new Color(247, 147, 30) : new Color(95, 200, 255);
	    Color TEXT    = new Color(220, 220, 235);

	    // For knife slot, match any knife/glove (the knife section)
	    java.util.List<InventoryItem> matches = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	    for (InventoryItem item : inventoryList) {
	        String cleanName = item.name.replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();
	        boolean isKnifeSlot  = slot.equals("Knife_T")  || slot.equals("Knife_CT");
	        boolean isGlovesSlot = slot.equals("Gloves_T") || slot.equals("Gloves_CT");
	        if (isKnifeSlot) {
	            String r = item.rarity != null ? item.rarity : "";
	            if (r.equalsIgnoreCase("Knife") || cleanName.contains("Knife") ||
	                cleanName.contains("Bayonet") || cleanName.contains("Karambit")) {
	                matches.add(item);
	            }
	        } else if (isGlovesSlot) {
	            String r = item.rarity != null ? item.rarity : "";
	            if (r.equalsIgnoreCase("Gloves") || cleanName.contains("Gloves")) {
	                matches.add(item);
	            }
	        } else {
	            if (cleanName.toLowerCase().startsWith(slot.toLowerCase())) {
	                matches.add(item);
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    matches.sort((a, b) -> {
	        java.util.List<String> order = java.util.Arrays.asList(
	            "Factory New","Minimal Wear","Field-Tested","Well-Worn","Battle-Scarred");
	        int ai = order.indexOf(a.condition), bi = order.indexOf(b.condition);
	        return Integer.compare(ai < 0 ? 99 : ai, bi < 0 ? 99 : bi);
	    });

	    String slotLabel = slot.replaceAll("_(T|CT)$", "");
	    JDialog dialog = new JDialog(this, "Select skin for " + slotLabel, true);
	    dialog.setSize(640, 440);
	    dialog.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    dialog.getContentPane().setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    dialog.setLayout(new BorderLayout());

	    JLabel hdr = new JLabel("  " + slotLabel + "  \u2014  Select a skin", SwingConstants.LEFT);
	    hdr.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 15));
	    hdr.setForeground(ACCENT);
	    hdr.setOpaque(true);
	    hdr.setBackground(new Color(18, 18, 30));
	    hdr.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 2, 0, ACCENT),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 16, 10, 16)));
	    dialog.add(hdr, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new WrapLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 10, 10));
	    grid.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));

	    JPanel defaultCard = buildPickerCard(null, slot, BG_CARD, ACCENT, TEXT, loadout.get(slot) == null);
	    defaultCard.addMouseListener(new java.awt.event.MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override public void mouseClicked(java.awt.event.MouseEvent e) {
	            // Capture scroll position BEFORE dispose() — dispose can trigger repaints that reset scroll to 0
	            int scrollY = isTSide
	                ? (loadoutScrollPaneT  != null ? loadoutScrollPaneT.getVerticalScrollBar().getValue()  : 0)
	                : (loadoutScrollPaneCT != null ? loadoutScrollPaneCT.getVerticalScrollBar().getValue() : 0);
	            loadout.remove(slot);
	            dialog.dispose();
	            if (isTSide) loadoutScrollYT  = scrollY;
	            else         loadoutScrollYCT = scrollY;
	            refreshLoadoutTab();
	        }
	    });
	    grid.add(defaultCard);

	    for (InventoryItem item : matches) {
	        boolean isEquipped = item.equals(loadout.get(slot));
	        JPanel skinCard = buildPickerCard(item, slot, BG_CARD, ACCENT, TEXT, isEquipped);
	        skinCard.addMouseListener(new java.awt.event.MouseAdapter() {
	            @Override public void mouseClicked(java.awt.event.MouseEvent e) {
	                // Capture scroll position BEFORE dispose()
	                int scrollY = isTSide
	                    ? (loadoutScrollPaneT  != null ? loadoutScrollPaneT.getVerticalScrollBar().getValue()  : 0)
	                    : (loadoutScrollPaneCT != null ? loadoutScrollPaneCT.getVerticalScrollBar().getValue() : 0);
	                loadout.put(slot, item);
	                dialog.dispose();
	                if (isTSide) loadoutScrollYT  = scrollY;
	                else         loadoutScrollYCT = scrollY;
	                refreshLoadoutTab();
	            }
	        });
	        grid.add(skinCard);
	    }

	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid,
	        JScrollPane.VERTICAL_SCROLLBAR_AS_NEEDED,
	        JScrollPane.HORIZONTAL_SCROLLBAR_NEVER);
	    scroll.setBorder(null);
	    scroll.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    dialog.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    if (matches.isEmpty()) {
	        JLabel noSkins = new JLabel("You have no " + slotLabel + " skins in your inventory.", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        noSkins.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	        noSkins.setForeground(new Color(130, 130, 160));
	        noSkins.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(6, 0, 6, 0));
	        dialog.add(noSkins, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    }
	    dialog.setVisible(true);
	}

	private JPanel buildPickerCard(InventoryItem item, String slot,
	        Color BG_CARD, Color ACCENT, Color TEXT, boolean isSelected) {
	    boolean isDefault = (item == null);
	    Color border = isSelected ? ACCENT : new Color(45, 45, 65);

	    boolean isPickerST = !isDefault && item.isStattrak;
	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(0, 3));
	    card.setBackground(isSelected ? new Color(30, 35, 55) : BG_CARD);
	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(border, isSelected ? 2 : 1),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(6, 6, 6, 6)));
	    card.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(130, 115));
	    card.setCursor(java.awt.Cursor.getPredefinedCursor(java.awt.Cursor.HAND_CURSOR));

	    JLabel imgLbl;
	    if (!isDefault && item.image != null) {
	        Image src = item.image.getImage();
	        int iw = src.getWidth(null), ih = src.getHeight(null);
	        if (iw <= 0 || ih <= 0) { iw = 100; ih = 65; }
	        double pscale = Math.min(100.0 / iw, 65.0 / ih);
	        int sw = (int)(iw * pscale), sh = (int)(ih * pscale);
	        Image scaled = src.getScaledInstance(sw, sh, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH);
	        imgLbl = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        imgLbl.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(100, 65));
	    } else {
	        imgLbl = new JLabel(isDefault ? "NONE" : "?", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        imgLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, isDefault ? 12 : 18));
	        imgLbl.setForeground(isDefault ? new Color(100, 100, 130) : new Color(60, 60, 80));
	        imgLbl.setOpaque(true);
	        imgLbl.setBackground(new Color(18, 18, 28));
	        imgLbl.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(100, 65));
	    }
	    card.add(imgLbl, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    // Show "ST <name>" inline — the ST prefix makes StatTrak items immediately identifiable
	    String displayName = isDefault ? "None"
	        : (isPickerST ? "ST " + item.name.replace("StatTrak ", "") : item.name);
	    JPanel textPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1, 0, 1));
	    textPanel.setBackground(card.getBackground());
	    JLabel nameLbl = new JLabel(displayName, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    nameLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 9));
	    nameLbl.setForeground(isSelected ? ACCENT : isPickerST ? new Color(207, 106, 50) : TEXT);
	    JLabel condLbl = new JLabel(isDefault ? "" : item.condition, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    condLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 8));
	    condLbl.setForeground(new Color(130, 140, 170));
	    textPanel.add(nameLbl);
	    textPanel.add(condLbl);
	    card.add(textPanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    card.addMouseListener(new java.awt.event.MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override public void mouseEntered(java.awt.event.MouseEvent e) {
	            if (!isSelected) {
	                card.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 52));
	                card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	                    BorderFactory.createLineBorder(ACCENT, 1),
	                    BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(6, 6, 6, 6)));
	            }
	        }
	        @Override public void mouseExited(java.awt.event.MouseEvent e) {
	            if (!isSelected) {
	                card.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	                card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	                    BorderFactory.createLineBorder(border, 1),
	                    BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(6, 6, 6, 6)));
	            }
	        }
	    });
	    return card;
	}


	private void refreshGeneralTab() {

	    int genIdx = 6; 
	    JPanel genPanel = (JPanel) mainTabs.getComponentAt(genIdx);
	    genPanel.removeAll();
	    genPanel.setLayout(new BorderLayout());

	    Color BG_DARK = new Color(15, 15, 20);
	    Color BG_CARD = new Color(30, 30, 40);
	    Color ACCENT = new Color(247, 147, 30);
	    Color ACCENT2 = new Color(95, 200, 255);
	    Color TEXT_DIM = new Color(140, 140, 155);
	    Color BORDER = new Color(45, 45, 60);

	    genPanel.setBackground(BG_DARK);

	    JLabel title = new JLabel("General", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    title.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 22));
	    title.setForeground(ACCENT);
	    title.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(20, 0, 20, 0));
	    genPanel.add(title, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel btnGrid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 2, 16, 16));
	    btnGrid.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    btnGrid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(20, 60, 20, 60));

	    String[][] btnDefs = {
	        {"TRADES",           "View & manage incoming trade offers"},
	        {"COLLECTION",       "See all skins you've ever unboxed"},
	        {"ACHIEVEMENTS",     "Track your achievements"},
	        {"STATS",            "Opening statistics & breakdowns"},
	        {"LEADERBOARD",      "Global inventory leaderboard"},
	        {"ROI STATS",        "Return on investment by case type"},
	        {"ANALYTICS",        "Skin price analytics & charts"},
	        {"INV LEADERBOARD",  "Top 100 richest inventories worldwide"},
	        {"MISSIONS",        "Complete missions to earn Stars"},
	        {"ODDS",            "Drop rates for Armoury pass & Cases"},
	    };

	    JButton[] btns = {tradesButton, collectionButton, achievementsButton, statsButton, leaderboardButton, roiButton, analyticsButton, inventoryLeaderboardButton, missionsButton, armouryOddsButton};

	    for (int i = 0; i < btnDefs.length; i++) {
	        final int idx2 = i;

	        JButton card = new JButton();
	        card.setLayout(new BorderLayout(4, 6));
	        card.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	        card.setFocusPainted(false);
	        card.setBorderPainted(true);
	        card.setOpaque(true);
	        card.setCursor(new Cursor(Cursor.HAND_CURSOR));
	        card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(BORDER, 1),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(18, 20, 18, 20)));
	        card.addActionListener(btns[idx2].getActionListeners()[0]);
	        card.setActionCommand(btns[idx2].getActionCommand() != null
	            ? btns[idx2].getActionCommand() : btnDefs[idx2][0]);
	        card.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	            Color orig = BG_CARD;
	            public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) { card.setBackground(orig.brighter()); }
	            public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e)  { card.setBackground(orig); }
	        });

	        JLabel title2 = new JLabel(btnDefs[idx2][0], SwingConstants.LEFT);
	        title2.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        title2.setForeground(ACCENT2);
	        title2.setOpaque(false);

	        JLabel desc = new JLabel(btnDefs[idx2][1], SwingConstants.LEFT);
	        desc.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	        desc.setForeground(TEXT_DIM);
	        desc.setOpaque(false);

	        card.add(title2, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        card.add(desc,   BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	        btnGrid.add(card);
	    }

	    genPanel.add(btnGrid, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    genPanel.revalidate();
	    genPanel.repaint();
	}

	public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
	    playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
	    String cmd = e.getActionCommand();
	    if (cmd.equals("OPEN")) {
	        if (!isAnimating) {
	            openCrateWithAnimation();
	        }
	    } else if (cmd.equals("CLOSE")) {
	        resetCrate();
	    } else if (cmd.equals("AUTO")) {
	        if (autoTimer != null && autoTimer.isRunning()) {
	            autoTimer.stop();
	            autoTimer = null;
	            autoStateOpen = false;
	            autoOpenButton.setText("AUTO OPEN");
	            resetCrate();
	        } else {
	            autoStateOpen = false;
	            autoOpenButton.setText("STOP OPEN");
	            autoTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(50, new ActionListener() {
	                @Override
	                public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent ev) {
	                    if (autoTimer == null || !autoTimer.isRunning())
	                        return;

	                    if (!autoStateOpen) {
	                        if (balance < currentCase.price) {
	                            stopAutoOpen();
	                            return;
	                        }
	                        openCrate();
	                        autoStateOpen = true;
	                    } else {
	                        resetCrate();
	                        autoStateOpen = false;
	                    }
	                }
	            });
	            autoTimer.setRepeats(true);
	            autoTimer.start();
	        }
	    } else if (e.getActionCommand().equals("TRADES")) {
	        showTradesWindow();
	    } else if (e.getActionCommand().equals("COLLECTION")) {
	        showCollectionWindow();
	    } else if (e.getActionCommand().equals("ACHIEVEMENTS")) {
	        showAchievementsWindow();
	    } else if (e.getActionCommand().equals("STATS")) {
	        showStatsWindow();
	    } else if (e.getSource() == saveButton) {
	        saveProgress();
	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "Game saved successfully!", "Save Complete", JOptionPane.INFORMATION_MESSAGE);
	    } else if (e.getSource() == loadButton) {
	        int confirm = JOptionPane.showConfirmDialog(this, 
	            "Load saved game? Current progress will be lost if not saved.", 
	            "Confirm Load", 
	            JOptionPane.YES_NO_OPTION);
	        if (confirm == JOptionPane.YES_OPTION) {
	            loadProgress();
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "Game loaded successfully!", "Load Complete", JOptionPane.INFORMATION_MESSAGE);
	        }
	    } else if (cmd.equals("SELECT CASE")) {
	        showCaseSelection();
	    } else if (e.getActionCommand().equals("LEADERBOARD")) {
	        showLeaderboard();
	    } else if (e.getActionCommand().equals("ROI")) {
	        showROIWindow();
	    } else if (e.getActionCommand().equals("ANALYTICS")) {
	        showMarketAnalytics();
	    } else if (e.getActionCommand().equals("INV_LEADERBOARD")) {
	        showInventoryLeaderboard();
	    } else if (e.getActionCommand().equals("MISSIONS")) {
	        showMissionsWindow();
	    } else if (e.getActionCommand().equals("ARMOURY_TAB")) {
	        mainTabs.setSelectedIndex(1);
	    } else if (e.getActionCommand().equals("ARMOURY_ODDS")) {
	        showArmouryOddsWindow();
	    }
	}

	private void loadSound(String filename, int soundType) {
	    try {
	        File soundFile = new File(filename);
	        AudioInputStream audioIn = AudioSystem.getAudioInputStream(soundFile);
	        Clip clip = AudioSystem.getClip();
	        clip.open(audioIn);
	        
	        switch(soundType) {
	            case 2: unboxSound = clip; break;
	            case 4: purchaseSound = clip; break;
	        }
	    } catch (UnsupportedAudioFileException e) {
	        System.err.println("Error loading sound: " + filename);
	        e.printStackTrace();
	    } catch (IOException e) {
	        System.err.println("Error loading sound: " + filename);
	        e.printStackTrace();
	    } catch (LineUnavailableException e) {
	        System.err.println("Error loading sound: " + filename);
	        e.printStackTrace();
	    }
	}
	
	private final Map<String, Clip> soundCache = new HashMap<>();

	private void playSoundFile(String filename) {
	    try {

	        Clip cached = soundCache.get(filename);
	        if (cached != null && !cached.isRunning()) {
	            cached.setFramePosition(0);
	            cached.start();
	            return;
	        }

	        if (cached != null && cached.isRunning() && filename.equals("button_click.wav")) {
	            return;
	        }
	        
	        File soundFile = new File(filename);
	        if (!soundFile.exists()) return;
	        
	        AudioInputStream audioIn = AudioSystem.getAudioInputStream(soundFile);
	        Clip clip = AudioSystem.getClip();
	        clip.open(audioIn);
	        clip.addLineListener(event -> {
	            if (event.getType() == LineEvent.Type.STOP) {

	            }
	        });
	        soundCache.put(filename, clip);
	        clip.start();
	    } catch (Exception e) {

	    }
	}

	private void playSound(Clip clip) {
	    if (clip != null) {
	        clip.setFramePosition(0);
	        clip.start();
	    }
	}
	
	private static class GameState implements java.io.Serializable {
	    private static final long serialVersionUID = 5L; 
	    
	    double balance;
	    double inventoryValue;
	    double openingProfit;
	    double totalMarketProfit;
	    int totalCrates;
	    int totMil, totRes, totClass, totCov, totKnife, totGlove;
	    double lowestFloat;
	    String currentCaseType;
	    int playerStars;
	    
	    Map<String, CaseTypeStats> caseStats;
	    
	    ArrayList<SerializableInventoryItem> inventory;
	    ArrayList<SerializableInventoryItem> activeListingItems;
	    ArrayList<Double>                    activeListingPrices;
	    ArrayList<String> unlockedAchievements;
	    Set<String> unboxedSkins;
	    Map<String, Integer> achievementProgress;
	    Map<String, String> tLoadoutKeys;
	    Map<String, String> ctLoadoutKeys;
	    
	    static class CaseTypeStats implements java.io.Serializable {
	        private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	        int timesOpened;
	        double totalSpent;
	        double totalReceived;
	    }
	    
	    static class SerializableInventoryItem implements java.io.Serializable {
	        private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	        String name, condition, rarity, blueGemTier, collection;
	        double price, itemFloat, basePrice;
	        boolean isStattrak;
	        int patternID;
	    }
	}
	
	private void saveProgress() {
	    try {
	        GameState state = new GameState();
	        state.balance = balance;
	        state.inventoryValue = inventoryValue;
	        state.openingProfit = openingProfit;
	        state.totalMarketProfit = totalMarketProfit;
	        state.totalCrates = totalCrates;
	        state.totMil = totMil;
	        state.totRes = totRes;
	        state.totClass = totClass;
	        state.totCov = totCov;
	        state.totKnife = totKnife;
	        state.totGlove = totGlove;
	        state.lowestFloat = lowestFloat;
	        state.currentCaseType = currentCase.name();
	        state.caseStats = new HashMap<>();
	        for (CaseType caseType : CaseType.values()) {
	            GameState.CaseTypeStats stats = new GameState.CaseTypeStats();
	            stats.timesOpened = caseType.timesOpened;
	            stats.totalSpent = caseType.totalSpent;
	            stats.totalReceived = caseType.totalReceived;
	            state.caseStats.put(caseType.name(), stats);
	        }
	        state.unlockedAchievements = new ArrayList<>(unlockedAchievements);
	        state.unboxedSkins = new HashSet<>(unboxedSkins);

	        state.activeListingItems = new ArrayList<>();
	        state.activeListingPrices = new ArrayList<>();
	        for (MarketListing ml : activeListings) {
	            GameState.SerializableInventoryItem sItem = new GameState.SerializableInventoryItem();
	            sItem.name = normalizeSkinName(ml.item.name);
	            sItem.condition = ml.item.condition;
	            sItem.rarity = normalizeSkinName(ml.item.rarity);
	            sItem.price = ml.item.price.doubleValue();
	            sItem.itemFloat = ml.item.itemFloat;
	            sItem.isStattrak = ml.item.isStattrak;
	            sItem.patternID = ml.item.patternID;
	            sItem.blueGemTier = ml.item.blueGemTier != null ? normalizeSkinName(ml.item.blueGemTier) : null;
	            sItem.basePrice = ml.item.basePrice;
	            state.activeListingItems.add(sItem);
	            state.activeListingPrices.add(ml.listPrice);
	        }
	        
	        state.inventory = new ArrayList<>();
	        for (InventoryItem item : inventoryList) {
	            GameState.SerializableInventoryItem sItem = new GameState.SerializableInventoryItem();
	            
	            sItem.name = normalizeSkinName(item.name);
	            sItem.condition = item.condition;
	            sItem.rarity = normalizeSkinName(item.rarity);
	            sItem.price = item.price.doubleValue();
	            sItem.itemFloat = item.itemFloat;
	            sItem.isStattrak = item.isStattrak;
	            sItem.patternID = item.patternID;
	            sItem.blueGemTier = item.blueGemTier != null ? normalizeSkinName(item.blueGemTier) : null;
	            sItem.basePrice = item.basePrice;
	            sItem.collection = item.collection;
	            state.inventory.add(sItem);
	        }
	        
	        state.playerStars = playerStars;

	        // Save loadout: store as slot->skinName strings
	        state.tLoadoutKeys   = new HashMap<>();
	        state.ctLoadoutKeys  = new HashMap<>();
	        for (Map.Entry<String, InventoryItem> e : tLoadout.entrySet()) {
	            if (e.getValue() != null) state.tLoadoutKeys.put(e.getKey(), e.getValue().name);
	        }
	        for (Map.Entry<String, InventoryItem> e : ctLoadout.entrySet()) {
	            if (e.getValue() != null) state.ctLoadoutKeys.put(e.getKey(), e.getValue().name);
	        }

	        state.achievementProgress = new HashMap<>();
	        for (Map.Entry<String, Achievement> entry : achievements.entrySet()) {
	            state.achievementProgress.put(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue().progress);
	        }
	        
	        try (java.io.ObjectOutputStream oos = new java.io.ObjectOutputStream(
	                new java.io.FileOutputStream(SAVE_FILE))) {
	            oos.writeObject(state);
	        }
	        
	        System.out.println("Save successful! Inventory items: " + state.inventory.size());
	        
	    } catch (Exception e) {
	        System.err.println("Failed to save progress: " + e.getMessage());
	        e.printStackTrace();
	    }
	}
    
	private void loadProgress() {
	    try {
	        java.io.File saveFile = new java.io.File(SAVE_FILE);
	        if (!saveFile.exists()) {
	            System.out.println("No save file found");
	            return;
	        }
	        
	        GameState state;
	        try (java.io.ObjectInputStream ois = new java.io.ObjectInputStream(
	                new java.io.FileInputStream(SAVE_FILE))) {
	            state = (GameState) ois.readObject();
	        }
	        
	        System.out.println("Loading save file with " + state.inventory.size() + " items");
	        
	        balance = state.balance;
	        inventoryValue = state.inventoryValue;
	        openingProfit = state.openingProfit;
	        totalMarketProfit = state.totalMarketProfit;
	        totalCrates = state.totalCrates;
	        totMil = state.totMil;
	        totRes = state.totRes;
	        totClass = state.totClass;
	        totCov = state.totCov;
	        totKnife = state.totKnife;
	        totGlove = state.totGlove;
	        lowestFloat = state.lowestFloat;
	        playerStars = state.playerStars;
	        if (starsLabel != null) starsLabel.setText("* " + playerStars + " Stars");
	        
	        if (state.currentCaseType != null) {
	            try {
	                currentCase = CaseType.valueOf(state.currentCaseType);
	                currentCaseLabel.setText(currentCase.name);
	                openCrateButton.setText(String.format("OPEN ($%.2f)", currentCase.price));
	            } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
	                currentCase = CaseType.WEAPON_CASE_ONE;
	                currentCaseLabel.setText(currentCase.name);
	                openCrateButton.setText(String.format("OPEN ($%.2f)", currentCase.price));
	            }
	        }
	        
	        if (state.caseStats != null) {
	            for (CaseType caseType : CaseType.values()) {
	                GameState.CaseTypeStats stats = state.caseStats.get(caseType.name());
	                if (stats != null) {
	                    caseType.timesOpened = stats.timesOpened;
	                    caseType.totalSpent = stats.totalSpent;
	                    caseType.totalReceived = stats.totalReceived;
	                }
	            }
	        }
	        
	        unlockedAchievements = new ArrayList<>(state.unlockedAchievements);
	        unboxedSkins = new HashSet<>(state.unboxedSkins);

	        activeListings.clear();
	        if (state.activeListingItems != null && state.activeListingPrices != null) {
	            for (int i = 0; i < state.activeListingItems.size(); i++) {
	                GameState.SerializableInventoryItem sItem = state.activeListingItems.get(i);
	                double listPrice = state.activeListingPrices.get(i);
	                String cleanName = normalizeSkinName(sItem.name);
	                Image img = getSkinImageFromName(cleanName);
	                InventoryItem item = new InventoryItem(
	                    img != null ? new ImageIcon(img) : null,
	                    cleanName, sItem.condition,
	                    normalizeSkinName(sItem.rarity),
	                    BigDecimal.valueOf(sItem.price).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                    sItem.itemFloat, sItem.isStattrak, sItem.patternID,
	                    sItem.blueGemTier != null ? normalizeSkinName(sItem.blueGemTier) : null,
	                    sItem.basePrice);
	                int sellTime = calculateSellTime(listPrice, sItem.price);
	                activeListings.add(new MarketListing(item, listPrice, sellTime, true));
	            }
	        }
	        
	        inventoryList.clear();
	        for (GameState.SerializableInventoryItem sItem : state.inventory) {
	            String cleanName = normalizeSkinName(sItem.name);
	            String cleanRarity = normalizeSkinName(sItem.rarity);
	            String cleanBlueGem = sItem.blueGemTier != null ? normalizeSkinName(sItem.blueGemTier) : null;
	            
	            Image img = getSkinImageFromName(cleanName);
	            InventoryItem item = new InventoryItem(
	                img != null ? new ImageIcon(img) : null,
	                cleanName,
	                sItem.condition,
	                cleanRarity,
	                BigDecimal.valueOf(sItem.price).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                sItem.itemFloat,
	                sItem.isStattrak,
	                sItem.patternID,
	                cleanBlueGem,
	                sItem.basePrice
	            );
	            item.collection = sItem.collection;
	            inventoryList.add(item);
	            System.out.println("Loaded item: " + cleanName);
	        }
	        
	        for (Map.Entry<String, Integer> entry : state.achievementProgress.entrySet()) {
	            Achievement ach = achievements.get(entry.getKey());
	            if (ach != null) {
	                ach.progress = entry.getValue();
	                if (unlockedAchievements.contains(entry.getKey())) {
	                    ach.isUnlocked = true;
	                }
	            }
	        }
	        
	        // Restore loadout: find matching InventoryItem for each saved skin name
	        tLoadout.clear(); ctLoadout.clear();
	        if (state.tLoadoutKeys != null) {
	            for (Map.Entry<String, String> e : state.tLoadoutKeys.entrySet()) {
	                for (InventoryItem inv : inventoryList) {
	                    if (inv.name.equals(e.getValue())) { tLoadout.put(e.getKey(), inv); break; }
	                }
	            }
	        }
	        if (state.ctLoadoutKeys != null) {
	            for (Map.Entry<String, String> e : state.ctLoadoutKeys.entrySet()) {
	                for (InventoryItem inv : inventoryList) {
	                    if (inv.name.equals(e.getValue())) { ctLoadout.put(e.getKey(), inv); break; }
	                }
	            }
	        }

	        skinImage = null;
	        crateImage = new ImageIcon("crate.png").getImage();
	        
	        rarityLabel.setText("");
	        nameLabel.setText("");
	        priceLabel.setText("");
	        floatLabel.setText("");
	        conditionLabel.setText("");
	        patternId.setText("");
	        collectionLabel.setText("");
	        
	        openCrateButton.setVisible(true);
	        closeCrateButton.setVisible(false);
	        lowFloatLabel.setVisible(true);
	        
	        updateBalanceLabel();
	        writeStats();
	        newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	        totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	        lowFloatLabel.setText(String.format("Lowest Float: %.10f", lowestFloat));
	        
	        BigDecimal roundedProfit = BigDecimal.valueOf(openingProfit).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	        if (roundedProfit.signum() >= 0) {
	            profitLabel.setForeground(new Color(0, 160, 0));
	            profitLabel.setText("Opening Profit: +$" + roundedProfit);
	        } else {
	            profitLabel.setForeground(Color.RED);
	            profitLabel.setText("Opening Profit: -$" + roundedProfit.abs());
	        }
	        
	        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	            revalidate();
	            repaint();
	        });
	        
	        System.out.println("Load complete! Items in inventory: " + inventoryList.size());
	        System.out.println("Current case type: " + currentCase.name);
	        
	    } catch (Exception e) {
	        System.err.println("Failed to load progress: " + e.getMessage());
	        e.printStackTrace();
	        
	        skinImage = null;
	        crateImage = new ImageIcon("crate.png").getImage();
	        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	            revalidate();
	            repaint();
	        });
	    }
	}

	public void resetCrate() {
	    openCrateButton.setEnabled(true);
	    openCrateButton.setVisible(true);
	    closeCrateButton.setVisible(false);
	    autoOpenButton.setVisible(true);
	    autoOpenButton.setEnabled(true);
	    skinImage = null;
	    crateImage = null;
	    updateCrateImageDisplay();
	    rarityLabel.setText("");
	    nameLabel.setText("");
	    priceLabel.setText("");
	    floatLabel.setText("");
	    conditionLabel.setText("");
	    patternId.setText("");
	    collectionLabel.setText("");
	    repaint();
	}

	private static final class FloatRange { 
		final Double min; final Double max; 
		FloatRange(Double min, Double max) { 
			this.min = min; 
			this.max = max; 
		} 
	}

	private double applyFloatLimits(String skinName, double value) {
		FloatRange r = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(skinName);
		if (r == null) {
			for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet()) {
				String key = e.getKey();
				if (skinName.startsWith(key)) {
					r = e.getValue();
					break;
				}
			}
		}
		if (r == null) return value;
		double min = (r.min == null) ? 0.00 : r.min;
		double max = (r.max == null) ? 1.00 : r.max;
		return min + random.nextDouble() * (max - min);
		}

	public static class TradeUpCollection {
	    final String collectionName;
	    final String[] industrialSkins; 
	    final String[] milspecSkins;
	    final String[] restrictedSkins;
	    final String[] classifiedSkins;
	    final String[] covertSkins;

	    
	    public TradeUpCollection(String n, String[] mil, String[] res, String[] cls, String[] cov) {
	        this.collectionName  = n;
	        this.industrialSkins = new String[0];
	        this.milspecSkins    = mil != null ? mil : new String[0];
	        this.restrictedSkins = res != null ? res : new String[0];
	        this.classifiedSkins = cls != null ? cls : new String[0];
	        this.covertSkins     = cov != null ? cov : new String[0];
	    }

	    
	    public TradeUpCollection(String n, String[] ind, String[] mil, String[] res, String[] cls, String[] cov) {
	        this.collectionName  = n;
	        this.industrialSkins = ind != null ? ind : new String[0];
	        this.milspecSkins    = mil != null ? mil : new String[0];
	        this.restrictedSkins = res != null ? res : new String[0];
	        this.classifiedSkins = cls != null ? cls : new String[0];
	        this.covertSkins     = cov != null ? cov : new String[0];
	    }

	    public String getTierForSkin(String name) {
	        String n = name.replace("StatTrak ","").replace("StatTrak ","").trim();
	        int p = n.indexOf(" ("); if (p > 0) n = n.substring(0, p).trim();
	        for (String s : industrialSkins) if (s.equalsIgnoreCase(n)) return "Industrial";
	        for (String s : milspecSkins)    if (s.equalsIgnoreCase(n)) return "Milspec";
	        for (String s : restrictedSkins) if (s.equalsIgnoreCase(n)) return "Restricted";
	        for (String s : classifiedSkins) if (s.equalsIgnoreCase(n)) return "Classified";
	        for (String s : covertSkins)     if (s.equalsIgnoreCase(n)) return "Covert";
	        return null;
	    }

	    public String[] getOutcomePool(String inputRarity) {
	        switch (inputRarity) {
	            case "Industrial": return milspecSkins;    
	            case "Milspec":    return restrictedSkins;
	            case "Restricted": return classifiedSkins;
	            case "Classified": return covertSkins;
	            default:           return new String[0];
	        }
	    }
	}

	private TradeUpCollection findCollection(String skinName) {
	    for (TradeUpCollection col : TRADE_UP_COLLECTIONS)
	        if (col.getTierForSkin(skinName) != null) return col;
	    if (ARMOURY_TRADE_UP_COLLECTIONS != null) {
	        for (TradeUpCollection col : ARMOURY_TRADE_UP_COLLECTIONS)
	            if (col.getTierForSkin(skinName) != null) return col;
	    }
	    return null;
	}

	/** Returns the TradeUpCollection for the currently selected case. */
	private TradeUpCollection getCurrentCaseCollection() {
	    String colName;
	    if      (currentCase == CaseType.WEAPON_CASE_ONE) colName = "Weapon Case One";
	    else if (currentCase == CaseType.BRAVO)           colName = "Bravo Collection";
	    else if (currentCase == CaseType.BREAKOUT)        colName = "Breakout Collection";
	    else                                               colName = "Spectrum Collection";
	    for (TradeUpCollection c : TRADE_UP_COLLECTIONS)
	        if (c.collectionName.equals(colName)) return c;
	    return null;
	}

	private String getCollectionName(String skinName) {
	    TradeUpCollection col = findCollection(skinName);
	    return col != null ? col.collectionName : null;
	}

	private String[] resolveOutcomePool(ArrayList<InventoryItem> selectedItems, String baseRarity) {

	    java.util.LinkedHashMap<String, Integer> colCounts = new java.util.LinkedHashMap<>();
	    java.util.LinkedHashMap<String, TradeUpCollection> colMap = new java.util.LinkedHashMap<>();
	    int unknownCount = 0;
	    for (InventoryItem item : selectedItems) {
	        TradeUpCollection col = findCollection(item.name);
	        if (col == null) { unknownCount++; continue; }
	        colCounts.merge(col.collectionName, 1, Integer::sum);
	        colMap.put(col.collectionName, col);
	    }

	    java.util.List<String> weightedPool = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	    for (java.util.Map.Entry<String, Integer> e : colCounts.entrySet()) {
	        TradeUpCollection col = colMap.get(e.getKey());
	        String[] outcomes = col.getOutcomePool(baseRarity);
	        int count = e.getValue();
	        for (int rep = 0; rep < count; rep++)
	            for (String skin : outcomes)
	                weightedPool.add(skin);
	    }

	    if (!weightedPool.isEmpty()) return weightedPool.toArray(new String[0]);

	    java.util.LinkedHashSet<String> all = new java.util.LinkedHashSet<>();
	    for (TradeUpCollection col : TRADE_UP_COLLECTIONS)
	        for (String s : col.getOutcomePool(baseRarity)) all.add(s);
	    return all.toArray(new String[0]);
	}

    private static final Map<String, List<Integer>> BUTTERFLY_BG = Map.of(
    	"T1", List.of(182, 494, 838),
    	"T2", List.of(194,283,694,703,838,891,913,917),
    	"T3", List.of(
    	    29,194,214,263,283,330,371,396,398,478,488,494,510,612,638,652,694,
    	    703,717,749,800,868,881,891,913,917,928
    	),
    	"T4", List.of(
    	    27,38,42,43,61,72,73,78,92,98,112,130,147,256,282,318,320,335,358,
    	    407,411,424,426,457,458,474,499,515,534,618,628,629,642,643,655,
    	    664,702,705,711,721,767,768,770,782,798,799,808,811,839,846,858,
    	    872,885,902,907,913,919,924,958,964,965
    	    )
    	);

    private String getBlueGemTier(String skinName, int patternID) {
        if (patternID < 0 || patternID > 1000) return null;
        if (!skinName.contains("Case Hardened")) return null;

        if (skinName.contains("Flip Knife")) {
            for (var e : FLIP_KNIFE_BG.entrySet()) {
                if (e.getValue().contains(patternID)) return "Blue Gem " + e.getKey();
            }
        }

        if (skinName.contains("M9 Bayonet")) {
            for (var e : M9_BG.entrySet()) {
                if (e.getValue().contains(patternID)) return "Blue Gem " + e.getKey();
            }
        }

        if (skinName.contains("AK-47")) {
            for (var e : AK_BG.entrySet()) {
                if (e.getValue().contains(patternID)) return "Blue Gem " + e.getKey();
            }
        }
        
        if (skinName.contains("Butterfly Knife")) {
            for (var e : BUTTERFLY_BG.entrySet()) {
                if (e.getValue().contains(patternID)) {
                    return "Blue Gem " + e.getKey();
                }
            }
        }

        return null;
    }
    
    private boolean isBlueGem(InventoryItem item) {
        return item.blueGemTier != null && item.blueGemTier.contains("Blue Gem");
    }
    
    private boolean isCappedKnife(String skinName) {
        FloatRange fr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(skinName);
        return fr != null && fr.max != null && fr.max <= 0.10;
    }

    private double getRelativeFloat(String skinName, double itemFloat) {
        FloatRange fr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(skinName);
        if (fr == null) return itemFloat;

        double min = (fr.min != null) ? fr.min : 0.0;
        double max = (fr.max != null) ? fr.max : 1.0;

        return (itemFloat - min) / (max - min);
    }
    
    private void sellItemsByRarity(String rarity) {
        double soldValue = 0.0;
        double rawValue  = 0.0;
        int soldCount = 0;

        var it = inventoryList.iterator();
        while (it.hasNext()) {
            InventoryItem item = it.next();

            if (rarity.equals("All") || (!rarity.equals("Default") && item.rarity.contains(rarity))) {

                String mKey = normalizeSkinName(item.name);
                if (item.isStattrak) mKey = "StatTrak " + mKey;
                NpcBuyOrder best = getBestNpcBuyOrder(mKey, item.condition);
                double salePrice = (best != null) ? best.price : item.price.doubleValue();
                if (best != null) {
                    best.filled = Math.min(best.filled + 1, best.quantity);
                    best.lastFillTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
                }
                soldValue += salePrice;
                rawValue  += item.price.doubleValue();
                soldCount++;
                it.remove();
                writeStats();
            }
        }

        if (soldCount == 0) {
            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "No items to sell.");
            return;
        }

        balance += soldValue;
        inventoryValue = Math.max(0.0, inventoryValue - rawValue);

        updateLeaderboard();

        newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue)
                .setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

        totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
        updateBalanceLabel();
        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, String.format(
            "Sold %d item(s) for $%.2f", soldCount, soldValue));
    }

    public void openCrate() {
        lowFloatLabel.setVisible(true);
        double casePrice = currentCase.price;
        
        currentCase.timesOpened++;
        missionCasesOpened++;
        checkMissionProgress();
        currentCase.totalSpent += casePrice;
        
        if (balance < casePrice) {
            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "Out of money! Auto-open stopped.");
            stopAutoOpen();
            resetCrate();
            return;
        }

        balance -= casePrice;
        updateBalanceLabel();

        crateImage = null;
        openCrateButton.setVisible(false);
        closeCrateButton.setVisible(true);
        casesTabPanel.repaint();

        totalCrates += 1;
        String item = crateItem(currentCase);
        rarityLabel.setForeground(rarityColor);
        rarityLabel.setText(item);
        String selectedSkinName = "";
        Image originalSkin = null;
        
        if (item.contains("Gloves")) {
            totGlove += 1;
            missionGlovesUnboxed++;

            int i = random.nextInt(gloveSkins.length);
            originalSkin = gloveSkins[i];

            String[] gloveNames = {
                "Bloodhound Gloves | Bronzed",
                "Bloodhound Gloves | Charred",
                "Bloodhound Gloves | Guerrilla",
                "Bloodhound Gloves | Snakebite",
                "Driver Gloves | Convoy",
                "Driver Gloves | Crimson Weave",
                "Driver Gloves | Diamondback",
                "Driver Gloves | Lunar Weave",
                "Hand Wraps | Badlands",
                "Hand Wraps | Leather",
                "Hand Wraps | Slaughter",
                "Hand Wraps | Spruce DDPAT",
                "Moto Gloves | Boom!",
                "Moto Gloves | Cool Mint",
                "Moto Gloves | Eclipse",
                "Moto Gloves | Spearmint",
                "Specialist Gloves | Crimson Kimono",
                "Specialist Gloves | Emerald Web",
                "Specialist Gloves | Forest DDPAT",
                "Specialist Gloves | Foundation",
                "Sport Gloves | Arid",
                "Sport Gloves | Hedge Maze",
                "Sport Gloves | Pandora's Box",
                "Sport Gloves | Superconductor"
            };
            selectedSkinName = gloveNames[i % gloveNames.length];
        } else if (item.contains("Knife")) {
            totKnife += 1;
            missionKnivesUnboxed++;

            int i = random.nextInt(knifeSkins.length);
            originalSkin = knifeSkins[i];

            String[] names = {
                "Karambit | Slaughter",
                "M9 Bayonet | Crimson Web",
                "Flip Knife | Vanilla",
                "Gut Knife | Fade",
                "Bayonet | Scorched",
                "Bayonet | Boreal Forest",
                "Bayonet | Fade",
                "Flip Knife | Case Hardened",
                "Gut Knife | Forest DDPAT",
                "Gut Knife | Safari Mesh",
                "Karambit | Night",
                "Karambit | Crimson Web",
                "Karambit | Scorched",
                "Karambit | Urban Masked",
                "M9 Bayonet | Blue Steel",
                "M9 Bayonet | Case Hardened",
                "M9 Bayonet | Slaughter",
                "M9 Bayonet | Doppler",
                "Karambit | Doppler",
                "Butterfly Knife | Case Hardened",
                "Butterfly Knife | Crimson Web",
                "Butterfly Knife | Fade",
                "Butterfly Knife | Safari Mesh",
                "Butterfly Knife | Slaughter",
                "Butterfly Knife | Urban Masked",
                "Butterfly Knife | Vanilla",
                "Butterfly Knife | Ultraviolet",
                "Huntsman Knife | Marble Fade",
                "Huntsman Knife | Tiger Tooth",
                "Bowie Knife | Marble Fade",
                "Bowie Knife | Tiger Tooth",
                "Falchion Knife | Marble Fade",
                "Falchion Knife | Tiger Tooth"
            };
            selectedSkinName = names[i % names.length];

            if (selectedSkinName.contains("Doppler")) {
                double dr = random.nextDouble();
                if (dr < 0.05) {
                    String[] gems = { "Sapphire", "Ruby", "Black Pearl" };
                    String gem = gems[random.nextInt(gems.length)];
                    selectedSkinName += " (" + gem + ")";
                } else {
                    int phase = 1 + random.nextInt(4);
                    selectedSkinName += " (Phase " + phase + ")";
                }
            }
        } else if (item.contains("Covert")) {
            totCov += 1;
            TradeUpCollection col = getCurrentCaseCollection();
            String[] covertPool = (col != null && col.covertSkins.length > 0) ? col.covertSkins : new String[]{"AWP | Lightning Strike"};
            selectedSkinName = covertPool[random.nextInt(covertPool.length)];
            originalSkin = skinImageMap.getOrDefault(selectedSkinName, redSkins[0]);
        } else if (item.contains("Classified")) {
            totClass += 1;
            TradeUpCollection col = getCurrentCaseCollection();
            String[] classifiedPool = (col != null && col.classifiedSkins.length > 0) ? col.classifiedSkins : new String[]{"Desert Eagle | Hypnotic"};
            selectedSkinName = classifiedPool[random.nextInt(classifiedPool.length)];
            originalSkin = skinImageMap.getOrDefault(selectedSkinName, pinkSkins[0]);
        } else if (item.contains("Restricted")) {
            totRes += 1;
            TradeUpCollection col = getCurrentCaseCollection();
            String[] restrictedPool = (col != null && col.restrictedSkins.length > 0) ? col.restrictedSkins : new String[]{"Glock-18 | Dragon Tattoo"};
            selectedSkinName = restrictedPool[random.nextInt(restrictedPool.length)];
            originalSkin = skinImageMap.getOrDefault(selectedSkinName, purpleSkins[0]);
        } else if (item.contains("Milspec")) {
            totMil += 1;
            TradeUpCollection col = getCurrentCaseCollection();
            String[] milspecPool = (col != null && col.milspecSkins.length > 0) ? col.milspecSkins : new String[]{"MP7 | Skulls"};
            selectedSkinName = milspecPool[random.nextInt(milspecPool.length)];
            originalSkin = skinImageMap.getOrDefault(selectedSkinName, blueSkins[0]);
        }

        Image dopplerOverride = getKnifeImage(selectedSkinName);
        if (dopplerOverride != null) {
            originalSkin = dopplerOverride;
        }

        if (originalSkin != null) {
            int maxWidth = 280;
            int maxHeight = 200;
            int origWidth = originalSkin.getWidth(null);
            int origHeight = originalSkin.getHeight(null);
            double scale = Math.min((double) maxWidth / origWidth, (double) maxHeight / origHeight);
            int newWidth = (int) (origWidth * scale);
            int newHeight = (int) (origHeight * scale);
            skinImage = originalSkin.getScaledInstance(newWidth, newHeight, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH);
        }

        itemFloat = applyFloatLimits(selectedSkinName,random.nextDouble());
        String rarityKey = item.replace("StatTrak ", "");
        double marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarityKey, 1.0);
        double basePrice = getBasePrice(selectedSkinName);

        if (itemFloat <= 0.07) {
            condition = "Factory New";
        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.15) {
            condition = "Minimal Wear";
        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.38) {
            condition = "Field-Tested";
        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.45) {
            condition = "Well-Worn";
        } else {
            condition = "Battle-Scarred";
        }

        double variance = 0.85 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.3);
        bonusPrice = basePrice * marketMulti * variance * priceMulti;

        boolean isAnyDoppler = selectedSkinName.contains("Doppler");
        
        if (item.contains("Gloves")) {
            double gloveBasePrice = getGloveBasePrice(selectedSkinName);
            bonusPrice = calculateGlovePrice(selectedSkinName, condition, gloveBasePrice);
            bonusPrice *= marketMulti * variance;
        } else if (!item.contains("Knife")) {
            if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
                bonusPrice *= 2.5;
            } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
                bonusPrice *= 1.7;
            } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
                bonusPrice *= 1.0;
            } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
                bonusPrice *= 0.7;
            } else if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
                bonusPrice *= 0.3;
            }
            
            if (itemFloat <= 0.0005) {
                bonusPrice *= 3.0;
            } else if (itemFloat <= 0.001) {
                bonusPrice *= 2.0;
            } else if (itemFloat <= 0.005) {
                bonusPrice *= 1.5;
            } else if (itemFloat <= 0.02) {
                bonusPrice *= 1.25;
            }
        } else if (!isAnyDoppler) {
            double rel = getRelativeFloat(selectedSkinName, itemFloat);
            if (!isCappedKnife(selectedSkinName)) {
                if (rel <= 0.01) {
                    bonusPrice *= 2.5;
                } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
                    bonusPrice *= 1.5;
                } else if (rel <= 0.20) {
                    bonusPrice *= 1.1;
                }
            } else {
                if (rel <= 0.01) {
                    bonusPrice *= 1.15;
                } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
                    bonusPrice *= 1.05;
                }
            }
        }

        if (isStattrak == 1 && !item.contains("Gloves")) {
            if (item.contains("Knife")) {
                if (selectedSkinName.contains("Crimson Web")) {
                    bonusPrice *= 1.0;
                } else if (selectedSkinName.contains("Doppler")) {
                    bonusPrice *= 0.80;
                } else {
                    bonusPrice *= 0.95;
                }
            } else {
                double stGunMult = 1.70 + random.nextDouble() * 0.30;
                bonusPrice *= stGunMult;
            }
        }

        newBonusPrice = BigDecimal.valueOf(bonusPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

        patternID = random.nextInt(1000);

        String blueGemTier = getBlueGemTier(selectedSkinName, patternID);
        if (blueGemTier != null) {
            selectedSkinName = selectedSkinName + " (" + blueGemTier + ")";
            
            double baseBeforeBlueGem = getBasePrice(selectedSkinName.replace(" (" + blueGemTier + ")", ""));
            
            if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
                baseBeforeBlueGem *= 2.5;
            } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
                baseBeforeBlueGem *= 1.7;
            } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
                baseBeforeBlueGem *= 1.0;
            } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
                baseBeforeBlueGem *= 0.7;
            } else if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
                baseBeforeBlueGem *= 0.3;
            }
            
            baseBeforeBlueGem = applyBlueGemMultiplier(
                    selectedSkinName.replace(" (" + blueGemTier + ")", ""),
                    patternID,
                    blueGemTier,
                    baseBeforeBlueGem
            );
            
            boolean isKnife = item.contains("Knife");
            if (isStattrak == 1) {
                if (isKnife) {
                    baseBeforeBlueGem *= 1.15;
                } else {
                    baseBeforeBlueGem *= 3.0;
                }
            }
            
            rarityKey = item.replace("StatTrak ", "");
            marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarityKey, 1.0);
            bonusPrice = baseBeforeBlueGem * marketMulti;
            
            newBonusPrice = BigDecimal.valueOf(bonusPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
        }

        bonusPrice = capPriceToMarket(selectedSkinName, condition, isStattrak == 1, bonusPrice, blueGemTier);
        newBonusPrice = BigDecimal.valueOf(bonusPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

        if (lowestFloat > itemFloat) {
            lowestFloat = itemFloat;
        }
        
        inventoryValue += bonusPrice;
        newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

        gunName = selectedSkinName;
        nameLabel.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 30));
        nameLabel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(1000, 30));

        String displayName = selectedSkinName;

        if (isStattrak == 1 && !item.contains("Gloves")) {
            displayName = "StatTrak " + selectedSkinName;         
            nameLabel.setForeground(new Color(255, 140, 0));
        } else {
        	nameLabel.setForeground(new Color(230, 230, 235));
        }

        nameLabel.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 44));
        nameLabel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(780, 44));

        // Auto-scale font to fit name on one line
        {
            int fontSize = 28;
            Font testFont = new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, fontSize);
            java.awt.FontMetrics fm = nameLabel.getFontMetrics(testFont);
            while (fontSize > 14 && fm.stringWidth(displayName) > 755) {
                fontSize -= 2;
                testFont = new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, fontSize);
                fm = nameLabel.getFontMetrics(testFont);
            }
            nameLabel.setFont(testFont);
        }
        nameLabel.setText("<html><span style='white-space: nowrap;'>"
                + displayName +
                "</span></html>");

        BigDecimal finalDisplayPrice = BigDecimal
                .valueOf(bonusPrice)
                .setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

        priceLabel.setText("Price: $" + finalDisplayPrice);
        floatLabel.setText(String.format("Float: %.10f", itemFloat));
        conditionLabel.setText("Wear: " + condition);
        patternId.setText("Pattern: " + patternID);
        String autoColName = getCollectionName(selectedSkinName);
        collectionLabel.setText(autoColName != null ? "Collection: " + autoColName : "");
        lowFloatLabel.setText(String.format("Lowest Float: %.10f", lowestFloat));
        totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);

        openingProfit += (bonusPrice - casePrice);

        BigDecimal roundedProfit = BigDecimal
                .valueOf(openingProfit)
                .setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

        if (roundedProfit.signum() >= 0) {
            profitLabel.setForeground(new Color(0, 160, 0));
            profitLabel.setText("Opening Profit: +$" + roundedProfit);
        } else {
            profitLabel.setForeground(Color.RED);
            profitLabel.setText("Opening Profit: -$" + roundedProfit.abs());
        }

        writeStats();

        addUnboxedSkin(selectedSkinName);

        String cleanItemRarity;

        if (isStattrak == 1 && !item.contains("Gloves")) {
            cleanItemRarity = "StatTrak " + item.replace("StatTrak ", "");
        } else {
            cleanItemRarity = item;
        }

        // Downscale to 130x88 max before storing in InventoryItem to save memory
        Image storeImg4 = skinImage;
        if (storeImg4 != null) {
            int iw4 = storeImg4.getWidth(null), ih4 = storeImg4.getHeight(null);
            if (iw4 > 130 || ih4 > 88) {
                double s4 = Math.min(130.0/iw4, 88.0/ih4);
                storeImg4 = storeImg4.getScaledInstance((int)(iw4*s4),(int)(ih4*s4), Image.SCALE_FAST);
            }
        }
        InventoryItem autoItem = new InventoryItem(new ImageIcon(storeImg4), gunName, condition,
                cleanItemRarity, newBonusPrice, itemFloat, (isStattrak == 1 && !item.contains("Gloves")),
                patternID, blueGemTier, bonusPrice);
        autoItem.collection = getCollectionName(gunName);
        inventoryList.add(autoItem);

        currentCase.totalReceived += bonusPrice;
        
        checkUnboxingAchievements(item, gunName, bonusPrice, itemFloat, blueGemTier, 
                                 totMil, totRes, totClass, totCov, totKnife, isStattrak);
        
        repaint();
    }
    
    private void trackOpeningStreak() {
        double caseProfit = finalPrice - currentCase.price;
        
        if (caseProfit > 0) {
            profitStreakCount++;
            lossStreakCount = 0;
        } else {
            lossStreakCount++;
            profitStreakCount = 0;
        }
        
        if (profitStreakCount >= 10 && !achievements.get("profit_streak").isUnlocked) {
            unlockAchievement("profit_streak");
        }
        
        if (lossStreakCount >= 10 && !achievements.get("loss_streak").isUnlocked) {
            unlockAchievement("loss_streak");
        }
    }
    
    private double capPriceToMarket(String skinName, String condition, boolean isStattrak, 
            double calculatedPrice, String blueGemTier) {
        
        String marketKey = isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + skinName : skinName;
        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey);

        if (listings == null || listings.isEmpty()) {
            return calculatedPrice;
        }

        ArrayList<MarketListing> sameCondition = new ArrayList<>();
        ArrayList<MarketListing> snapshot;
        synchronized (globalMarketListings) {
            snapshot = new ArrayList<>(listings);
        }
        for (MarketListing listing : snapshot) {
            if (listing.item.condition.equals(condition)) {
                sameCondition.add(listing);
            }
        }

        if (sameCondition.isEmpty()) {
            return calculatedPrice;
        }

        sameCondition.sort(Comparator.comparingDouble(l -> l.listPrice));
        double lowestMarketPrice = sameCondition.get(0).listPrice;

        return lowestMarketPrice;
    }
	
	private double applyBlueGemMultiplier(String skinName, int patternID, String blueGemTier, double price) {
	    if (blueGemTier == null) {
	        return price;
	    }

	    if (blueGemTier.contains("T1")) {

	        if (skinName.equals("AK-47 | Case Hardened") && (patternID == 661 || patternID == 670)) {
	            return price * 350;
	        }

	        if (skinName.equals("Flip Knife | Case Hardened") && patternID == 670) {
	            return price * 45;
	        }

	        if (skinName.equals("M9 Bayonet | Case Hardened")
	                && (patternID == 601 || patternID == 58 || patternID == 150)) {
	            return price * 85;
	        }

	        return price * 50;

	    } else if (blueGemTier.contains("T2")) {
	        return price * 10;
	    } else if (blueGemTier.contains("T3")) {
	        return price * 3;
	    } else if (blueGemTier.contains("T4")) {
	        return price * 1.5;
	    }

	    return price;
	}

	private double getBasePrice(String skinName) {
		String lowerName = skinName.toLowerCase();
	    boolean isSapphire = lowerName.contains("sapphire");
	    boolean isRuby = lowerName.contains("ruby");
	    boolean isBlackPearl = lowerName.contains("black pearl");
	    boolean isGem = isSapphire || isRuby || isBlackPearl;
		if (isGem) {
			return 10000.00;
		}
		
		if (skinName.contains("Gloves") || skinName.contains("Hand Wraps")) {
		    return getGloveBasePrice(skinName);
		    
		} else if (skinName.equals("Karambit | Slaughter")) {	
			return 1150.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("M9 Bayonet | Crimson Web")) {
			return 650.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Flip Knife | Vanilla")) {
			return 180.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Gut Knife | Fade")) {
			return 230.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Bayonet | Scorched")) {
			return 230.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Bayonet | Boreal Forest")) {
			return 195.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Bayonet | Fade")) {
			return 660.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Flip Knife | Case Hardened")) {
			return 250.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Gut Knife | Forest DDPAT")) {
			return 90.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Gut Knife | Safari Mesh")) {
			return 90.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Karambit | Night")) {
			return 700.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Karambit | Crimson Web")) {
			return 650.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Karambit | Scorched")) {
			return 320.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Karambit | Urban Masked")) {
			return 300.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("M9 Bayonet | Blue Steel")) {
			return 380.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("M9 Bayonet | Case Hardened")) {
			return 420.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("M9 Bayonet | Slaughter")) {
			return 650.00;

		} else if (skinName.contains("M9 Bayonet | Doppler")) {

			if (skinName.contains("Phase 1")) {
				return 1000.00;
			} else if (skinName.contains("Phase 2")) {
				return 1500.00;
			} else if (skinName.contains("Phase 3")) {
				return 1100.00;
			} else if (skinName.contains("Phase 4")) {
				return 1150.00;
			}
			return 1000.0;

		} else if (skinName.contains("Karambit | Doppler")) {

			if (skinName.contains("Phase 1")) {
				return 1300.00;
			} else if (skinName.contains("Phase 2")) {
				return 2300.00;
			} else if (skinName.contains("Phase 3")) {
				return 1400.00;
			} else if (skinName.contains("Phase 4")) {
				return 1350.00;
			}
			return 1000.0;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Butterfly Knife | Case Hardened")) {
			return 750.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Butterfly Knife | Crimson Web")) {
			return 700.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Butterfly Knife | Fade")) {
			return 2500.00;

		} else if (skinName.equals("Butterfly Knife | Slaughter")) {

	private double calculateGlovePrice(String gloveName, String condition, double basePrice) {

	    double price = basePrice;
	    
	    if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
	        price = basePrice;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	        price = basePrice * 1.5;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	        price = basePrice * 1.5 * 1.5;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	        price = basePrice * 1.5 * 1.5 * 1.5;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	        price = basePrice * 1.5 * 1.5 * 1.5 * 4.0;
	    }
	    
	    return price;
	}

	public void writeStats() {
		totalMilspec.setText("Total Milspecs: " + totMil);
		totalRestrict.setText("Total Restricteds: " + totRes);
		totalClass.setText("Total Classifieds: " + totClass);
		totalCovert.setText("Total Coverts: " + totCov);
		totalKnife.setText("Total Knifes: " + totKnife);
		totalGlove.setText("Total Gloves: " + totGlove);
	}

	public static String crateItem(CaseType caseType) {
	    String item = "";
	    isStattrak = 1 + random.nextInt(10);
	    
	    itemNum = 1 + random.nextInt(1000);
	    
	    int goldThreshold = 997;
	    int covertThreshold = 991;
	    int classifiedThreshold = 959;
	    int restrictedThreshold = 799;
	    
	    if (itemNum > goldThreshold) {
	        // Weapon Case One and Bravo: knives only. Breakout and Spectrum: gloves only.
	        if (caseType == CaseType.WEAPON_CASE_ONE || caseType == CaseType.BRAVO) {
	            item = "Knife";
	            priceMulti = 1.0;
	            rarityColor = new Color(228, 174, 57);
	        } else {
	            item = "Gloves";
	            priceMulti = 1.0;
	            isStattrak = 0;
	            rarityColor = new Color(228, 174, 57);
	        }
	    } else if (itemNum > covertThreshold) {
	        item = "Covert";
	        priceMulti = 1.0;
	        rarityColor = new Color(235, 75, 75);
	    } else if (itemNum > classifiedThreshold) {
	        item = "Classified"; 
	        priceMulti = 1.0;
	        rarityColor = new Color(211, 44, 230);
	    } else if (itemNum > restrictedThreshold) {
	        item = "Restricted"; 
	        priceMulti = 1.0;
	        rarityColor = new Color(136, 71, 255);
	    } else {
	        item = "Milspec";
	        priceMulti = 1.0;
	        rarityColor = new Color(75, 105, 255);
	    }
	    return item;
	}

	public static class InventoryItem {
	    ImageIcon image;
	    String name, condition, rarity;
	    BigDecimal price;
	    double itemFloat;
	    boolean isStattrak;
	    int patternID;
	    String blueGemTier;
	    double basePrice;
	    String collection;
	    // Cached thumbnails — computed once, reused across all panels
	    transient ImageIcon thumb110x75;
	    transient ImageIcon thumb130x88;

	    public InventoryItem(ImageIcon image, String name, String condition, String rarity, BigDecimal price,
	            double itemFloat, boolean isStattrak, int patternID, String blueGemTier, double basePrice) {
	        this.image = image;
	        this.name = name;
	        this.condition = condition;
	        this.rarity = rarity;
	        this.price = price;
	        this.itemFloat = itemFloat;
	        this.isStattrak = isStattrak;
	        this.patternID = patternID;
	        this.blueGemTier = blueGemTier;
	        this.basePrice = basePrice;
	    }
	    /** Returns a 110x75 thumbnail, computing and caching it on first call. */
	    public ImageIcon getThumb110() {
	        if (thumb110x75 == null && image != null) {
	            Image src = image.getImage();
	            int w = src.getWidth(null), h = src.getHeight(null);
	            if (w > 0 && h > 0) {
	                double s = Math.min(110.0 / w, 75.0 / h);
	                thumb110x75 = new ImageIcon(src.getScaledInstance((int)(w*s),(int)(h*s), Image.SCALE_FAST));
	            } else {
	                thumb110x75 = image;
	            }
	        }
	        return thumb110x75 != null ? thumb110x75 : image;
	    }
	    /** Returns a 130x88 thumbnail, computing and caching it on first call. */
	    public ImageIcon getThumb130() {
	        if (thumb130x88 == null && image != null) {
	            Image src = image.getImage();
	            int w = src.getWidth(null), h = src.getHeight(null);
	            if (w > 0 && h > 0) {
	                double s = Math.min(130.0 / w, 88.0 / h);
	                thumb130x88 = new ImageIcon(src.getScaledInstance((int)(w*s),(int)(h*s), Image.SCALE_FAST));
	            } else {
	                thumb130x88 = image;
	            }
	        }
	        return thumb130x88 != null ? thumb130x88 : image;
	    }
	}

	public void showInventory() {
	    if (inventoryList.isEmpty()) {
	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "Inventory is empty!");
	        return;
	    }

	    JFrame invFrame = new JFrame("Inventory");
	    invFrame.setSize(700, 550);
	    invFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    invFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    invFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(true);

	    JPanel controlPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(3, 1));
	    
	    JPanel searchPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));
	    JLabel searchLabel = new JLabel("Search:");
	    searchLabel.setForeground(Color.BLACK);
	    searchLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    JTextField searchField = new JTextField(20);
	    searchField.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 14));
	    searchPanel.add(searchLabel);
	    searchPanel.add(searchField);
	    
	    JPanel sortPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));
	    JPanel sellPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));

	    JLabel sortPriceLabel = new JLabel("Sort by Price:");
	    JComboBox<String> priceSortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[] {
	        "Default", "Lowest Price", "Highest Price"
	    });
	    styleComboBox(priceSortBox);

	    JLabel sortRarityLabel = new JLabel("Filter by Rarity:");
	    JComboBox<String> raritySortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[] {
	        "Default", "Knife", "Gloves", "Covert", "Classified", "Restricted", "Milspec"
	    });
	    styleComboBox(raritySortBox);
