	    JLabel sortFloatLabel = new JLabel("Sort by Float:");
	    JComboBox<String> floatSortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[] {
	        "Default", "Lowest Float", "Highest Float"
	    });
	    styleComboBox(floatSortBox);

	    // Collection filter
	    java.util.Set<String> colSetInv = new java.util.LinkedHashSet<>();
	    colSetInv.add("All");
	    for (InventoryItem it : inventoryList) {
	        if (it.collection != null && !it.collection.isEmpty()) colSetInv.add(it.collection);
	    }
	    JLabel sortColLabel = new JLabel("Collection:");
	    JComboBox<String> collectionSortBox = new JComboBox<>(colSetInv.toArray(new String[0]));
	    styleComboBox(collectionSortBox);

	    JComboBox<String> sellRarityBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[] {
	        "Default", "Knife", "Gloves", "Covert", "Classified", "Restricted", "Milspec"
	    });
	    styleComboBox(sellRarityBox);

	    JButton sellAllButton = new JButton("SELL ALL");
	    sellAllButton.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override
	        public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) {
	            playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
	        }
	    });

	    sortPanel.add(sortPriceLabel);
	    sortPanel.add(priceSortBox);
	    sortPanel.add(sortRarityLabel);
	    sortPanel.add(raritySortBox);
	    sortPanel.add(sortFloatLabel);
	    sortPanel.add(floatSortBox);
	    sortPanel.add(sortColLabel);
	    sortPanel.add(collectionSortBox);

	    sellPanel.add(new JLabel("Sell:"));
	    sellPanel.add(sellRarityBox);
	    sellPanel.add(sellAllButton);

	    controlPanel.add(searchPanel);
	    controlPanel.add(sortPanel);
	    controlPanel.add(sellPanel);

	    invFrame.add(controlPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 2, 10, 10));
	    grid.setBackground(Color.DARK_GRAY);
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));

	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    optimizeScrollPane(scroll);
	    invFrame.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    // Use the class-level RARITY_ORDER instead of allocating a new map every time
	    // Thumbnails are fetched via item.getThumb130() which caches on first access — no separate map needed

	    Runnable rebuildGrid = () -> {
	        grid.removeAll();
	        
	        String searchText = searchField.getText().toLowerCase().trim();
	        String priceOrder = (String) priceSortBox.getSelectedItem();
	        String raritySelection = (String) raritySortBox.getSelectedItem();
	        String floatOrder = (String) floatSortBox.getSelectedItem();
	        String collectionOrder = (String) collectionSortBox.getSelectedItem();

	        List<InventoryItem> filtered = new ArrayList<>(inventoryList);

	        if (!searchText.isEmpty()) {
	            filtered.removeIf(item -> !item.name.toLowerCase().contains(searchText) &&
	                              !item.condition.toLowerCase().contains(searchText) &&
	                              !item.rarity.toLowerCase().contains(searchText));
	        }
	        if (!"Default".equals(raritySelection)) {
	            filtered.removeIf(it -> !it.rarity.contains(raritySelection));
	        }
	        if (!"All".equals(collectionOrder)) {
	            filtered.removeIf(it -> !collectionOrder.equals(it.collection));
	        }

	        // Sort by rarity using class-level RARITY_ORDER map (no stream allocation)
	        filtered.sort((a, b) -> Integer.compare(
	            RARITY_ORDER.getOrDefault(a.rarity.replace("StatTrak ", ""), 99),
	            RARITY_ORDER.getOrDefault(b.rarity.replace("StatTrak ", ""), 99)));

	        if ("Lowest Price".equals(priceOrder)) {
	            filtered.sort(Comparator.comparing(a -> a.price));
	        } else if ("Highest Price".equals(priceOrder)) {
	            filtered.sort((a, b) -> b.price.compareTo(a.price));
	        }
	        if ("Lowest Float".equals(floatOrder)) {
	            filtered.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(a.itemFloat, b.itemFloat));
	        } else if ("Highest Float".equals(floatOrder)) {
	            filtered.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.itemFloat, a.itemFloat));
	        }

	        int maxInitialRender = 50;
	        int itemsToRender = Math.min(maxInitialRender, filtered.size());
	        
	        for (int i = 0; i < itemsToRender; i++) {
	            InventoryItem item = filtered.get(i);
	            JPanel card = createInventoryCardFast(item, item.getThumb130());
	            grid.add(card);
	        }
	        
	        if (filtered.size() > maxInitialRender) {
	            JPanel loadMorePanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	            loadMorePanel.setBackground(Color.DARK_GRAY);
	            JButton loadMoreBtn = new JButton("Load All? (" + (filtered.size() - maxInitialRender) + " items)");
	            loadMoreBtn.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	            loadMoreBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	                loadMorePanel.setVisible(false);
	                for (int i = maxInitialRender; i < filtered.size(); i++) {
	                    InventoryItem item = filtered.get(i);
	                    JPanel card = createInventoryCardFast(item, item.getThumb130());
	                    grid.add(card, grid.getComponentCount() - 1);
	                }
	                grid.revalidate();
	                grid.repaint();
	            });
	            loadMorePanel.add(loadMoreBtn, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	            grid.add(loadMorePanel);
	        }

	        grid.revalidate();
	        grid.repaint();
	    };

	    grid.putClientProperty("rebuildGrid", rebuildGrid);
	    javax.swing.Timer searchTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(300, e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    searchTimer.setRepeats(false);
	    
	    searchField.addKeyListener(new KeyAdapter() {
	        public void keyReleased(KeyEvent e) {
	            searchTimer.restart();
	        }
	    });

	    priceSortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    raritySortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    floatSortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    collectionSortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());

	    SwingUtilities.invokeLater(rebuildGrid);
	    
	    sellAllButton.addActionListener(e -> {
	        String rarity = (String) sellRarityBox.getSelectedItem();
	        
	        String message;
	        if (rarity.equals("Gloves")) {
	            message = "Instasell all Glove items?";
	        } else if (rarity.equals("Knife")) {
	            message = "Instasell all Knife items?";
	        } else {
	            message = "Instasell all " + rarity + " items?";
	        }

	        int confirm = JOptionPane.showConfirmDialog(
	            invFrame,
	            message,
	            "Confirm Sell",
	            JOptionPane.YES_NO_OPTION
	        );

	        if (confirm != JOptionPane.YES_OPTION) return;

	        sellItemsByRarity(rarity);
	        rebuildGrid.run();
	        refreshMainUI();
	    });
	    
	    invFrame.setVisible(true);
	    
	    javax.swing.Timer timer = new javax.swing.Timer(100, e -> {
	        invFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(false);
	        invFrame.toFront();
	        invFrame.requestFocus();
	    });
	    timer.setRepeats(false);
	    timer.start();
	}
	
	private JPanel createInventoryCardFast(InventoryItem item, ImageIcon cachedImage) {
	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    card.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 40));
	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(getRarityColor(item.rarity), 2));
	    card.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(220, 165));
	    card.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(220, 165));

	    JLabel imgLabel;
	    if (cachedImage != null) {
	        imgLabel = new JLabel(cachedImage);
	    } else if (item.image != null) {
	        Image scaled = item.getThumb110().getImage();
	        imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	    } else {
	        String cleanName = item.name.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("* ", "").trim();
	        if (item.blueGemTier != null && cleanName.contains("(Blue Gem")) cleanName = cleanName.substring(0, cleanName.indexOf("(Blue Gem")).trim();
	        Image img = getSkinImageFromName(cleanName);
	        if (img != null) {
	            Image scaled = img.getScaledInstance(110, 75, Image.SCALE_FAST);
	            imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	            item.image = new ImageIcon(img);
	        } else {
	            imgLabel = new JLabel("?", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	            imgLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	        }
	    }
	    imgLabel.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    imgLabel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(110, 75));

	    String displayName = item.isStattrak ? "ST " + item.name : item.name;
	    JLabel n = new JLabel(displayName, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    n.setForeground(item.isStattrak ? new Color(255, 153, 51) : Color.WHITE);
	    n.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));

	    JLabel c = new JLabel(item.condition, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    c.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY); c.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9));

	    JLabel p = new JLabel("$" + item.price, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    p.setForeground(Color.YELLOW); p.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));

	    JLabel r = new JLabel(item.rarity, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    r.setForeground(getRarityColor(item.rarity)); r.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9));

	    if (item.collection == null) item.collection = getCollectionName(item.name);
	    JLabel col = new JLabel(item.collection != null ? item.collection : "", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    col.setForeground(new Color(170, 130, 255)); col.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.ITALIC, 8));

	    JPanel text = new JPanel(new GridLayout(5, 1, 0, 0));
	    text.setBackground(new Color(22, 22, 30));
	    text.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(2, 2, 2, 2));
	    text.add(n); text.add(c); text.add(r); text.add(p); text.add(col);

	    card.add(imgLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    card.add(text, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    card.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        public void mouseClicked(MouseEvent e) { showItemPopup(item); }
	    });
	    return card;
	}

	public void showItemPopup(InventoryItem item) {
	    JDialog dialog = new JDialog((Frame) null, "Item Details", true);
	    dialog.setSize(460, 480);
	    dialog.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    dialog.setDefaultCloseOperation(JDialog.DISPOSE_ON_CLOSE);

	    Color BG      = new Color(18, 18, 26);
	    Color BG_CARD = new Color(28, 28, 40);
	    Color ACCENT  = getRarityColor(item.rarity);
	    Color TEXT    = new Color(230, 230, 235);
	    Color DIM     = new Color(140, 140, 155);

	    JPanel root = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(0, 0));
	    root.setBackground(BG);
	    root.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(ACCENT, 2));

	    JPanel header = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(12, 0));
	    header.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	    header.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(12, 16, 12, 16));

	    if (item.image != null) {
	        Image scaled = item.getThumb110().getImage();
	        JLabel imgLbl = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	        imgLbl.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(ACCENT, 1));
	        header.add(imgLbl, BorderLayout.WEST);
	    }

	    JPanel nameMeta = new JPanel();
	    nameMeta.setLayout(new BoxLayout(nameMeta, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    nameMeta.setBackground(BG_CARD);

	    String displayName = (item.isStattrak ? "StatTrak " : "") + item.name;
	    JLabel nameL = new JLabel("<html><body style=\'width:220px\'>" + displayName + "</body></html>");
	    nameL.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));
	    nameL.setForeground(item.isStattrak ? new Color(255, 153, 51) : TEXT);
	    nameL.setAlignmentX(java.awt.Component.LEFT_ALIGNMENT);

	    JLabel rarityL = new JLabel(item.rarity);
	    rarityL.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    rarityL.setForeground(ACCENT);
	    rarityL.setAlignmentX(java.awt.Component.LEFT_ALIGNMENT);

	    JLabel condL = new JLabel(item.condition);
	    condL.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	    condL.setForeground(DIM);
	    condL.setAlignmentX(java.awt.Component.LEFT_ALIGNMENT);

	    nameMeta.add(nameL);
	    nameMeta.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 4)));
	    nameMeta.add(rarityL);
	    nameMeta.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 3)));
	    nameMeta.add(condL);

	    if (item.collection == null) item.collection = getCollectionName(item.name);
	    if (item.collection != null) {
	        JLabel colL = new JLabel(item.collection);
	        colL.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.ITALIC, 10));
	        colL.setForeground(new Color(170, 130, 255));
	        colL.setAlignmentX(java.awt.Component.LEFT_ALIGNMENT);
	        nameMeta.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 3)));
	        nameMeta.add(colL);
	    }
	    header.add(nameMeta, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    root.add(header, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    double currentPrice = item.price.doubleValue();
	    String itemMarketKey = normalizeSkinName(item.name);
	    if (item.isStattrak) itemMarketKey = "StatTrak " + itemMarketKey;
	    final String finalMarketKey = itemMarketKey;

	    NpcBuyOrder bestOrder = getBestNpcBuyOrder(finalMarketKey, item.condition);
	    double npcBuyPrice = (bestOrder != null) ? bestOrder.price : currentPrice * (1 - QUICK_SELL_DISCOUNT);

	    JPanel statsPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 2, 8, 6));
	    statsPanel.setBackground(BG);
	    statsPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(12, 18, 6, 18));

	    java.util.List<String[]> statsList = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	    statsList.add(new String[]{"Market Price",   String.format("$%.2f", currentPrice)});
	    statsList.add(new String[]{"Best Buy Order", bestOrder != null
	        ? String.format("$%.2f  (%s)", npcBuyPrice, bestOrder.buyerName != null ? bestOrder.buyerName : "NPC")
	        : "None"});
	    statsList.add(new String[]{"Float",       String.format("%.8f", item.itemFloat)});
	    statsList.add(new String[]{"Pattern ID",  String.valueOf(item.patternID)});
	    if (item.blueGemTier != null) statsList.add(new String[]{"Blue Gem", item.blueGemTier});

	    for (String[] row : statsList) {
	        JLabel key = new JLabel(row[0]);
	        key.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	        key.setForeground(DIM);
	        JLabel val = new JLabel(row[1]);
	        val.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	        val.setForeground(TEXT);
	        statsPanel.add(key);
	        statsPanel.add(val);
	    }
	    root.add(statsPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JPanel btnOuter = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(0, 6));
	    btnOuter.setBackground(BG);
	    btnOuter.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 16, 14, 16));

	    String qsLabel = bestOrder != null
	        ? String.format("Quick Sell  |  $%.2f  (Buy Order)", npcBuyPrice)
	        : String.format("Quick Sell  |  $%.2f  (no orders, discounted)", npcBuyPrice);
	    JButton quickSellBtn  = new JButton(qsLabel);
	    quickSellBtn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    quickSellBtn.setForeground(new Color(80, 220, 120));

	    JButton listBtn      = new JButton("List on Market");
	    JButton viewChartBtn = new JButton("View Price Chart");

	    for (JButton btn : new JButton[]{quickSellBtn, listBtn, viewChartBtn}) {
	        btn.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	        if (btn != quickSellBtn) {
	            btn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	            btn.setForeground(TEXT);
	        }
	        btn.setFocusPainted(false);
	        btn.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(60, 60, 80), 1),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(7, 10, 7, 10)));
	        btn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	            @Override public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) { playSoundFile("button_click.wav"); }
	            @Override public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) { btn.setBackground(new Color(55, 55, 75)); }
	            @Override public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e)  { btn.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52)); }
	        });
	    }

	    JPanel bottomRow = new JPanel(new GridLayout(1, 2, 8, 0));
	    bottomRow.setBackground(BG);
	    bottomRow.add(listBtn);
	    bottomRow.add(viewChartBtn);

	    btnOuter.add(quickSellBtn, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    btnOuter.add(bottomRow, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    root.add(btnOuter, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    viewChartBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	        dialog.dispose();
	        showSkinPriceChart(finalMarketKey, item.condition, null);
	    });

	    quickSellBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	        NpcBuyOrder order = getBestNpcBuyOrder(finalMarketKey, item.condition);
	        double salePrice;
	        if (order != null) {
	            salePrice = order.price;
	            order.filled = Math.min(order.filled + 1, order.quantity);
	            order.lastFillTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
	        } else {
	            salePrice = currentPrice * (1 - QUICK_SELL_DISCOUNT);
	        }
	        balance += salePrice;
	        inventoryValue = Math.max(0.0, inventoryValue - item.price.doubleValue());
	        inventoryList.remove(item);
	        writeStats();
	        newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	        totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	        updateBalanceLabel();
	        refreshMainUI();
	        dialog.dispose();
	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, order != null
	            ? String.format("Sold for $%.2f", salePrice)
	            : String.format("Sold for $%.2f", salePrice));
	        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> refreshInventoryTab());
	    });

	    listBtn.addActionListener(e -> {

	        JDialog listDialog = new JDialog(dialog, "List on Market", true);
	        listDialog.setSize(360, 240);
	        listDialog.setLocationRelativeTo(dialog);
	        listDialog.setDefaultCloseOperation(JDialog.DISPOSE_ON_CLOSE);

	        JPanel lroot = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(0, 0));
	        lroot.setBackground(BG);
	        lroot.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(ACCENT, 2));

	        JPanel lheader = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	        lheader.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	        lheader.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(12, 16, 12, 16));
	        JLabel lTitle = new JLabel("List on Market");
	        lTitle.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        lTitle.setForeground(ACCENT);
	        JLabel lSkin = new JLabel(displayName + "  ·  " + item.condition);
	        lSkin.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	        lSkin.setForeground(DIM);
	        lheader.add(lTitle, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	        lheader.add(lSkin, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	        lroot.add(lheader, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	        JPanel lform = new JPanel(new GridBagLayout());
	        lform.setBackground(BG);
	        lform.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(14, 20, 8, 20));
	        GridBagConstraints lgc = new GridBagConstraints();
	        lgc.insets = new java.awt.Insets(6, 4, 6, 4);
	        lgc.fill = GridBagConstraints.HORIZONTAL;

	        lgc.gridx = 0; lgc.gridy = 0; lgc.weightx = 0.4;
	        JLabel mktLbl = new JLabel("Market price:");
	        mktLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	        mktLbl.setForeground(DIM);
	        lform.add(mktLbl, lgc);
	        lgc.gridx = 1; lgc.weightx = 0.6;
	        JLabel mktVal = new JLabel(String.format("$%.2f", currentPrice));
	        mktVal.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	        mktVal.setForeground(TEXT);
	        lform.add(mktVal, lgc);

	        lgc.gridx = 0; lgc.gridy = 1; lgc.weightx = 0.4;
	        JLabel priceLbl = new JLabel("Your price ($):");
	        priceLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	        priceLbl.setForeground(DIM);
	        lform.add(priceLbl, lgc);
	        lgc.gridx = 1; lgc.weightx = 0.6;
	        JTextField priceField = new JTextField(String.format("%.2f", currentPrice));
	        priceField.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	        priceField.setForeground(TEXT);
	        priceField.setCaretColor(TEXT);
	        priceField.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	        priceField.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(60, 60, 80), 1),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 8, 4, 8)));
	        lform.add(priceField, lgc);

	        lgc.gridx = 0; lgc.gridy = 2; lgc.gridwidth = 2;
	        JLabel estLbl = new JLabel(" ");
	        estLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.ITALIC, 10));
	        estLbl.setForeground(new Color(100, 210, 255));
	        lform.add(estLbl, lgc);

	        priceField.getDocument().addDocumentListener(new javax.swing.event.DocumentListener() {
	            void update() {
	                try {
	                    double p = Double.parseDouble(priceField.getText().trim());
	                    int t = calculateSellTime(p, currentPrice);
	                    estLbl.setText("Est. sell time: ~" + t + "s");
	                } catch (NumberFormatException ex) { estLbl.setText("Enter a valid price"); }
	            }
	            public void insertUpdate(javax.swing.event.DocumentEvent e) { update(); }
	            public void removeUpdate(javax.swing.event.DocumentEvent e) { update(); }
	            public void changedUpdate(javax.swing.event.DocumentEvent e) { update(); }
	        });

	        int initTime = calculateSellTime(currentPrice, currentPrice);
	        estLbl.setText("Est. sell time: ~" + initTime + "s");

	        lroot.add(lform, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	        JButton lConfirm = new JButton("List Item");
	        JButton lCancel  = new JButton("Cancel");
	        for (JButton b : new JButton[]{lConfirm, lCancel}) {
	            b.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	            b.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	            b.setForeground(TEXT);
	            b.setFocusPainted(false);
	            b.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	                BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(60, 60, 80), 1),
	                BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(7, 16, 7, 16)));
	            b.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	                @Override public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) { b.setBackground(new Color(55, 55, 75)); }
	                @Override public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e)  { b.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52)); }
	            });
	        }
	        lConfirm.setForeground(new Color(80, 220, 120));

	        JPanel lbtns = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.RIGHT, 8, 8));
	        lbtns.setBackground(BG);
	        lbtns.add(lCancel);
	        lbtns.add(lConfirm);
	        lroot.add(lbtns, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	        lCancel.addActionListener(ev -> listDialog.dispose());
	        lConfirm.addActionListener(ev -> {
	            try {
	                double listPrice = Double.parseDouble(priceField.getText().trim());
	                if (listPrice <= 0) { JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(listDialog, "Price must be positive!"); return; }
	                int sellTime = calculateSellTime(listPrice, currentPrice);
	                activeListings.add(new MarketListing(item, listPrice, sellTime, true));
	                inventoryValue = Math.max(0.0, inventoryValue - item.price.doubleValue());
	                inventoryList.remove(item);
	                writeStats();
	                newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	                totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	                refreshMainUI();
	                listDialog.dispose();
	                dialog.dispose();
	                JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(hGui.this,
	                    String.format("Listed for $%.2f  ·  Est. sell time: ~%ds", listPrice, sellTime));
	                SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> refreshInventoryTab());
	            } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
	                JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(listDialog, "Invalid price format!");
	            }
	        });

	        listDialog.setContentPane(lroot);
	        listDialog.setVisible(true);
	    });

	    dialog.setContentPane(root);
	    dialog.setVisible(true);
	}

	private void showGenerateSkinDialog() {
	    Color BG      = new Color(18, 18, 26);
	    Color BG_CARD = new Color(28, 28, 40);
	    Color TEXT    = new Color(230, 230, 235);
	    Color DIM     = new Color(140, 140, 155);
	    Color ACCENT  = new Color(40, 120, 200);

	    JDialog dialog = new JDialog((Frame) null, "Generate Skin", true);
	    dialog.setSize(500, 440);
	    dialog.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    dialog.setDefaultCloseOperation(JDialog.DISPOSE_ON_CLOSE);

	    JPanel root = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(0, 0));
	    root.setBackground(BG);
	    root.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(ACCENT, 2));

	    JPanel header = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    header.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	    header.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(12, 18, 12, 18));
	    JLabel title = new JLabel("Generate Skin into Inventory");
	    title.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 15));
	    title.setForeground(ACCENT);
	    header.add(title, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    JLabel sub = new JLabel("Create any skin at any float for testing");
	    sub.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.ITALIC, 11));
	    sub.setForeground(DIM);
	    header.add(sub, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    root.add(header, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    java.util.List<String> skinList = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	    for (String k : globalMarketListings.keySet()) {
	        if (!k.startsWith("StatTrak ") && !k.startsWith("StatTrak ")) skinList.add(k);
	    }
	    java.util.Collections.sort(skinList);
	    String[] skinArray = skinList.toArray(new String[0]);

	    JPanel form = new JPanel(new GridBagLayout());
	    form.setBackground(BG);
	    form.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(16, 22, 8, 22));
	    GridBagConstraints gc = new GridBagConstraints();
	    gc.insets = new java.awt.Insets(7, 5, 7, 5);
	    gc.fill = GridBagConstraints.HORIZONTAL;
	    Font lf = new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11);
	    Font vf = new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11);

	    gc.gridx = 0; gc.gridy = 0; gc.weightx = 0.35;
	    JLabel skinLbl = new JLabel("Skin:");
	    skinLbl.setForeground(DIM); skinLbl.setFont(lf);
	    form.add(skinLbl, gc);
	    gc.gridx = 1; gc.weightx = 0.65;
	    JComboBox<String> skinBox = new JComboBox<>(skinArray);
	    skinBox.setEditable(true);
	    skinBox.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	    skinBox.setForeground(TEXT);
	    skinBox.setFont(vf);

	    javax.swing.text.JTextComponent skinEditor = (javax.swing.text.JTextComponent) skinBox.getEditor().getEditorComponent();
	    skinEditor.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	    skinEditor.setForeground(TEXT);
	    skinEditor.setCaretColor(TEXT);
	    form.add(skinBox, gc);

	    gc.gridx = 0; gc.gridy = 1; gc.weightx = 0.35;
	    JLabel floatLbl = new JLabel("Float:");
	    floatLbl.setForeground(DIM); floatLbl.setFont(lf);
	    form.add(floatLbl, gc);
	    gc.gridx = 1; gc.weightx = 0.65;
	    JTextField floatField = new JTextField("0.15");
	    floatField.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	    floatField.setForeground(TEXT);
	    floatField.setCaretColor(TEXT);
	    floatField.setFont(vf);
	    floatField.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(60, 60, 80), 1),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 8, 4, 8)));
	    form.add(floatField, gc);

	    gc.gridx = 0; gc.gridy = 2; gc.gridwidth = 2;
	    JLabel rangeHint = new JLabel(" ");
	    rangeHint.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.ITALIC, 10));
	    rangeHint.setForeground(new Color(100, 210, 255));
	    form.add(rangeHint, gc);
	    gc.gridwidth = 1;

	    gc.gridx = 0; gc.gridy = 3; gc.weightx = 0.35;
	    JLabel qtyLbl = new JLabel("Quantity:");
	    qtyLbl.setForeground(DIM); qtyLbl.setFont(lf);
	    form.add(qtyLbl, gc);
	    gc.gridx = 1; gc.weightx = 0.65;
	    JSpinner qtySpinner2 = new JSpinner(new SpinnerNumberModel(1, 1, 100, 1));
	    qtySpinner2.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	    qtySpinner2.setFont(vf);
	    form.add(qtySpinner2, gc);

	    gc.gridx = 0; gc.gridy = 4; gc.gridwidth = 2;
	    JCheckBox stCheck = new JCheckBox("StatTrak");
	    stCheck.setBackground(BG);
	    stCheck.setForeground(new Color(255, 153, 51));
	    stCheck.setFont(vf);
	    form.add(stCheck, gc);
	    gc.gridwidth = 1;

	    root.add(form, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    Runnable updateHint = () -> {
	        String sel = skinBox.getEditor().getItem().toString();
	        String bare = sel.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();
	        FloatRange fr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(bare);
	        if (fr == null) {
	            for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e2 : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet())
	                if (bare.startsWith(e2.getKey())) { fr = e2.getValue(); break; }
	        }
	        double mn = (fr != null && fr.min != null) ? fr.min : 0.0;
	        double mx = (fr != null && fr.max != null) ? fr.max : 1.0;
	        rangeHint.setText(String.format("Float range for this skin: %.4f  –  %.4f", mn, mx));
	    };
	    skinBox.addActionListener(e -> updateHint.run());
	    skinEditor.getDocument().addDocumentListener(new javax.swing.event.DocumentListener() {
	        public void insertUpdate(javax.swing.event.DocumentEvent e) { updateHint.run(); }
	        public void removeUpdate(javax.swing.event.DocumentEvent e) { updateHint.run(); }
	        public void changedUpdate(javax.swing.event.DocumentEvent e) { updateHint.run(); }
	    });
	    updateHint.run();

	    JButton genBtn    = new JButton("Generate");
	    JButton cancelBtn = new JButton("Cancel");
	    for (JButton btn : new JButton[]{genBtn, cancelBtn}) {
	        btn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	        btn.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	        btn.setForeground(TEXT);
	        btn.setFocusPainted(false);
	        btn.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(60, 60, 80), 1),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 18, 8, 18)));
	        btn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	            @Override public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) { btn.setBackground(new Color(55, 55, 75)); }
	            @Override public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e)  { btn.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52)); }
	        });
	    }
	    genBtn.setForeground(new Color(80, 220, 120));

	    JPanel btnRow = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.RIGHT, 10, 10));
	    btnRow.setBackground(BG);
	    btnRow.add(cancelBtn);
	    btnRow.add(genBtn);
	    root.add(btnRow, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    cancelBtn.addActionListener(e -> dialog.dispose());

	    genBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	        String rawSkin = skinBox.getEditor().getItem().toString().trim();
	        String bareSkin = rawSkin.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();

	        double floatVal;
	        try {
	            floatVal = Double.parseDouble(floatField.getText().trim());
	        } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(dialog, "Invalid float value."); return;
	        }

	        FloatRange fr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(bareSkin);
	        if (fr == null) {
	            for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e2 : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet())
	                if (bareSkin.startsWith(e2.getKey())) { fr = e2.getValue(); break; }
	        }
	        double minF = (fr != null && fr.min != null) ? fr.min : 0.0;
	        double maxF = (fr != null && fr.max != null) ? fr.max : 1.0;

	        if (floatVal < minF || floatVal > maxF) {
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(dialog,
	                String.format("Float %.4f is outside the valid range for this skin (%.4f – %.4f).", floatVal, minF, maxF));
	            return;
	        }

	        boolean isST = stCheck.isSelected();
	        int qty = (Integer) qtySpinner2.getValue();

	        String condition;
	        if      (floatVal <= 0.07) condition = "Factory New";
	        else if (floatVal <= 0.15) condition = "Minimal Wear";
	        else if (floatVal <= 0.38) condition = "Field-Tested";
	        else if (floatVal <= 0.45) condition = "Well-Worn";
	        else                       condition = "Battle-Scarred";

	        String rarity = getSkinRarity(bareSkin);
	        double basePrice = getBasePrice(bareSkin);
	        double mMult = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarity, 1.0);
	        basePrice *= condition.equals("Factory New") ? 2.5 :
	                     condition.equals("Minimal Wear") ? 1.7 :
	                     condition.equals("Field-Tested") ? 1.0 :
	                     condition.equals("Well-Worn") ? 0.7 : 0.3;
	        basePrice *= mMult;
	        if (isST) {
	            boolean isCW9 = bareSkin.contains("Crimson Web");
	            boolean isD9  = bareSkin.contains("Doppler");
	            if (isCW9)                            basePrice *= 2.0;
	            else if (isD9)                        basePrice *= 0.80;
	            else if (rarity.equals("Knife"))      basePrice *= 0.90;
	            else                                  basePrice *= 1.85;
	        }

	        int pid = random.nextInt(1000);
	        String bgTier = getBlueGemTier(bareSkin, pid);
	        String finalSkinName = bgTier != null ? bareSkin + " (" + bgTier + ")" : bareSkin;
	        if (bgTier != null) basePrice = applyBlueGemMultiplier(bareSkin, pid, bgTier, basePrice);

	        String displayRarity = isST ? "StatTrak " + rarity : rarity;
	        Image img = getSkinImageFromName(bareSkin);

	        for (int i = 0; i < qty; i++) {
	            int thisPid = random.nextInt(1000);
	            String thisBgTier = getBlueGemTier(bareSkin, thisPid);
	            String thisSkinName = thisBgTier != null ? bareSkin + " (" + thisBgTier + ")" : bareSkin;
	            double thisPrice = basePrice;
	            if (thisBgTier != null) thisPrice = applyBlueGemMultiplier(bareSkin, thisPid, thisBgTier, getBasePrice(bareSkin) * mMult);

	            InventoryItem generated = new InventoryItem(
	                img != null ? new ImageIcon(img) : null,
	                thisSkinName, condition, displayRarity,
	                BigDecimal.valueOf(thisPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                floatVal, isST, thisPid, thisBgTier, thisPrice);
	            generated.collection = getCollectionName(bareSkin);
	            inventoryList.add(generated);
	            inventoryValue += thisPrice;
	        }

	        newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	        totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	        writeStats();
	        refreshMainUI();
	        dialog.dispose();

	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, String.format(
	            "Generated %d× %s%s\nCondition: %s  ·  Float: %.6f",
	            qty, isST ? "StatTrak " : "", bareSkin, condition, floatVal));
	        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> refreshInventoryTab());
	    });

	    dialog.setContentPane(root);
	    dialog.setVisible(true);
	}

	public Color getRarityColor(String rarity) {
	    if (rarity.contains("Knife"))      return new Color(228, 174,  57);
	    if (rarity.contains("Golds"))      return new Color(228, 174,  57);
	    if (rarity.contains("Gloves"))     return new Color(228, 174,  57);
	    if (rarity.contains("Covert"))     return new Color(235,  75,  75);
	    if (rarity.contains("Classified")) return new Color(211,  44, 230);
	    if (rarity.contains("Restricted")) return new Color(136,  71, 255);
    if (rarity.contains("Milspec"))    return new Color(75, 105, 255);
    if (rarity.contains("Industrial")) return new Color(110, 190, 110);
	    return new Color(75, 105, 255);
	}

	public void tradeUp() {
	    if (inventoryList.size() < 10) {
	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "Not enough skins to trade up!");
	        return;
	    }

	    JFrame tradeFrame = new JFrame("Select 10 Skins for Trade-Up");
	    tradeFrame.setSize(900, 600);
	    tradeFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    tradeFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());

	    JPanel controlPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1));
	    
	    JPanel searchPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));
	    JLabel searchLabel = new JLabel("Search:");
	    JTextField searchField = new JTextField(20);
	    searchPanel.add(searchLabel);
	    searchPanel.add(searchField);
	    
	    JPanel filterPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));
	    JLabel sortFloatLabel = new JLabel("Sort by Float:");
	    JComboBox<String> floatSortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[] { "Ascending", "Descending" });
	    styleComboBox(floatSortBox);

	    JLabel sortRarityLabel = new JLabel("Sort by Rarity:");
	    JComboBox<String> raritySortBox = new JComboBox<>(
	            new String[] { "Default", "Milspec", "Restricted", "Classified" });
	    styleComboBox(raritySortBox);

	    filterPanel.add(sortFloatLabel);
	    filterPanel.add(floatSortBox);
	    filterPanel.add(sortRarityLabel);
	    filterPanel.add(raritySortBox);
	    
	    controlPanel.add(searchPanel);
	    controlPanel.add(filterPanel);
	    tradeFrame.add(controlPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 3, 10, 10));
	    grid.setBackground(Color.DARK_GRAY);
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));

	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    optimizeScrollPane(scroll);
	    tradeFrame.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JButton confirm = new JButton("Trade-Up");
	    tradeFrame.add(confirm, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    
	    confirm.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override
	        public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) {
	            playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
	        }
	    });

	    ArrayList<InventoryItem> selectedItems = new ArrayList<>();
	    // Thumbnails are fetched via item.getThumb130() which caches on first access — no separate map needed

	    Runnable rebuildGrid = () -> {
	        grid.removeAll();
	        
	        String searchText = searchField.getText().toLowerCase().trim();
	        List<InventoryItem> items = new ArrayList<>(inventoryList);

	        items.removeIf(it -> it.rarity.contains("Knife") || it.rarity.contains("Covert"));
	        
	        if (!searchText.isEmpty()) {
	            items.removeIf(item -> !item.name.toLowerCase().contains(searchText));
	        }

	        Map<String, Integer> rarityOrder = new HashMap<>();
	        rarityOrder.put("Milspec", 1);
	        rarityOrder.put("Restricted", 2);
	        rarityOrder.put("Classified", 3);

	        String selectedRarity = (String) raritySortBox.getSelectedItem();
	        String floatOrder = (String) floatSortBox.getSelectedItem();

	        if (!"Default".equals(selectedRarity)) {
	            items.removeIf(it -> !it.rarity.contains(selectedRarity));
	        }

	        items.sort((a, b) -> {
	            int orderA = rarityOrder.entrySet().stream().filter(e -> a.rarity.contains(e.getKey()))
	                    .map(Map.Entry::getValue).findFirst().orElse(999);
	            int orderB = rarityOrder.entrySet().stream().filter(e -> b.rarity.contains(e.getKey()))
	                    .map(Map.Entry::getValue).findFirst().orElse(999);
	            return Integer.compare(orderA, orderB);
	        });

	        if ("Ascending".equals(floatOrder)) {
	            items.sort(Comparator.comparingDouble(a -> a.itemFloat));
	        } else if ("Descending".equals(floatOrder)) {
	            items.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.itemFloat, a.itemFloat));
	        }

	        int maxInitialRender = 60;
	        int itemsToRender = Math.min(maxInitialRender, items.size());
	        
	        for (int i = 0; i < itemsToRender; i++) {
	            InventoryItem item = items.get(i);
	            JPanel card = createTradeUpCardFast(item, item.getThumb130(), selectedItems, grid);
	            grid.add(card);
	        }
	        
	        if (items.size() > maxInitialRender) {
	            JPanel loadMorePanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	            loadMorePanel.setBackground(Color.DARK_GRAY);
	            JButton loadMoreBtn = new JButton("Load All? (" + (items.size() - maxInitialRender) + " items)");
	            loadMoreBtn.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	            loadMoreBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	                loadMorePanel.setVisible(false);
	                for (int i = maxInitialRender; i < items.size(); i++) {
	                    InventoryItem item = items.get(i);
	                    JPanel card = createTradeUpCardFast(item, item.getThumb130(), selectedItems, grid);
	                    grid.add(card, grid.getComponentCount() - 1);
	                }
	                grid.revalidate();
	                grid.repaint();
	            });
	            loadMorePanel.add(loadMoreBtn, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	            grid.add(loadMorePanel);
	        }
	        
	        grid.revalidate();
	        grid.repaint();
	    };

	    grid.putClientProperty("rebuildGrid", rebuildGrid);
	    javax.swing.Timer searchTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(300, e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    searchTimer.setRepeats(false);
	    
	    searchField.addKeyListener(new KeyAdapter() {
	        public void keyReleased(KeyEvent e) {
	            searchTimer.restart();
	        }
	    });

	    floatSortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());
	    raritySortBox.addActionListener(e -> rebuildGrid.run());

	    SwingUtilities.invokeLater(rebuildGrid);

	    confirm.addActionListener(ev -> {
	        if (selectedItems.size() != 10) {
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(tradeFrame, "Please select exactly 10 skins!");
	            return;
	        }

	        String baseRarity = selectedItems.get(0).rarity.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        for (InventoryItem item : selectedItems) {
	            if (!item.rarity.replace("StatTrak ", "").equals(baseRarity)) {
	                JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(tradeFrame, "All selected skins must be of the same rarity!");
	                return;
	            }
	        }
	        
	        double selectedValue = 0;
	        for (InventoryItem item : selectedItems)
	            selectedValue += item.price.doubleValue();

	        inventoryList.removeAll(selectedItems);
	        inventoryValue = Math.max(0.0, inventoryValue - selectedValue);

	        String newRarity = "";
	        Image[] possibleSkins = null;
	        String[] names = null;

	        if (baseRarity.equals("Milspec")) {
	            newRarity = "Restricted";
	            possibleSkins = purpleSkins;
	            names = new String[]{
	                "Glock-18 | Dragon Tattoo", "MAC-10 | Graven", "M4A1-S | Dark Water",
	                "M4A1-S | Bright Water", "USP-S | Dark Water", "M4A4 | Zirka",
	                "USP-S | Overgrowth", "Nova | Koi", "PP-Bizon | Osiris",
	                "CZ75-Auto | Tigris", "P250 | Supernova",
	                "M249 | Emerald Poison Dart", "MAC-10 | Last Dive", "UMP-45 | Scaffold",
	                "XM1014 | Seasons", "Galil AR | Crimson Tsunami"
	            };
	            totMil = Math.max(0, totMil - 10);
	            totRes++;
	        } else if (baseRarity.equals("Restricted")) {
	            newRarity = "Classified";
	            possibleSkins = pinkSkins;
	            names = new String[]{
	                "Desert Eagle | Hypnotic", "P90 | Emerald Dragon", "AK-47 | Case Hardened",
	                "P2000 | Ocean Foam", "AWP | Graphite", "Five-SeveN | Fowl Play",
	                "Desert Eagle | Conspiracy", "Glock-18 | Water Elemental",
	                "CZ75-Auto | Xiangliu", "AWP | Fever Dream", "M4A1-S | Decimator"
	            };
	            totRes = Math.max(0, totRes - 10);
	            totClass++;
	        } else if (baseRarity.equals("Classified")) {
	            newRarity = "Covert";
	            possibleSkins = redSkins;
	            names = new String[]{
	                "AWP | Lightning Strike", "Desert Eagle | Golden Koi",
	                "AK-47 | Fire Serpent", "P90 | Asiimov", "M4A1-S | Cyrex",
	                "AK-47 | Bloodsport", "USP-S | Neo Noir"
	            };
	            totClass = Math.max(0, totClass - 10);
	            totCov++;
	        }

	        writeStats();
	        repaint();

	        int i = random.nextInt(possibleSkins.length);
	        Image skin = possibleSkins[i];
	        String skinName = names[i];

	        FloatRange outputFR = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(skinName);
	        if (outputFR == null) {
	            for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet()) {
	                if (skinName.startsWith(e.getKey())) {
	                    outputFR = e.getValue();
	                    break;
	                }
	            }
	        }

	        double outputMin = (outputFR != null && outputFR.min != null) ? outputFR.min : 0.0;
	        double outputMax = (outputFR != null && outputFR.max != null) ? outputFR.max : 1.0;

	        double outputFloat;

	        {
	            double totalNormalizedFloat = 0.0;
	            for (InventoryItem item : selectedItems) {
	                FloatRange inputFR = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(item.name);
	                if (inputFR == null) {
	                    for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet()) {
	                        if (item.name.startsWith(e.getKey())) {
	                            inputFR = e.getValue();
	                            break;
	                        }
	                    }
	                }
	                double inputMin = (inputFR != null && inputFR.min != null) ? inputFR.min : 0.0;
	                double inputMax = (inputFR != null && inputFR.max != null) ? inputFR.max : 1.0;
	                double normalizedFloat = (item.itemFloat - inputMin) / Math.max(0.0001, inputMax - inputMin);
	                totalNormalizedFloat += normalizedFloat;
	            }
	            double avgNormalizedFloat = totalNormalizedFloat / selectedItems.size();
	            outputFloat = outputMin + (avgNormalizedFloat * (outputMax - outputMin));
	            outputFloat = Math.max(outputMin, Math.min(outputMax, outputFloat));
	        }

	        String condition;
	        if (outputFloat <= 0.07) {
	            condition = "Factory New";
	        } else if (outputFloat <= 0.15) {
	            condition = "Minimal Wear";
	        } else if (outputFloat <= 0.38) {
	            condition = "Field-Tested";
	        } else if (outputFloat <= 0.45) {
	            condition = "Well-Worn";
	        } else {
	            condition = "Battle-Scarred";
	        }

	        double marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(newRarity, 1.0);
	        double basePrice = getBasePrice(skinName);

	        if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	            basePrice *= 2.5;
	        } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	            basePrice *= 1.7;
	        } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	            basePrice *= 1.0;
	        } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	            basePrice *= 0.7;
	        } else if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
	            basePrice *= 0.3;
	        }
	        
	        basePrice *= marketMulti;

	        boolean allStatTrak = selectedItems.stream().allMatch(it -> it.isStattrak);
	        boolean isStatTrakOutput = allStatTrak;
	        
	        if (isStatTrakOutput) {
	            basePrice *= 2.0;
	        }

	        String rarityLabel = isStatTrakOutput ? "StatTrak " + newRarity : newRarity;

	        int maxWidth = 280, maxHeight = 200;
	        int origWidth = skin.getWidth(null);
	        int origHeight = skin.getHeight(null);
	        double scale = Math.min((double) maxWidth / origWidth, (double) maxHeight / origHeight);
	        Image scaledSkin = skin.getScaledInstance((int) (origWidth * scale), (int) (origHeight * scale), Image.SCALE_SMOOTH);

	        int outPatternID = random.nextInt(1000);
	        String outBlueGem = getBlueGemTier(skinName, outPatternID);
	        if (outBlueGem != null) {
	            skinName = skinName + " (" + outBlueGem + ")";
	            basePrice = applyBlueGemMultiplier(
	                    skinName.replace(" (" + outBlueGem + ")", ""),
	                    outPatternID,
	                    outBlueGem,
	                    basePrice
	            );
	        }

	        inventoryList.add(new InventoryItem(
	            new ImageIcon(scaledSkin),
	            skinName,
	            condition,
	            rarityLabel,
	            BigDecimal.valueOf(basePrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	            outputFloat,
	            isStatTrakOutput,
	            outPatternID,
	            outBlueGem,
	            basePrice 
	        ));

	        inventoryValue += basePrice;
	        newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	        totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);

	        newAvgFloat = BigDecimal.valueOf(outputFloat).setScale(6, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

	        if (lowestFloat > outputFloat) {
	            lowestFloat = outputFloat;
	        }

	        String displayMessage;
	        if (isStatTrakOutput) {
	            displayMessage = "Trade-Up successful! You received:\n StatTrak " + skinName +
	                " (" + newRarity + ")\nCondition: " + condition +
	                "\nFloat: " + newAvgFloat + "\nValue: $" + String.format("%.2f", basePrice);
	        } else {
	            displayMessage = "Trade-Up successful! You received:\n" + skinName +
	                " (" + newRarity + ")\nCondition: " + condition +
	                "\nFloat: " + newAvgFloat + "\nValue: $" + String.format("%.2f", basePrice);
	        }
	        
	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(tradeFrame, displayMessage);
	        tradeFrame.dispose();
	    });

	    tradeFrame.setVisible(true);
	}

	private JPanel createTradeUpCardFast(InventoryItem item, ImageIcon cachedImage,
	        ArrayList<InventoryItem> selectedItems, JPanel grid) {
	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    card.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 40));
	    card.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(220, 165));
	    card.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(220, 165));
	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(getRarityColor(item.rarity), 2));

	    JLabel imgLabel;
	    if (cachedImage != null) {
	        imgLabel = new JLabel(cachedImage);
	    } else if (item.image != null) {
	        Image scaled = item.getThumb110().getImage();
	        imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	    } else {
	        String cleanName = item.name.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("* ", "").trim();
	        if (item.blueGemTier != null && cleanName.contains("(Blue Gem")) cleanName = cleanName.substring(0, cleanName.indexOf("(Blue Gem")).trim();
	        Image img = getSkinImageFromName(cleanName);
	        if (img != null) {
	            Image scaled = img.getScaledInstance(110, 75, Image.SCALE_FAST);
	            imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	            item.image = new ImageIcon(img);
	        } else {
	            imgLabel = new JLabel("?", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	            imgLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	        }
	    }
	    imgLabel.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    imgLabel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(110, 75));

	    String displayName = item.isStattrak ? "ST " + item.name : item.name;
	    JLabel n = new JLabel(displayName, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    n.setForeground(item.isStattrak ? new Color(255, 153, 51) : Color.WHITE);
	    n.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));

	    JLabel c = new JLabel(item.condition, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    c.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY); c.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9));

	    JLabel f = new JLabel(String.format("Float: %.6f", item.itemFloat), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    f.setForeground(new Color(95, 200, 255)); f.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9));

	    JLabel r = new JLabel(item.rarity, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    r.setForeground(getRarityColor(item.rarity)); r.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9));

	    if (item.collection == null) item.collection = getCollectionName(item.name);
	    JLabel col = new JLabel(item.collection != null ? item.collection : "", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    col.setForeground(new Color(170, 130, 255)); col.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.ITALIC, 8));

	    JPanel text = new JPanel(new GridLayout(5, 1, 0, 0));
	    text.setBackground(new Color(22, 22, 30));
	    text.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(2, 2, 2, 2));
	    text.add(n); text.add(c); text.add(r); text.add(f); text.add(col);

	    card.add(imgLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    card.add(text, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    if (selectedItems.contains(item)) {
	        card.setBackground(new Color(20, 60, 20));
	        text.setBackground(new Color(15, 45, 15));
	        card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(80, 220, 80), 3));
	    }

	    card.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override public void mouseClicked(MouseEvent e) {
	            if (selectedItems.contains(item)) {
	                selectedItems.remove(item);
	                card.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 40));
	                text.setBackground(new Color(22, 22, 30));
	                card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(getRarityColor(item.rarity), 2));
	                card.setEnabled(true);
	                Object rb = grid.getClientProperty("rebuildGrid");
	                if (rb instanceof Runnable) SwingUtilities.invokeLater((Runnable) rb);
	            } else {
	                if (!selectedItems.isEmpty()) {
	                    String lockedRarity = selectedItems.get(0).rarity;
	                    if (!item.rarity.equals(lockedRarity)) {
	                        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(grid.getTopLevelAncestor(),
	                            "All skins must match: " + lockedRarity + "\n(StatTrak and non-StatTrak cannot be mixed)");
	                        return;
	                    }
	                }
	                if (selectedItems.size() < 10) {
	                    selectedItems.add(item);
	                    card.setBackground(new Color(20, 60, 20));
	                    text.setBackground(new Color(15, 45, 15));
	                    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(80, 220, 80), 3));
	                    Object rb = grid.getClientProperty("rebuildGrid");
	                    if (rb instanceof Runnable) SwingUtilities.invokeLater((Runnable) rb);
	                } else {
	                    JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(grid.getTopLevelAncestor(), "You can only select 10 skins!");
	                }
	            }
	        }
	        @Override public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) {
	            if (!selectedItems.contains(item)) card.setBackground(new Color(40, 40, 55));
	        }
	        @Override public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e) {
	            if (!selectedItems.contains(item)) card.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 40));
	        }
	    });
	    return card;
	}

	private void initializeMarketPrices() {
	    marketPriceMultipliers.put("Knife", 1.0);
	    marketPriceMultipliers.put("Gloves", 1.0);
	    marketPriceMultipliers.put("Covert", 1.0);
	    marketPriceMultipliers.put("Classified", 1.0);
	    marketPriceMultipliers.put("Restricted", 1.0);
	    marketPriceMultipliers.put("Milspec", 1.0);
	    marketPriceMultipliers.put("Industrial", 1.0);
	}

	private void startMarketFluctuationTimer() {
	    generateGlobalMarketListings();
	    generateNpcBuyOrders();
	    purgeStaleNpcBuyOrders();

	    marketTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(MARKET_UPDATE_INTERVAL, e -> {

	        SwingWorker<Void, Void> worker = new SwingWorker<Void, Void>() {
	            @Override
	            protected Void doInBackground() {

	                for (String rarity : marketPriceMultipliers.keySet()) {
	                    double oldMultiplier = marketPriceMultipliers.get(rarity);

	                    double rawChange = (random.nextDouble() - 0.5) * 0.06;

	                    if (random.nextDouble() < 0.08) {
	                        rawChange += (random.nextDouble() - 0.5) * 0.12;
	                    }

	                    double meanReversion = (1.0 - oldMultiplier) * 0.03;
	                    double dampedChange = rawChange * 0.7 + meanReversion;
	                    double newMultiplier = oldMultiplier + dampedChange;
	                    newMultiplier = Math.max(0.55, Math.min(1.8, newMultiplier));

	                    marketPriceMultipliers.put(rarity, newMultiplier);

	                    if (dampedChange > 0) {
	                        handlePriceIncrease(rarity, oldMultiplier, newMultiplier);
	                    } else if (dampedChange < 0) {
	                        handlePriceDecrease(rarity, oldMultiplier, newMultiplier);
	                    }

	                    priceHistory
	                        .computeIfAbsent(rarity, r -> new ArrayList<>())
	                        .add(newMultiplier);

	                    ArrayList<Double> history = priceHistory.get(rarity);
	                    if (history.size() > 60) {
	                        history.remove(0);
	                    }
	                }

	                Map<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> marketSnapshot;
	                synchronized (globalMarketListings) {
	                    marketSnapshot = new HashMap<>();
	                    for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> e : globalMarketListings.entrySet()) {
	                        marketSnapshot.put(e.getKey(), new ArrayList<>(e.getValue()));
	                    }
	                }
	                totalMarketCap = 0.0;
	                for (ArrayList<MarketListing> listings : marketSnapshot.values()) {
	                    for (MarketListing listing : listings) {
	                        totalMarketCap += listing.listPrice;
	                    }
	                }
	                
	                for (InventoryItem item : new ArrayList<>(inventoryList)) {
	                    totalMarketCap += item.price.doubleValue();
	                }
	                
	                if (totalMarketCap > peakTotalMarketCap) {
	                	peakTotalMarketCap = totalMarketCap;
	                }
	                
	                marketCapHistory.add(totalMarketCap);
	                if (marketCapHistory.size() > 60) {
	                    marketCapHistory.removeFirst();
	                }
	                
	                for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> entry : marketSnapshot.entrySet()) {
	                    String skinName = entry.getKey();
	                    ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = entry.getValue();
	                    
	                    if (listings != null && !listings.isEmpty()) {

	                        Map<String, List<MarketListing>> byCondition = listings.stream()
	                            .collect(Collectors.groupingBy(l -> l.item.condition));
	                        
	                        for (Map.Entry<String, List<MarketListing>> condEntry : byCondition.entrySet()) {
	                            String condition = condEntry.getKey();
	                            
	                            double lowestPrice = condEntry.getValue().stream()
	                                .mapToDouble(l -> l.listPrice)
	                                .min()
	                                .orElse(0);
	                            
	                            if (lowestPrice > 0) {
	                                String historyKey = skinName + ":" + condition;

	                                skinConditionPriceHistory
	                                    .computeIfAbsent(historyKey, k -> new ArrayList<>())
	                                    .add(lowestPrice);
	                                ArrayList<Double> history = skinConditionPriceHistory.get(historyKey);
	                                if (history.size() > 300) history.remove(0);

	                                String normalizedForBO = normalizeSkinName(skinName);
	                                ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder> boList = npcBuyOrders.get(normalizedForBO);
	                                if (boList != null) {
	                                    final String condSnap = condition;
	                                    double bestBO = boList.stream()
	                                        .filter(o -> o.condition.equals(condSnap) && o.remaining() > 0)
	                                        .mapToDouble(o -> o.price)
	                                        .max().orElse(0);
	                                    if (bestBO > 0) {
	                                        buyOrderPriceHistory
	                                            .computeIfAbsent(historyKey, k -> new ArrayList<>())
	                                            .add(bestBO);
	                                        ArrayList<Double> boHist = buyOrderPriceHistory.get(historyKey);
	                                        if (boHist.size() > 300) boHist.remove(0);
	                                    }
	                                }
	                            }
	                        }
	                    }
	                }
	                
	                ensureMinimumListings();

	                maintainNpcBuyOrders();

	                artificiallyFillNpcOrders();

	                replenishThinMarketListings();

	                return null;
	            }

	            @Override
	            protected void done() {

	                SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	                    synchronized (inventoryList) {
	                        inventoryValue = 0.0;
	                        for (InventoryItem item : inventoryList) {
	                            if (isBlueGem(item)) {
	                                inventoryValue += item.price.doubleValue();
	                            } else {
	                                String marketKey = item.isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + item.name : item.name;
	                                ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey);
	                                
	                                if (listings != null && !listings.isEmpty()) {
	                                    double lowestPrice = Double.MAX_VALUE;
	                                    boolean foundMatch = false;
	                                    
	                                    for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	                                        if (ml.item.condition.equals(item.condition)) {
	                                            if (ml.listPrice < lowestPrice) {
	                                                lowestPrice = ml.listPrice;
	                                                foundMatch = true;
	                                            }
	                                        }
	                                    }
	                                    
	                                    if (foundMatch) {

	                                        item.price = BigDecimal.valueOf(lowestPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

	                                        inventoryValue += lowestPrice;
	                                    } else {

	                                        double currentPrice = getCurrentMarketPrice(item);
	                                        item.price = BigDecimal.valueOf(currentPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	                                        inventoryValue += currentPrice;
	                                    }
	                                } else {

	                                    double currentPrice = getCurrentMarketPrice(item);
	                                    item.price = BigDecimal.valueOf(currentPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	                                    inventoryValue += currentPrice;
	                                }
	                            }
	                        }
	                    }

	                    newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	                    totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);

	                    updateTradeOfferPrices();
	                    simulateMarketActivity();
	                    updateActiveListings();
	                    processBuyOrders();
	                });
	            }
	        };
	        
	        worker.execute();
	    });

	    marketTimer.start();
	}
	
	private void updateTradeOfferPrices() {
	    ArrayList<TradeOffer> tradesToCancel = new ArrayList<>();
	    
	    synchronized (pendingTrades) {
	        for (TradeOffer trade : pendingTrades) {
	            double newOfferedValue = 0.0;
	            for (InventoryItem item : trade.npcOfferedItems) {
	                if (isBlueGem(item)) {
	                    newOfferedValue += item.price.doubleValue();
	                } else {
	                    double currentPrice = getCurrentMarketPrice(item);
	                    synchronized (item) {
	                        item.price = BigDecimal.valueOf(currentPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

	                    }
	                    newOfferedValue += currentPrice;
	                }
	            }
	            
	            double newRequestedValue = 0.0;
	            for (InventoryItem item : trade.npcRequestedItems) {
	                synchronized (inventoryList) {
	                    if (!inventoryList.contains(item)) {
	                        tradesToCancel.add(trade);
	                        break;
	                    }
	                }
	                
	                if (isBlueGem(item)) {
	                    newRequestedValue += item.price.doubleValue();
	                } else {
	                    for (InventoryItem invItem : inventoryList) {
	                        if (invItem == item) {
	                            double currentPrice = getCurrentMarketPrice(invItem);
	                            synchronized (item) {
	                                item.price = BigDecimal.valueOf(currentPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

	                            }
	                            newRequestedValue += currentPrice;
	                            break;
	                        }
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	            newRequestedValue += trade.npcRequestedMoney;
	            
	            double offeredTotal = newOfferedValue + trade.npcOfferedMoney;
	            double requestedTotal = newRequestedValue;

	            if (requestedTotal > 0 && offeredTotal > 0) {
	                double lossRatio = offeredTotal / requestedTotal;
	                
	                if (lossRatio > 1.15) {
	                    if (random.nextDouble() > 0.25) {
	                        if (!tradesToCancel.contains(trade)) {
	                            tradesToCancel.add(trade);
	                        }
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    
	    if (!tradesToCancel.isEmpty()) {
	        synchronized (pendingTrades) {
	            pendingTrades.removeAll(tradesToCancel);
	        }
	        
	        unreadTradesCount = Math.max(0, unreadTradesCount - tradesToCancel.size());
	        updateTradeNotification();
	        
	        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	            String cancelMsg = tradesToCancel.size() == 1
	                ? tradesToCancel.get(0).npcName + " cancelled their offer"
	                : tradesToCancel.size() + " trade offers were cancelled";
	            showTradeCancelNotification(cancelMsg);
	        });
	    }
	}
	
	private void generateNpcBuyOrders() {
	    npcBuyOrders.clear();

	    for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> entry : globalMarketListings.entrySet()) {
	        String rawKey = entry.getKey();
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = entry.getValue();
	        if (listings == null || listings.isEmpty()) continue;

	        String marketKey = normalizeSkinName(rawKey);
	        String cleanKey  = marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        String rarity    = getSkinRarity(cleanKey);

	        Map<String, Double> cheapestByCondition = new HashMap<>();
	        for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	            if (!ml.isPlayerListing) {
	                cheapestByCondition.merge(ml.item.condition, ml.listPrice, Math::min);
	            }
	        }
	        // If no NPC listings exist, seed from any listing so every skin always has buy orders
	        if (cheapestByCondition.isEmpty()) {
	            for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	                cheapestByCondition.merge(ml.item.condition, ml.listPrice, Math::min);
	            }
	        }
	        if (cheapestByCondition.isEmpty()) continue;

	        int numConditions = Math.max(1, cheapestByCondition.size());
	        int totalQtyForSkin = npcTotalQuantity(rarity);

	        ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder> orders = new ArrayList<>();
	        int conditionsProcessed = 0;
	        int qtyRemaining = totalQtyForSkin;

	        for (Map.Entry<String, Double> ce : cheapestByCondition.entrySet()) {
	            String condition = ce.getKey();
	            double cheapest  = ce.getValue();
	            conditionsProcessed++;

	            int qtyForCondition;
	            if (conditionsProcessed == numConditions) {
	                qtyForCondition = Math.max(1, qtyRemaining);
	            } else {
	                double evenShare = (double) totalQtyForSkin / numConditions;
	                double skew = 0.80 + random.nextDouble() * 0.40;
	                int conditionsLeft = numConditions - conditionsProcessed;
	                int maxAlloc = qtyRemaining - conditionsLeft;
	                qtyForCondition = Math.max(1, Math.min(maxAlloc, (int)(evenShare * skew)));
	                qtyRemaining -= qtyForCondition;
	            }

	            int orderCount = npcOrderCount(rarity);

	            double topFraction  = 0.88 + random.nextDouble() * 0.04;
	            double bottomFloor  = 0.75;
	            double totalDrop    = topFraction - bottomFloor;
	            double stepDown     = orderCount > 1 ? totalDrop / (orderCount - 1) : 0;

	            int tierRemaining = qtyForCondition;
	            for (int i = 0; i < orderCount; i++) {
	                double fraction   = Math.max(bottomFloor, topFraction - (i * stepDown));
	                double orderPrice = cheapest * fraction;

	                int qty;
	                if (i == orderCount - 1) {
	                    qty = Math.max(1, tierRemaining);
	                } else {
	                    double share = (i == 0) ? 0.40 : (0.60 / (orderCount - 1));
	                    qty = Math.max(1, (int)(qtyForCondition * share));
	                    tierRemaining -= qty;
	                    if (tierRemaining < 1) tierRemaining = 1;
	                }

	                String bName = NPC_BUYER_NAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_BUYER_NAMES.length)];
	                orders.add(new NpcBuyOrder(marketKey, condition, orderPrice, qty, bName));
	            }
	        }

	        if (!orders.isEmpty()) {
	            npcBuyOrders.put(marketKey, orders);
	        }
	    }
	}
	
	private void purgeStaleNpcBuyOrders() {
        for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder>> entry : npcBuyOrders.entrySet()) {
            String marketKey = entry.getKey();
            ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder> orders = entry.getValue();
            if (orders == null || orders.isEmpty()) continue;

            ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey);
            if (listings == null) {
                listings = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "StatTrak "));
            }
            if (listings == null) continue;

            Map<String, Double> cheapestByCondition = new HashMap<>();
            for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
                if (!ml.isPlayerListing) {
                    cheapestByCondition.merge(ml.item.condition, ml.listPrice, Math::min);
                }
            }

            orders.removeIf(o -> {
                double cheapest = cheapestByCondition.getOrDefault(o.condition, Double.MAX_VALUE);
                if (cheapest == Double.MAX_VALUE) return false;
                return o.price < cheapest * 0.75;
            });
        }
    }

	private int npcOrderCount(String rarity) {

	    switch (rarity) {
	        case "Milspec":    return 9 + random.nextInt(4);
	        case "Restricted": return 7 + random.nextInt(4);
	        case "Classified": return 5 + random.nextInt(4);
	        case "Covert":     return 4 + random.nextInt(3);
	        case "Knife":      return 3 + random.nextInt(3);
	        case "Gloves":     return 3 + random.nextInt(3);
	        default:           return 6;
	    }
	}

	private int npcTotalQuantity(String rarity) {

	    switch (rarity) {
	        case "Milspec":    return 80 + random.nextInt(25);
	        case "Restricted": return 70 + random.nextInt(25);
	        case "Classified": return 55 + random.nextInt(25);
	        case "Covert":     return 40 + random.nextInt(20);
	        case "Knife":      return 25 + random.nextInt(15);
	        case "Gloves":     return 25 + random.nextInt(15);
	        default:           return 50;
	    }
	}

	private void maintainNpcBuyOrders() {
	    long now = System.currentTimeMillis();

	    for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder>> entry : npcBuyOrders.entrySet()) {
	        String marketKey = entry.getKey();
	        ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder> orders = entry.getValue();
	        if (orders == null || orders.isEmpty()) continue;

	        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey);
	        if (listings == null) {
	        	listings = globalMarketListings.get(normalizeSkinName(marketKey));
	        }
	        if (listings == null) {
	            for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> e : globalMarketListings.entrySet()) {
	                if (normalizeSkinName(e.getKey()).equals(marketKey)) {
	                    listings = e.getValue();
	                    break;
	                }
	            }
	        }
	        double cheapestListing = Double.MAX_VALUE;
	        if (listings != null) {
	            for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	                if (!ml.isPlayerListing && ml.listPrice < cheapestListing) {
	                    cheapestListing = ml.listPrice;
	                }
	            }
	        }
	        if (cheapestListing == Double.MAX_VALUE) continue;

	        String cleanKey = marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        String rarity   = getSkinRarity(cleanKey);

	        Map<String, List<NpcBuyOrder>> byCondition = new HashMap<>();
	        for (NpcBuyOrder o : orders) {
	            byCondition.computeIfAbsent(o.condition, k -> new ArrayList<>()).add(o);
	        }

	        for (Map.Entry<String, List<NpcBuyOrder>> ce : byCondition.entrySet()) {
	            String condition = ce.getKey();
	            List<NpcBuyOrder> condOrders = ce.getValue();

	            double condCheapest = Double.MAX_VALUE;
	            if (listings != null) {
	                for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	                    if (ml.item.condition.equals(condition) && !ml.isPlayerListing) {
	                        condCheapest = Math.min(condCheapest, ml.listPrice);
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	            if (condCheapest == Double.MAX_VALUE) continue;

	            double priceFloor = condCheapest * 0.75;
	            orders.removeIf(o -> o.condition.equals(condition) && o.price < priceFloor * 0.95);
	            condOrders.removeIf(o -> o.price < priceFloor * 0.95);
	            if (condOrders.isEmpty()) continue;

	            double bestPrice = condOrders.stream()
	                .mapToDouble(o -> o.price).max().orElse(0);

	            int numTiers = Math.max(1, condOrders.size());
	            int avgTierQty = Math.max(1,
	                condOrders.stream().mapToInt(o -> o.quantity).sum() / numTiers);

	            for (NpcBuyOrder o : condOrders) {
	                if (o.remaining() <= 0) {
	                    o.quantity     = avgTierQty;
	                    o.filled       = 0;
	                    o.lastFillTime = now;
	                }
	            }

	            boolean anyRecentFill = condOrders.stream()
	                .anyMatch(o -> (now - o.lastFillTime) < 60_000L && o.filled > 0);

	            if (!anyRecentFill) {
	                double bump = bestPrice * (0.02 + random.nextDouble() * 0.03);
	                double newPrice = bestPrice + bump;

	                if (newPrice < priceFloor) {
	                    newPrice = priceFloor * (0.97 + random.nextDouble() * 0.02);
	                }

	                double ceiling = condCheapest * 0.97;
	                if (newPrice >= ceiling) newPrice = ceiling * (0.95 + random.nextDouble() * 0.02);
	                if (newPrice <= 0 || newPrice >= condCheapest) continue;

	                int qty = avgTierQty;
	                String escalName = NPC_BUYER_NAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_BUYER_NAMES.length)];
	                NpcBuyOrder escalated = new NpcBuyOrder(marketKey, condition, newPrice, qty, escalName);
	                escalated.lastFillTime = now;
	                orders.add(escalated);

	                int maxOrders = npcOrderCount(rarity) * 3;
	                List<NpcBuyOrder> condList = orders.stream()
	                    .filter(o -> o.condition.equals(condition))
	                    .sorted((a, b) -> Double.compare(a.price, b.price))
	                    .collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.toList());
	                while (condList.size() > maxOrders) {
	                    orders.remove(condList.remove(0));
	                }
	            }
	        }
	    }
	}

	private void artificiallyFillNpcOrders() {
	    long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
	    for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder>> entry : npcBuyOrders.entrySet()) {
	        String marketKey = entry.getKey();
	        ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder> orders = entry.getValue();
	        if (orders == null || orders.isEmpty()) continue;

	        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey);
	        if (listings == null) {
	            String tmKey = marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "StatTrak ");
	            listings = globalMarketListings.get(tmKey);
	        }
	        if (listings == null || listings.isEmpty()) continue;

	        Map<String, Double> cheapestPerCond = new HashMap<>();
	        for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	            if (!ml.isPlayerListing) {
	                cheapestPerCond.merge(ml.item.condition, ml.listPrice, Math::min);
	            }
	        }

	        String cleanKey = marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        String rarity = getSkinRarity(cleanKey);

	        orders.removeIf(o -> {
	            double condCheapest = cheapestPerCond.getOrDefault(o.condition, Double.MAX_VALUE);
	            return o.price >= condCheapest && o.remaining() > 0;
	        });

	        List<NpcBuyOrder> sortedOrders = new ArrayList<>(orders);
	        sortedOrders.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.price, a.price));

	        for (NpcBuyOrder o : sortedOrders) {
	            if (o.remaining() <= 0) continue;

	            long fillIntervalMs;
	            switch (rarity) {
	                case "Milspec":    fillIntervalMs =  8_000 + (long)(random.nextDouble() * 12_000); break;
	                case "Restricted": fillIntervalMs = 15_000 + (long)(random.nextDouble() * 20_000); break;
	                case "Classified": fillIntervalMs = 25_000 + (long)(random.nextDouble() * 30_000); break;
