	                case "Covert":     fillIntervalMs = 40_000 + (long)(random.nextDouble() * 40_000); break;
	                case "Knife":      fillIntervalMs = 30_000 + (long)(random.nextDouble() * 60_000); break;
	                case "Gloves":     fillIntervalMs = 30_000 + (long)(random.nextDouble() * 60_000); break;
	                default:           fillIntervalMs = 15_000; break;
	            }

	            if ((now - o.lastFillTime) >= fillIntervalMs) {
	                o.filled = Math.min(o.quantity, o.filled + 1);
	                o.lastFillTime = now;
	            }
	        }
	    }
	}

	@SuppressWarnings("unused")
	private void processPlayerBuyOrderFills() {  }

	private void showTradeCancelNotification(String message) {
	    JPanel notif = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(6, 0));
	    notif.setBackground(new Color(35, 20, 20));
	    notif.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(220, 60, 60), 2),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 10, 8, 10)
	    ));
	    notif.setCursor(new Cursor(Cursor.HAND_CURSOR));
	    notif.setToolTipText("Click to dismiss");

	    JLabel icon = new JLabel("❌", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    icon.setFont(new Font("Segoe UI Emoji", Font.PLAIN, 22));
	    notif.add(icon, BorderLayout.WEST);

	    JPanel textPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1, 0, 2));
	    textPanel.setBackground(new Color(35, 20, 20));
	    JLabel titleLbl = new JLabel("TRADE CANCELLED");
	    titleLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));
	    titleLbl.setForeground(new Color(220, 80, 80));
	    JLabel msgLbl = new JLabel(message);
	    msgLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    msgLbl.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    textPanel.add(titleLbl);
	    textPanel.add(msgLbl);
	    notif.add(textPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    int w = 340, h = 72;
	    JLayeredPane layered = getLayeredPane();
	    int x = layered.getWidth() - w - 12;
	    int y = layered.getHeight() - h - 12;
	    notif.setBounds(x, y, w, h);
	    layered.add(notif, JLayeredPane.POPUP_LAYER);
	    layered.revalidate();
	    layered.repaint();

	    MouseAdapter dismiss = new MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override public void mouseClicked(MouseEvent e) { layered.remove(notif); layered.repaint(); }
	    };
	    notif.addMouseListener(dismiss);
	    for (java.awt.Component c : notif.getComponents()) c.addMouseListener(dismiss);
	    for (java.awt.Component c : textPanel.getComponents()) c.addMouseListener(dismiss);
	    javax.swing.Timer t = new javax.swing.Timer(5000, e -> { layered.remove(notif); layered.repaint(); });
	    t.setRepeats(false);
	    t.start();
	}

	private void showBuyOrderFillNotification(String skinName, String condition, double pricePaid) {
	    JPanel notif = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(6, 0));
	    notif.setBackground(new Color(20, 35, 20));
	    notif.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(80, 200, 80), 2),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 10, 8, 10)
	    ));
	    notif.setCursor(new Cursor(Cursor.HAND_CURSOR));

	    JLabel icon = new JLabel("📦", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    icon.setFont(new Font("Segoe UI Emoji", Font.PLAIN, 22));
	    notif.add(icon, BorderLayout.WEST);

	    JPanel textPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(3, 1, 0, 1));
	    textPanel.setBackground(new Color(20, 35, 20));
	    JLabel titleLbl = new JLabel("BUY ORDER FILLED");
	    titleLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));
	    titleLbl.setForeground(new Color(80, 220, 80));
	    JLabel nameLbl = new JLabel(skinName);
	    nameLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    nameLbl.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    JLabel detailLbl = new JLabel(String.format("%s  •  paid $%.2f", condition, pricePaid));
	    detailLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 10));
	    detailLbl.setForeground(new Color(140, 220, 140));
	    textPanel.add(titleLbl); textPanel.add(nameLbl); textPanel.add(detailLbl);
	    notif.add(textPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    int w = 340, h = 72;
	    JLayeredPane layered = getLayeredPane();
	    int x = layered.getWidth() - w - 12;
	    int y = layered.getHeight() - h - 12;
	    notif.setBounds(x, y, w, h);
	    layered.add(notif, JLayeredPane.POPUP_LAYER);
	    layered.revalidate(); layered.repaint();

	    MouseAdapter dismiss = new MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override public void mouseClicked(MouseEvent e) { layered.remove(notif); layered.repaint(); }
	    };
	    notif.addMouseListener(dismiss);
	    for (java.awt.Component c : notif.getComponents()) c.addMouseListener(dismiss);
	    for (java.awt.Component c : textPanel.getComponents()) c.addMouseListener(dismiss);
	    javax.swing.Timer t = new javax.swing.Timer(5000, e -> { layered.remove(notif); layered.repaint(); });
	    t.setRepeats(false); t.start();
	}

	private NpcBuyOrder getBestNpcBuyOrder(String marketKey, String condition) {
	    ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder> orders = npcBuyOrders.get(marketKey);
	    if (orders == null) orders = npcBuyOrders.get(normalizeSkinName(marketKey));
	    if (orders == null) return null;
	    NpcBuyOrder best = null;
	    for (NpcBuyOrder o : orders) {
	        if (o.condition.equals(condition) && o.remaining() > 0) {
	            if (best == null || o.price > best.price) {
	                best = o;
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    return best;
	}

		private void ensureMinimumListings() {

	    final int MIN_STATTRAK_MILSPEC = 30;
	    final int MIN_MILSPEC          = 80;
	    final int MIN_STATTRAK_RESTRICTED = 20;
	    final int MIN_RESTRICTED       = 60;
	    final int MIN_CLASSIFIED       = 40;
	    final int MIN_COVERT           = 20;
	    final int MIN_KNIFE            = 10;
	    final int MIN_GLOVES           = 10;

	    synchronized (globalMarketListings) {
	        for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> entry : globalMarketListings.entrySet()) {
	            String marketKey = entry.getKey();
	            ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = entry.getValue();
	            if (listings == null) continue;

	            boolean isStatTrak = marketKey.startsWith("StatTrak");
	            String cleanKey = marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	            String rarity = getSkinRarity(cleanKey);
	            boolean isGlove = rarity.equals("Gloves");

	            int minimum;
	            switch (rarity) {
	                case "Milspec":    minimum = isStatTrak ? MIN_STATTRAK_MILSPEC : MIN_MILSPEC; break;
	                case "Restricted": minimum = isStatTrak ? MIN_STATTRAK_RESTRICTED : MIN_RESTRICTED; break;
	                case "Classified": minimum = MIN_CLASSIFIED; break;
	                case "Covert":     minimum = MIN_COVERT; break;
	                case "Knife":      minimum = MIN_KNIFE; break;
	                case "Gloves":     minimum = MIN_GLOVES; break;
	                default:           minimum = MIN_MILSPEC; break;
	            }

	            int deficit = minimum - listings.size();
	            if (deficit <= 0) continue;

	            double marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarity, 1.0);
	            String[] availableConditions = getAvailableConditions(cleanKey);
	            boolean isDopplerGem = cleanKey.contains("Sapphire") || cleanKey.contains("Ruby") || cleanKey.contains("Black Pearl");
	            if (isDopplerGem) continue;

	            for (int i = 0; i < deficit; i++) {
	                String condition = availableConditions[random.nextInt(availableConditions.length)];
	                double itemFloat = generateFloatForCondition(cleanKey, condition);
	                double variance = 0.92 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.16);

	                double listPrice;
	                if (isGlove) {
	                    double gloveBasePrice = getGloveBasePrice(cleanKey);
	                    listPrice = calculateGlovePrice(cleanKey, condition, gloveBasePrice);
	                    listPrice *= marketMulti * variance;
	                } else {
	                    double basePrice = getBasePrice(cleanKey);
	                    listPrice = basePrice * marketMulti * variance;
	                    if      (condition.equals("Factory New"))    listPrice *= 2.5;
	                    else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear"))   listPrice *= 1.7;
	                    else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn"))      listPrice *= 0.7;
	                    else if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) listPrice *= 0.3;
	                    boolean isAnyDopplerT = cleanKey.contains("Doppler");
	                    if (rarity.equals("Knife") && !isAnyDopplerT) {
	                        FloatRange tFr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(cleanKey);
	                        double tMin = (tFr != null && tFr.min != null) ? tFr.min : 0.0;
	                        if (condition.equals("Factory New") && tMin >= 0.06) {
	                            listPrice *= 2.87;
	                        } else {
	                            double rel = getRelativeFloat(cleanKey, itemFloat);
	                            if (!isCappedKnife(cleanKey)) {
	                                if (rel <= 0.01) listPrice *= 2.5;
	                                else if (rel <= 0.05) listPrice *= 1.5;
	                                else if (rel <= 0.20) listPrice *= 1.1;
	                            } else {
	                                if (rel <= 0.01) listPrice *= 1.15;
	                                else if (rel <= 0.05) listPrice *= 1.05;
	                            }
	                        }
	                    }
	                    if (isStatTrak && !isGlove) {
	                        boolean isCW1 = cleanKey.contains("Crimson Web");
	                        boolean isD1  = cleanKey.contains("Doppler");
	                        if (isCW1)                            listPrice *= 2.0;
	                        else if (isD1)                        listPrice *= 0.80;
	                        else if (rarity.equals("Knife"))      listPrice *= 0.90;
	                        else                                  listPrice *= 1.70 + random.nextDouble() * 0.30;
	                    }
	                }

	                int sellTime = 30 + random.nextInt(150);
	                double trueBasePrice = listPrice / marketMulti;
	                String displayRarity = isStatTrak ? "StatTrak " + rarity : rarity;
	                Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(cleanKey);

	                InventoryItem dummyItem = new InventoryItem(
	                    skinImg != null ? new ImageIcon(skinImg) : null,
	                    cleanKey, condition, displayRarity,
	                    BigDecimal.valueOf(listPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                    itemFloat, isStatTrak, random.nextInt(1000), null, trueBasePrice
	                );

	                MarketListing listing = new MarketListing(dummyItem, listPrice, sellTime, false);
	                listings.add(listing);
	            }
	        }
	    }
	}

	private void repriceExistingNpcListings(String rarity, double oldMultiplier, double newMultiplier) {
	    if (oldMultiplier <= 0) return;
	    double ratio = newMultiplier / oldMultiplier;
	    for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> entry : globalMarketListings.entrySet()) {
	        String key = entry.getKey();
	        String cleanKey2 = key.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();
	        if (!getSkinRarity(cleanKey2).equals(rarity)) continue;
	        for (MarketListing ml : entry.getValue()) {
	            if (!ml.isPlayerListing && ml.item.blueGemTier == null) {
	                ml.listPrice = BigDecimal.valueOf(ml.listPrice * ratio)
	                    .setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP).doubleValue();
	                ml.item.price = BigDecimal.valueOf(ml.listPrice)
	                    .setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	                ml.item.basePrice = ml.item.basePrice * ratio;
	            }
	        }
	    }
	}

		private void handlePriceIncrease(String rarity, double oldMultiplier, double newMultiplier) {
	    
	    
	    repriceExistingNpcListings(rarity, oldMultiplier, newMultiplier);

	    for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> entry : globalMarketListings.entrySet()) {
	        String skinName = entry.getKey();
	        String cleanSkinName = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "")
	                    .replace("StatTrak ", "")
	                    .replace(" StatTrak ", "");
	        String skinRarity = getSkinRarity(cleanSkinName);
	        
	        if (skinRarity.equals(rarity)) {
	            ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = entry.getValue();
	            ArrayList<MarketListing> toRemove = new ArrayList<>();
	            int totalItemsRemoved = 0;
	            
	            for (MarketListing listing : listings) {
	                boolean isBlueGem = listing.item.blueGemTier != null;
	                
	                if (!listing.isPlayerListing && !isBlueGem) {

	                    String cleanForPrice = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	                    double basePrice = getBasePrice(cleanForPrice);
	                    double expectedPrice = basePrice * newMultiplier;
	                    
	                    if (listing.item.condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	                        expectedPrice *= 2.5;
	                    } else if (listing.item.condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	                        expectedPrice *= 1.7;
	                    } else if (listing.item.condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	                        expectedPrice *= 1.0;
	                    } else if (listing.item.condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	                        expectedPrice *= 0.7;
	                    } else if (listing.item.condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
	                        expectedPrice *= 0.3;
	                    }

	                    if (listing.item.isStattrak) {
	                        boolean isCW6 = cleanSkinName.contains("Crimson Web");
	                        boolean isD6  = cleanSkinName.contains("Doppler");
	                        if (isCW6)                                expectedPrice *= 2.0;
	                        else if (isD6)                            expectedPrice *= 0.80;
	                        else if (skinRarity.equals("Knife"))      expectedPrice *= 0.90;
	                        else                                      expectedPrice *= 1.85;
	                    }
	                   
	                    if (listing.listPrice < expectedPrice * 0.90 && random.nextDouble() < 0.6) {
	                        toRemove.add(listing);
	                        totalItemsRemoved++;
	                    }
	                } else if (listing.isPlayerListing) {
	                    String cleanForPrice2 = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	                    double basePrice = getBasePrice(cleanForPrice2);
	                    double minPrice = basePrice * newMultiplier * 0.85;
	                    
	                    if (listing.item.condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	                        minPrice *= 2.5;
	                    } else if (listing.item.condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	                        minPrice *= 1.7;
	                    } else if (listing.item.condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	                        minPrice *= 1.0;
	                    } else if (listing.item.condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	                        minPrice *= 0.7;
	                    } else if (listing.item.condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
	                        minPrice *= 0.3;
	                    }
	                    
	                    if (listing.listPrice < minPrice) {
	                        toRemove.add(listing);
	                        inventoryList.add(listing.item);
	                        inventoryValue += listing.item.price.doubleValue();
	                        activeListings.remove(listing);
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	            
	            synchronized (globalMarketListings) {
	                listings.removeAll(toRemove);
	            }
	            
	            if (totalItemsRemoved > 0) {
	                boolean isRareDopplerGem = (skinName.contains("Sapphire") || 
	                           skinName.contains("Ruby") || 
	                           skinName.contains("Black Pearl"));
	                
	                int newListingsToAdd;
	                
	                if (isRareDopplerGem) {
	                    newListingsToAdd = random.nextDouble() < 0.15 ? 1 : 0;
	                } else {

	                    newListingsToAdd = (int)(totalItemsRemoved * (0.1 + random.nextDouble() * 0.2));
	                    
	                    switch (rarity) {
	                        case "Milspec":
	                            newListingsToAdd = Math.max(3, newListingsToAdd);
	                            break;
	                        case "Restricted":
	                            newListingsToAdd = Math.max(2, newListingsToAdd);
	                            break;
	                        case "Classified":
	                            newListingsToAdd = Math.max(2, newListingsToAdd);
	                            break;
	                        case "Covert":
	                            newListingsToAdd = Math.max(1, newListingsToAdd);
	                            break;
	                        case "Knife":
	                            newListingsToAdd = Math.max(1, Math.min(2, newListingsToAdd));
	                            break;
	                    }
	                }
	                
	                int maxAllowed;
	                switch (rarity) {
	                    case "Milspec":     maxAllowed = 600; break;
	                    case "Restricted":  maxAllowed = 450; break;
	                    case "Classified":  maxAllowed = 350; break;
	                    case "Covert":      maxAllowed = 220; break;
	                    case "Knife":       maxAllowed = 100; break;
	                    case "Gloves":      maxAllowed = 100; break;
	                    default:            maxAllowed = 300; break;
	                }
	                if (listings.size() >= maxAllowed) newListingsToAdd = 0;
	                else newListingsToAdd = Math.min(newListingsToAdd, maxAllowed - listings.size());

	                for (int i = 0; i < newListingsToAdd; i++) {
	                    String cleanSkin = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	                    boolean isStatTrak = skinName.startsWith("StatTrak") || skinName.startsWith("StatTrak ");
	                    
	                    String[] availableConditions = getAvailableConditions(cleanSkin);
	                    String condition = availableConditions[random.nextInt(availableConditions.length)];
	                    
	                    double basePrice = getBasePrice(cleanSkin);
	                    double itemFloat = generateFloatForCondition(cleanSkin, condition);
	                    
	                    double variance = 0.95 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.20);
	                    
	                    double listPrice = basePrice * newMultiplier * variance;
	                    
	                    boolean isGlove = rarity.equals("Gloves");
	                    if (isGlove) {
	                        double gloveBasePrice = getGloveBasePrice(cleanSkin);
	                        listPrice = calculateGlovePrice(cleanSkin, condition, gloveBasePrice);
	                        listPrice *= newMultiplier * variance;

	                        double gloveFloor = calculateGlovePrice(cleanSkin, condition, gloveBasePrice) * 0.75;
	                        if (listPrice < gloveFloor) listPrice = gloveFloor;
	                    } else if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	                        listPrice *= 2.5;
	                    } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	                        listPrice *= 1.7;
	                    } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	                        listPrice *= 1.0;
	                    } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	                        listPrice *= 0.7;
	                    } else if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
	                        listPrice *= 0.3;
	                    }
	                    
	                    boolean isAnyDoppler = cleanSkin.contains("Doppler");
	                    if (!rarity.equals("Knife")) {
	                        if (itemFloat <= 0.0005) {
	                            listPrice *= 3.0;
	                        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.001) {
	                            listPrice *= 2.0;
	                        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.005) {
	                            listPrice *= 1.5;
	                        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.02) {
	                            listPrice *= 1.25;
	                        }
	                    } else if (!isAnyDoppler) {
	                        boolean appliedFnScarcity = false;
	                        if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	                            FloatRange kfr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(cleanSkin);
	                            if (kfr == null) for (Map.Entry<String,FloatRange> e2 : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet())
	                                if (cleanSkin.startsWith(e2.getKey())) { kfr = e2.getValue(); break; }
	                            double kMin = (kfr != null && kfr.min != null) ? kfr.min : 0.0;
	                            if (kMin >= 0.06) {
	                                listPrice *= 2.87;
	                                appliedFnScarcity = true;
	                            }
	                        }
	                        if (!appliedFnScarcity) {
	                            double rel = getRelativeFloat(cleanSkin, itemFloat);
	                            if (!isCappedKnife(cleanSkin)) {
	                                if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                                    listPrice *= 2.5;
	                                } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                                    listPrice *= 1.5;
	                                } else if (rel <= 0.20) {
	                                    listPrice *= 1.1;
	                                }
	                            } else {
	                                if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                                    listPrice *= 1.15;
	                                } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                                    listPrice *= 1.05;
	                                }
	                            }
	                        }
	                    }
	                    
	                    if (isStatTrak && !isGlove) {
	                        boolean isCW2 = cleanSkin.contains("Crimson Web");
	                        boolean isD2  = cleanSkin.contains("Doppler");
	                        if (isCW2)                            listPrice *= 2.0;
	                        else if (isD2)                        listPrice *= 0.80;
	                        else if (rarity.equals("Knife"))      listPrice *= 0.90;
	                        else                                  listPrice *= 1.70 + random.nextDouble() * 0.30;
	                    }
	                    
	                    int sellTime = 30 + random.nextInt(150);
	                    double trueBasePrice = listPrice / newMultiplier;
	                    
	                    String displayRarity = isStatTrak ? "StatTrak " + rarity : rarity;
	                    
	                    Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(cleanSkin);
	                    
	                    InventoryItem dummyItem = new InventoryItem(
	                        skinImg != null ? new ImageIcon(skinImg) : null,
	                        cleanSkin, 
	                        condition, 
	                        displayRarity,
	                        BigDecimal.valueOf(listPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                        itemFloat, 
	                        isStatTrak, 
	                        random.nextInt(1000), 
	                        null, 
	                        trueBasePrice
	                    );
	                    
	                    MarketListing listing = new MarketListing(dummyItem, listPrice, sellTime, false);
	                    listings.add(listing);
	                }
	            }
	        }
	    }

	    repriceNpcBuyOrdersForRarity(rarity, newMultiplier);
	}

	private void repriceNpcBuyOrdersForRarity(String rarity, double newMultiplier) {
	    long now = System.currentTimeMillis();

	    for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder>> entry : npcBuyOrders.entrySet()) {
	        String marketKey = entry.getKey();
	        ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder> orders = entry.getValue();
	        if (orders == null || orders.isEmpty()) continue;

	        String cleanKey = marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        if (!getSkinRarity(cleanKey).equals(rarity)) continue;

	        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey);
	        if (listings == null) {
	            listings = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "StatTrak "));
	        }
	        if (listings == null || listings.isEmpty()) continue;

	        Map<String, Double> cheapestPerCond = new HashMap<>();
	        for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	            if (!ml.isPlayerListing) {
	                cheapestPerCond.merge(ml.item.condition, ml.listPrice, Math::min);
	            }
	        }
	        if (cheapestPerCond.isEmpty()) continue;

	        Map<String, Double> bestPricePerCond = new HashMap<>();
	        for (NpcBuyOrder o : orders) {
	            bestPricePerCond.merge(o.condition, o.price, Math::max);
	        }

	        for (Map.Entry<String, Double> ce : cheapestPerCond.entrySet()) {
	            String condition  = ce.getKey();
	            double cheapest   = ce.getValue();
	            double bestExisting = bestPricePerCond.getOrDefault(condition, 0.0);

	            double newTopPrice = cheapest * (0.90 + random.nextDouble() * 0.04);
	            if (newTopPrice <= bestExisting * 1.02) continue;

	            int avgQty = Math.max(1, npcTotalQuantity(rarity) / Math.max(1, npcOrderCount(rarity)));
	            String buyer = NPC_BUYER_NAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_BUYER_NAMES.length)];
	            NpcBuyOrder fresh = new NpcBuyOrder(marketKey, condition, newTopPrice, avgQty, buyer);
	            fresh.lastFillTime = now;
	            orders.add(fresh);

	            int maxOrders = npcOrderCount(rarity) * 3;
	            List<NpcBuyOrder> condList = orders.stream()
	                .filter(o -> o.condition.equals(condition))
	                .sorted(Comparator.comparingDouble(o -> o.price))
	                .collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.toList());
	            while (condList.size() > maxOrders) {
	                orders.remove(condList.remove(0));
	            }
	        }
	    }
	}
	
	private void handlePriceDecrease(String rarity, double oldMultiplier, double newMultiplier) {
	    
	    repriceExistingNpcListings(rarity, oldMultiplier, newMultiplier);

	    ArrayList<String> skinsOfRarity = new ArrayList<>();
	    for (String skinName : globalMarketListings.keySet()) {
	        String cleanName = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        if (getSkinRarity(cleanName).equals(rarity)) {
	            skinsOfRarity.add(skinName);
	        }
	    }
	    
	    if (skinsOfRarity.isEmpty()) return;

	    double dropRatio = newMultiplier / Math.max(0.01, oldMultiplier);
	    for (String skinName : skinsOfRarity) {
	        if (skinName.contains("Sapphire") || skinName.contains("Ruby") || skinName.contains("Black Pearl")) continue;
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(skinName);
	        if (listings == null) continue;
	        String cleanSkin = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        boolean isStatTrak = skinName.startsWith("StatTrak") || skinName.startsWith("StatTrak ");
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> toRemove = new ArrayList<>();
	        for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	            if (ml.isPlayerListing) continue;

	            double base = rarity.equals("Gloves")
	                ? calculateGlovePrice(cleanSkin, ml.item.condition, getGloveBasePrice(cleanSkin))
	                : getBasePrice(cleanSkin);
	            if (!rarity.equals("Gloves")) {
	                switch (ml.item.condition) {
	                    case "Factory New":    base *= 2.5; break;
	                    case "Minimal Wear":   base *= 1.7; break;
	                    case "Well-Worn":      base *= 0.7; break;
	                    case "Battle-Scarred": base *= 0.3; break;
	                }
	                if (isStatTrak) {
	                    boolean isCW8 = cleanSkin.contains("Crimson Web");
	                    boolean isD8  = cleanSkin.contains("Doppler");
	                    if (isCW8)                            base *= 2.0;
	                    else if (isD8)                        base *= 0.80;
	                    else if (rarity.equals("Knife"))      base *= 0.90;
	                    else                                  base *= 1.85;
	                }
	            }
	            double expectedNew = base * newMultiplier;

	            if (expectedNew > 0 && ml.listPrice > expectedNew * 1.15) {
	                double overshoot = (ml.listPrice - expectedNew * 1.15) / expectedNew;
	                double removalProb = Math.min(0.80, 0.30 + overshoot * 0.5);
	                if (random.nextDouble() < removalProb) {
	                    toRemove.add(ml);
	                }
	            }
	        }
	        listings.removeAll(toRemove);
	    }

	    boolean isRareDopplerGem = false;
	    for (String skinName : skinsOfRarity) {
	        if (skinName.contains("Sapphire") || skinName.contains("Ruby") || skinName.contains("Black Pearl")) {
	            isRareDopplerGem = true;
	            break;
	        }
	    }
	    
	    int totalNewListings;
	    if (isRareDopplerGem) {
	        totalNewListings = random.nextDouble() < 0.20 ? 1 : 0;
	    } else {
	        switch (rarity) {
	            case "Milspec":
	                totalNewListings = 5 + random.nextInt(5);
	                break;
	            case "Restricted":
	                totalNewListings = 4 + random.nextInt(4);
	                break;
	            case "Classified":
	                totalNewListings = 3 + random.nextInt(3); 
	                break;
	            case "Covert":
	                totalNewListings = 2 + random.nextInt(2);
	                break;
	            case "Knife":
	                totalNewListings = 1 + random.nextInt(2); 
	                break;
	            case "Gloves":
	                totalNewListings = 1 + random.nextInt(2);
	                break;
	            default:
	                totalNewListings = 3;
	        }
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < totalNewListings; i++) {
	        String skinName = skinsOfRarity.get(random.nextInt(skinsOfRarity.size()));
	        String cleanSkin = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        boolean isStatTrak = skinName.startsWith("StatTrak") || skinName.startsWith("StatTrak ");
	            
	            String[] availableConditions = getAvailableConditions(cleanSkin);
	            String condition = availableConditions[random.nextInt(availableConditions.length)];
	            
	            double basePrice = getBasePrice(cleanSkin);
	            double itemFloat = generateFloatForCondition(cleanSkin, condition);
	            
	            double variance = 0.85 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.30);
	            
	            double listPrice = basePrice * newMultiplier * variance;
	            
	            boolean isGlove = rarity.equals("Gloves");
	            if (isGlove) {
	                double gloveBasePrice = getGloveBasePrice(cleanSkin);
	                listPrice = calculateGlovePrice(cleanSkin, condition, gloveBasePrice);
	                listPrice *= newMultiplier * variance;

	                double gloveFloor = calculateGlovePrice(cleanSkin, condition, gloveBasePrice) * 0.75;
	                if (listPrice < gloveFloor) listPrice = gloveFloor;
	            } else if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	                listPrice *= 2.5;
	            } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	                listPrice *= 1.7;
	            } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	                listPrice *= 1.0;
	            } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	                listPrice *= 0.7;
	            } else if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
	                listPrice *= 0.3;
	            }
	            
	            boolean isAnyDoppler = cleanSkin.contains("Doppler");
	            if (!rarity.equals("Knife") && !isGlove) {
	                if (itemFloat <= 0.0005) {
	                    listPrice *= 3.0;
	                } else if (itemFloat <= 0.001) {
	                    listPrice *= 2.0;
	                } else if (itemFloat <= 0.005) {
	                    listPrice *= 1.5;
	                } else if (itemFloat <= 0.02) {
	                    listPrice *= 1.25;
	                }
	            } else if (rarity.equals("Knife") && !isAnyDoppler && !isGlove) {
	                boolean appliedFnS = false;
	                if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	                    FloatRange dFr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(cleanSkin);
	                    double dMin = (dFr != null && dFr.min != null) ? dFr.min : 0.0;
	                    if (dMin >= 0.06) { listPrice *= 2.87; appliedFnS = true; }
	                }
	                if (!appliedFnS) {
	                    double rel = getRelativeFloat(cleanSkin, itemFloat);
	                    if (!isCappedKnife(cleanSkin)) {
	                        if (rel <= 0.01) listPrice *= 2.5;
	                        else if (rel <= 0.05) listPrice *= 1.5;
	                        else if (rel <= 0.20) listPrice *= 1.1;
	                    } else {
	                        if (rel <= 0.01) listPrice *= 1.15;
	                        else if (rel <= 0.05) listPrice *= 1.05;
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	            
	            if (isStatTrak && !isGlove) {
	                boolean isCW3 = cleanSkin.contains("Crimson Web");
	                boolean isD3  = cleanSkin.contains("Doppler");
	                if (isCW3)                            listPrice *= 2.0;
	                else if (isD3)                        listPrice *= 0.80;
	                else if (rarity.equals("Knife"))      listPrice *= 0.90;
	                else                                  listPrice *= 1.70 + random.nextDouble() * 0.30;
	            }
	            
	            int sellTime = 30 + random.nextInt(150);
	            double trueBasePrice = listPrice / newMultiplier;
	            
	            String displayRarity = isStatTrak ? "StatTrak " + rarity : rarity;

	            Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(cleanSkin);
	            
	            InventoryItem dummyItem = new InventoryItem(
	                skinImg != null ? new ImageIcon(skinImg) : null,
	                cleanSkin, 
	                condition, 
	                displayRarity,
	                BigDecimal.valueOf(listPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                itemFloat, 
	                isStatTrak, 
	                random.nextInt(1000), 
	                null, 
	                trueBasePrice
	            );
	            
	            MarketListing listing = new MarketListing(dummyItem, listPrice, sellTime, false);
	            
	            if (!globalMarketListings.containsKey(skinName)) {
	                globalMarketListings.put(skinName, new ArrayList<>());
	            }

	            int maxDecreaseAllowed;
	            switch (rarity) {
	                case "Milspec":    maxDecreaseAllowed = 600; break;
	                case "Restricted": maxDecreaseAllowed = 450; break;
	                case "Classified": maxDecreaseAllowed = 350; break;
	                case "Covert":     maxDecreaseAllowed = 220; break;
	                default:           maxDecreaseAllowed = 100; break;
	            }
	            if (globalMarketListings.get(skinName).size() < maxDecreaseAllowed) {
	                globalMarketListings.get(skinName).add(listing);
	            }
	        }

	    downpriceNpcBuyOrdersForRarity(rarity, newMultiplier);
	}

	private void downpriceNpcBuyOrdersForRarity(String rarity, double newMultiplier) {
	    for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder>> entry : npcBuyOrders.entrySet()) {
	        String marketKey = entry.getKey();
	        ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder> orders = entry.getValue();
	        if (orders == null || orders.isEmpty()) continue;

	        String cleanKey = marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        if (!getSkinRarity(cleanKey).equals(rarity)) continue;

	        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey);
	        if (listings == null)
	            listings = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "StatTrak "));

	        Map<String, Double> cheapestPerCond = new HashMap<>();
	        if (listings != null) {
	            for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	                if (!ml.isPlayerListing)
	                    cheapestPerCond.merge(ml.item.condition, ml.listPrice, Math::min);
	            }
	        }

	        orders.removeIf(o -> {
	            double cheapest = cheapestPerCond.getOrDefault(o.condition, Double.MAX_VALUE);
	            return o.price >= cheapest * 0.99 || o.price < 0.01;
	        });
	    }
	}

	private void updateActiveListings() {
	    ArrayList<MarketListing> sold = new ArrayList<>();
	    for (MarketListing listing : activeListings) {
	        listing.timeRemaining -= 5;
	        if (listing.timeRemaining <= 0) {
	            balance += listing.listPrice;
	            missionMarketSellCount++;
	            
	            double profit = listing.listPrice - listing.item.basePrice;
	            if (profit > 0) {
	                totalMarketProfit += profit;
	            }
	            
	            sold.add(listing);
	        }
	    }
	    activeListings.removeAll(sold);
	    
	    if (!sold.isEmpty()) {
	        if (sold.size() == 1) {
	            MarketListing s = sold.get(0);
	            tradeNotificationLabel.setText("SOLD: " + s.item.name + " - $" + String.format("%.2f", s.listPrice));
	        } else {
	            double totalSold = sold.stream().mapToDouble(l -> l.listPrice).sum();
	            tradeNotificationLabel.setText("SOLD " + sold.size() + " items - $" + String.format("%.2f", totalSold));
	        }

	        javax.swing.Timer clearNotif = new javax.swing.Timer(5000, e -> tradeNotificationLabel.setText(""));
	        clearNotif.setRepeats(false);
	        clearNotif.start();
	    }
	    
	    if (!sold.isEmpty() && !achievements.get("first_sale").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("first_sale");
	    }
	    
	    if (totalMarketProfit >= 10000 && !achievements.get("market_profit_10k").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("market_profit_10k");
	    }
	    
	    if (!sold.isEmpty()) updateBalanceLabel();
	}

	private double getCurrentMarketPrice(InventoryItem item) {
	    if (isBlueGem(item)) {

	        return item.price.doubleValue();
	    }

	    String rarityKey = item.rarity.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	    boolean isGloveRarity = rarityKey.equals("Gloves");

	    double rawBase;
	    if (isGloveRarity) {

	        double gloveBase = getGloveBasePrice(item.name);
	        rawBase = calculateGlovePrice(item.name, item.condition, gloveBase);
	    } else {
	        rawBase = getBasePrice(item.name);

	        switch (item.condition) {
	            case "Factory New":    rawBase *= 2.5; break;
	            case "Minimal Wear":   rawBase *= 1.7; break;
	            case "Well-Worn":      rawBase *= 0.7; break;
	            case "Battle-Scarred": rawBase *= 0.3; break;

	        }

	        if (item.isStattrak) {
	            rawBase *= rarityKey.equals("Knife") ? 1.15 : 2.0;
	        }
	    }

	    double currentMarketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarityKey, 1.0);
	    return rawBase * currentMarketMulti;
	}

	private int calculateSellTime(double listPrice, double marketPrice) {
	    double ratio = listPrice / marketPrice;
	    if (ratio <= 0.8) return 15 + random.nextInt(30);
	    else if (ratio <= 0.9) return 30 + random.nextInt(30);
	    else if (ratio <= 1.0) return 60 + random.nextInt(30);
	    else if (ratio <= 1.1) return 90 + random.nextInt(30);
	    else if (ratio <= 1.3) return 120 + random.nextInt(30);
	    else return 180 + random.nextInt(100);
	}
	
	private void generateGlobalMarketListings() {	  
		if (!globalMarketListings.isEmpty()) {
	        for (MarketListing playerListing : activeListings) {
	            String cleanName = normalizeSkinName(playerListing.item.name);
	            String marketKey = playerListing.item.isStattrak ? 
	                "StatTrak " + cleanName : cleanName;
	            
	            marketKey = normalizeSkinName(marketKey);
	            
	            if (!globalMarketListings.containsKey(marketKey)) {
	                globalMarketListings.put(marketKey, new ArrayList<>());
	            }
	            
	            boolean alreadyListed = false;
	            for (MarketListing l : globalMarketListings.get(marketKey)) {
	                if (l == playerListing) {
	                    alreadyListed = true;
	                    break;
	                }
	            }
	            if (!alreadyListed) {
	                globalMarketListings.get(marketKey).add(playerListing);
	            }
	        }
	        return;
	    }
	    
	    globalBlueGemCounts.clear();

	    String[] allKnifeSkins = {
	        "Karambit | Slaughter", "Karambit | Crimson Web", "Karambit | Scorched",
	        "Karambit | Urban Masked", "Karambit | Night",
	        "Karambit | Doppler (Phase 1)", "Karambit | Doppler (Phase 2)",
	        "Karambit | Doppler (Phase 3)", "Karambit | Doppler (Phase 4)",
	        "Karambit | Doppler (Sapphire)", "Karambit | Doppler (Ruby)",
	        "Karambit | Doppler (Black Pearl)",
	        "M9 Bayonet | Slaughter", "M9 Bayonet | Crimson Web",
	        "M9 Bayonet | Blue Steel", "M9 Bayonet | Case Hardened",
	        "M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Phase 1)", "M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Phase 2)",
	        "M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Phase 3)", "M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Phase 4)",
	        "M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Sapphire)", "M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Ruby)",
	        "M9 Bayonet | Doppler (Black Pearl)",
	        "Bayonet | Scorched", "Bayonet | Boreal Forest", "Bayonet | Fade",
	        "Flip Knife | Vanilla", "Flip Knife | Case Hardened",
	        "Gut Knife | Fade", "Gut Knife | Forest DDPAT", "Gut Knife | Safari Mesh",
	        "Butterfly Knife | Case Hardened", "Butterfly Knife | Crimson Web",
	        "Butterfly Knife | Fade", "Butterfly Knife | Safari Mesh",
	        "Butterfly Knife | Slaughter", "Butterfly Knife | Urban Masked",
	        "Butterfly Knife | Vanilla", "Butterfly Knife | Ultraviolet",
	        "Huntsman Knife | Marble Fade", "Huntsman Knife | Tiger Tooth",
	        "Bowie Knife | Marble Fade", "Bowie Knife | Tiger Tooth",
	        "Falchion Knife | Marble Fade", "Falchion Knife | Tiger Tooth"
	    };
	    
	    String[] allGloveSkins = {
	        "Bloodhound Gloves | Bronzed",
	        "Bloodhound Gloves | Charred",
	        "Bloodhound Gloves | Guerrilla",
	        "Bloodhound Gloves | Snakebite",
	        "Driver Gloves | Convoy",
	        "Driver Gloves | Crimson Weave",
	        "Driver Gloves | Diamondback",
	        "Driver Gloves | Lunar Weave",
	        "Hand Wraps | Badlands",
	        "Hand Wraps | Leather",
	        "Hand Wraps | Slaughter",
	        "Hand Wraps | Spruce DDPAT",
	        "Moto Gloves | Boom!",
	        "Moto Gloves | Cool Mint",
	        "Moto Gloves | Eclipse",
	        "Moto Gloves | Spearmint",
	        "Specialist Gloves | Crimson Kimono",
	        "Specialist Gloves | Emerald Web",
	        "Specialist Gloves | Forest DDPAT",
	        "Specialist Gloves | Foundation",
	        "Sport Gloves | Arid",
	        "Sport Gloves | Hedge Maze",
	        "Sport Gloves | Pandora's Box",
	        "Sport Gloves | Superconductor"
	    };

	    String[] allGunSkins = {
	        "AWP | Lightning Strike", "Desert Eagle | Golden Koi", "AK-47 | Fire Serpent",
	        "P90 | Asiimov", "M4A1-S | Cyrex", "AK-47 | Bloodsport", "USP-S | Neo Noir",
	        
	        "Desert Eagle | Hypnotic", "P90 | Emerald Dragon", "AK-47 | Case Hardened",
	        "P2000 | Ocean Foam", "AWP | Graphite", "Five-SeveN | Fowl Play",
	        "Desert Eagle | Conspiracy", "Glock-18 | Water Elemental",
	        "CZ75-Auto | Xiangliu", "AWP | Fever Dream", "M4A1-S | Decimator",
	        
	        "Glock-18 | Dragon Tattoo", "MAC-10 | Graven", "M4A1-S | Dark Water",
	        "M4A1-S | Bright Water", "USP-S | Dark Water", "M4A4 | Zirka",
	        "USP-S | Overgrowth", "Nova | Koi", "PP-Bizon | Osiris",
	        "CZ75-Auto | Tigris", "P250 | Supernova",
	        "M249 | Emerald Poison Dart", "MAC-10 | Last Dive", "UMP-45 | Scaffold",
	        "XM1014 | Seasons", "Galil AR | Crimson Tsunami",
	        
	        "MP7 | Skulls", "AUG | Wings", "Galil AR | Shattered",
	        "SG 553 | Ultraviolet", "SG 553 | Wave Spray", "G3SG1 | Demeter",
	        "Nova | Tempest", "Dual Berettas | Black Limba", "Negev | Desert-Strike",
	        "UMP-45 | Labyrinth", "P2000 | Ivory", "MP7 | Urban Hazard", "SSG 08 | Abyss",
	        "PP-Bizon | Jungle Slipstream", "Sawed-Off | Zander", "MP7 | Akoben",
	        "P250 | Ripple", "SCAR-20 | Blueprint", "Five-SeveN | Capillary",
	        "Desert Eagle | Oxide Blaze"
	    };
	    
	    String[] allSkins = new String[allKnifeSkins.length + allGloveSkins.length + allGunSkins.length];
	    System.arraycopy(allKnifeSkins, 0, allSkins, 0, allKnifeSkins.length);
	    System.arraycopy(allGloveSkins, 0, allSkins, allKnifeSkins.length, allGloveSkins.length);
	    System.arraycopy(allGunSkins, 0, allSkins, allKnifeSkins.length + allGloveSkins.length, allGunSkins.length);
	    
	    for (String skinName : allSkins) {
	        double basePrice = getBasePrice(skinName);
	        String rarity = getSkinRarity(skinName);
	        double marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarity, 1.0);

	        boolean isRareDopplerGem = skinName.contains("Sapphire") || 
	                                   skinName.contains("Ruby") || 
	                                   skinName.contains("Black Pearl");
	        
	        boolean isGlove = rarity.equals("Gloves");

	        String[] availableConditions = getAvailableConditions(skinName);

	        int statTrakLoopEnd = isGlove ? 1 : 2;
	        
	        for (int statTrakVersion = 0; statTrakVersion < statTrakLoopEnd; statTrakVersion++) {
	            boolean isStattrak = (statTrakVersion == 1);
	            
	            String normalizedSkinName = normalizeSkinName(skinName);
	            String marketKey;
	            if (isStattrak) {
	                marketKey = "StatTrak " + normalizedSkinName;
	            } else {
	                marketKey = normalizedSkinName;
	            }
	            
	            marketKey = normalizeSkinName(marketKey);

	            if (isRareDopplerGem) {
	                int totalListings = 10 + random.nextInt(6); 
	                
	                int fnCount = (int)(totalListings * 0.75); 
	                int mwCount = totalListings - fnCount;    
	                
	                for (int i = 0; i < fnCount; i++) {
	                    String condition = "Factory New";
	                    double variance = 0.90 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.20); 
	                    double itemFloat = generateFloatForCondition(skinName, condition);
	                    double listPrice = basePrice * marketMulti * variance;

	                    if (isStattrak) {
	                        listPrice *= 0.80;
	                    }

	                    listPrice *= 2.5;

	                    boolean isAnyDoppler = skinName.contains("Doppler");
	                    if (!isAnyDoppler) {
	                        double rel = getRelativeFloat(skinName, itemFloat);
	                        if (!isCappedKnife(skinName)) {
	                            if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                                listPrice *= 2.5;
	                            } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                                listPrice *= 1.5;
	                            } else if (rel <= 0.20) {
	                                listPrice *= 1.1;
	                            }
	                        } else {
	                            if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                                listPrice *= 1.15;
	                            } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                                listPrice *= 1.05;
	                            }
	                        }
	                    }
	                    
	                    int sellTime = 30 + random.nextInt(150);
	                    double trueBasePrice = listPrice / marketMulti;
	                    
	                    Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(skinName);
	                    
	                    String displayRarity = isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + rarity : rarity;
	                    
	                    InventoryItem dummyItem = new InventoryItem(
	                        skinImg != null ? new ImageIcon(skinImg) : null,
	                        skinName, 
	                        condition, 
	                        displayRarity,
	                        BigDecimal.valueOf(listPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                        itemFloat, 
	                        isStattrak, 
	                        random.nextInt(1000), 
	                        null, 
	                        trueBasePrice
	                    );
	                    
	                    MarketListing listing = new MarketListing(dummyItem, listPrice, sellTime, false);
	                    
	                    if (!globalMarketListings.containsKey(marketKey)) {
	                        globalMarketListings.put(marketKey, new ArrayList<>());
	                    }
	                    globalMarketListings.get(marketKey).add(listing);
	                }
	                
	                for (int i = 0; i < mwCount; i++) {
	                    String condition = "Minimal Wear";
	                    double variance = 0.90 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.20); 
	                    double itemFloat = generateFloatForCondition(skinName, condition);
	                    double listPrice = basePrice * marketMulti * variance;

	                    if (isStattrak) {
	                        listPrice *= 0.80;
	                    }

	                    listPrice *= 1.7;

	                    boolean isAnyDoppler = skinName.contains("Doppler");
	                    if (!isAnyDoppler) {
	                        double rel = getRelativeFloat(skinName, itemFloat);
	                        if (!isCappedKnife(skinName)) {
	                            if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                                listPrice *= 2.5;
	                            } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                                listPrice *= 1.5;
	                            } else if (rel <= 0.20) {
	                                listPrice *= 1.1;
	                            }
	                        } else {
	                            if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                                listPrice *= 1.15;
	                            } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                                listPrice *= 1.05;
	                            }
	                        }
	                    }
	                    
	                    int sellTime = 30 + random.nextInt(150);
	                    double trueBasePrice = listPrice / marketMulti;
	                    
	                    Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(skinName);
	                    
	                    String displayRarity = isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + rarity : rarity;
	                    
	                    InventoryItem dummyItem = new InventoryItem(
	                        skinImg != null ? new ImageIcon(skinImg) : null,
	                        skinName, 
	                        condition, 
	                        displayRarity,
	                        BigDecimal.valueOf(listPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                        itemFloat, 
	                        isStattrak, 
	                        random.nextInt(1000), 
	                        null, 
	                        trueBasePrice
	                    );
	                    
	                    MarketListing listing = new MarketListing(dummyItem, listPrice, sellTime, false);
	                    
	                    if (!globalMarketListings.containsKey(marketKey)) {
	                        globalMarketListings.put(marketKey, new ArrayList<>());
	                    }
	                    globalMarketListings.get(marketKey).add(listing);
	                }
	                
	                continue; 
	            }

	            FloatRange fr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(skinName);
	            if (fr == null) {
	                for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet()) {
	                    if (skinName.startsWith(e.getKey())) {
	                        fr = e.getValue();
	                        break;
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	            
	            double floatMin = (fr != null && fr.min != null) ? fr.min : 0.0;
	            double floatMax = (fr != null && fr.max != null) ? fr.max : 1.0;
	            
	            if (isGlove) {
	                floatMin = 0.06;
	                floatMax = 0.80;
	            }
	            
	            Map<String, Double> wearDistribution = new HashMap<>();
	            double totalRange = 0;
	            
	            boolean isSpecialCapped = (floatMax <= 0.10);
	            
	            for (String condition : availableConditions) {
	                double condMin, condMax;
	                
	                if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	                    condMin = Math.max(floatMin, 0.00);
	                    condMax = Math.min(floatMax, 0.07);
	                } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	                    condMin = Math.max(floatMin, 0.07);
	                    condMax = Math.min(floatMax, 0.15);
	                } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	                    condMin = Math.max(floatMin, 0.15);
	                    condMax = Math.min(floatMax, 0.38);
	                } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	                    condMin = Math.max(floatMin, 0.38);
	                    condMax = Math.min(floatMax, 0.45);
	                } else {
	                    condMin = Math.max(floatMin, 0.45);
	                    condMax = Math.min(floatMax, 1.00);
	                }
	                
	                double range = Math.max(0, condMax - condMin);
	                
	                if (isSpecialCapped && floatMax <= 0.08) {
	                    if (condition.equals("Factory New") && range > 0) {
	                        range *= 1.1;
	                    }
	                }
	                
	                wearDistribution.put(condition, range);
	                totalRange += range;
	            }
	            
	            int baseListings;
	            
	            if (rarity.equals("Knife")) {
	                baseListings = 80 + random.nextInt(20); 
	            } else if (rarity.equals("Gloves")) {
	                baseListings = 80 + random.nextInt(20);
	            } else if (rarity.equals("Covert")) {
	                baseListings = 200 + random.nextInt(30);
	            } else if (rarity.equals("Classified")) {
	                baseListings = 300 + random.nextInt(40);
	            } else if (rarity.equals("Restricted")) {
	                baseListings = 400 + random.nextInt(50);
	            } else { 
	                baseListings = 550 + random.nextInt(60); 
	            }

	            if (isStattrak && !isGlove) {
	                baseListings = (int)(baseListings * (0.4 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.3)));
	            }

	            for (String condition : availableConditions) {
	                double conditionRange = wearDistribution.get(condition);
	                if (conditionRange == 0) continue;
	                
	                double percentage = conditionRange / totalRange;
	                
	                
	                
	                
	                int rawCount = (int)(baseListings * percentage);
	                int numListings;
	                if (conditionRange < 0.02) {
	                    
	                    
	                    numListings = Math.max(2, Math.min(rawCount, 4));
	                } else if (conditionRange < 0.05) {
	                    numListings = Math.max(3, Math.min(rawCount, 8));
	                } else {
	                    numListings = Math.max(5, rawCount);
	                }
	                
	                for (int i = 0; i < numListings; i++) {
	                    double variance = 0.85 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.3);
	                    double itemFloat = generateFloatForCondition(skinName, condition);
	                    double listPrice = basePrice * marketMulti * variance;

	                    if (isGlove) {
	                        double gloveBasePrice = getGloveBasePrice(skinName);
	                        double price = calculateGlovePrice(skinName, condition, gloveBasePrice);
	                        price *= marketMulti * variance;
	                        listPrice = price;
	                        
		                    if (listPrice < gloveBasePrice * 0.5 && isGlove) {
		                        gloveBasePrice = getGloveBasePrice(skinName);
		                        listPrice = calculateGlovePrice(skinName, condition, gloveBasePrice);
		                        listPrice *= marketMulti * 0.90;
		                    }
	                    } else if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	                        listPrice *= 2.5;
	                    } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	                        listPrice *= 1.7;
	                    } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	                        listPrice *= 1.0;
	                    } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	                        listPrice *= 0.7;
	                    } else if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
	                        listPrice *= 0.3;
	                    }
	                    
	                    double priceFloor = basePrice * marketMulti * 0.15;
	                    if (listPrice < priceFloor) listPrice = priceFloor;

	                    boolean allowsUltraLow = floatMin <= 0.02;      

	                    if (!rarity.equals("Knife") && !isGlove && allowsUltraLow) {
	                        if (itemFloat <= 0.0005) {
	                            listPrice *= 3.0;
	                        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.001) {
	                            listPrice *= 2.0;
	                        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.005) {
	                            listPrice *= 1.5;
	                        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.02) {
	                            listPrice *= 1.25;
	                        }
	                    }

	                    boolean isAnyDoppler = skinName.contains("Doppler");
	                    if (rarity.equals("Knife") && !isAnyDoppler && !isGlove) {
	                        boolean appliedFnScarcity = false;

	                        if (condition.equals("Factory New") && floatMin >= 0.06) {
	                            listPrice *= 2.87;
	                            appliedFnScarcity = true;
	                        }
	                        if (!appliedFnScarcity) {
	                            double rel = getRelativeFloat(skinName, itemFloat);
	                            if (!isCappedKnife(skinName)) {
	                                if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                                    listPrice *= 2.5;
	                                } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                                    listPrice *= 1.5;
	                                } else if (rel <= 0.20) {
	                                    listPrice *= 1.1;
	                                }
	                            } else {
	                                if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                                    listPrice *= 1.15;
	                                } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                                    listPrice *= 1.05;
	                                }
	                            }
	                        }
	                    }

	                    if (isStattrak && !isGlove) {
	                        boolean isCW4 = skinName.contains("Crimson Web");
	                        boolean isD4  = skinName.contains("Doppler");
	                        if (isCW4)                            listPrice *= 2.0;
	                        else if (isD4)                        listPrice *= 0.80;
	                        else if (rarity.equals("Knife"))      listPrice *= 0.90;
	                        else                                  listPrice *= 1.70 + random.nextDouble() * 0.30;
	                    }
	                    
	                    int sellTime = 30 + random.nextInt(150);
	                    double trueBasePrice = listPrice / marketMulti;
	                    
	                    Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(skinName);
	                    
	                    String displayRarity = isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + rarity : rarity;
	                    
	                    InventoryItem dummyItem = new InventoryItem(
	                        skinImg != null ? new ImageIcon(skinImg) : null,
	                        skinName, 
	                        condition, 
	                        displayRarity,
	                        BigDecimal.valueOf(listPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                        itemFloat, 
	                        isStattrak, 
	                        random.nextInt(1000), 
	                        null, 
	                        trueBasePrice
	                    );
	                    
	                    MarketListing listing = new MarketListing(dummyItem, listPrice, sellTime, false);
	                    
	                    if (!globalMarketListings.containsKey(marketKey)) {
	                        globalMarketListings.put(marketKey, new ArrayList<>());
	                    }
	                    globalMarketListings.get(marketKey).add(listing);
	                }
	            }	            
	        }
	    }
	    
	    for (MarketListing playerListing : activeListings) {
	        String cleanName = normalizeSkinName(playerListing.item.name);
	        String marketKey = playerListing.item.isStattrak ? 
	            "StatTrak " + cleanName : cleanName;
	        
	        if (!globalMarketListings.containsKey(marketKey)) {
	            globalMarketListings.put(marketKey, new ArrayList<>());
	        }
	        globalMarketListings.get(marketKey).add(playerListing);
	    }

	    
	    if (ARMOURY_COLLECTIONS != null) {
	        String[] conditions  = {"Factory New", "Minimal Wear", "Field-Tested", "Well-Worn", "Battle-Scarred"};
	        double[] condMults   = {2.2, 1.5, 1.0, 0.65, 0.3};
	        for (ArmouryCollection ac : ARMOURY_COLLECTIONS) {
	            String[][] nameTiers  = {ac.industrialNames, ac.milspecNames, ac.restrictedNames, ac.classifiedNames, ac.covertNames};
	            double[][] priceTiers = {ac.industrialPrices, ac.milspecPrices, ac.restrictedPrices, ac.classifiedPrices, ac.covertPrices};
	            String[] rarityLabels = {"Industrial", "Milspec", "Restricted", "Classified", "Covert"};
	            for (int t = 0; t < nameTiers.length; t++) {
	                if (nameTiers[t] == null) continue;
	                for (int s = 0; s < nameTiers[t].length; s++) {
	                    String sName  = nameTiers[t][s];
	                    double baseP  = priceTiers[t][s];
	                    String rar    = rarityLabels[t];
	                    for (int c = 0; c < conditions.length; c++) {
	                        String mKey = normalizeSkinName(sName);
	                        globalMarketListings.computeIfAbsent(mKey, k -> new ArrayList<>());
	                        int listingCount = 3 + random.nextInt(4);
	                        for (int n = 0; n < listingCount; n++) {
	                            double listPrice = baseP * condMults[c] * (0.88 + random.nextDouble() * 0.24);
	                            double flt = random.nextDouble() * 0.80;
	                            InventoryItem mi = new InventoryItem(null, sName, conditions[c],
	                                rar,
	                                BigDecimal.valueOf(listPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                                flt, false, random.nextInt(1000), null, listPrice);
	                            mi.collection = ac.name;
	                            globalMarketListings.get(mKey).add(
	                                new MarketListing(mi, listPrice, 300 + random.nextInt(600), false));
	                        }
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	        }
	    }
	}
	
	private double generateFloatForCondition(String skinName, String condition) {
	    if (skinName.contains("Gloves") || skinName.contains("Hand Wraps")) {
	        double min = 0.06;
	        double max = 0.80;
	        
	        double condMin, condMax;
	        
	        if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	            condMin = 0.06;
	            condMax = Math.min(max, 0.07);
	        } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	            condMin = Math.max(min, 0.07);
	            condMax = Math.min(max, 0.15);
	        } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	            condMin = Math.max(min, 0.15);
	            condMax = Math.min(max, 0.38);
	        } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	            condMin = Math.max(min, 0.38);
	            condMax = Math.min(max, 0.45);
	        } else {
	            condMin = Math.max(min, 0.45);
	            condMax = Math.min(max, 0.80);
	        }
	        
	        if (condMin >= condMax) {
	            return condMin;
	        }
	        
	        return condMin + (random.nextDouble() * (condMax - condMin));
	    }
	    
	    FloatRange fr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(skinName);
	    if (fr == null) {
	        for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet()) {
	            if (skinName.startsWith(e.getKey())) {
	                fr = e.getValue();
	                break;
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    
	    double min = (fr != null && fr.min != null) ? fr.min : 0.0;
	    double max = (fr != null && fr.max != null) ? fr.max : 1.0;
	    
	    double condMin, condMax;
	    
	    if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	        condMin = Math.max(min, 0.00);
	        condMax = Math.min(max, 0.07);
	    } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	        condMin = Math.max(min, 0.07);
	        condMax = Math.min(max, 0.15);
	    } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	        condMin = Math.max(min, 0.15);
	        condMax = Math.min(max, 0.38);
	    } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	        condMin = Math.max(min, 0.38);
	        condMax = Math.min(max, 0.45);
	    } else { 
	        condMin = Math.max(min, 0.45);
	        condMax = Math.min(max, 1.00);
	    }
	    
	    if (condMin >= condMax) {
	        return condMin;
	    }
	    
	    boolean isDoppler = skinName.contains("Doppler");
	    boolean isFade = skinName.contains("Fade");
	    
	    if ((isDoppler || isFade) && max <= 0.08) {
	        double range = condMax - condMin;
	        double bias = random.nextDouble();
	        bias = Math.pow(bias, 2.5);
	        return condMin + (bias * range);
	    }
	    
	    return condMin + (random.nextDouble() * (condMax - condMin));
	}
	
	private final Map<String, String> rarityCache = new HashMap<>();
	private String getSkinRarity(String skinName) {
	    String cached = rarityCache.get(skinName);
	    if (cached != null) return cached;
	    if (rarityCache.size() > 2000) rarityCache.clear();
	    String original = skinName;

	    String spaceless = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "")
	                               .replace("StatTrak ", "")
	                               .replaceAll("[^a-zA-Z0-9\\s\\-|]+", "")
	                               .trim();

	    if (spaceless.contains("Bloodhound Gloves") || spaceless.contains("Driver Gloves") ||
	        spaceless.contains("Hand Wraps") || spaceless.contains("Moto Gloves") ||
	        spaceless.contains("Specialist Gloves") || spaceless.contains("Sport Gloves")) {
	        rarityCache.put(original, "Gloves"); return "Gloves";
	    }

	    if (spaceless.contains("Karambit") || spaceless.contains("M9 Bayonet") ||
	        spaceless.contains("Flip Knife") || spaceless.contains("Gut Knife") ||
	        spaceless.contains("Butterfly Knife") || spaceless.contains("Bayonet") ||
	        spaceless.contains("Huntsman Knife") || spaceless.contains("Bowie Knife") ||
	        spaceless.contains("Falchion Knife")) {
	        rarityCache.put(original, "Knife"); return "Knife";
	    }

	        // Normalize for matching: lowercase, remove spaces, pipes, dashes
    String normName = spaceless.toLowerCase().replace(" ", "").replace("|", "").replace("-", "");

    String[][] rarityGroups = {
        // Covert
        {"Covert",
         "AWP|LightningStrike", "DesertEagle|GoldenKoi", "AK47|FireSerpent",
         "P90|Asiimov", "M4A1S|Cyrex", "AK47|Bloodsport", "USPS|NeoNoir",
         "M4A1S|Fade", "AK47|BtheMonster", "AWP|CMYK"},
        // Classified
        {"Classified",
         "DesertEagle|Hypnotic", "P90|EmeraldDragon", "AK47|CaseHardened",
         "P2000|OceanFoam", "AWP|Graphite", "FiveSeveN|FowlPlay",
         "DesertEagle|Conspiracy", "Glock18|WaterElemental",
         "CZ75Auto|Xiangliu", "AWP|FeverDream", "M4A1S|Decimator",
         "Glock18|AXIA", "GalilAR|RainbowSpoon",
         "Zeusx27|DragonSnore", "AWP|Crakow",
         "DesertEagle|Starcade", "AUG|LilPig"},
        // Restricted
        {"Restricted",
         "Glock|DragonTattoo", "MAC10|Graven", "M4A1S|DarkWater",
         "M4A1S|BrightWater", "USPS|DarkWater", "M4A4|Zirka",
         "USPS|Overgrowth", "Nova|Koi", "PPBizon|Osiris",
         "CZ75Auto|Tigris", "P250|Supernova", "M249|EmeraldPoisonDart",
         "MAC10|LastDive", "UMP45|Scaffold", "XM1014|Seasons",
         "GalilAR|CrimsonTsunami",
         "UMP45|CrimsonFoil", "MP9|ArcticTriTone", "FiveSeveN|HeatTreated",
         "XM1014|MonsterMelt", "DualBerettas|SweetLittleAngels", "AUG|EyeofZapems",
         "P90|AttackVector", "M4A4|Polysoup", "CZ75Auto|Slalom"},
        // Milspec
        {"Milspec",
         "MP7|Skulls", "AUG|Wings", "GalilAR|Shattered", "SG553|Ultraviolet",
         "SG553|WaveSpray", "G3SG1|Demeter", "Nova|Tempest", "DualBerettas|BlackLimba",
         "Negev|DesertStrike", "UMP45|Labyrinth", "P2000|Ivory", "MP7|UrbanHazard",
         "SSG08|Abyss", "PPBizon|JungleSlipstream", "SawedOff|Zander",
         "MP7|Akoben", "P250|Ripple", "SCAR20|Blueprint", "FiveSeveN|Capillary",
         "DesertEagle|OxideBlaze",
         "USPS|AlpineCamo", "SSG08|Zeno", "P250|SmallGame", "Nova|Yorkshire",
         "Nova|WurstHolle", "MAC10|Pipsqueak", "Glock18|TealGraf", "GalilAR|MetallicSqueezer",
         "XM1014|HalftoneShift", "SG553|BerryGelCoat", "SCAR20|WildBerry", "AK47|Crossfade"},
        // Industrial
        {"Industrial",
         "MP5SD|SavannahHalftone", "PPBizon|ColdCell", "Tec9|TigerStencil",
         "MAG7|Wildwood", "FAMAS|HalfSleeve", "AK47|OlivePolycam",
         "MP5SD|NeonSqueezer", "P90|Washme", "Negev|WallBang",
         "M4A1S|Washmeplz", "FiveSeveN|MidnightPaintover", "DesertEagle|Tilted",
         "SSG08|HalftoneWhorl", "P2000|CoralHalftone", "MP7|Astrolabe",
         "M249|Spectrogram", "GalilAR|NV", "FAMAS|HalftoneWash"}
    };

    for (String[] group : rarityGroups) {
        String rarity = group[0];
        for (int gi = 1; gi < group.length; gi++) {
            String normSkin = group[gi].toLowerCase().replace(" ", "").replace("|", "").replace("-", "");
            if (normName.equals(normSkin) || normName.contains(normSkin)) {
                rarityCache.put(original, rarity); return rarity;
            }
        }
    }

    rarityCache.put(original, "Milspec"); 
	    return "Milspec";
	}
	
	private void processBuyOrders() {
	    if (buyOrders.isEmpty()) return;

	    buyOrders.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.maxPrice, a.maxPrice));

	    long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
	    ArrayList<String> notifications = new ArrayList<>();
	    List<BuyOrder> toRemove = new ArrayList<>();

	    for (BuyOrder order : buyOrders) {
	        if (order.isComplete()) { toRemove.add(order); continue; }

	        String lookupKey = normalizeSkinName(order.skinName);
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(lookupKey);
	        if (listings == null) {
	            listings = globalMarketListings.get(lookupKey.replace("StatTrak ", ""));
	        }

	        boolean filledThisTick = false;

	        if (listings != null && !listings.isEmpty()) {
	            MarketListing bestMatch = null;
	            double bestMatchPrice = Double.MAX_VALUE;
	            for (MarketListing listing : listings) {
	                if (listing.isPlayerListing) continue;
	                boolean conditionMatches = order.desiredCondition.equals("Any") ||
	                                           listing.item.condition.equals(order.desiredCondition);
	                if (conditionMatches
	                        && listing.listPrice <= order.maxPrice
	                        && listing.listPrice < bestMatchPrice) {
	                    bestMatch = listing;
	                    bestMatchPrice = listing.listPrice;
	                }
	            }

	            if (bestMatch != null && balance >= bestMatch.listPrice) {
	                balance -= bestMatch.listPrice;
	                playSound(purchaseSound);

	                Image itemImg = getSkinImageFromName(bestMatch.item.name);
	                if (itemImg != null) bestMatch.item.image = new ImageIcon(itemImg);

	                inventoryList.add(bestMatch.item);
	                inventoryValue += bestMatch.item.price.doubleValue();
	                listings.remove(bestMatch);

	                recordSale(bestMatch.item.name, bestMatch.listPrice,
	                            bestMatch.item.condition, bestMatch.item.itemFloat);
	                updateBalanceLabel();
	                writeStats();
	                newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	                totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	                refreshMainUI();

	                order.filled++;
	                order.lastFillTime = now;
	                filledThisTick = true;

	                final double pricePaid = bestMatch.listPrice;
	                final String filledSkin = order.skinName;
	                final String filledCond = bestMatch.item.condition;
	                String fillMsg = order.isComplete()
	                    ? String.format("Buy order complete!\nReceived: %s\nPrice: $%.2f\nCondition: %s", bestMatch.item.name, pricePaid, filledCond)
	                    : String.format("Buy order partially filled (%d/%d)\nReceived: %s\nPrice: $%.2f", order.filled, order.quantity, bestMatch.item.name, pricePaid);
	                notifications.add(fillMsg);
	                if (order.isComplete() || order.filled == 1) {
	                    SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() ->
	                        showBuyOrderFillNotification(filledSkin, filledCond, pricePaid));
	                }

	                if (!achievements.get("buy_order_filled").isUnlocked) {
	                    unlockAchievement("buy_order_filled");
	                }
	                if (order.isComplete()) toRemove.add(order);
	            }
	        }

	        if (!filledThisTick && !order.isComplete()) {
	            double marketPrice = getLowestListingPrice(lookupKey, order.desiredCondition);
	            if (marketPrice > 0) {

	                double gap = Math.max(0, Math.min(1,
	                    (marketPrice - order.maxPrice) / marketPrice));

	                String cleanForRarity = normalizeSkinName(order.skinName)
	                                            .replace("StatTrak ", "")
	                                            .replace("StatTrak ", "");
	                String rarity = getSkinRarity(cleanForRarity);

	                long baseDelay;
	                switch (rarity) {
	                    case "Milspec":    baseDelay = 15_000;  break;
	                    case "Restricted": baseDelay = 25_000;  break;
	                    case "Classified": baseDelay = 45_000;  break;
	                    case "Covert":     baseDelay = 90_000;  break;
	                    case "Knife":
	                    case "Gloves":     baseDelay = 150_000; break;
	                    default:           baseDelay = 30_000;  break;
	                }

	                long fillDelay = (long)(baseDelay * (1.0 + gap * 8.0));

	                if ((now - order.lastFillTime) >= fillDelay && balance >= order.maxPrice) {

	                    double pricePaid = order.maxPrice;
	                    balance -= pricePaid;
	                    order.filled++;
	                    order.lastFillTime = now;

	                    InventoryItem syntheticItem = buildSyntheticItemForBuyOrder(
	                            order.skinName, order.desiredCondition, pricePaid, lookupKey);
	                    if (syntheticItem != null) {
	                        inventoryList.add(syntheticItem);
	                        inventoryValue += syntheticItem.price.doubleValue();
	                    }

	                    String fillCond = order.desiredCondition.equals("Any")
	                                      ? "Field-Tested" : order.desiredCondition;
	                    recordSale(order.skinName, pricePaid, fillCond, 0.20);
	                    updateBalanceLabel();
	                    writeStats();
	                    newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	                    totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	                    refreshMainUI();

	                    final double fp = pricePaid;
	                    final String fs = order.skinName;
	                    final String fc = fillCond;
	                    String fillMsgB = order.isComplete()
	                        ? String.format("Buy order complete!\nReceived: %s\nPrice: $%.2f\nCondition: %s", order.skinName, fp, fc)
	                        : String.format("Buy order partially filled (%d/%d)\nReceived: %s\nPrice: $%.2f", order.filled, order.quantity, order.skinName, fp);
	                    notifications.add(fillMsgB);
	                    if (order.isComplete() || order.filled == 1) {
	                        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() ->
	                            showBuyOrderFillNotification(fs, fc, fp));
	                    }

	                    if (!achievements.get("buy_order_filled").isUnlocked) {
	                        unlockAchievement("buy_order_filled");
	                    }
	                    if (order.isComplete()) toRemove.add(order);
	                }
	            }
	        }
	    }

	    buyOrders.removeAll(toRemove);

	    if (!notifications.isEmpty()) {
