	        StringBuilder message = new StringBuilder("=== BUY ORDERS FILLED ===\n\n");
	        for (String notif : notifications) {
	            message.append(notif).append("\n\n");
	        }
	        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, message.toString(),
	                "Buy Orders Filled", JOptionPane.INFORMATION_MESSAGE);
	        });
	    }
	}
	
	private final Set<String> armourySkinNameCache = new HashSet<>();
	private boolean armouryCacheBuilt = false;
	private boolean isArmourySkin(String skinName) {
	    if (ARMOURY_COLLECTIONS == null) return false;
	    if (!armouryCacheBuilt) {
	        for (ArmouryCollection ac : ARMOURY_COLLECTIONS) {
	            String[][] allNames = {ac.covertNames, ac.classifiedNames, ac.restrictedNames,
	                                   ac.milspecNames, ac.industrialNames};
	            for (String[] tier : allNames) {
	                if (tier == null) continue;
	                for (String n : tier) armourySkinNameCache.add(n.toLowerCase());
	            }
	        }
	        armouryCacheBuilt = true;
	    }
	    String bare = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").trim().toLowerCase();
	    return armourySkinNameCache.contains(bare);
	}

		private void replenishThinMarketListings() {

	    for (MarketListing playerListing : activeListings) {
	        String cleanName = normalizeSkinName(playerListing.item.name);
	        String marketKey = playerListing.item.isStattrak
	                ? normalizeSkinName("StatTrak " + cleanName) : cleanName;
	        globalMarketListings.computeIfAbsent(marketKey, k -> new ArrayList<>());
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> bucket = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey);
	        boolean alreadyPresent = false;
	        for (MarketListing ml : bucket) {
	            if (ml == playerListing) { alreadyPresent = true; break; }
	        }
	        if (!alreadyPresent) bucket.add(playerListing);
	    }

	    for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> entry : globalMarketListings.entrySet()) {
	        String marketKey = entry.getKey();
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = entry.getValue();

	        boolean isStattrak = marketKey.startsWith("StatTrak ");
	        String bareName = marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();

	        double basePrice = getBasePrice(bareName);
	        if (basePrice <= 0) continue;

	        String rarity = getSkinRarity(bareName);
	        double marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarity, 1.0);
	        String[] availableConditions = getAvailableConditions(bareName);
	        boolean isGlove = rarity.equals("Gloves");
	        boolean isDopplerGem = bareName.contains("Sapphire") || bareName.contains("Ruby") || bareName.contains("Black Pearl");

	        
	        FloatRange repFr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(bareName);
	        if (repFr == null) {
	            for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e2 : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet()) {
	                if (bareName.startsWith(e2.getKey())) { repFr = e2.getValue(); break; }
	            }
	        }
	        double repFloatMin = (repFr != null && repFr.min != null) ? repFr.min : 0.0;
	        double repFloatMax = (repFr != null && repFr.max != null) ? repFr.max : 1.0;
	        if (isGlove) { repFloatMin = 0.06; repFloatMax = 0.80; }

	        Map<String, Double> repWearDist = new HashMap<>();
	        double repTotalRange = 0;
	        for (String c : availableConditions) {
	            double cMin, cMax;
	            if      (c.equals("Factory New"))    { cMin = Math.max(repFloatMin, 0.00); cMax = Math.min(repFloatMax, 0.07); }
	            else if (c.equals("Minimal Wear"))   { cMin = Math.max(repFloatMin, 0.07); cMax = Math.min(repFloatMax, 0.15); }
	            else if (c.equals("Field-Tested"))   { cMin = Math.max(repFloatMin, 0.15); cMax = Math.min(repFloatMax, 0.38); }
	            else if (c.equals("Well-Worn"))      { cMin = Math.max(repFloatMin, 0.38); cMax = Math.min(repFloatMax, 0.45); }
	            else                                 { cMin = Math.max(repFloatMin, 0.45); cMax = Math.min(repFloatMax, 1.00); }
	            double r = Math.max(0, cMax - cMin);
	            repWearDist.put(c, r);
	            repTotalRange += r;
	        }

	        int baseTarget;
	        switch (rarity) {
	            case "Knife":
	            case "Gloves":     baseTarget = 15; break;
	            case "Covert":     baseTarget = 35; break;
	            case "Classified": baseTarget = 55; break;
	            case "Restricted": baseTarget = 70; break;
	            default:           baseTarget = 95; break;
	        }

	        for (String condition : availableConditions) {

	            int npcForCondition = 0;
	            for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	                if (!ml.isPlayerListing && ml.item.condition.equals(condition)) npcForCondition++;
	            }

	            
	            
	            
	            double condRange = repTotalRange > 0 ? repWearDist.getOrDefault(condition, 0.0) : 0;
	            if (condRange == 0) continue;
	            double condPct = condRange / repTotalRange;
	            int repBaseListings;
	            switch (rarity) {
	                case "Knife":
	                case "Gloves":     repBaseListings = 90;  break;
	                case "Covert":     repBaseListings = 215; break;
	                case "Classified": repBaseListings = 320; break;
	                case "Restricted": repBaseListings = 425; break;
	                default:           repBaseListings = 580; break;
	            }
	            int rawTarget = (int)(repBaseListings * condPct);
	            int minPerCondition;
	            if (condRange < 0.02) {
	                
	                minPerCondition = Math.max(2, Math.min(rawTarget, 4));
	            } else if (condRange < 0.05) {
	                minPerCondition = Math.max(3, Math.min(rawTarget, 8));
	            } else {
	                minPerCondition = Math.max(5, rawTarget);
	            }

	            int deficit = minPerCondition - npcForCondition;
	            if (deficit <= 0) continue;
	            if (isDopplerGem && npcForCondition > 0) continue;

	            for (int i = 0; i < deficit; i++) {
	                double variance = 0.85 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.30);
	                double itemFloat = generateFloatForCondition(bareName, condition);
	                double listPrice;

	                if (isGlove) {
	                    double gloveBase = getGloveBasePrice(bareName);
	                    listPrice = calculateGlovePrice(bareName, condition, gloveBase) * marketMulti * variance;
	                    if (listPrice < gloveBase * 0.5)
	                        listPrice = calculateGlovePrice(bareName, condition, gloveBase) * marketMulti * 0.90;
	                } else {
	                    listPrice = basePrice * marketMulti * variance;
	                    switch (condition) {
	                        case "Factory New":    listPrice *= 2.5;  break;
	                        case "Minimal Wear":   listPrice *= 1.7;  break;
	                        case "Field-Tested":   listPrice *= 1.0;  break;
	                        case "Well-Worn":      listPrice *= 0.7;  break;
	                        case "Battle-Scarred": listPrice *= 0.3;  break;
	                    }
	                    if (rarity.equals("Knife") && !isDopplerGem) {
	                        boolean appliedFnSc = false;
	                        if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	                            FloatRange scFr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(bareName);
	                            double scMin = (scFr != null && scFr.min != null) ? scFr.min : 0.0;
	                            if (scMin >= 0.06) { listPrice *= 2.87; appliedFnSc = true; }
	                        }
	                        if (!appliedFnSc) {
	                            double rel = getRelativeFloat(bareName, itemFloat);
	                            if (!isCappedKnife(bareName)) {
	                                if (rel <= 0.01) listPrice *= 2.5;
	                                else if (rel <= 0.05) listPrice *= 1.5;
	                                else if (rel <= 0.20) listPrice *= 1.1;
	                            } else {
	                                if (rel <= 0.01) listPrice *= 1.15;
	                                else if (rel <= 0.05) listPrice *= 1.05;
	                            }
	                        }
	                    }
	                    if (isStattrak) {
	                        boolean isCW5 = bareName.contains("Crimson Web");
	                        boolean isD5  = bareName.contains("Doppler");
	                        if (isCW5)                            listPrice *= 2.0;
	                        else if (isD5)                        listPrice *= 0.80;
	                        else if (rarity.equals("Knife"))      listPrice *= 0.90;
	                        else                                  listPrice *= 1.70 + random.nextDouble() * 0.30;
	                    }
	                    double priceFloor = basePrice * marketMulti * 0.15;
	                    if (listPrice < priceFloor) listPrice = priceFloor;
	                }

	                int sellTime = 30 + random.nextInt(150);
	                double trueBase = listPrice / marketMulti;
	                String displayRarity = isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + rarity : rarity;
	                Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(bareName);

	                InventoryItem dummy = new InventoryItem(
	                    skinImg != null ? new ImageIcon(skinImg) : null,
	                    bareName, condition, displayRarity,
	                    BigDecimal.valueOf(listPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                    itemFloat, isStattrak, random.nextInt(1000), null, trueBase
	                );
	                listings.add(new MarketListing(dummy, listPrice, sellTime, false));
	            }
	        }
	    }
	}

	private double getLowestListingPrice(String lookupKey, String desiredCondition) {
	    ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(lookupKey);
	    if (listings == null) listings = globalMarketListings.get(lookupKey.replace("StatTrak ", ""));
	    if (listings == null) return 0;
	    double lowest = Double.MAX_VALUE;
	    for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	        if (ml.isPlayerListing) continue;
	        boolean condMatch = desiredCondition.equals("Any") ||
	                            ml.item.condition.equals(desiredCondition);
	        if (condMatch && ml.listPrice < lowest) lowest = ml.listPrice;
	    }
	    return lowest == Double.MAX_VALUE ? 0 : lowest;
	}
	
	private InventoryItem buildSyntheticItemForBuyOrder(
	        String skinName, String desiredCondition, double pricePaid, String lookupKey) {
	    ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(lookupKey);
	    if (listings == null) listings = globalMarketListings.get(lookupKey.replace("StatTrak ", ""));

	    String condition = desiredCondition.equals("Any") ? "Field-Tested" : desiredCondition;

	    if (listings != null) {
	        MarketListing template = null;
	        double bestPrice = Double.MAX_VALUE;
	        for (MarketListing ml : listings) {
	            if (!ml.isPlayerListing && ml.item.condition.equals(condition)
	                    && ml.listPrice < bestPrice) {
	                template = ml;
	                bestPrice = ml.listPrice;
	            }
	        }
	        if (template != null) {
	            return new InventoryItem(
	                template.item.image,
	                template.item.name,
	                template.item.condition,
	                template.item.rarity,
	                BigDecimal.valueOf(pricePaid).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                template.item.itemFloat,
	                template.item.isStattrak,
	                template.item.patternID,
	                template.item.blueGemTier,
	                pricePaid
	            );
	        }
	    }

	    boolean isStattrak = skinName.startsWith("StatTrak ");
	    String bareName = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();
	    double fallbackFloat = generateFloatForCondition(bareName, condition);
	    String rarity = getSkinRarity(bareName);
	    String displayRarity = isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + rarity : rarity;
	    Image img = getSkinImageFromName(skinName);
	    return new InventoryItem(
	        img != null ? new ImageIcon(img) : null,
	        skinName, condition, displayRarity,
	        BigDecimal.valueOf(pricePaid).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	        fallbackFloat, isStattrak, random.nextInt(1000), null, pricePaid
	    );
	}
	
	private JPanel createMyListingsPanel() {
	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 2, 10, 10));
	    grid.setBackground(Color.DARK_GRAY);
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    
	    for (MarketListing listing : activeListings) {
	        JPanel card = createMyListingCard(listing);
	        grid.add(card);
	    }
	    
	    if (activeListings.isEmpty()) {
	        JLabel emptyLabel = new JLabel("No active listings", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        emptyLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 24));
	        panel.add(emptyLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    } else {
	        panel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    }
	    
	    return panel;
	}
	
	private JPanel createMainMarketPanel(String marketFilter) {
	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());

	    JPanel filterPanel = new JPanel();
	    filterPanel.setLayout(new BoxLayout(filterPanel, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    filterPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    filterPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));

	    JPanel filterRow1 = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 6, 2));
	    filterRow1.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    JPanel filterRow2 = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 6, 2));
	    filterRow2.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));

	    JComboBox<String> searchField = createSearchFieldWithHistory();
	    
	    JComboBox<String> rarityFilter = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{
	    	    "All", "Knife", "Gloves", "Covert", "Classified", "Restricted", "Milspec", "Industrial"
	    });
	    styleComboBox(rarityFilter);

	    JButton refreshButton = new JButton("Refresh Market");
	    refreshButton.setBackground(new Color(70, 130, 180));
	    refreshButton.setForeground(Color.BLACK);
	    refreshButton.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    
	    refreshButton.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override
	        public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) {
	            playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
	        }
	    });
	    
	    JLabel searchLabel = new JLabel("Search:");
	    searchLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    searchLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));

	    JLabel rarityLabel = new JLabel("Rarity:");
	    rarityLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    rarityLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));

	    JLabel stLabel = new JLabel("StatTrak:");
	    stLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    stLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    JComboBox<String> stattrakFilter = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{"All", "StatTrak Only", "Non-StatTrak"});
	    styleComboBox(stattrakFilter);

	    JLabel priceSortLabel = new JLabel("Sort:");
	    priceSortLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    priceSortLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    JComboBox<String> priceSortFilter = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{"Default", "Lowest Price", "Highest Price"});
	    styleComboBox(priceSortFilter);

	    filterRow1.add(searchLabel);
	    filterRow1.add(searchField);
	    filterRow1.add(rarityLabel);
	    filterRow1.add(rarityFilter);
	    filterRow1.add(stLabel);
	    filterRow1.add(stattrakFilter);
	    filterRow2.add(priceSortLabel);
	    filterRow2.add(priceSortFilter);

	    // Collection filter - shown for regular and armoury tabs
	    if ("armoury".equals(marketFilter) || "regular".equals(marketFilter)) {
	        JLabel collectionLabel2 = new JLabel("Collection:");
	        collectionLabel2.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	        collectionLabel2.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
	        java.util.List<String> colNames = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	        colNames.add("All");
	        if ("armoury".equals(marketFilter)) {
	            for (ArmouryCollection ac : ARMOURY_COLLECTIONS) colNames.add(ac.name);
	        } else {
	            for (TradeUpCollection tc : TRADE_UP_COLLECTIONS) colNames.add(tc.collectionName);
	        }
	        JComboBox<String> collectionFilter = new JComboBox<>(colNames.toArray(new String[0]));
	        styleComboBox(collectionFilter);
	        filterRow2.add(collectionLabel2);
	        filterRow2.add(collectionFilter);
	        filterPanel.putClientProperty("collectionFilter", collectionFilter);
	    }

	    filterRow2.add(refreshButton);
	    filterPanel.add(filterRow1);
	    filterPanel.add(filterRow2);

	    panel.add(filterPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 2, 10, 10));
	    grid.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));

	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    scroll.setBorder(null);
	    panel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JPanel statusPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));
	    statusPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    JLabel statusLabel = new JLabel("Loading...");
	    statusLabel.setForeground(Color.CYAN);
	    statusPanel.add(statusLabel);
	    panel.add(statusPanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    Runnable updateGrid = () -> {
	        grid.removeAll();
	        statusLabel.setText("Updating...");

	        String search = "";
	        Object selected = searchField.getSelectedItem();
	        if (selected != null) {
	            search = selected.toString().toLowerCase();
	        }
	        
	        Component editor = searchField.getEditor().getEditorComponent();
	        if (editor instanceof JTextField) {
	            String editorText = ((JTextField)editor).getText().toLowerCase();
	            if (!editorText.isEmpty()) {
	                search = editorText;
	            }
	        }
	        
	        String selectedRarity = (String) rarityFilter.getSelectedItem();
	        String selectedST = (String) stattrakFilter.getSelectedItem();
	        String selectedPriceSort = (String) priceSortFilter.getSelectedItem();

	        // Get collection filter if present (armoury tab only)
	        JComboBox<?> colFilterBox = (JComboBox<?>) filterPanel.getClientProperty("collectionFilter");
	        String selectedCollection = (colFilterBox != null) ? (String) colFilterBox.getSelectedItem() : "All";

	        // Build skin->collection lookup once per rebuild for collection filtering
	        java.util.Map<String, String> skinToCol = new java.util.HashMap<>();
	        if (!"All".equals(selectedCollection)) {
	            if ("armoury".equals(marketFilter)) {
	                for (ArmouryCollection ac : ARMOURY_COLLECTIONS) {
	                    String[][] allNames = {ac.covertNames, ac.classifiedNames, ac.restrictedNames,
	                                           ac.milspecNames, ac.industrialNames};
	                    for (String[] tier : allNames) {
	                        if (tier == null) continue;
	                        for (String n : tier) skinToCol.put(n.toLowerCase(), ac.name);
	                    }
	                }
	            } else if ("regular".equals(marketFilter)) {
	                for (TradeUpCollection tc : TRADE_UP_COLLECTIONS) {
	                    for (String[] tier : new String[][]{tc.milspecSkins, tc.restrictedSkins,
	                                                        tc.classifiedSkins, tc.covertSkins}) {
	                        if (tier == null) continue;
	                        for (String n : tier) skinToCol.put(n.toLowerCase(), tc.collectionName);
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	        }

	        List<Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>>> entries =
	                new ArrayList<>(globalMarketListings.entrySet());

	        final String finalSearch = search;
	        entries.removeIf(entry -> {
	            String skinName = entry.getKey();
	            String cleanName = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();
	            String rar = getSkinRarity(cleanName);
	            boolean knife = rar.equals("Knife");
	            boolean glove = rar.equals("Gloves");
	            boolean armoury = isArmourySkin(cleanName);
	            if ("knives".equals(marketFilter) && !knife) return true;
	            if ("gloves".equals(marketFilter) && !glove) return true;
	            if ("regular".equals(marketFilter) && (knife || glove || armoury)) return true;
	            if ("armoury".equals(marketFilter) && !armoury) return true;
	            if (!finalSearch.isEmpty() && !skinName.toLowerCase().contains(finalSearch)) return true;
	            if (!selectedRarity.equals("All") && !rar.equals(selectedRarity)) return true;
	            boolean isStatTrak = skinName.startsWith("StatTrak");
	            if ("StatTrak Only".equals(selectedST) && !isStatTrak) return true;
	            if ("Non-StatTrak".equals(selectedST) && isStatTrak) return true;
	            if (!"All".equals(selectedCollection) && !selectedCollection.equals(
	                    skinToCol.get(cleanName.toLowerCase()))) return true;
	            return entry.getValue().isEmpty();
	        });

	        if ("Lowest Price".equals(selectedPriceSort)) {
	            entries.sort((a, b) -> {
	                double pA = a.getValue().stream().mapToDouble(l -> l.listPrice).min().orElse(0);
	                double pB = b.getValue().stream().mapToDouble(l -> l.listPrice).min().orElse(0);
	                return Double.compare(pA, pB);
	            });
	        } else if ("Highest Price".equals(selectedPriceSort)) {
	            entries.sort((a, b) -> {
	                double pA = a.getValue().stream().mapToDouble(l -> l.listPrice).max().orElse(0);
	                double pB = b.getValue().stream().mapToDouble(l -> l.listPrice).max().orElse(0);
	                return Double.compare(pB, pA);
	            });
	        } else {
	        entries.sort((a, b) -> {
	            String nameA = cleanStatTrakEncoding(a.getKey());
	            String nameB = cleanStatTrakEncoding(b.getKey());

	            boolean isStatTrakA = nameA.contains("StatTrak");
	            boolean isStatTrakB = nameB.contains("StatTrak");

	            String cleanNameA = nameA.replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();
	            String cleanNameB = nameB.replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();

	            String rarityA = getSkinRarity(cleanNameA);
	            String rarityB = getSkinRarity(cleanNameB);

	            int rarityCompare = Integer.compare(
	                    RARITY_ORDER.getOrDefault(rarityA, 999),
	                    RARITY_ORDER.getOrDefault(rarityB, 999)
	            );
	            if (rarityCompare != 0) return rarityCompare;
	            
	            String weaponTypeA = extractWeaponType(cleanNameA);
	            String weaponTypeB = extractWeaponType(cleanNameB);

	            int weaponCompare = weaponTypeA.compareTo(weaponTypeB);
	            if (weaponCompare != 0) return weaponCompare;

	            boolean isDopplerA = cleanNameA.contains("Doppler");
	            boolean isDopplerB = cleanNameB.contains("Doppler");

	            if (isDopplerA && isDopplerB) {
	                int orderA = getDopplerOrder(cleanNameA);
	                int orderB = getDopplerOrder(cleanNameB);

	                if (orderA != orderB) {
	                    return Integer.compare(orderA, orderB);
	                }
	            }

	            int skinCompare = cleanNameA.compareTo(cleanNameB);
	            if (skinCompare != 0) return skinCompare;

	            if (!isStatTrakA && isStatTrakB) return -1;
	            if (isStatTrakA && !isStatTrakB) return 1;

	            return 0;
	        });
	        } 

	        int count = 0;
	        for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> entry : entries) {
	            String skinName = entry.getKey();
	            ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = entry.getValue();

	            JPanel card = createMarketSkinCard(skinName, listings, null);
	            grid.add(card);
	            count++;
	        }

	        statusLabel.setText(String.format("Showing %d skins", count));
	        
	        grid.revalidate();
	        grid.repaint();
	    };

	    javax.swing.Timer searchTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(300, e -> updateGrid.run());
	    searchTimer.setRepeats(false);
	    
	    Component editorComponent = searchField.getEditor().getEditorComponent();
	    if (editorComponent instanceof JTextField) {
	        ((JTextField)editorComponent).addKeyListener(new KeyAdapter() {
	            public void keyReleased(KeyEvent e) {
	                String text = ((JTextField)searchField.getEditor().getEditorComponent()).getText();
	                if (!text.trim().isEmpty()) {
	                    addToSearchHistory(text);
	                }
	                searchTimer.restart();
	            }
	        });
	    }
	    
	    searchField.addActionListener(e -> {
	        Object selected = searchField.getSelectedItem();
	        if (selected != null) {
	            addToSearchHistory(selected.toString());
	        }
	        updateGrid.run();
	    });

	    rarityFilter.addActionListener(e -> updateGrid.run());
	    stattrakFilter.addActionListener(e -> updateGrid.run());
	    priceSortFilter.addActionListener(e -> updateGrid.run());
	    // Wire collection filter listener if present
	    JComboBox<?> colFB = (JComboBox<?>) filterPanel.getClientProperty("collectionFilter");
	    if (colFB != null) colFB.addActionListener(e -> updateGrid.run());
	    refreshButton.addActionListener(e -> {
	        replenishThinMarketListings();
	        updateGrid.run();
	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Market refreshed!", "Success",
	                JOptionPane.INFORMATION_MESSAGE);
	    });

	    SwingUtilities.invokeLater(updateGrid);
	    
	    return panel;
	}
	
	private int getDopplerOrder(String skinName) {
	    if (skinName.contains("Phase 1")) return 1;
	    if (skinName.contains("Phase 2")) return 2;
	    if (skinName.contains("Phase 3")) return 3;
	    if (skinName.contains("Phase 4")) return 4;
	    if (skinName.contains("Black Pearl")) return 5;
	    if (skinName.contains("Ruby")) return 6;
	    if (skinName.contains("Sapphire")) return 7;
	    return 0;
	}
	
	private String extractWeaponType(String skinName) {
	    skinName = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "")
	                .replace("StatTrak ", "")
	                .replace("* StatTrak ", "");
	  
	    if (skinName.contains("Bloodhound Gloves")) return "Bloodhound Gloves";
	    if (skinName.contains("Driver Gloves")) return "Driver Gloves";
	    if (skinName.contains("Hand Wraps")) return "Hand Wraps";
	    if (skinName.contains("Moto Gloves")) return "Moto Gloves";
	    if (skinName.contains("Specialist Gloves")) return "Specialist Gloves";
	    if (skinName.contains("Sport Gloves")) return "Sport Gloves";
	    
	    if (skinName.contains("|")) {
	        String weaponType = skinName.split("\\|")[0].trim();
	        return weaponType;
	    }
	    
	    if (skinName.contains("Karambit")) return "Karambit";
	    if (skinName.contains("M9 Bayonet")) return "M9 Bayonet";
	    if (skinName.contains("Bayonet")) return "Bayonet";
	    if (skinName.contains("Butterfly Knife")) return "Butterfly Knife";
	    if (skinName.contains("Flip Knife")) return "Flip Knife";
	    if (skinName.contains("Gut Knife")) return "Gut Knife";
	    
	    return skinName;
	}
	
	private JPanel createMarketSkinCard(String skinName, ArrayList<MarketListing> listings, JFrame parent) {
	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    card.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 40));

	    String normalizedName = skinName;
	    boolean isStatTrak = normalizedName.startsWith("StatTrak ");
	    String baseName = normalizedName.replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();
	    String rarity = getSkinRarity(baseName);
	    boolean isKnife = rarity.equals("Knife");

	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(getRarityColor(rarity), 2));
	    card.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(220, 165));
	    card.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(220, 165));

	    String displayName = isStatTrak ? "ST " + baseName : baseName;

	    Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(baseName);
	    JLabel imgLabel;
	    if (skinImg != null) {
	        Image scaled = skinImg.getScaledInstance(110, 75, Image.SCALE_FAST);
	        imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	    } else {
	        imgLabel = new JLabel("?", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        imgLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    }
	    imgLabel.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    imgLabel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(110, 75));

	    JLabel name = new JLabel(displayName, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    name.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));
	    if (isStatTrak) name.setForeground(new Color(255, 153, 51));
	    else if (isKnife) name.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
	    else name.setForeground(Color.WHITE);

	    java.util.List<Double> allPrices = listings.stream()
	        .map(l -> l.listPrice).sorted().collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.toList());
	    double medianPrice = allPrices.isEmpty() ? 0.0 : allPrices.get(allPrices.size() / 2);
	    JLabel price = new JLabel("Average: $" + String.format("%.2f", medianPrice), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    price.setForeground(Color.YELLOW); price.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));

	    String countText;
	    if (baseName.contains("Case Hardened")) {
	        Integer bgc = globalBlueGemCounts.get(normalizedName);
	        countText = listings.size() + " listings" + (bgc!=null&&bgc>0?" ("+bgc+" BG)":"");
	    } else {
	        countText = listings.size() + " listings";
	    }
	    JLabel count = new JLabel(countText, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    count.setForeground(new Color(95, 200, 255)); count.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9));

	    JLabel rarityLbl = new JLabel(rarity, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    rarityLbl.setForeground(getRarityColor(rarity)); rarityLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9));

	    String colName = getCollectionName(baseName);
	    JLabel colLbl = new JLabel(colName != null ? colName : "", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    colLbl.setForeground(new Color(170, 130, 255)); colLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.ITALIC, 8));

	    JPanel text = new JPanel(new GridLayout(5, 1, 0, 0));
	    text.setBackground(new Color(22, 22, 30));
	    text.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(2, 2, 2, 2));
	    text.add(name); text.add(rarityLbl); text.add(price); text.add(count); text.add(colLbl);

	    card.add(imgLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    card.add(text, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    card.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        public void mouseClicked(MouseEvent e) { showDetailedListings(normalizedName, listings, parent); }
	        public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) {
	            card.setCursor(new Cursor(Cursor.HAND_CURSOR));
	            card.setBackground(new Color(40, 40, 55));
	            card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(95, 200, 255), 3));
	        }
	        public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e) {
	            card.setCursor(new Cursor(Cursor.DEFAULT_CURSOR));
	            card.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 40));
	            card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(getRarityColor(rarity), 2));
	        }
	    });
	    return card;
	}

	private void showDetailedListings(String skinName, ArrayList<MarketListing> listings, JFrame parent) {
		
		String normalizedName = normalizeSkinName(skinName);
		String marketKey = skinName;
		boolean isStatTrak = marketKey.startsWith("StatTrak ");
		String baseName = marketKey.replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();
	    
	    String rarity = getSkinRarity(baseName);
	    
	    String displayName;
	    if (isStatTrak) {
	        displayName = "StatTrak " + baseName;
	    } else {
	        displayName = baseName;
	    }
	    
	    JFrame detailFrame = new JFrame(displayName + " - Market Listings");
	    detailFrame.setSize(900, 700);
	    detailFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(parent);
	    detailFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    detailFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(true);
	    
	    JPanel topPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    topPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    topPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    JLabel titleLabel = new JLabel("<html><div style='text-align:center;'>" + 
	                                   displayName + "</div></html>", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    titleLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 20));
	    titleLabel.setForeground(getRarityColor(rarity));
	    topPanel.add(titleLabel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    double lowestPrice = listings.stream().mapToDouble(l -> l.listPrice).min().orElse(0);
	    double highestPrice = listings.stream().mapToDouble(l -> l.listPrice).max().orElse(0);
	    double avgFloat = listings.stream().mapToDouble(l -> l.item.itemFloat).average().orElse(0);
	    
	    JLabel statsLabel = new JLabel(String.format(
	        "Price Range: $%.2f - $%.2f | Avg Float: %.6f | %d Listings", 
	        lowestPrice, highestPrice, avgFloat, listings.size()), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    statsLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 14));
	    statsLabel.setForeground(Color.CYAN);
	    topPanel.add(statsLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    String[] availableConditions = getAvailableConditions(baseName);
	    JLabel condLabel = new JLabel("Available: " + String.join(", ", availableConditions), 
	                                  SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    condLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	    topPanel.add(condLabel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    
	    detailFrame.add(topPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JTabbedPane tabbedPane = new JTabbedPane();
	    
	    Map<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> byCondition = new HashMap<>();
	    for (MarketListing listing : listings) {
	        byCondition.computeIfAbsent(listing.item.condition, k -> new ArrayList<>()).add(listing);
	    }
	    
	    for (String condition : availableConditions) {
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> condListings = byCondition.getOrDefault(condition, new ArrayList<>());
	        JPanel condPanel = createConditionPanel(condListings, condition, normalizedName, detailFrame);
	        String tabTitle = String.format("%s (%d)", condition, condListings.size());
	        tabbedPane.addTab(tabTitle, condPanel);
	    }
	    
	    if (baseName.contains("Case Hardened")) {
	        JPanel blueGemPanel = createBlueGemPanel(normalizedName, detailFrame);
	        tabbedPane.addTab("Blue Gems", blueGemPanel);
	    }
	    
	    detailFrame.add(tabbedPane, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    JPanel bottomPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout());
	    bottomPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    
	    JButton buyOrderBtn = new JButton("Create Buy Order");
	    buyOrderBtn.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	    buyOrderBtn.setBackground(new Color(70, 130, 180));
	    buyOrderBtn.setForeground(Color.BLACK);
	    buyOrderBtn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override
	        public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) {
	            playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
	        }
	    });
	    buyOrderBtn.addActionListener(e -> createBuyOrder(normalizedName, detailFrame));
	    bottomPanel.add(buyOrderBtn);
	    
	    JButton refreshBtn = new JButton("Refresh Listings");
	    refreshBtn.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	    refreshBtn.setBackground(new Color(100, 150, 100));
	    refreshBtn.setForeground(Color.BLACK);
	    refreshBtn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override
	        public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) {
	            playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
	        }
	    });
	    refreshBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	        detailFrame.dispose();
	        showDetailedListings(
	        	    marketKey,
	        	    globalMarketListings.get(marketKey),
	        	    parent
	        	);
	    });
	    bottomPanel.add(refreshBtn);
	    
	    detailFrame.add(bottomPanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    detailFrame.setVisible(true);
	    
	    javax.swing.Timer timer = new javax.swing.Timer(100, e -> {
	        detailFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(false);
	        detailFrame.toFront();
	        detailFrame.requestFocus();
	    });
	    timer.setRepeats(false);
	    timer.start();
	}
	
	private JPanel createBlueGemPanel(String skinName, JFrame parent) {
	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    JPanel filterPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));
	    JComboBox<String> tierFilter = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{"All Tiers", "T1", "T2", "T3", "T4"});
	    styleComboBox(tierFilter);
	    filterPanel.add(new JLabel("Filter by Tier:"));
	    filterPanel.add(tierFilter);
	    panel.add(filterPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 1, 5, 5));
	    grid.setBackground(Color.DARK_GRAY);
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    panel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    boolean isStatTrak = skinName.startsWith("StatTrak") || 
	                        skinName.startsWith("StatTrak ") ||
	                        skinName.contains("StatTrak");
	    
	    String cleanSkinName = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "")
	                                   .replace("StatTrak ", "")
	                                   .trim();
	    
	    Map<String, List<Integer>> patterns = null;
	    if (cleanSkinName.contains("Flip Knife")) {
	        patterns = FLIP_KNIFE_BG;
	    } else if (cleanSkinName.contains("M9 Bayonet")) {
	        patterns = M9_BG;
	    } else if (cleanSkinName.contains("AK-47")) {
	        patterns = AK_BG;
	    } else if (cleanSkinName.contains("Butterfly Knife")) {
	        patterns = BUTTERFLY_BG;
	    }
	    
	    if (patterns == null) {
	        JLabel noGems = new JLabel("No Blue Gem patterns available", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        noGems.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 18));
	        grid.add(noGems);
	        return panel;
	    }
	    
	    String rarity = getSkinRarity(cleanSkinName);
	    boolean isKnife = rarity.equals("Knife");
	    
	    final ArrayList<JPanel> allCards = new ArrayList<>();
	    
	    for (Map.Entry<String, List<Integer>> entry : patterns.entrySet()) {
	        String tier = entry.getKey();
	        List<Integer> patternIds = entry.getValue();
	        int numToShow = Math.min(5, patternIds.size());
	        
	        for (int i = 0; i < numToShow; i++) {
	            int patternId = patternIds.get(random.nextInt(patternIds.size()));
	            
	            double itemFloat = 0.01 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.30);
	            String condition;
	            
	            if (itemFloat <= 0.07) {
	                condition = "Factory New";
	            } else if (itemFloat <= 0.15) {
	                condition = "Minimal Wear";
	            } else if (itemFloat <= 0.38) {
	                condition = "Field-Tested";
	            } else {
	                condition = "Well-Worn";
	            }
	            
	            double basePrice = getBasePrice(cleanSkinName);
	            
	            if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	                basePrice *= 2.5;
	            } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	                basePrice *= 1.7;
	            } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	                basePrice *= 1.0;
	            } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	                basePrice *= 0.7;
	            }
	           
	            String blueGemTier = "Blue Gem " + tier;
	            double price = applyBlueGemMultiplier(cleanSkinName, patternId, blueGemTier, basePrice);
	           
	            if (isStatTrak) {
	                if (isKnife) {
	                    price *= 1.15;
	                } else {
	                    price *= 3.0;
	                }
	            }
	            
	            JPanel card = createBlueGemCard(skinName, patternId, tier, condition, itemFloat, price, parent);
	            
	            card.putClientProperty("tier", tier);
	            allCards.add(card);
	        }
	    }
	    
	    Runnable updateGrid = () -> {
	        grid.removeAll();
	        String selectedTier = (String) tierFilter.getSelectedItem();
	        
	        for (JPanel card : allCards) {
	            String cardTier = (String) card.getClientProperty("tier");
	            if (selectedTier.equals("All Tiers") || cardTier.equals(selectedTier)) {
	                grid.add(card);
	            }
	        }
	        
	        grid.revalidate();
	        grid.repaint();
	    };
	    
	    tierFilter.addActionListener(e -> updateGrid.run());
	    updateGrid.run();
	    
	    return panel;
	}
	
	private JPanel createBlueGemCard(String skinName, int patternId, String tier, String condition, double itemFloat, double price, JFrame parent) {
	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    card.setBackground(Color.GRAY);
	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(Color.CYAN, 3));
	    card.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(800, 100));

	    boolean isStatTrak = skinName.startsWith("StatTrak");
	    String cleanSkinName = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	    
	    Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(cleanSkinName);
	    if (skinImg != null) {
	        Image scaled = skinImg.getScaledInstance(130, 88, Image.SCALE_FAST);
	        JLabel imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	        card.add(imgLabel, BorderLayout.WEST);
	    }
	    
	    JPanel info = new JPanel(new GridLayout(4, 1));
	    info.setBackground(Color.GRAY);
	    
	    String displayName = (isStatTrak ? "StatTrak " : "") + cleanSkinName + " (Blue Gem " + tier + ")";
	    JLabel nameLabel = new JLabel(displayName);
	    nameLabel.setForeground(isStatTrak ? new Color(255, 153, 51) : Color.CYAN);
	    nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));

	    JLabel patternLabel = new JLabel("Pattern: #" + patternId);
	    patternLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);

	    JLabel condLabel = new JLabel(condition + " | Float: " + String.format("%.6f", itemFloat));
	    condLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);

	    JLabel priceLabel = new JLabel("$" + String.format("%.2f", price));
	    priceLabel.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
	    priceLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));

	    info.add(nameLabel);
	    info.add(patternLabel);
	    info.add(condLabel);
	    info.add(priceLabel);

	    card.add(info, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        
	    JButton buyBtn = new JButton("BUY");
	    buyBtn.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(100, 80));
	    buyBtn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override
	        public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) {
	            playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
	        }
	    });
	    buyBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	        if (balance < price) {
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(parent, "Insufficient funds!");
	            return;
	        }

	        int confirm = JOptionPane.showConfirmDialog(parent,
	        String.format("Buy %s\nBlue Gem %s\nPattern: #%d\nCondition: %s\nFloat: %.10f\nPrice: $%.2f?",
	        displayName, tier, patternId, condition, itemFloat, price),
	        "Confirm Purchase", JOptionPane.YES_NO_OPTION);

	        if (confirm == JOptionPane.YES_OPTION) {
	            balance -= price;

	            String rarity = getSkinRarity(cleanSkinName);
	            if (isStatTrak) {
	                rarity = "StatTrak " + rarity;
	            }
	            String blueGemTier = "Blue Gem " + tier;
	            String fullName = cleanSkinName + " (" + blueGemTier + ")";

	            double fixedBasePrice = price; 
	            
	            InventoryItem item = new InventoryItem(
	                skinImg != null ? new ImageIcon(skinImg) : null,
	                fullName,
	                condition,
	                rarity,
	                BigDecimal.valueOf(price).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	                itemFloat,
	                isStatTrak,
	                patternId,
	                blueGemTier,
	                fixedBasePrice
	            );
	            
	            inventoryList.add(item);
	            inventoryValue += price;

	            updateBalanceLabel();
	            writeStats();
	            newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	            totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	            refreshMainUI();

	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(parent, "Purchase successful!");

	            Window[] windows = Window.getWindows();
	            for (Window window : windows) {
	                if (window instanceof JFrame) {
	                    JFrame frame = (JFrame) window;
	                    if (frame.getTitle().contains("Market") || frame.getTitle().contains("Listings")) {
	                        frame.dispose();
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	        }
	    });

	    card.add(buyBtn, BorderLayout.EAST);

	    return card;
	}
	
	private JPanel createConditionPanel(ArrayList<MarketListing> listings, String condition, String skinName, JFrame parent) {
	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());

	    JPanel topBar = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    topBar.setBackground(new Color(45, 45, 50));
	    topBar.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 10, 8, 10));

	    JPanel sortPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 8, 0));
	    sortPanel.setBackground(new Color(45, 45, 50));
	    JLabel sortLabel = new JLabel("Sort by:");
	    sortLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    sortLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    sortPanel.add(sortLabel);
	    JComboBox<String> sortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{
	        "Lowest Price", "Highest Price", "Lowest Float", "Highest Float"
	    });
	    styleComboBox(sortBox);
	    sortPanel.add(sortBox);

	    JButton chartBtn = new JButton("📈 Price Chart");
	    chartBtn.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    chartBtn.setBackground(new Color(55, 80, 110));
	    chartBtn.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    chartBtn.setFocusPainted(false);
	    chartBtn.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(80, 120, 170), 1),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(3, 8, 3, 8)));
	    chartBtn.setCursor(new Cursor(Cursor.HAND_CURSOR));
	    chartBtn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) { playSoundFile("button_click.wav"); }
	        @Override public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) { chartBtn.setBackground(new Color(70, 100, 140)); }
	        @Override public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e)  { chartBtn.setBackground(new Color(55, 80, 110)); }
	    });
	    chartBtn.addActionListener(e -> showSkinPriceChart(skinName, condition, parent));
	    sortPanel.add(chartBtn);

	    topBar.add(sortPanel, BorderLayout.WEST);

	    JLabel statsLabel = new JLabel("", SwingConstants.RIGHT);
	    statsLabel.setForeground(Color.CYAN);
	    statsLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    statsLabel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(0, 0, 0, 4));
	    topBar.add(statsLabel, BorderLayout.EAST);

	    panel.add(topBar, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    if (listings.isEmpty()) {
	        JLabel emptyLabel = new JLabel("No " + condition + " listings available", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        emptyLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 18));
	        emptyLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	        panel.add(emptyLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        return panel;
	    }

	    ScrollablePanel listingsContainer = new ScrollablePanel();
	    listingsContainer.setLayout(new BoxLayout(listingsContainer, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    listingsContainer.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    listingsContainer.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 8, 8, 8));

	    JScrollPane listingsScroll = new JScrollPane(listingsContainer);
	    listingsScroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    listingsScroll.setHorizontalScrollBarPolicy(JScrollPane.HORIZONTAL_SCROLLBAR_NEVER);
	    listingsScroll.setBorder(null);
	    listingsScroll.getViewport().setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));

	    JPanel buyOrdersRight = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    buyOrdersRight.setBackground(new Color(28, 28, 33));

	    JLabel boHeader = new JLabel("  NPC Buy Orders", SwingConstants.LEFT);
	    boHeader.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	    boHeader.setForeground(new Color(100, 200, 255));
	    boHeader.setOpaque(true);
	    boHeader.setBackground(new Color(35, 50, 70));
	    boHeader.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 8, 8, 8));
	    buyOrdersRight.add(boHeader, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel boContainer = new JPanel();
	    boContainer.setLayout(new BoxLayout(boContainer, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    boContainer.setBackground(new Color(28, 28, 33));
	    boContainer.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(6, 6, 6, 6));

	    String normalizedKey = normalizeSkinName(skinName);
	    ArrayList<NpcBuyOrder> allOrders = npcBuyOrders.get(normalizedKey);
	    if (allOrders == null) {

	        allOrders = npcBuyOrders.get(normalizedKey.replace("StatTrak ", ""));
	    }

	    List<NpcBuyOrder> condOrders = new ArrayList<>();
	    if (allOrders != null) {
	        for (NpcBuyOrder o : allOrders) {
	            if (o.condition.equals(condition)) condOrders.add(o);
	        }
	        condOrders.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.price, a.price));
	    }

	    if (condOrders.isEmpty()) {
	        JLabel noneLabel = new JLabel("<html><center>No active buy orders<br>for " + condition + "</center></html>", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        noneLabel.setForeground(Color.GRAY);
	        noneLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	        noneLabel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(20, 8, 8, 8));
	        boContainer.add(noneLabel);
	    } else {
	        String normalizedForPlayer = normalizeSkinName(skinName);
	        List<BuyOrder> playerOrdersForSkin = new ArrayList<>();
	        for (BuyOrder pbo : buyOrders) {
	            if (!normalizeSkinName(pbo.skinName).equals(normalizedForPlayer)) continue;
	            if (!pbo.desiredCondition.equals("Any") && !pbo.desiredCondition.equals(condition)) continue;
	            playerOrdersForSkin.add(pbo);
	        }

	        boContainer.removeAll();
	        List<Object> combined = new ArrayList<>();
	        combined.addAll(condOrders);
	        combined.addAll(playerOrdersForSkin);
	        combined.sort((a, b) -> {
	            double pa = (a instanceof NpcBuyOrder) ? ((NpcBuyOrder)a).price : ((BuyOrder)a).maxPrice;
	            double pb = (b instanceof NpcBuyOrder) ? ((NpcBuyOrder)b).price : ((BuyOrder)b).maxPrice;
	            return Double.compare(pb, pa);
	        });

	        for (Object entry : combined) {
	            if (entry instanceof NpcBuyOrder) {
	                NpcBuyOrder o = (NpcBuyOrder) entry;
	                JPanel row = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	                row.setBackground(new Color(38, 44, 55));
	                row.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	                    BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 1, 0, new Color(55, 65, 80)),
	                    BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 10, 8, 10)
	                ));
	                row.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 60));
	                JLabel priceL = new JLabel(String.format("$%.2f", o.price));
	                priceL.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 15));
	                priceL.setForeground(new Color(100, 230, 100));
	                int remaining = o.quantity - o.filled;
	                String displayName = (o.buyerName != null && !o.buyerName.isEmpty()) ? o.buyerName : "NPC";
	                JLabel buyerL = new JLabel(displayName);
	                buyerL.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.ITALIC, 10));
	                buyerL.setForeground(new Color(140, 180, 220));
	                JLabel qtyL = new JLabel(remaining + " wanted");
	                qtyL.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	                qtyL.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	                JPanel left = new JPanel();
	                left.setLayout(new BoxLayout(left, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	                left.setOpaque(false);
	                left.add(priceL); left.add(buyerL); left.add(qtyL);
	                int pct = o.quantity > 0 ? (int)(100.0 * o.filled / o.quantity) : 0;
	                JProgressBar bar = new JProgressBar(0, 100);
	                bar.setValue(pct);
	                bar.setStringPainted(false);
	                bar.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(60, 8));
	                bar.setForeground(new Color(70, 160, 70));
	                bar.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	                bar.setBorder(null);
	                JLabel pctL = new JLabel(pct + "% filled");
	                pctL.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 10));
	                pctL.setForeground(Color.GRAY);
	                JPanel right = new JPanel();
	                right.setLayout(new BoxLayout(right, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	                right.setOpaque(false);
	                right.add(bar); right.add(pctL);
	                row.add(left, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	                row.add(right, BorderLayout.EAST);
	                boContainer.add(row);
	            } else {
	                BuyOrder pbo = (BuyOrder) entry;
	                JPanel pRow = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	                pRow.setBackground(new Color(35, 50, 35));
	                pRow.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	                    BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 1, 0, new Color(60, 90, 60)),
	                    BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 10, 8, 10)
	                ));
	                pRow.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 65));
	                JLabel pPriceL = new JLabel(String.format("$%.2f", pbo.maxPrice));
	                pPriceL.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 15));
	                pPriceL.setForeground(new Color(255, 200, 60));
	                JLabel pNameL = new JLabel("YOU  >>  " + pbo.filled + "/" + pbo.quantity + " filled");
	                pNameL.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.ITALIC, 10));
	                pNameL.setForeground(new Color(255, 220, 120));
	                JLabel pQtyL = new JLabel(pbo.remaining() + " remaining");
	                pQtyL.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	                pQtyL.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	                JPanel pLeft = new JPanel();
	                pLeft.setLayout(new BoxLayout(pLeft, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	                pLeft.setOpaque(false);
	                pLeft.add(pPriceL); pLeft.add(pNameL); pLeft.add(pQtyL);
	                pRow.add(pLeft, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	                boContainer.add(pRow);
	            }
	        }

	        int totalWanted = condOrders.stream().mapToInt(o -> o.quantity - o.filled).sum()
	            + playerOrdersForSkin.stream().mapToInt(BuyOrder::remaining).sum();
	        double bestPrice = combined.isEmpty() ? 0 :
	            (combined.get(0) instanceof NpcBuyOrder
	                ? ((NpcBuyOrder)combined.get(0)).price
	                : ((BuyOrder)combined.get(0)).maxPrice);
	        JLabel summaryL = new JLabel(String.format("<html><center>Best offer: <b>$%.2f</b><br>Total wanted: <b>%d</b></center></html>", bestPrice, totalWanted), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        summaryL.setForeground(new Color(180, 220, 255));
	        summaryL.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	        summaryL.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 4, 4, 4));
	        boContainer.add(summaryL);
	    }

	    JScrollPane boScroll = new JScrollPane(boContainer);
	    boScroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(12);
	    boScroll.setBorder(null);
	    boScroll.getViewport().setBackground(new Color(28, 28, 33));
	    buyOrdersRight.add(boScroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JSplitPane split = new JSplitPane(JSplitPane.HORIZONTAL_SPLIT, listingsScroll, buyOrdersRight);
	    split.setResizeWeight(0.72);
	    split.setDividerSize(4);
	    split.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    panel.add(split, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    Runnable updateListings = () -> {
	        listingsContainer.removeAll();

	        ArrayList<MarketListing> sortedListings = new ArrayList<>(listings);
	        String sortType = (String) sortBox.getSelectedItem();
	        switch (sortType) {
	            case "Lowest Price":  sortedListings.sort(Comparator.comparingDouble(l -> l.listPrice)); break;
	            case "Highest Price": sortedListings.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.listPrice, a.listPrice)); break;
	            case "Lowest Float":  sortedListings.sort(Comparator.comparingDouble(l -> l.item.itemFloat)); break;
	            case "Highest Float": sortedListings.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.item.itemFloat, a.item.itemFloat)); break;
	        }

	        double avgPrice = sortedListings.stream().mapToDouble(l -> l.listPrice).average().orElse(0);
	        double avgFloat = sortedListings.stream().mapToDouble(l -> l.item.itemFloat).average().orElse(0);
	        statsLabel.setText(String.format("Listings: %d | Avg $%.2f | Float: %.6f   ",
	            sortedListings.size(), avgPrice, avgFloat));

	        int maxVisible = 50;
	        int itemsToShow = Math.min(maxVisible, sortedListings.size());
	        for (int i = 0; i < itemsToShow; i++) {
	            JPanel listingCard = createOptimizedListingCard(sortedListings.get(i), parent);
	            listingsContainer.add(listingCard);
	            listingsContainer.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 4)));
	        }

	        if (sortedListings.size() > maxVisible) {
	            JButton loadMoreBtn = new JButton("Load More (" + (sortedListings.size() - maxVisible) + " remaining)");
	            loadMoreBtn.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 13));
	            loadMoreBtn.setBackground(new Color(70, 130, 180));
	            loadMoreBtn.setForeground(Color.BLACK);
	            loadMoreBtn.setAlignmentX(Component.CENTER_ALIGNMENT);
	            loadMoreBtn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	                @Override public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) { playSoundFile("button_click.wav"); }
	            });
	            loadMoreBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	                loadMoreBtn.setVisible(false);
	                for (int i = maxVisible; i < sortedListings.size(); i++) {
	                    JPanel card = createOptimizedListingCard(sortedListings.get(i), parent);
	                    listingsContainer.add(card, listingsContainer.getComponentCount() - 1);
	                    listingsContainer.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 4)), listingsContainer.getComponentCount() - 1);
	                }
	                listingsContainer.revalidate();
	                listingsContainer.repaint();
	            });
	            listingsContainer.add(loadMoreBtn);
	        }

	        listingsContainer.revalidate();
	        listingsContainer.repaint();
	    };

	    sortBox.addActionListener(e -> updateListings.run());
	    updateListings.run();

	    return panel;
	}
	
	private void showSkinPriceChart(String skinName, String condition, JFrame parent) {
	    String normalizedSkin = normalizeSkinName(skinName);
	    String historyKey     = normalizedSkin + ":" + condition;

	    String simListKey = "sim5y:listing:" + historyKey;
	    String simBoKey   = "sim5y:bo:"      + historyKey;

	    if (!skinConditionPriceHistory.containsKey(simListKey)) {

	        ArrayList<Double> liveList = skinConditionPriceHistory.get(historyKey);
	        double seedPrice;
	        if (liveList != null && !liveList.isEmpty()) {
	            seedPrice = liveList.get(liveList.size() - 1);
	        } else {
	            String cleanKey = normalizedSkin.replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();
	            String rarity   = getSkinRarity(cleanKey);
	            double multi    = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarity, 1.0);
	            boolean isGlove = rarity.equals("Gloves");
	            if (isGlove) {
	                seedPrice = calculateGlovePrice(cleanKey, condition, getGloveBasePrice(cleanKey)) * multi;
	            } else {
	                seedPrice = getBasePrice(cleanKey) * multi;
	                if      (condition.equals("Factory New"))    seedPrice *= 2.5;
	                else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear"))   seedPrice *= 1.7;
	                else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn"))      seedPrice *= 0.7;
	                else if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) seedPrice *= 0.3;
	            }
	            if (seedPrice <= 0.01) seedPrice = 10.0;
	        }

	        final int SIM_PTS = 43800;
	        ArrayList<Double> simListing = new ArrayList<>(SIM_PTS);
	        ArrayList<Double> simBo      = new ArrayList<>(SIM_PTS);

	        double price   = seedPrice * (0.6 + random.nextDouble() * 0.8);
	        double boPrice = price * (0.84 + random.nextDouble() * 0.08);
	        double trend   = 0.0;
	        int    trendLeft = 0;

	        for (int w = 0; w < 500; w++) {
	            if (trendLeft <= 0) { trend = (random.nextDouble() - 0.47) * 0.0004; trendLeft = 48 + random.nextInt(192); }
	            trendLeft--;
	            double wnoise = (random.nextDouble() - 0.5) * 0.006 * price;
	            double wrevert = (seedPrice - price) * 0.003;
	            price = Math.max(seedPrice * 0.12, price + wnoise + trend * price + wrevert);
	        }

	        double spikeMomentum = 0.0;
	        int    spikeLeft     = 0;

	        for (int i = 0; i < SIM_PTS; i++) {
	            if (trendLeft <= 0) {

	                trend     = (random.nextDouble() - 0.47) * 0.0004;
	                trendLeft = 48 + random.nextInt(192);
	            }
	            trendLeft--;

	            if (spikeLeft <= 0 && random.nextDouble() < 0.0008) {
	                int spikeLen   = 12 + random.nextInt(36);
	                double spikeDir  = random.nextDouble() < 0.45 ? -1 : 1;
	                double spikeMag  = 0.04 + random.nextDouble() * 0.10;

	                spikeMomentum = spikeDir * spikeMag * price / spikeLen;
	                spikeLeft     = spikeLen;
	            }

	            double spikeContrib = 0.0;
	            if (spikeLeft > 0) {
	                spikeContrib  = spikeMomentum;
	                spikeMomentum *= 0.88;
	                spikeLeft--;
	            }

	            double noise  = (random.nextDouble() - 0.5) * 0.006 * price;

	            double revert = (seedPrice - price) * 0.003;
	            price   = Math.max(seedPrice * 0.12, price + noise + spikeContrib + trend * price + revert);
	            double targetBo = price * (0.78 + random.nextDouble() * 0.13);
	            boPrice = boPrice * 0.90 + targetBo * 0.10;
	            boPrice = Math.min(boPrice, price * 0.97);
	            simListing.add(price);
	            simBo.add(boPrice);
	        }

	        skinConditionPriceHistory.put(simListKey, simListing);
	        buyOrderPriceHistory.put(simBoKey, simBo);
	    }

	    JFrame chartFrame = new JFrame(normalizedSkin + "  ·  " + condition + "  -  Price History");
	    chartFrame.setSize(940, 560);
	    chartFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(parent);
	    chartFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    chartFrame.getContentPane().setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 18));

	    String[] timeRangeLabels  = {"1 Hour", "24 Hours", "1 Week", "1 Month", "1 Year", "5 Years"};
	    int[]    simPointsPerRange = {  -1,      96,        168,     720,       8760,     43800};

	    String[][] xAxisLabels = {
	        {"55m", "40m", "25m", "10m", "Now"},
	        {"20h ago", "16h ago", "12h ago", "6h ago", "Now"},
	        {"Mon","Tue","Wed","Thu","Fri","Sat","Sun","Now"},
	        {"Wk1","Wk2","Wk3","Now"},
	        {"Jan","Apr","Jul","Oct","Now"},
	        {"2020","2021","2022","2023","2024","Now"}
	    };

	    final int[] selectedRangeIdx = {5};

	    JPanel topBar = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(12, 0));
	    topBar.setBackground(new Color(16, 16, 24));
	    topBar.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 1, 0, new Color(35, 38, 60)),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 16, 10, 16)));

	    JLabel titleLbl = new JLabel(normalizedSkin + "  ·  " + condition, SwingConstants.LEFT);
	    titleLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 14));
	    titleLbl.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    topBar.add(titleLbl, BorderLayout.WEST);

	    JComboBox<String> rangeBox = new JComboBox<>(timeRangeLabels);
	    rangeBox.setSelectedIndex(5);
	    rangeBox.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    rangeBox.setBackground(new Color(28, 32, 48));
	    rangeBox.setForeground(new Color(190, 200, 255));
	    rangeBox.setFocusable(false);
	    JPanel centerBar = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.CENTER, 0, 0));
	    centerBar.setOpaque(false);
	    centerBar.add(rangeBox);
	    topBar.add(centerBar, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JPanel legend = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.RIGHT, 18, 0));
	    legend.setOpaque(false);
	    JLabel listingLegend = new JLabel("━━  Listing Price");
	    listingLegend.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    listingLegend.setForeground(new Color(80, 155, 255));
	    JLabel boLegend = new JLabel("━━  Best Buy Order");
	    boLegend.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    boLegend.setForeground(new Color(70, 210, 110));
	    legend.add(listingLegend); legend.add(boLegend);
	    topBar.add(legend, BorderLayout.EAST);
	    chartFrame.add(topBar, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel statsBar = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.CENTER, 32, 7));
	    statsBar.setBackground(new Color(14, 14, 22));
	    statsBar.setBorder(BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(1, 0, 0, 0, new Color(32, 36, 58)));

	    JLabel highLbl    = new JLabel("High: -");
	    JLabel lowLbl     = new JLabel("Low:  -");
	    JLabel currentLbl = new JLabel("Current: -");
	    JLabel changeLbl  = new JLabel("Change: -");
	    for (JLabel l : new JLabel[]{highLbl, lowLbl, currentLbl, changeLbl}) {
	        l.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	        l.setForeground(new Color(150, 160, 200));
	        statsBar.add(l);
	    }
	    chartFrame.add(statsBar, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    JPanel chartPanel = new JPanel() {
	        @Override
	        protected void paintComponent(Graphics g) {
	            super.paintComponent(g);
	            Graphics2D g2 = (Graphics2D) g.create();
	            g2.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_ANTIALIASING,      RenderingHints.VALUE_ANTIALIAS_ON);
	            g2.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_TEXT_ANTIALIASING, RenderingHints.VALUE_TEXT_ANTIALIAS_ON);

	            int w = getWidth(), h = getHeight();
	            int ml = 72, mr = 18, mt = 22, mb = 44;
	            int gw = w - ml - mr, gh = h - mt - mb;
	            if (gw < 10 || gh < 10) { g2.dispose(); return; }

	            g2.setColor(new Color(10, 10, 16)); g2.fillRect(0, 0, w, h);
	            g2.setColor(new Color(16, 18, 28)); g2.fillRect(ml, mt, gw, gh);

	            int rangeIdx = selectedRangeIdx[0];
	            ArrayList<Double> listingData, boData;

	                ArrayList<Double> liveList = skinConditionPriceHistory.get(historyKey);
	                double currentLivePrice = (liveList != null && !liveList.isEmpty())
	                    ? liveList.get(liveList.size() - 1) : -1;

	            if (rangeIdx == 0) {

	                listingData = liveList;
	                boData      = buyOrderPriceHistory.get(historyKey);
	                if (listingData != null && listingData.size() > 30) {
	                    int from = listingData.size() - 30;
	                    listingData = new ArrayList<>(listingData.subList(from, listingData.size()));
	                    if (boData != null && boData.size() > 30)
	                        boData = new ArrayList<>(boData.subList(boData.size() - 30, boData.size()));
	                }
	            } else {

	                ArrayList<Double> fullL  = skinConditionPriceHistory.get(simListKey);
	                ArrayList<Double> fullBO = buyOrderPriceHistory.get(simBoKey);
	                int pts = simPointsPerRange[rangeIdx];
	                if (fullL != null && fullL.size() >= pts) {
	                    listingData = new ArrayList<>(fullL.subList(fullL.size() - pts, fullL.size()));
	                    boData = (fullBO != null && fullBO.size() >= pts)
	                        ? new ArrayList<>(fullBO.subList(fullBO.size() - pts, fullBO.size())) : null;
	                } else {
	                    listingData = fullL != null ? new ArrayList<>(fullL) : null;
	                    boData = fullBO != null ? new ArrayList<>(fullBO) : null;
	                }

	                if (listingData != null && listingData.size() >= 2 && currentLivePrice > 0) {
	                    int anchorLen = Math.min(200, listingData.size());
	                    int anchorStart = listingData.size() - anchorLen;
	                    double anchorFrom = listingData.get(anchorStart);
	                    for (int ai = anchorStart; ai < listingData.size(); ai++) {
	                        double t = (double)(ai - anchorStart) / (anchorLen - 1);
	                        double ease = t * t * (3 - 2 * t);
	                        listingData.set(ai, listingData.get(ai) * (1 - ease) + currentLivePrice * ease);
	                    }
	                    if (boData != null && boData.size() >= 2) {
	                        double boTarget = currentLivePrice * 0.88;
	                        int bLen = Math.min(200, boData.size());
	                        int bStart = boData.size() - bLen;
	                        for (int ai = bStart; ai < boData.size(); ai++) {
	                            double t = (double)(ai - bStart) / (bLen - 1);
	                            double ease = t * t * (3 - 2 * t);
	                            boData.set(ai, boData.get(ai) * (1 - ease) + boTarget * ease);
	                        }
	                    }
	                }
	            }

	            if (listingData == null || listingData.size() < 2) {
	                g2.setColor(new Color(90, 95, 130));
	                g2.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 13));
	                String msg = rangeIdx <= 1 ? "No live data yet - wait a few market cycles"
	                                          : "No simulated data available";
	                FontMetrics fm = g2.getFontMetrics(); 
	                g2.drawString(msg, ml + (gw - fm.stringWidth(msg))/2, mt + gh/2);
	                g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1.5f)); g2.setColor(new Color(40, 45, 70));
	                g2.drawRect(ml, mt, gw, gh);
	                g2.dispose(); return;
	            }

	            double minVal = Double.MAX_VALUE, maxVal = Double.MIN_VALUE;
	            for (double v : listingData) { if (v < minVal) minVal=v; if (v > maxVal) maxVal=v; }
	            if (boData != null) for (double v : boData) { if (v < minVal) minVal=v; if (v > maxVal) maxVal=v; }

	            double allHigh  = listingData.stream().mapToDouble(d->d).max().orElse(0);
	            double allLow   = listingData.stream().mapToDouble(d->d).min().orElse(0);
	            double current  = listingData.get(listingData.size() - 1);
	            double first    = listingData.get(0);
	            double changePct = first > 0 ? ((current - first) / first) * 100.0 : 0;

	            highLbl.setText(String.format("High: $%.2f", allHigh));
	            highLbl.setForeground(new Color(80, 220, 90));
	            lowLbl.setText(String.format("Low: $%.2f", allLow));
	            lowLbl.setForeground(new Color(220, 80, 80));
	            currentLbl.setText(String.format("Current: $%.2f", current));
	            currentLbl.setForeground(new Color(190, 200, 255));
	            changeLbl.setText(String.format("Change: %+.1f%%", changePct));
	            changeLbl.setForeground(changePct >= 0 ? new Color(80, 220, 90) : new Color(220, 80, 80));

	            double pad = Math.max(0.01, (maxVal - minVal) * 0.10);
	            minVal -= pad; maxVal += pad;
	            if (maxVal <= minVal) maxVal = minVal + 0.01;

	            int GRID = 5;
	            g2.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 10));
	            float[] dashArr = {4f, 5f};
	            for (int i = 0; i <= GRID; i++) {
	                double val = minVal + (maxVal - minVal) * (GRID - i) / (double) GRID;
	                int gy     = mt + (int)((double) i / GRID * gh);
	                g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1f, BasicStroke.CAP_BUTT, BasicStroke.JOIN_BEVEL, 0, dashArr, 0));
	                g2.setColor(new Color(30, 34, 54)); g2.drawLine(ml, gy, ml + gw, gy);
	                g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1f));
	                g2.setColor(new Color(110, 115, 155));
	                String yLbl = val >= 1000 ? String.format("$%.0f", val) : String.format("$%.2f", val);
	                FontMetrics yfm = g2.getFontMetrics();
	                g2.drawString(yLbl, ml - yfm.stringWidth(yLbl) - 4, gy + 4);
	            }

	            float[] athDash = {6f, 4f};
	            int gyHigh = mt + gh - (int)(((allHigh - minVal) / (maxVal - minVal)) * gh);
	            int gyLow  = mt + gh - (int)(((allLow  - minVal) / (maxVal - minVal)) * gh);
	            gyHigh = Math.max(mt, Math.min(mt + gh, gyHigh));
	            gyLow  = Math.max(mt, Math.min(mt + gh, gyLow));
	            g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1f, BasicStroke.CAP_BUTT, BasicStroke.JOIN_BEVEL, 0, athDash, 0));
	            g2.setColor(new Color(80, 220, 90, 90));  g2.drawLine(ml, gyHigh, ml + gw, gyHigh);
	            g2.setColor(new Color(220, 80, 80, 90));  g2.drawLine(ml, gyLow,  ml + gw, gyLow);

	            g2.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9));
	            g2.setColor(new Color(80, 220, 90, 160));
	            g2.drawString(String.format("ATH $%.0f", allHigh), ml + gw + 2, gyHigh + 4);
	            g2.setColor(new Color(220, 80, 80, 160));
	            g2.drawString(String.format("ATL $%.0f", allLow),  ml + gw + 2, gyLow  + 4);

	            String[] xLbls = xAxisLabels[rangeIdx];
	            g2.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 10));
	            g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1f));
	            for (int i = 0; i < xLbls.length; i++) {
	                int xp = ml + (int)((double) i / (xLbls.length - 1) * gw);
	                FontMetrics xfm = g2.getFontMetrics();
	                g2.setColor(new Color(80, 85, 125));
	                g2.drawString(xLbls[i], xp - xfm.stringWidth(xLbls[i]) / 2, mt + gh + 18);
	                g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1f, BasicStroke.CAP_BUTT, BasicStroke.JOIN_BEVEL, 0, dashArr, 0));
	                g2.setColor(new Color(28, 32, 52));
	                g2.drawLine(xp, mt, xp, mt + gh);
	                g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1f));
	            }

	            drawLine(g2, boData,      new Color(70, 210, 110),  new Color(70, 210, 110, 22),
	                     ml, mt, gw, gh, minVal, maxVal);

	            drawLine(g2, listingData, new Color(80, 155, 255),  new Color(80, 155, 255, 30),
	                     ml, mt, gw, gh, minVal, maxVal);

	            g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1.5f));
	            g2.setColor(new Color(44, 50, 80));
	            g2.drawRect(ml, mt, gw, gh);

	            g2.dispose();
	        }

	        private void drawLine(Graphics2D g2, ArrayList<Double> data, Color lineCol, Color fillCol,
	                              int ml, int mt, int gw, int gh, double minV, double maxV) {
	            if (data == null || data.size() < 2) return;
	            int n = data.size();
	            int[] xs = new int[n], ys = new int[n];
	            for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
	                xs[i] = ml + (int)((double) i / (n - 1) * gw);
	                double norm = (data.get(i) - minV) / (maxV - minV);
	                ys[i] = Math.max(mt, Math.min(mt + gh, mt + gh - (int)(norm * gh)));
	            }

	            int[] px = new int[n + 2], py = new int[n + 2];
	            System.arraycopy(xs, 0, px, 0, n); System.arraycopy(ys, 0, py, 0, n);
	            px[n] = ml + gw; py[n] = mt + gh; px[n+1] = ml; py[n+1] = mt + gh;
	            g2.setColor(fillCol); g2.fillPolygon(px, py, n + 2);

	            g2.setColor(lineCol);
	            g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1.2f, BasicStroke.CAP_ROUND, BasicStroke.JOIN_ROUND));
	            for (int i = 1; i < n; i++) g2.drawLine(xs[i-1], ys[i-1], xs[i], ys[i]);

	            int lx = xs[n-1], ly = ys[n-1];
	            g2.setColor(new Color(255, 255, 255, 200)); g2.fillOval(lx - 4, ly - 4, 8, 8);
	            g2.setColor(lineCol); g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1.5f)); g2.drawOval(lx - 4, ly - 4, 8, 8);
	            g2.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));
	            String lbl = String.format("$%.2f", data.get(n - 1));
	            FontMetrics fm = g2.getFontMetrics();
	            int lw = fm.stringWidth(lbl);
	            int lx2 = (lx + 6 + lw <= ml + gw) ? lx + 6 : lx - lw - 6;

	            g2.setColor(new Color(10, 10, 16, 200));
	            g2.fillRoundRect(lx2 - 2, ly - 8, lw + 4, 13, 4, 4);
	            g2.setColor(lineCol);
	            g2.drawString(lbl, lx2, ly + 3);
	        }
	    };
	    chartPanel.setBackground(new Color(10, 10, 16));
	    chartFrame.add(chartPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    rangeBox.addActionListener(e -> {
	        selectedRangeIdx[0] = rangeBox.getSelectedIndex();
	        chartPanel.repaint();
	    });

	    chartFrame.setVisible(true);

	    javax.swing.Timer refreshTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(MARKET_UPDATE_INTERVAL, e -> chartPanel.repaint());
	    refreshTimer.setRepeats(true); refreshTimer.start();
	    chartFrame.addWindowListener(new java.awt.event.WindowAdapter() {
	        @Override public void windowClosing(java.awt.event.WindowEvent e) { refreshTimer.stop(); }
	        @Override public void windowClosed (java.awt.event.WindowEvent e) { refreshTimer.stop(); }
	    });
	    javax.swing.Timer focus = new javax.swing.Timer(100, e -> { chartFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(false); chartFrame.toFront(); });
	    focus.setRepeats(false); focus.start();
	}

	private JPanel createOptimizedListingCard(MarketListing listing, JFrame parent) {
	    JPanel listingCard = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    listingCard.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    listingCard.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(Color.GRAY, 2));
	    listingCard.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 120));
	    
	    JPanel imagePanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    imagePanel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(120, 80));
	    imagePanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    
	    if (listing.item.image != null) {
	        Image scaled = listing.item.getThumb130().getImage();
	        JLabel imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	        imagePanel.add(imgLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    } else {
	        String cleanName = listing.item.name.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(cleanName);
	        if (skinImg != null) {
	            Image scaled = skinImg.getScaledInstance(130, 88, Image.SCALE_FAST);
	            JLabel imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	            imagePanel.add(imgLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        }
	    }
	    listingCard.add(imagePanel, BorderLayout.WEST);
