	    JPanel infoPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(5, 1));
	    infoPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    infoPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(5, 10, 5, 10));
	    
	    JLabel nameLabel;
	    if (listing.item.isStattrak) {

	        nameLabel = new JLabel("StatTrak " + listing.item.name);
	        nameLabel.setForeground(new Color(255, 153, 51));
	        nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 13));
	    } else {
	        nameLabel = new JLabel(listing.item.name);
	        nameLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	        nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 13));
	    }
	    
	    JLabel patternLabel = new JLabel("Pattern: #" + listing.item.patternID);
	    patternLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    patternLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    
	    JLabel floatLabel = new JLabel(String.format("Float: %.8f", listing.item.itemFloat));
	    floatLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    
	    if (listing.item.itemFloat < 0.07) {
	        floatLabel.setForeground(new Color(100, 255, 100));
	    } else if (listing.item.itemFloat < 0.15) {
	        floatLabel.setForeground(new Color(150, 255, 150));
	    } else if (listing.item.itemFloat < 0.38) {
	        floatLabel.setForeground(new Color(255, 255, 100));
	    } else if (listing.item.itemFloat < 0.45) {
	        floatLabel.setForeground(new Color(255, 200, 100));
	    } else {
	        floatLabel.setForeground(new Color(255, 150, 150));
	    }
	    
	    JLabel priceLabel = new JLabel("$" + String.format("%.2f", listing.listPrice));
	    priceLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    priceLabel.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
	    
	    JPanel sellerPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 5, 2));
	    sellerPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    
	    JLabel sellerPrefix = new JLabel("SELLER: ");
	    sellerPrefix.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    sellerPrefix.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	    sellerPanel.add(sellerPrefix);
	    
	    if (listing.isPlayerListing) {
	        JLabel playerAvatarLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(playerAvatar.getScaledInstance(16, 16, Image.SCALE_FAST)));
	        sellerPanel.add(playerAvatarLabel);
	        
	        JLabel youLabel = new JLabel("YOU");
	        youLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 11));
	        youLabel.setForeground(new Color(100, 200, 100));
	        sellerPanel.add(youLabel);
	    } else {
	        if (listing.sellerAvatar != null) {
	            JLabel avatarLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(listing.sellerAvatar.getScaledInstance(16, 16, Image.SCALE_FAST)));
	            sellerPanel.add(avatarLabel);
	        }
	        
	        JLabel usernameLabel = new JLabel(listing.sellerName);
	        usernameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	        usernameLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	        sellerPanel.add(usernameLabel);
	    }
	    
	    infoPanel.add(nameLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(patternLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(floatLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(priceLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(sellerPanel);
	    
	    listingCard.add(infoPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    if (listing.isPlayerListing) {
	        JLabel yourListingLabel = new JLabel("YOUR LISTING");
	        yourListingLabel.setForeground(Color.ORANGE);
	        yourListingLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        yourListingLabel.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        yourListingLabel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(150, 80));
	        listingCard.add(yourListingLabel, BorderLayout.EAST);
	    } else {
	        JButton buyBtn = new JButton("<html><center>BUY<br>$" + String.format("%.2f", listing.listPrice) + "</center></html>");
	        buyBtn.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        buyBtn.setBackground(new Color(50, 150, 50));
	        buyBtn.setForeground(Color.BLACK);
	        buyBtn.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(150, 80));
	        buyBtn.setFocusPainted(false);
	        
	        buyBtn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
                @Override
                public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) {
                    playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
                }
            });
	        
	        buyBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	            buyItemNow(listing, parent);
	        });
	        
	        listingCard.add(buyBtn, BorderLayout.EAST);
	    }
	    
	    return listingCard;
	}
	
	private void buyItemNow(MarketListing listing, JFrame parent) {
	    if (balance < listing.listPrice) {
	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(parent, 
	            "Insufficient funds! Need $" + String.format("%.2f", listing.listPrice));
	        return;
	    }
	    
	    int confirm = JOptionPane.showConfirmDialog(parent,
	        String.format("Buy %s%s\nCondition: %s\nFloat: %.10f\nPrice: $%.2f?",
	            listing.item.isStattrak ? "StatTrak " : "",
	            listing.item.name, listing.item.condition, listing.item.itemFloat, listing.listPrice),
	        "Confirm Purchase", JOptionPane.YES_NO_OPTION);
	    
	    if (confirm == JOptionPane.YES_OPTION) {
	        balance -= listing.listPrice;
	        playSound(purchaseSound);

	        if (listing.item.image == null) {
	            String cleanName = listing.item.name.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	            Image img = getSkinImageFromName(cleanName);
	            if (img != null) {
	                listing.item.image = new ImageIcon(img);
	            }
	        }
	        
	        String marketKey = listing.item.isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + listing.item.name : listing.item.name;
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> allListings = globalMarketListings.get(marketKey);
	        
	        double lowestMarketPrice = listing.listPrice; 
	        
	        if (allListings != null && !allListings.isEmpty()) {
	            ArrayList<MarketListing> sameCondition = new ArrayList<>();
	            for (MarketListing ml : allListings) {
	                if (ml.item.condition.equals(listing.item.condition)) {
	                    sameCondition.add(ml);
	                }
	            }
	            
	            if (!sameCondition.isEmpty()) {
	                sameCondition.sort(Comparator.comparingDouble(l -> l.listPrice));
	                lowestMarketPrice = sameCondition.get(0).listPrice;
	            }
	        }
	        
	        String rarityKey = listing.item.rarity.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        double currentMarketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarityKey, 1.0);
	        double trueBasePrice = lowestMarketPrice / currentMarketMulti;
	        
	        listing.item.price = BigDecimal.valueOf(lowestMarketPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	        listing.item.basePrice = trueBasePrice;
	        
	        updateIdenticalItemPrices(listing.item.name, listing.item.condition, 
	                                  listing.item.isStattrak, trueBasePrice);
	        
	        inventoryList.add(listing.item);
	        inventoryValue += lowestMarketPrice;
	        
	        updateLeaderboard();

	        String specialVariant = null;
	        if (listing.item.blueGemTier != null) {
	            specialVariant = listing.item.blueGemTier;
	        } else if (listing.item.name.contains("Doppler")) {
	            specialVariant = "Doppler";
	        }
	        
	        String saleDisplayName = listing.item.isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + listing.item.name : listing.item.name;
	        saleDisplayName = cleanStatTrakEncoding(saleDisplayName);
	        
	        recordSale(listing.item.name, listing.listPrice, listing.item.condition, listing.item.itemFloat);
	        addSaleRecord(new SaleRecord(saleDisplayName, listing.listPrice, 
	            listing.item.condition, listing.item.itemFloat, specialVariant));
	        playerPurchases.add(new SaleRecord(saleDisplayName, listing.listPrice,
	            listing.item.condition, listing.item.itemFloat, specialVariant));
        missionMarketSpent += listing.listPrice;
        checkMissionProgress();
	        if (playerPurchases.size() > MAX_SALES_HISTORY) {
	            playerPurchases.removeFirst();
	        }

	        String skinName = listing.item.isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + listing.item.name : listing.item.name;
	        if (globalMarketListings.containsKey(skinName)) {
	            globalMarketListings.get(skinName).remove(listing);
	        }

	        replenishThinMarketListings();

	        updateBalanceLabel();
	        writeStats();
	        newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	        totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	        refreshMainUI();
	        
	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(parent, "Purchase successful!");

	        String currentSkinName = listing.item.isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + listing.item.name : listing.item.name;

	        Window[] windows = Window.getWindows();
	        for (Window window : windows) {
	            if (window instanceof JFrame) {
	                JFrame frame = (JFrame) window;
	                if (frame.getTitle().contains("Market") || frame.getTitle().contains("Listings")) {
	                    frame.dispose();
	                }
	            }
	        }

	        ArrayList<MarketListing> remainingListings = globalMarketListings.get(currentSkinName);
	        if (remainingListings != null && !remainingListings.isEmpty()) {
	            showDetailedListings(currentSkinName, remainingListings, this);
	        }
	    }
	}

	private void updateIdenticalItemPrices(String skinName, String condition, boolean isStattrak, double newBasePrice) {
	    synchronized (inventoryList) {
	        for (InventoryItem item : inventoryList) {
	            if (item.name.equals(skinName) && 
	                item.condition.equals(condition) && 
	                item.isStattrak == isStattrak &&
	                item.blueGemTier == null) {
	                
	                item.basePrice = newBasePrice;
	                
	                String rarityKey = item.rarity.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	                double currentMarketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarityKey, 1.0);
	                double newPrice = newBasePrice * currentMarketMulti;
	                
	                item.price = BigDecimal.valueOf(newPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	            }
	        }
	        
	        inventoryValue = 0.0;
	        for (InventoryItem item : inventoryList) {
	            inventoryValue += item.price.doubleValue();
	        }
	        
	        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	            newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	            totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	        });
	    }
	}

		private Image getSkinImageFromName(String skinName) {
	    if (imageCache.containsKey(skinName)) {
	        return imageCache.get(skinName);
	    }
	    // Cap the cache size to avoid unbounded memory use
	    if (imageCache.size() > 300) imageCache.clear();

	    if (skinName.contains("Doppler") && !skinName.contains("Phase") && 
	        !skinName.contains("Sapphire") && !skinName.contains("Ruby") && 
	        !skinName.contains("Black Pearl")) {

	        Image dopplerImg = getKnifeImage(skinName + " (Phase 1)");
	        if (dopplerImg != null) {
	            return dopplerImg; 
	        }
	    }
	    
	    Map<String, String> skinToFile = SKIN_TO_FILE;

	    Image dopplerImg = getKnifeImage(skinName);
	    if (dopplerImg != null) {
	        imageCache.put(skinName, dopplerImg);
	        return dopplerImg;
	    }

	    String filename = skinToFile.get(skinName);
	    if (filename != null) {
	        try {
	            Image img = new ImageIcon(filename).getImage();
	            imageCache.put(skinName, img);
	            return img;
	        } catch (Exception e) {
	        }
	    }

	    if (ARMOURY_COLLECTIONS != null) {
	        for (ArmouryCollection ac : ARMOURY_COLLECTIONS) {
	            String[][] allNames = {ac.covertNames, ac.classifiedNames, ac.restrictedNames, ac.milspecNames, ac.industrialNames};
	            String[][] allFiles = {ac.covert, ac.classified, ac.restricted, ac.milspec, ac.industrial};
	            for (int ti = 0; ti < allNames.length; ti++) {
	                if (allNames[ti] == null) continue;
	                for (int si = 0; si < allNames[ti].length; si++) {
	                    if (skinName.equalsIgnoreCase(allNames[ti][si])) {
	                        Image img2 = new ImageIcon(allFiles[ti][si] + ".png").getImage();
	                        imageCache.put(skinName, img2);
	                        return img2;
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	        }
	    }

	    return null;
	}

		private JPanel createBuyOrdersPanel() {
	    Color BG_DARK  = new Color(15, 15, 20);
	    Color BG_CARD  = new Color(30, 30, 40);
	    Color BG_INFO  = new Color(22, 22, 30);
	    Color BORDER   = new Color(45, 45, 60);

	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    panel.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    
	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 2, 10, 10));
	    grid.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    scroll.getViewport().setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    scroll.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(BORDER, 1));
	    
	    for (BuyOrder order : buyOrders) {
	        JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	        card.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	        card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(200, 130, 30), 2),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 4, 4, 4)));
	        card.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(300, 200));

	        String cleanName = order.skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(cleanName);
	        if (skinImg != null) {
	            Image scaled = skinImg.getScaledInstance(130, 88, Image.SCALE_FAST);
	            JLabel imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	            imgLabel.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.CENTER);
	            card.add(imgLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        }
	        
	        JPanel info = new JPanel(new GridLayout(6, 1));
	        info.setBackground(BG_INFO);
	        
	        JLabel nameLabel = new JLabel(order.skinName, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        nameLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	        nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
	        
	        JLabel rarityLabel = new JLabel(order.rarity, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        rarityLabel.setForeground(getRarityColor(order.rarity));
	        rarityLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 11));
	        
	        JLabel conditionLabel = new JLabel("Condition: " + order.desiredCondition, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        conditionLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	        
	        JLabel priceLabel = new JLabel("Max Price: $" + String.format("%.2f", order.maxPrice), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        priceLabel.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
	        priceLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        
	        String qtyText = order.filled > 0
	            ? String.format("Filled: %d / %d", order.filled, order.quantity)
	            : String.format("Qty: %d  ·  ⏳ Waiting...", order.quantity);
	        JLabel statusLabel = new JLabel(qtyText, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        statusLabel.setForeground(order.filled > 0 ? new Color(80, 220, 120) : Color.CYAN);
	        statusLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 11));
	        
	        JButton cancelBtn = new JButton("Cancel Order");
	        cancelBtn.setBackground(new Color(220, 60, 60));
	        cancelBtn.setForeground(Color.BLACK);
	        cancelBtn.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
	        cancelBtn.setBorderPainted(false);
	        cancelBtn.setBorder(null);
	        cancelBtn.setFocusPainted(false);
	        cancelBtn.setContentAreaFilled(true);
	        cancelBtn.setOpaque(true);
	        
	        cancelBtn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
                @Override
                public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) {
                    playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
                }
            });

	        cancelBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	            buyOrders.remove(order);

	            Window w = SwingUtilities.getWindowAncestor(cancelBtn);
	            if (w != null) w.dispose();
	        });
	        
	        info.add(nameLabel);
	        info.add(rarityLabel);
	        info.add(conditionLabel);
	        info.add(priceLabel);
	        info.add(statusLabel);
	        info.add(cancelBtn);
	        
	        card.add(info, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	        grid.add(card);
	    }
	    
	    if (buyOrders.isEmpty()) {
	        JLabel emptyLabel = new JLabel("No active buy orders", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        emptyLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 24));
	        emptyLabel.setForeground(new Color(140, 140, 155));
	        panel.add(emptyLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    } else {
	        panel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    }
	    
	    return panel;
	}
	
	private JPanel createMyListingCard(MarketListing listing) {
	    Color BG_CARD = new Color(30, 30, 40);
	    Color BG_INFO = new Color(22, 22, 30);

	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    card.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(getRarityColor(listing.item.rarity), 2),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 4, 4, 4)));
	    
	    if (listing.item.image != null) {
	        Image scaled = listing.item.getThumb130().getImage();
	        JLabel imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	        imgLabel.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        card.add(imgLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    }
	    
	    JPanel info = new JPanel(new GridLayout(6, 1));
	    info.setBackground(BG_INFO);
	    
	    JLabel name = new JLabel(listing.item.name, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    name.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    
	    JLabel price = new JLabel("$" + String.format("%.2f", listing.listPrice), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    price.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
	    
	    JLabel floatLabel = new JLabel(String.format("Float: %.10f", listing.item.itemFloat), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    floatLabel.setForeground(Color.CYAN);
	    
	    JLabel time = new JLabel("Sells in: " + listing.timeRemaining + "s", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    time.setForeground(Color.CYAN);
	    
	    JLabel cond = new JLabel(listing.item.condition, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    cond.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	    
	    JButton cancelBtn = new JButton("Cancel Listing");
	    cancelBtn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
            @Override
            public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) {
                playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
            }
        });
	    cancelBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	        activeListings.remove(listing);
	        inventoryList.add(listing.item);
	        inventoryValue += listing.item.price.doubleValue();
	        writeStats();
	        newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	        totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	        refreshMainUI();
	        
	        Window w = SwingUtilities.getWindowAncestor(cancelBtn);
	        if (w != null) w.dispose();
	    });
	    
	    info.add(name);
	    info.add(cond);
	    info.add(floatLabel);
	    info.add(price);
	    info.add(time);
	    info.add(cancelBtn);
	    
	    card.add(info, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    return card;
	}
	
	private void createBuyOrder(String skinName, JFrame parent) {
	    String cleanSkin = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").replace("StatTrak ", "");
	    String[] availableConditions = getAvailableConditions(cleanSkin);
	    String[] conditionOptions = new String[availableConditions.length + 1];
	    conditionOptions[0] = "Any";
	    System.arraycopy(availableConditions, 0, conditionOptions, 1, availableConditions.length);
	    String normKey = normalizeSkinName(skinName);

	    JDialog dialog = new JDialog(parent, "Create Buy Order", true);
	    dialog.setSize(460, 360);
	    dialog.setLocationRelativeTo(parent);
	    dialog.setDefaultCloseOperation(JDialog.DISPOSE_ON_CLOSE);

	    Color BG      = new Color(18, 18, 26);
	    Color BG_CARD = new Color(28, 28, 40);
	    Color TEXT    = new Color(230, 230, 235);
	    Color DIM     = new Color(140, 140, 155);
	    Color ACCENT  = new Color(80, 155, 255);

	    JPanel root = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(0, 0));
	    root.setBackground(BG);
	    root.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(ACCENT, 2));

	    JPanel header = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    header.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	    header.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(14, 20, 14, 20));

	    JLabel title = new JLabel("Create Buy Order");
	    title.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    title.setForeground(ACCENT);
	    header.add(title, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JLabel skinLbl = new JLabel("<html><body style='width:380px'>" + skinName + "</body></html>");
	    skinLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 13));
	    skinLbl.setForeground(TEXT);
	    skinLbl.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(6, 0, 0, 0));
	    header.add(skinLbl, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    root.add(header, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel form = new JPanel(new GridBagLayout());
	    form.setBackground(BG);
	    form.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(16, 24, 8, 24));
	    GridBagConstraints gc = new GridBagConstraints();
	    gc.insets = new java.awt.Insets(7, 6, 7, 6);
	    gc.fill = GridBagConstraints.HORIZONTAL;
	    gc.weightx = 0.35;

	    Font labelFont = new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12);
	    Font fieldFont = new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12);

	    gc.gridx = 0; gc.gridy = 0; gc.weightx = 0.35;
	    JLabel condLbl = new JLabel("Condition:");
	    condLbl.setForeground(DIM); condLbl.setFont(labelFont);
	    form.add(condLbl, gc);
	    gc.gridx = 1; gc.weightx = 0.65;
	    JComboBox<String> conditionBox = new JComboBox<>(conditionOptions);
	    conditionBox.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	    conditionBox.setForeground(TEXT);
	    conditionBox.setFont(fieldFont);
	    form.add(conditionBox, gc);

	    gc.gridx = 0; gc.gridy = 1; gc.gridwidth = 2;
	    JLabel topOrderLbl = new JLabel(" ");
	    topOrderLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.ITALIC, 11));
	    topOrderLbl.setForeground(new Color(100, 210, 255));
	    form.add(topOrderLbl, gc);
	    gc.gridwidth = 1;

	    Runnable updateTopOrder = () -> {
	        String sel = (String) conditionBox.getSelectedItem();
	        if (sel == null || sel.equals("Any")) {
	            topOrderLbl.setText("Select a condition to see the current top order");
	            return;
	        }
	        NpcBuyOrder best = getBestNpcBuyOrder(normKey, sel);
	        topOrderLbl.setText(best != null
	            ? String.format("Top order: $%.2f by %s", best.price, best.buyerName != null ? best.buyerName : "NPC")
	            : "No existing buy orders for this condition");
	    };
	    conditionBox.addActionListener(e -> updateTopOrder.run());
	    updateTopOrder.run();

	    gc.gridx = 0; gc.gridy = 2; gc.weightx = 0.35;
	    JLabel priceLbl = new JLabel("Your price ($):");
	    priceLbl.setForeground(DIM); priceLbl.setFont(labelFont);
	    form.add(priceLbl, gc);
	    gc.gridx = 1; gc.weightx = 0.65;
	    JTextField priceField = new JTextField("100.00");
	    priceField.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	    priceField.setForeground(TEXT);
	    priceField.setCaretColor(TEXT);
	    priceField.setFont(fieldFont);
	    priceField.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(60, 60, 80), 1),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 8, 4, 8)));
	    form.add(priceField, gc);

	    gc.gridx = 0; gc.gridy = 3; gc.weightx = 0.35;
	    JLabel qtyLbl = new JLabel("Quantity:");
	    qtyLbl.setForeground(DIM); qtyLbl.setFont(labelFont);
	    form.add(qtyLbl, gc);
	    gc.gridx = 1; gc.weightx = 0.65;
	    JSpinner qtySpinner = new JSpinner(new SpinnerNumberModel(1, 1, 999, 1));
	    qtySpinner.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	    qtySpinner.setForeground(TEXT);
	    qtySpinner.setFont(fieldFont);
	    form.add(qtySpinner, gc);

	    root.add(form, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JButton confirmBtn = new JButton("Place Order");
	    JButton cancelBtn  = new JButton("Cancel");
	    for (JButton btn : new JButton[]{confirmBtn, cancelBtn}) {
	        btn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	        btn.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52));
	        btn.setForeground(TEXT);
	        btn.setFocusPainted(false);
	        btn.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(60, 60, 80), 1),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 20, 8, 20)));
	        btn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	            @Override public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) { btn.setBackground(new Color(55, 55, 75)); }
	            @Override public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e)  { btn.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 52)); }
	        });
	    }
	    confirmBtn.setForeground(new Color(80, 220, 120));

	    JPanel btnRow = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.RIGHT, 10, 10));
	    btnRow.setBackground(BG);
	    btnRow.add(cancelBtn);
	    btnRow.add(confirmBtn);
	    root.add(btnRow, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    cancelBtn.addActionListener(e -> dialog.dispose());

	    confirmBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	        try {
	            double maxPrice = Double.parseDouble(priceField.getText().trim());
	            if (maxPrice <= 0) { JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(dialog, "Price must be positive!"); return; }
	            int qty = (Integer) qtySpinner.getValue();
	            String rarity = getSkinRarity(cleanSkin);
	            String selectedCondition = (String) conditionBox.getSelectedItem();
	            buyOrders.add(new BuyOrder(skinName, maxPrice, rarity, selectedCondition, qty));
	            balance -= maxPrice * qty;
	            updateBalanceLabel();
	            writeStats();
	            dialog.dispose();
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(parent,
	                String.format("Buy order placed: %s x%d @ $%.2f", skinName, qty, maxPrice));
	        } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(dialog, "Invalid price format!");
	        }
	    });

	    dialog.setContentPane(root);
	    dialog.setVisible(true);
	}

	private void showPriceHistoryChart() {
	    JFrame chartFrame = new JFrame("Market Price Trends");
	    chartFrame.setSize(1100, 620);
	    chartFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    chartFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    chartFrame.getContentPane().setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 18));

	    
	    JPanel topBar = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(12, 0));
	    topBar.setBackground(new Color(16, 16, 24));
	    topBar.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 1, 0, new Color(35, 38, 60)),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 16, 10, 16)));

	    JLabel titleLbl = new JLabel("Rarity Price Index  ·  % Change from Baseline", SwingConstants.LEFT);
	    titleLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 14));
	    titleLbl.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    topBar.add(titleLbl, BorderLayout.WEST);

	    
	    String[] trackedRarities = {"Knife", "Covert", "Classified", "Restricted", "Milspec", "Industrial"};
	    JPanel legend = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.RIGHT, 18, 0));
	    legend.setOpaque(false);
	    for (String r : trackedRarities) {
	        JLabel leg = new JLabel("━━  " + r);
	        leg.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	        leg.setForeground(getRarityColor(r));
	        legend.add(leg);
	    }
	    topBar.add(legend, BorderLayout.EAST);
	    chartFrame.add(topBar, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    
	    JPanel statsBar = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.CENTER, 32, 7));
	    statsBar.setBackground(new Color(14, 14, 22));
	    statsBar.setBorder(BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(1, 0, 0, 0, new Color(32, 36, 58)));
	    JLabel capLbl  = new JLabel(String.format("Total Market Cap: $%,.0f", totalMarketCap));
	    JLabel peakLbl = new JLabel(String.format("Peak Cap: $%,.0f",        peakTotalMarketCap));
	    JLabel tickLbl = new JLabel("Auto-updating every " + (MARKET_UPDATE_INTERVAL / 1000) + "s");
	    for (JLabel l : new JLabel[]{capLbl, peakLbl, tickLbl}) {
	        l.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	        l.setForeground(new Color(150, 160, 200));
	        statsBar.add(l);
	    }
	    capLbl.setForeground(new Color(255, 170, 60));
	    peakLbl.setForeground(new Color(80, 220, 90));
	    chartFrame.add(statsBar, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    
	    JPanel chartPanel = new JPanel() {
	        @Override
	        protected void paintComponent(Graphics g) {
	            super.paintComponent(g);
	            Graphics2D g2 = (Graphics2D) g.create();
	            g2.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_ANTIALIASING,      RenderingHints.VALUE_ANTIALIAS_ON);
	            g2.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_TEXT_ANTIALIASING, RenderingHints.VALUE_TEXT_ANTIALIAS_ON);

	            int w = getWidth(), h = getHeight();
	            int ml = 68, mr = 20, mt = 20, mb = 40;
	            int gw = w - ml - mr, gh = h - mt - mb;
	            if (gw < 10 || gh < 10) { g2.dispose(); return; }

	            
	            g2.setColor(new Color(10, 10, 16)); g2.fillRect(0, 0, w, h);
	            g2.setColor(new Color(16, 18, 28)); g2.fillRect(ml, mt, gw, gh);

	            
	            String[] rarities = {"Knife", "Covert", "Classified", "Restricted", "Milspec", "Industrial"};
	            double minVal =  Double.MAX_VALUE;
	            double maxVal = -Double.MAX_VALUE;
	            for (String r : rarities) {
	                ArrayList<Double> hist = priceHistory.get(r);
	                if (hist == null || hist.isEmpty()) continue;
	                for (double v : hist) {
	                    double pct = (v - 1.0) * 100.0;
	                    if (pct < minVal) minVal = pct;
	                    if (pct > maxVal) maxVal = pct;
	                }
	            }
	            if (minVal == Double.MAX_VALUE) { minVal = -10; maxVal = 10; }

	            
	            minVal = Math.min(minVal, 0);
	            maxVal = Math.max(maxVal, 0);

	            double pad = Math.max(2.0, (maxVal - minVal) * 0.12);
	            minVal -= pad; maxVal += pad;
	            if (maxVal <= minVal) maxVal = minVal + 1;

	            int GRID = 6;
	            float[] dashArr = {4f, 5f};
	            g2.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 10));

	            for (int i = 0; i <= GRID; i++) {
	                double val = maxVal - (maxVal - minVal) * i / (double) GRID;
	                int gy = mt + (int)((double) i / GRID * gh);
	                
	                g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1f, BasicStroke.CAP_BUTT, BasicStroke.JOIN_BEVEL, 0, dashArr, 0));
	                g2.setColor(new Color(30, 34, 54)); g2.drawLine(ml, gy, ml + gw, gy);
	                
	                g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1f));
	                g2.setColor(new Color(110, 115, 155));
	                String yLbl = String.format("%+.1f%%", val);
	                FontMetrics yfm = g2.getFontMetrics();
	                g2.drawString(yLbl, ml - yfm.stringWidth(yLbl) - 4, gy + 4);
	            }

	            
	            if (minVal < 0 && maxVal > 0) {
	                int gy0 = mt + (int)((maxVal / (maxVal - minVal)) * gh);
	                gy0 = Math.max(mt, Math.min(mt + gh, gy0));
	                g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1.2f));
	                g2.setColor(new Color(70, 75, 110)); g2.drawLine(ml, gy0, ml + gw, gy0);
	            }

	            
	            int maxPts = 0;
	            for (String r : rarities) {
	                ArrayList<Double> h2 = priceHistory.get(r);
	                if (h2 != null) maxPts = Math.max(maxPts, h2.size());
	            }
	            if (maxPts > 1) {
	                g2.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 10));
	                int steps = Math.min(6, maxPts - 1);
	                for (int i = 0; i <= steps; i++) {
	                    int dp   = (int)((double) i / steps * (maxPts - 1));
	                    int xp   = ml + (int)((double) dp / (maxPts - 1) * gw);
	                    int secs = dp * (MARKET_UPDATE_INTERVAL / 1000);
	                    String lbl = secs < 60 ? secs + "s" : (secs / 60) + "m";
	                    FontMetrics xfm = g2.getFontMetrics();
	                    g2.setColor(new Color(80, 85, 125));
	                    g2.drawString(lbl, xp - xfm.stringWidth(lbl) / 2, mt + gh + 18);
	                    g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1f, BasicStroke.CAP_BUTT, BasicStroke.JOIN_BEVEL, 0, dashArr, 0));
	                    g2.setColor(new Color(28, 32, 52));
	                    g2.drawLine(xp, mt, xp, mt + gh);
	                    g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1f));
	                }
	            }

	            
	            for (String r : rarities) {
	                ArrayList<Double> hist = priceHistory.get(r);
	                if (hist == null || hist.size() < 2) continue;

	                
	                ArrayList<Double> pctData = new ArrayList<>(hist.size());
	                for (double v : hist) pctData.add((v - 1.0) * 100.0);

	                Color lineCol = getRarityColor(r);
	                Color fillCol = new Color(lineCol.getRed(), lineCol.getGreen(), lineCol.getBlue(), 18);

	                int n = pctData.size();
	                int[] xs = new int[n], ys = new int[n];
	                for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
	                    xs[i] = ml + (int)((double) i / (n - 1) * gw);
	                    double norm = (pctData.get(i) - minVal) / (maxVal - minVal);
	                    ys[i] = Math.max(mt, Math.min(mt + gh, mt + gh - (int)(norm * gh)));
	                }

	                
	                int[] px = new int[n + 2], py = new int[n + 2];
	                System.arraycopy(xs, 0, px, 0, n); System.arraycopy(ys, 0, py, 0, n);
	                px[n] = ml + gw; py[n] = mt + gh; px[n+1] = ml; py[n+1] = mt + gh;
	                g2.setColor(fillCol); g2.fillPolygon(px, py, n + 2);

	                
	                g2.setColor(lineCol);
	                g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1.6f, BasicStroke.CAP_ROUND, BasicStroke.JOIN_ROUND));
	                for (int i = 1; i < n; i++) g2.drawLine(xs[i-1], ys[i-1], xs[i], ys[i]);

	                
	                int lx = xs[n-1], ly = ys[n-1];
	                g2.setColor(new Color(255, 255, 255, 200)); g2.fillOval(lx - 4, ly - 4, 8, 8);
	                g2.setColor(lineCol); g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1.5f)); g2.drawOval(lx - 4, ly - 4, 8, 8);
	                double currentPct = pctData.get(n - 1);
	                String endLbl = String.format("%+.1f%%", currentPct);
	                g2.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));
	                FontMetrics fm = g2.getFontMetrics();
	                int lw = fm.stringWidth(endLbl);
	                int lx2 = (lx + 6 + lw <= ml + gw) ? lx + 6 : lx - lw - 6;
	                g2.setColor(new Color(10, 10, 16, 200));
	                g2.fillRoundRect(lx2 - 2, ly - 8, lw + 4, 13, 4, 4);
	                g2.setColor(lineCol);
	                g2.drawString(endLbl, lx2, ly + 3);
	            }

	            
	            g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(1.5f));
	            g2.setColor(new Color(44, 50, 80));
	            g2.drawRect(ml, mt, gw, gh);

	            g2.dispose();
	        }
	    };
	    chartPanel.setBackground(new Color(10, 10, 16));
	    chartFrame.add(chartPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    
	    javax.swing.Timer refreshTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(MARKET_UPDATE_INTERVAL, ev -> {
	        chartPanel.repaint();
	        capLbl.setText(String.format("Total Market Cap: $%,.0f", totalMarketCap));
	        peakLbl.setText(String.format("Peak Cap: $%,.0f",        peakTotalMarketCap));
	    });
	    refreshTimer.setRepeats(true); refreshTimer.start();
	    chartFrame.addWindowListener(new java.awt.event.WindowAdapter() {
	        @Override public void windowClosing(java.awt.event.WindowEvent ev) { refreshTimer.stop(); }
	        @Override public void windowClosed (java.awt.event.WindowEvent ev) { refreshTimer.stop(); }
	    });

	    javax.swing.Timer focus = new javax.swing.Timer(100, ev -> {
	        chartFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(false); chartFrame.toFront();
	    });
	    focus.setRepeats(false); focus.start();
	    chartFrame.setVisible(true);
	}

		private String[] getAvailableConditions(String skinName) {
	    if (skinName.contains("Gloves") || skinName.contains("Hand Wraps")) {
	        return new String[]{"Factory New", "Minimal Wear", "Field-Tested", "Well-Worn", "Battle-Scarred"};
	    }
	    
	    FloatRange fr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(skinName);
	    if (fr == null) {
	        for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet()) {
	            if (skinName.startsWith(e.getKey())) {
	                fr = e.getValue();
	                break;
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    
	    if (fr == null) {
	        return new String[]{"Factory New", "Minimal Wear", "Field-Tested", "Well-Worn", "Battle-Scarred"};
	    }
	    
	    double min = (fr.min != null) ? fr.min : 0.0;
	    double max = (fr.max != null) ? fr.max : 1.0;
	    
	    ArrayList<String> conditions = new ArrayList<>();

	    if (min < 0.07 && max > 0.00) conditions.add("Factory New");

	    if (min < 0.15 && max > 0.07) conditions.add("Minimal Wear");

	    if (min < 0.38 && max > 0.15) conditions.add("Field-Tested");

	    if (min < 0.45 && max > 0.38) conditions.add("Well-Worn");

	    if (max > 0.45) conditions.add("Battle-Scarred");
	    
	    return conditions.toArray(new String[0]);
	}
	
	private void recordSale(String skinName, double price, String condition, double itemFloat) {
	    skinName = cleanStatTrakEncoding(skinName);
	    
	    if (!salesHistory.containsKey(skinName)) {
	        salesHistory.put(skinName, new HashMap<>());
	    }
	    Map<String, ArrayList<SaleRecord>> skinSales = salesHistory.get(skinName);
	    
	    if (!skinSales.containsKey(condition)) {
	        skinSales.put(condition, new ArrayList<>());
	    }
	    
	    ArrayList<SaleRecord> conditionSales = skinSales.get(condition);
	    conditionSales.add(new SaleRecord(price, System.currentTimeMillis(), condition, itemFloat));

	    if (conditionSales.size() > 20) {
	        conditionSales.remove(0);
	    }
	}
	
	private JPanel createRecentSalesPanel() {
	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    JPanel filterPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 6, 6));
	    filterPanel.setBackground(new Color(45, 45, 50));
	    filterPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 8, 4, 8));
	    
	    JLabel sortLabel = new JLabel("Sort:");
	    sortLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    sortLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    filterPanel.add(sortLabel);
	    
	    JComboBox<String> sortBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{
	        "Most Recent", "Highest Price", "Lowest Price"
	    });
	    styleComboBox(sortBox);
	    filterPanel.add(sortBox);
	    
	    JLabel rarityLabel = new JLabel("Rarity:");
	    rarityLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    rarityLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    filterPanel.add(rarityLabel);
	    
	    JComboBox<String> rarityBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{
	    	    "All", "Knife", "Gloves", "Covert", "Classified", "Restricted", "Milspec", "Industrial"
	    });
	    styleComboBox(rarityBox);
	    filterPanel.add(rarityBox);
	    
	    JLabel specialLabel = new JLabel("Special:");
	    specialLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    specialLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    filterPanel.add(specialLabel);
	    
	    JComboBox<String> specialBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{
	        "All", "Blue Gems Only", "Dopplers Only", "Regular Skins Only"
	    });
	    styleComboBox(specialBox);
	    filterPanel.add(specialBox);
	    
	    JLabel limitLabel = new JLabel("Show:");
	    limitLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    limitLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    filterPanel.add(limitLabel);
	    
	    JComboBox<String> limitBox = new JComboBox<>(new String[]{
	        "50 Sales", "100 Sales", "200 Sales", "500 Sales", "All Sales"
	    });
	    styleComboBox(limitBox);
	    filterPanel.add(limitBox);
	    
	    panel.add(filterPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JPanel salesContainer = new JPanel();
	    salesContainer.setLayout(new BoxLayout(salesContainer, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    salesContainer.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    salesContainer.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(salesContainer);
	    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    scroll.setBorder(null);
	    scroll.getViewport().setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    panel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    JPanel statsPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.CENTER));
	    statsPanel.setBackground(new Color(45, 45, 50));
	    statsPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(5, 5, 5, 5));
	    JLabel statsLabel = new JLabel("Total Sales: 0 | Average Price: $0.00");
	    statsLabel.setForeground(Color.CYAN);
	    statsLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    statsPanel.add(statsLabel);
	    panel.add(statsPanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    final int[] lastScrollValue = {0};
	    
	    Runnable updateSales = () -> {
	        lastScrollValue[0] = scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().getValue();
	        
	        String currentSort = (String) sortBox.getSelectedItem();
	        String currentRarity = (String) rarityBox.getSelectedItem();
	        String currentSpecial = (String) specialBox.getSelectedItem();
	        String currentLimit = (String) limitBox.getSelectedItem();
	        
	        salesContainer.removeAll();
	        
	        ArrayList<SaleRecord> filteredSales = new ArrayList<>(recentSales);
	        
	        if (!currentRarity.equals("All")) {
	            filteredSales.removeIf(sale -> {
	                String skinRarity = getSkinRarity(sale.skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").trim());
	                return !skinRarity.equals(currentRarity);
	            });
	        }
	        
	        if (currentSpecial.equals("Blue Gems Only")) {
	            filteredSales.removeIf(sale -> sale.specialVariant == null || !sale.specialVariant.contains("Blue Gem"));
	        } else if (currentSpecial.equals("Dopplers Only")) {
	            filteredSales.removeIf(sale -> !sale.skinName.contains("Doppler"));
	        } else if (currentSpecial.equals("Regular Skins Only")) {
	            filteredSales.removeIf(sale -> sale.specialVariant != null);
	        }
	        
	        if (currentSort.equals("Most Recent")) {
	            filteredSales.sort((a, b) -> Long.compare(b.timestamp, a.timestamp));
	        } else if (currentSort.equals("Highest Price")) {
	            filteredSales.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.price, a.price));
	        } else if (currentSort.equals("Lowest Price")) {
	            filteredSales.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(a.price, b.price));
	        }
	        
	        int displayLimit;
	        switch (currentLimit) {
	            case "50 Sales": displayLimit = 50; break;
	            case "100 Sales": displayLimit = 100; break;
	            case "200 Sales": displayLimit = 200; break;
	            case "500 Sales": displayLimit = 500; break;
	            default: displayLimit = Integer.MAX_VALUE; break;
	        }
	        
	        if (filteredSales.size() > displayLimit) {
	            filteredSales = new ArrayList<>(filteredSales.subList(0, displayLimit));
	        }
	        
	        double totalValue = filteredSales.stream().mapToDouble(s -> s.price).sum();
	        double avgPrice = filteredSales.isEmpty() ? 0 : totalValue / filteredSales.size();
	        statsLabel.setText(String.format("Showing %d of %d Sales | Average: $%.2f | Total Volume: $%.2f", 
	            filteredSales.size(), recentSales.size(), avgPrice, totalValue));
	        
	        for (SaleRecord sale : filteredSales) {
	            JPanel saleCard = createSaleCard(sale);
	            salesContainer.add(saleCard);
	            salesContainer.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 5)));
	        }
	        
	        salesContainer.revalidate();
	        salesContainer.repaint();
	        
	        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	            scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setValue(lastScrollValue[0]);
	        });
	    };
	    
	    sortBox.addActionListener(e -> updateSales.run());
	    rarityBox.addActionListener(e -> updateSales.run());
	    specialBox.addActionListener(e -> updateSales.run());
	    limitBox.addActionListener(e -> updateSales.run());

	    if (salesUpdateTimer != null) {
	        salesUpdateTimer.stop();
	    }
	    
	    salesUpdateTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(SALES_UI_UPDATE_INTERVAL, e -> updateSales.run());
	    salesUpdateTimer.start();
	    
	    updateSales.run();
	    
	    return panel;
	}

	private JPanel createSaleCard(SaleRecord sale) {
	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    card.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    card.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 72));
	    card.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(500, 72));
	    
	    String cleanName = sale.skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();
	    String rarity = getSkinRarity(cleanName.replaceAll("[^a-zA-Z0-9\\s\\-|]+", "").trim());
	    Color borderColor = getRarityColor(rarity);
	    
	    if (sale.specialVariant != null && sale.specialVariant.contains("Blue Gem")) {
	        borderColor = Color.CYAN;
	    }
	    
	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(borderColor, 2),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(3, 6, 3, 6)
	    ));
	    
	    String skinNameForImage = cleanName;
	    if (skinNameForImage.contains("(Blue Gem")) {
	        skinNameForImage = skinNameForImage.substring(0, skinNameForImage.indexOf("(Blue Gem")).trim();
	    }
	    
	    Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(skinNameForImage);
	    if (skinImg != null) {
	        Image scaled = skinImg.getScaledInstance(72, 50, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH);
	        JLabel imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	        imgLabel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(72, 50));
	        card.add(imgLabel, BorderLayout.WEST);
	    } else {
	        JLabel noImg = new JLabel("?", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        noImg.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(72, 50));
	        noImg.setForeground(Color.GRAY);
	        noImg.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	        noImg.setOpaque(true);
	        card.add(noImg, BorderLayout.WEST);
	    }
	    
	    JPanel infoPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(3, 1, 0, 0));
	    infoPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    infoPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(3, 8, 3, 8));
	    
	    JLabel nameLabel = new JLabel(sale.skinName);
	    if (sale.skinName.contains("StatTrak")) {
	        nameLabel.setForeground(new Color(255, 153, 51));
	        nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    } else {
	        nameLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	        nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    }
	    
	    JLabel condLabel = new JLabel(sale.condition + "  Float: " + String.format("%.4f", sale.itemFloat));
	    condLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	    condLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 10));
	    
	    JPanel buyerPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 3, 0));
	    buyerPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    JLabel buyerPrefix = new JLabel("BUYER: ");
	    buyerPrefix.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 9));
	    buyerPrefix.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	    buyerPanel.add(buyerPrefix);
	    if (sale.buyerAvatar != null) {
	        JLabel avatarLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(sale.buyerAvatar.getScaledInstance(16, 16, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH)));
	        buyerPanel.add(avatarLabel);
	    }
	    JLabel usernameLabel = new JLabel(sale.buyerName != null ? sale.buyerName : "Unknown");
	    usernameLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 9));
	    usernameLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    buyerPanel.add(usernameLabel);
	    
	    infoPanel.add(nameLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(condLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(buyerPanel);
	    
	    card.add(infoPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    JPanel rightPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1));
	    rightPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    rightPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    JLabel priceLabel = new JLabel("$" + String.format("%.2f", sale.price));
	    priceLabel.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
	    priceLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 18));
	    priceLabel.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.RIGHT);
	    
	    long secondsAgo = (System.currentTimeMillis() - sale.timestamp) / 1000;
	    String timeStr;
	    if (secondsAgo < 60) {
	        timeStr = secondsAgo + "s ago";
	    } else if (secondsAgo < 3600) {
	        timeStr = (secondsAgo / 60) + "m ago";
	    } else {
	        timeStr = (secondsAgo / 3600) + "h ago";
	    }
	    
	    JLabel timeLabel = new JLabel(timeStr);
	    timeLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	    timeLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	    timeLabel.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.RIGHT);
	    
	    rightPanel.add(priceLabel);
	    rightPanel.add(timeLabel);
	    
	    card.add(rightPanel, BorderLayout.EAST);
	    
	    return card;
	}
	
	private void startFakeSalesTimer() {
	    fakeSalesTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(FAKE_SALES_MIN_DELAY, e -> {
	        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	            double rarityRoll = random.nextDouble();
	            String targetRarity;
	            int nextDelay;

	            if (rarityRoll < 0.20) {
	                targetRarity = "Industrial";
	                nextDelay = 150 + random.nextInt(400);
	            } else if (rarityRoll < 0.42) {
	                targetRarity = "Milspec";
	                nextDelay = 200 + random.nextInt(500);
	            } else if (rarityRoll < 0.58) {
	                targetRarity = "Restricted";
	                nextDelay = 600 + random.nextInt(900);
	            } else if (rarityRoll < 0.70) {
	                targetRarity = "Classified";
	                nextDelay = 1500 + random.nextInt(2000);
	            } else if (rarityRoll < 0.80) {
	                targetRarity = "Covert";
	                nextDelay = 2500 + random.nextInt(2500);
	            } else if (rarityRoll < 0.89) {
	                targetRarity = "Knife";
	                nextDelay = 3000 + random.nextInt(3000);
	            } else {
	                targetRarity = "Gloves";
	                nextDelay = 3000 + random.nextInt(3000);
	            }
	            
	            fakeSalesTimer.setDelay(nextDelay);
	            
	            double saleType = random.nextDouble();
	            
	            if (saleType < 0.40) {
	                generateSaleFromActualListingByRarity(targetRarity);
	            } else if (saleType < 0.90) {
	                generateRegularFakeSaleByRarity(targetRarity);
	            } else {
	                if (targetRarity.equals("Knife") || targetRarity.equals("Classified")) {
	                    generateBlueGemSale();
	                } else {
	                    generateRegularFakeSaleByRarity(targetRarity);
	                }
	            }
	        });
	    });
	    fakeSalesTimer.start();
	}
	
	private void generateSaleFromActualListingByRarity(String targetRarity) {
	    ArrayList<String> availableSkins = new ArrayList<>();
	    for (String skinName : globalMarketListings.keySet()) {
	        String cleanName = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        if (getSkinRarity(cleanName).equals(targetRarity)) {
	            availableSkins.add(skinName);
	        }
	    }
	    
	    if (availableSkins.isEmpty()) {
	        generateSaleFromActualListing(); 
	        return;
	    }
	    
	    String randomSkin = availableSkins.get(random.nextInt(availableSkins.size()));
	    ArrayList<MarketListing> rawListings = globalMarketListings.get(randomSkin);
	    
	    if (rawListings == null || rawListings.isEmpty()) return;
	    
	    ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = new ArrayList<>(rawListings);
	    listings.sort(Comparator.comparingDouble(l -> l.listPrice));
	    double lowestPrice = listings.get(0).listPrice;
	    
	    MarketListing chosenListing;
	    if (listings.size() <= 3) {
	        chosenListing = listings.get(0);
	    } else {
	        double roll = random.nextDouble();
	        int index;
	        if (roll < 0.70) {
	            index = random.nextInt(listings.size() / 3);
	        } else if (roll < 0.95) {
	            index = listings.size() / 3 + random.nextInt(listings.size() / 3);
	        } else {
	            index = (listings.size() * 2) / 3 + random.nextInt(listings.size() / 3);
	        }
	        chosenListing = listings.get(Math.min(index, listings.size() - 1));
	    }
	    
	    if (chosenListing.listPrice > lowestPrice * 1.15) {
	        int maxIndex = Math.min(listings.size() / 2, listings.size() - 1);
	        chosenListing = listings.get(random.nextInt(maxIndex + 1));
	    }
	    
	    String displayName = chosenListing.item.isStattrak ? 
	        "StatTrak " + chosenListing.item.name : chosenListing.item.name;
	    displayName = cleanStatTrakEncoding(displayName);
	    
	    String specialVariant = null;
	    if (chosenListing.item.blueGemTier != null) {
	        specialVariant = chosenListing.item.blueGemTier;
	    } else if (chosenListing.item.name.contains("Doppler")) {
	        specialVariant = "Doppler";
	    }
	    
	    addSaleRecord(new SaleRecord(
	        displayName,
	        chosenListing.listPrice,
	        chosenListing.item.condition,
	        chosenListing.item.itemFloat,
	        specialVariant
	    ));
	}
	
	private void generateRegularFakeSaleByRarity(String targetRarity) {
	    ArrayList<String> skinsInRarity = new ArrayList<>();
	    for (String skinName : globalMarketListings.keySet()) {
	        String cleanName = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	        if (getSkinRarity(cleanName).equals(targetRarity)) {
	            skinsInRarity.add(skinName);
	        }
	    }
	    
	    if (skinsInRarity.isEmpty()) return;
	    
	    String randomSkin = skinsInRarity.get(random.nextInt(skinsInRarity.size()));
	    ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(randomSkin);
	    
	    if (listings != null && !listings.isEmpty()) {

	        ArrayList<MarketListing> sortedListings = new ArrayList<>(listings);
	        sortedListings.sort(Comparator.comparingDouble(l -> l.listPrice));
	        double lowestPrice = sortedListings.get(0).listPrice;
	        
	        int maxIndex = Math.max(1, (int)(sortedListings.size() * 0.60));
	        MarketListing soldListing = sortedListings.get(random.nextInt(maxIndex));
	        
	        if (soldListing.listPrice > lowestPrice * 1.15) {
	            soldListing = sortedListings.get(random.nextInt(Math.min(5, sortedListings.size())));
	        }
	        
	        String specialVariant = null;
	        if (soldListing.item.blueGemTier != null) {
	            specialVariant = soldListing.item.blueGemTier;
	        } else if (soldListing.item.name.contains("Doppler")) {
	            if (soldListing.item.name.contains("Sapphire")) specialVariant = "Sapphire";
	            else if (soldListing.item.name.contains("Ruby")) specialVariant = "Ruby";
	            else if (soldListing.item.name.contains("Black Pearl")) specialVariant = "Black Pearl";
	            else if (soldListing.item.name.contains("Phase")) {
	                specialVariant = "Doppler";
	            }
	        }
	        
	        String displayName = soldListing.item.isStattrak ? 
	            "StatTrak " + soldListing.item.name : soldListing.item.name;
	        displayName = cleanStatTrakEncoding(displayName);
	        
	        addSaleRecord(new SaleRecord(
	            displayName,
	            soldListing.listPrice,
	            soldListing.item.condition,
	            soldListing.item.itemFloat,
	            specialVariant
	        ));
	    }
	}
	
	private void generateSaleFromActualListing() {
	    ArrayList<String> availableSkins = new ArrayList<>(globalMarketListings.keySet());
	    if (availableSkins.isEmpty()) return;
	    
	    String randomSkin = availableSkins.get(random.nextInt(availableSkins.size()));
	    ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(randomSkin);
	    
	    if (listings == null || listings.isEmpty()) return;
	    
	    ArrayList<MarketListing> sortedListings2 = new ArrayList<>(listings);
	    sortedListings2.sort(Comparator.comparingDouble(l -> l.listPrice));
	    
	    MarketListing chosenListing;
	    if (sortedListings2.size() <= 3) {
	        chosenListing = sortedListings2.get(0);
	    } else {
	        double roll = random.nextDouble();
	        int index;
	        if (roll < 0.70) {
	            index = random.nextInt(sortedListings2.size() / 3);
	        } else if (roll < 0.95) {
	            index = sortedListings2.size() / 3 + random.nextInt(sortedListings2.size() / 3);
	        } else {
	            index = (sortedListings2.size() * 2) / 3 + random.nextInt(sortedListings2.size() / 3);
	        }
	        chosenListing = sortedListings2.get(Math.min(index, sortedListings2.size() - 1));
	    }
	    
	    String displayName = chosenListing.item.isStattrak ? 
	        "StatTrak " + chosenListing.item.name : chosenListing.item.name;
	    displayName = cleanStatTrakEncoding(displayName);
	    
	    String specialVariant = null;
	    if (chosenListing.item.blueGemTier != null) {
	        specialVariant = chosenListing.item.blueGemTier;
	    } else if (chosenListing.item.name.contains("Doppler")) {
	        specialVariant = "Doppler";
	    }
	    
	    addSaleRecord(new SaleRecord(
	        displayName,
	        chosenListing.listPrice, 
	        chosenListing.item.condition,
	        chosenListing.item.itemFloat,
	        specialVariant
	    ));
	}

	private void generateBlueGemSale() {
	    String[] blueGemSkins = {
	        "AK-47 | Case Hardened",
	        "Flip Knife | Case Hardened",
	        "M9 Bayonet | Case Hardened",
	        "Butterfly Knife | Case Hardened"
	    };
	    
	    String skinName = blueGemSkins[random.nextInt(blueGemSkins.length)];
	    String rarity = getSkinRarity(skinName);
	    boolean isKnife = rarity.equals("Knife");
	    
	    String tier;
	    double tierRoll = random.nextDouble();
	    if (tierRoll < 0.02) {
	        tier = "T1";
	    } else if (tierRoll < 0.10) {
	        tier = "T2";
	    } else if (tierRoll < 0.30) {
	        tier = "T3";
	    } else {
	        tier = "T4";
	    }
	    
	    int patternID = 0;
	    if (skinName.contains("Flip Knife")) {
	        List<Integer> patterns = FLIP_KNIFE_BG.get(tier);
	        if (patterns != null && !patterns.isEmpty()) {
	            patternID = patterns.get(random.nextInt(patterns.size()));
	        }
	    } else if (skinName.contains("M9 Bayonet")) {
	        List<Integer> patterns = M9_BG.get(tier);
	        if (patterns != null && !patterns.isEmpty()) {
	            patternID = patterns.get(random.nextInt(patterns.size()));
	        }
	    } else if (skinName.contains("AK-47")) {
	        List<Integer> patterns = AK_BG.get(tier);
	        if (patterns != null && !patterns.isEmpty()) {
	            patternID = patterns.get(random.nextInt(patterns.size()));
	        }
	    } else if (skinName.contains("Butterfly Knife")) {
	        List<Integer> patterns = BUTTERFLY_BG.get(tier);
	        if (patterns != null && !patterns.isEmpty()) {
	            patternID = patterns.get(random.nextInt(patterns.size()));
	        }
	    }
	    
	    String[] availableConditions = getAvailableConditions(skinName);
	    String condition = availableConditions[random.nextInt(availableConditions.length)];
	    double itemFloat = generateFloatForCondition(skinName, condition);
	    
	    double basePrice = getBasePrice(skinName);
	    
	    if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	        basePrice *= 2.5;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	        basePrice *= 1.7;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	        basePrice *= 1.0;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	        basePrice *= 0.7;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
	        basePrice *= 0.3;
	    }
	    
	    String blueGemTier = "Blue Gem " + tier;
	    double price = applyBlueGemMultiplier(skinName, patternID, blueGemTier, basePrice);
	    
	    boolean isStattrak = random.nextDouble() < 0.15;
	    if (isStattrak) {
	        if (isKnife) {
	            price *= 1.15; 
	        } else {
	            price *= 3.0; 
	        }
	    }
	    
	    double marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarity, 1.0);
	    price *= marketMulti;
	    
	    String displayName = (isStattrak ? "StatTrak " : "") + skinName + " (" + blueGemTier + ")";
	    displayName = cleanStatTrakEncoding(displayName);
	    
	    addSaleRecord(new SaleRecord(
	        displayName,
	        price,
	        condition,
	        itemFloat,
	        blueGemTier
	    ));
	}
	
	private JPanel createPlayerPurchasesPanel() {
	    Color BG_DARK  = new Color(15, 15, 20);
	    Color BG_PANEL = new Color(22, 22, 30);
	    Color BG_ROW   = new Color(30, 30, 40);
	    Color BG_ROW_ALT = new Color(25, 25, 35);
	    Color TEXT_MAIN = new Color(220, 220, 230);
	    Color ACCENT2   = new Color(95, 200, 255);
	    Color HEADER_BG = new Color(35, 50, 70);

	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    panel.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    
	    String[] columns = {"Time", "Skin", "Condition", "Float", "Price", "Special"};
	    DefaultTableModel model = new DefaultTableModel(columns, 0) {
	        @Override public boolean isCellEditable(int row, int column) { return false; }
	    };
	    
	    JTable table = new JTable(model);
	    table.setRowHeight(26);
	    table.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	    table.setBackground(BG_ROW);
	    table.setForeground(TEXT_MAIN);
	    table.setGridColor(new Color(40, 40, 55));
	    table.setSelectionBackground(new Color(50, 80, 110));
	    table.setSelectionForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    table.getTableHeader().setBackground(HEADER_BG);
	    table.getTableHeader().setForeground(ACCENT2);
	    table.getTableHeader().setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    table.setShowHorizontalLines(true);
	    table.setShowVerticalLines(false);

	    table.setDefaultRenderer(Object.class, new javax.swing.table.DefaultTableCellRenderer() {
	        @Override public java.awt.Component getTableCellRendererComponent(
	                JTable t, Object v, boolean sel, boolean foc, int row, int col) {
	            super.getTableCellRendererComponent(t, v, sel, foc, row, col);
	            setBackground(sel ? new Color(50, 80, 110) : (row % 2 == 0 ? BG_ROW : BG_ROW_ALT));
	            setForeground(col == 4 ? new Color(255, 210, 60) : TEXT_MAIN);
	            setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(0, 4, 0, 4));
	            return this;
	        }
	    });
	    table.getColumnModel().getColumn(0).setPreferredWidth(80);
	    table.getColumnModel().getColumn(1).setPreferredWidth(250);
	    table.getColumnModel().getColumn(2).setPreferredWidth(120);
	    table.getColumnModel().getColumn(3).setPreferredWidth(100);
	    table.getColumnModel().getColumn(4).setPreferredWidth(80);
	    table.getColumnModel().getColumn(5).setPreferredWidth(150);
	    
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(table);
	    scroll.getViewport().setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    scroll.setBorder(null);
	    panel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    JLabel infoLabel = new JLabel("  Your Purchase History", SwingConstants.LEFT);
	    infoLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));
	    infoLabel.setForeground(ACCENT2);
	    infoLabel.setOpaque(true);
	    infoLabel.setBackground(HEADER_BG);
	    infoLabel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 8, 8, 8));
	    panel.add(infoLabel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    final int[] lastKnownSize = {-1};
	    javax.swing.Timer updateTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(1000, e -> {

	        if (playerPurchases.size() != lastKnownSize[0]) {
	            lastKnownSize[0] = playerPurchases.size();
	            model.setRowCount(0);
	        } else {

	            for (int row = 0; row < model.getRowCount(); row++) {
	                int realIdx = playerPurchases.size() - 1 - row;
	                if (realIdx < 0) break;
	                long secondsAgo = (System.currentTimeMillis() - playerPurchases.get(realIdx).timestamp) / 1000;
	                String t = secondsAgo < 60 ? secondsAgo + "s ago" : secondsAgo < 3600 ? (secondsAgo/60) + "m ago" : (secondsAgo/3600) + "h ago";
	                model.setValueAt(t, row, 0);
	            }
	            return;
	        }
	        for (int i = playerPurchases.size() - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
	            SaleRecord sale = playerPurchases.get(i);
	            long secondsAgo = (System.currentTimeMillis() - sale.timestamp) / 1000;
	            String timeStr;
	            if (secondsAgo < 60) {
	                timeStr = secondsAgo + "s ago";
	            } else if (secondsAgo < 3600) {
	                timeStr = (secondsAgo / 60) + "m ago";
	            } else {
	                timeStr = (secondsAgo / 3600) + "h ago";
	            }
	            
	            model.addRow(new Object[]{
	                timeStr,
	                sale.skinName,
	                sale.condition,
	                String.format("%.6f", sale.itemFloat),
	                "$" + String.format("%.2f", sale.price),
	                sale.specialVariant != null ? sale.specialVariant : "-"
	            });
	        }
	    });

	    panel.addHierarchyListener(e -> {
	        if ((e.getChangeFlags() & java.awt.event.HierarchyEvent.SHOWING_CHANGED) != 0
	                && !panel.isShowing()) {
	            updateTimer.stop();
	        }
	    });
	    updateTimer.start();
	    
	    return panel;
	}
	
	private void openCrateWithAnimation() {
	    double casePrice = currentCase.price;

	    if (balance < casePrice) {
	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "Out of money!");
	        return;
	    }

	    if (animationFrame != null && animationFrame.isDisplayable()) {
	        animationFrame.dispose();
	    }

	    balance -= casePrice;
	    updateBalanceLabel();
	    totalCrates++;

	    currentCase.timesOpened++;
	    currentCase.totalSpent += casePrice;

	    isAnimating = true;

	    openCrateButton.setVisible(false);
	    openCrateButton.setEnabled(false);
	    closeCrateButton.setVisible(false);
	    autoOpenButton.setVisible(false);
	    mainTabs.setEnabled(false);

	    String item = crateItem(currentCase);
	    generateFinalSkinDetails(item);

	    JDialog animDialog = new JDialog(this, "Opening Case...", false);
	    animDialog.setSize(800, 300);
	    animDialog.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    animDialog.setUndecorated(true);
	    animDialog.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    animDialog.getRootPane().setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(247, 147, 30), 2));

	    animDialog.addWindowFocusListener(new java.awt.event.WindowFocusListener() {
	        public void windowGainedFocus(java.awt.event.WindowEvent e) {}
	        public void windowLostFocus(java.awt.event.WindowEvent e) {
	            if (animDialog.isVisible()) animDialog.toFront();
	        }
	    });

	    animationFrame = new JFrame("Opening Case...") {
	        @Override public void dispose() { animDialog.dispose(); super.dispose(); }
	        @Override public void setVisible(boolean v) {}
	        @Override public boolean isDisplayable() { return animDialog.isDisplayable(); }
	    };

	    animationPanel = new AnimationPanel();
	    animDialog.add(animationPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JLabel openingLabel = new JLabel("Opening " + currentCase.name + "...", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    openingLabel.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    openingLabel.setForeground(new Color(95, 200, 255));
	    openingLabel.setBackground(new Color(15, 15, 20));
	    openingLabel.setOpaque(true);
	    openingLabel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(6, 0, 6, 0));
	    animDialog.add(openingLabel, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel glass = new JPanel();
	    glass.setOpaque(false);
	    glass.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {});
	    glass.addMouseMotionListener(new java.awt.event.MouseMotionAdapter() {});
	    setGlassPane(glass);
	    glass.setVisible(true);

	    animDialog.setVisible(true);

	    double randomBias = (random.nextDouble() - 0.5) * 120.0;
	    final double targetPosition = animationPanel.getFinalSkinPosition()
	            - (animDialog.getWidth() / 2) + 75 + randomBias;

	    final double maxSpeed  = 58.0;
	    final double accel     = 2.4;
	    final double decelZone = 1800.0;
	    final double stopVel   = 0.15;

	    javax.swing.Timer scrollTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(16, null);
	    scrollTimer.addActionListener(new ActionListener() {
	        private double currentOffset = 0.0;
	        private double velocity = 0.0;

	        @Override
	        public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
	            double distance = targetPosition - currentOffset;

	            if (distance > decelZone) {
	                velocity = Math.min(velocity + accel, maxSpeed);
	            } else {
	                double factor = distance / decelZone;
	                velocity = maxSpeed * factor;
	            }

	            if (distance < 260) {
	                velocity *= 0.96;
	            }

	            velocity = Math.min(velocity, distance);
	            currentOffset += velocity;
	            animationPanel.setScrollOffset((int) currentOffset);

	            if (velocity < stopVel) {
	                scrollTimer.stop();
	                javax.swing.Timer delayTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(1000, evt -> {
	                    animDialog.dispose();
	                    getGlassPane().setVisible(false);
	                    isAnimating = false;
	                    displayFinalResult(item);
	                });
	                delayTimer.setRepeats(false);
	                delayTimer.start();
	            }
	        }
	    });

	    scrollTimer.start();
	}
	
	private void generateFinalSkinDetails(String item) {
	    String selectedSkinName = "";
	    Image originalSkin = null;
	    
	    if (item.contains("Gloves")) {
	        totGlove += 1;

	        int i = random.nextInt(gloveSkins.length);
	        originalSkin = gloveSkins[i];

	        String[] gloveNames = {
	            "Bloodhound Gloves | Bronzed",
	            "Bloodhound Gloves | Charred",
	            "Bloodhound Gloves | Guerrilla",
	            "Bloodhound Gloves | Snakebite",
	            "Driver Gloves | Convoy",
	            "Driver Gloves | Crimson Weave",
	            "Driver Gloves | Diamondback",
	            "Driver Gloves | Lunar Weave",
	            "Hand Wraps | Badlands",
	            "Hand Wraps | Leather",
	            "Hand Wraps | Slaughter",
	            "Hand Wraps | Spruce DDPAT",
	            "Moto Gloves | Boom!",
	            "Moto Gloves | Cool Mint",
	            "Moto Gloves | Eclipse",
	            "Moto Gloves | Spearmint",
	            "Specialist Gloves | Crimson Kimono",
	            "Specialist Gloves | Emerald Web",
	            "Specialist Gloves | Forest DDPAT",
	            "Specialist Gloves | Foundation",
	            "Sport Gloves | Arid",
	            "Sport Gloves | Hedge Maze",
	            "Sport Gloves | Pandora's Box",
	            "Sport Gloves | Superconductor"
	        };
	        selectedSkinName = gloveNames[i % gloveNames.length];
	    } else if (item.contains("Knife")) {
	        totKnife += 1;

	        int i = random.nextInt(knifeSkins.length);
	        originalSkin = knifeSkins[i];

	        String[] names = {
	            "Karambit | Slaughter",
	            "M9 Bayonet | Crimson Web",
	            "Flip Knife | Vanilla",
	            "Gut Knife | Fade",
	            "Bayonet | Scorched",
	            "Bayonet | Boreal Forest",
	            "Bayonet | Fade",
	            "Flip Knife | Case Hardened",
	            "Gut Knife | Forest DDPAT",
	            "Gut Knife | Safari Mesh",
	            "Karambit | Night",
	            "Karambit | Crimson Web",
	            "Karambit | Scorched",
	            "Karambit | Urban Masked",
	            "M9 Bayonet | Blue Steel",
	            "M9 Bayonet | Case Hardened",
	            "M9 Bayonet | Slaughter",
	            "M9 Bayonet | Doppler",
	            "Karambit | Doppler",
	            "Butterfly Knife | Case Hardened",
	            "Butterfly Knife | Crimson Web",
	            "Butterfly Knife | Fade",
	            "Butterfly Knife | Safari Mesh",
	            "Butterfly Knife | Slaughter",
	            "Butterfly Knife | Urban Masked",
	            "Butterfly Knife | Vanilla",
	            "Butterfly Knife | Ultraviolet",
	            "Huntsman Knife | Marble Fade",
	            "Huntsman Knife | Tiger Tooth",
	            "Bowie Knife | Marble Fade",
	            "Bowie Knife | Tiger Tooth",
	            "Falchion Knife | Marble Fade",
	            "Falchion Knife | Tiger Tooth"
	        };
	        selectedSkinName = names[i % names.length];

	        if (selectedSkinName.contains("Doppler")) {
	            double dr = random.nextDouble();
	            if (dr < 0.05) {
	                String[] gems = { "Sapphire", "Ruby", "Black Pearl" };
	                String gem = gems[random.nextInt(gems.length)];
	                selectedSkinName += " (" + gem + ")";
	            } else {
	                int phase = 1 + random.nextInt(4);
	                selectedSkinName += " (Phase " + phase + ")";
	            }
	        }
	    } else if (item.contains("Covert")) {
	        totCov += 1;
	        missionCovertsUnboxed++;
	        TradeUpCollection col = getCurrentCaseCollection();
	        String[] pool = (col != null && col.covertSkins.length > 0) ? col.covertSkins : new String[]{"AWP | Lightning Strike"};
	        selectedSkinName = pool[random.nextInt(pool.length)];
	        originalSkin = skinImageMap.getOrDefault(selectedSkinName, redSkins[0]);
	    } else if (item.contains("Classified")) {
	        totClass += 1;
	        missionClassifiedsUnboxed++;
	        TradeUpCollection col = getCurrentCaseCollection();
	        String[] pool = (col != null && col.classifiedSkins.length > 0) ? col.classifiedSkins : new String[]{"Desert Eagle | Hypnotic"};
	        selectedSkinName = pool[random.nextInt(pool.length)];
	        originalSkin = skinImageMap.getOrDefault(selectedSkinName, pinkSkins[0]);
	    } else if (item.contains("Restricted")) {
	        totRes += 1;
	        TradeUpCollection col = getCurrentCaseCollection();
	        String[] pool = (col != null && col.restrictedSkins.length > 0) ? col.restrictedSkins : new String[]{"Glock-18 | Dragon Tattoo"};
	        selectedSkinName = pool[random.nextInt(pool.length)];
	        originalSkin = skinImageMap.getOrDefault(selectedSkinName, purpleSkins[0]);
	    } else if (item.contains("Milspec")) {
	        totMil += 1;
	        TradeUpCollection col = getCurrentCaseCollection();
	        String[] pool = (col != null && col.milspecSkins.length > 0) ? col.milspecSkins : new String[]{"MP7 | Skulls"};
	        selectedSkinName = pool[random.nextInt(pool.length)];
	        originalSkin = skinImageMap.getOrDefault(selectedSkinName, blueSkins[0]);
	    }

	    Image dopplerOverride = getKnifeImage(selectedSkinName);
	    if (dopplerOverride != null) {
	        originalSkin = dopplerOverride;
	    }

	    double itemFloat = applyFloatLimits(selectedSkinName, random.nextDouble());
	    String rarityKey = item.replace("StatTrak ", "");
	    double marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarityKey, 1.0);
	    double basePrice = getBasePrice(selectedSkinName);

	    if (itemFloat <= 0.07) {
	        finalCondition = "Factory New";
	    } else if (itemFloat <= 0.15) {
	        finalCondition = "Minimal Wear";
	    } else if (itemFloat <= 0.38) {
	        finalCondition = "Field-Tested";
	    } else if (itemFloat <= 0.45) {
	        finalCondition = "Well-Worn";
	    } else {
	        finalCondition = "Battle-Scarred";
	    }

	    double variance = 0.85 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.3);
	    double bonusPrice = basePrice * marketMulti * variance * priceMulti;

	    if (item.contains("Gloves")) {
	        double gloveBasePrice = getGloveBasePrice(selectedSkinName);
	        bonusPrice = calculateGlovePrice(selectedSkinName, finalCondition, gloveBasePrice);
	        bonusPrice *= marketMulti * variance;
	    } else if (finalCondition.equals("Factory New")) {
	        bonusPrice *= 2.5;
	    } else if (finalCondition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	        bonusPrice *= 1.7;
	    } else if (finalCondition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	        bonusPrice *= 1.0;
	    } else if (finalCondition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	        bonusPrice *= 0.7;
	    } else if (finalCondition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
	        bonusPrice *= 0.3;
	    }

	    boolean isRareGem = selectedSkinName.contains("Sapphire") || 
	                        selectedSkinName.contains("Ruby") || 
	                        selectedSkinName.contains("Black Pearl");

	    if (!item.contains("Knife") && !item.contains("Gloves")) {
	        if (itemFloat <= 0.0005) {
	            bonusPrice *= 3.0;
	        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.001) {
	            bonusPrice *= 2.0;
	        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.005) {
	            bonusPrice *= 1.5;
	        } else if (itemFloat <= 0.02) {
	            bonusPrice *= 1.25;
	        }
	    } else if (item.contains("Knife") && !isRareGem) {
	        double rel = getRelativeFloat(selectedSkinName, itemFloat);
	        if (!isCappedKnife(selectedSkinName)) {
	            if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                bonusPrice *= 2.5;
	            } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                bonusPrice *= 1.5;
	            } else if (rel <= 0.20) {
	                bonusPrice *= 1.1;
	            }
	        } else {
	            if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                bonusPrice *= 1.15;
	            } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                bonusPrice *= 1.05;
	            }
	        }
	    }

	    if (isStattrak == 1 && !item.contains("Gloves")) {
	        if (item.contains("Knife")) {
	            if (selectedSkinName.contains("Crimson Web")) {
	                bonusPrice *= 1.0;
	            } else if (selectedSkinName.contains("Doppler")) {
	                bonusPrice *= 0.80;
	            } else {
	                bonusPrice *= 0.95;
	            }
	        } else {
	            double stGunMult = 1.70 + random.nextDouble() * 0.30;
	            bonusPrice *= stGunMult;
	        }
	    }

	    int patternID = random.nextInt(1000);
	    String blueGemTier = getBlueGemTier(selectedSkinName, patternID);
	    if (blueGemTier != null) {
	        selectedSkinName = selectedSkinName + " (" + blueGemTier + ")";
	        bonusPrice = applyBlueGemMultiplier(selectedSkinName, patternID, blueGemTier, bonusPrice);
	    }

	    bonusPrice = capPriceToMarket(selectedSkinName, finalCondition, isStattrak == 1, bonusPrice, blueGemTier);

	    finalSkin = originalSkin;
	    finalSkinName = selectedSkinName;
	    finalPrice = bonusPrice;
	    finalFloat = itemFloat;
	    finalPatternID = patternID;
	    finalBlueGemTier = blueGemTier;
	}
	
	private void displayFinalResult(String item) {
	    playSound(unboxSound);
	    crateImage = null;
