	    if (finalSkin != null) {
	        int maxWidth = 280;
	        int maxHeight = 200;
	        int origWidth = finalSkin.getWidth(null);
	        int origHeight = finalSkin.getHeight(null);
	        double scale = Math.min((double) maxWidth / origWidth, (double) maxHeight / origHeight);
	        int newWidth = (int) (origWidth * scale);
	        int newHeight = (int) (origHeight * scale);
	        skinImage = finalSkin.getScaledInstance(newWidth, newHeight, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH);
	    }
	    updateCrateImageDisplay();
	    
	    addUnboxedSkin(finalSkinName);
	       
	    String displayName = finalSkinName;
	    if (isStattrak == 1 && !item.contains("Gloves")) {
	        displayName = "StatTrak " + finalSkinName;
	    }
	    
	    rarityLabel.setForeground(rarityColor);
	    if (isStattrak == 1 && !item.contains("Gloves")) {
	        rarityLabel.setText("StatTrak " + item);
	    } else {
	        rarityLabel.setText(item);
	    }
	    
	    nameLabel.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 44));
	    nameLabel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(780, 44));
	    
	    if (isStattrak == 1 && !item.contains("Gloves")) {
	        nameLabel.setForeground(new Color(255, 140, 0));
	    } else {
	    	nameLabel.setForeground(new Color(230, 230, 235));
	    }
	    
	    // Auto-scale font to fit name on one line
	    {
	        int fontSize = 28;
	        Font testFont = new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, fontSize);
	        java.awt.FontMetrics fm = nameLabel.getFontMetrics(testFont);
	        while (fontSize > 14 && fm.stringWidth(displayName) > 755) {
	            fontSize -= 2;
	            testFont = new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, fontSize);
	            fm = nameLabel.getFontMetrics(testFont);
	        }
	        nameLabel.setFont(testFont);
	    }
	    nameLabel.setText("<html><span style='white-space: nowrap;'>" + displayName + "</span></html>");
	    
	    priceLabel.setText("Price: $" + String.format("%.2f", finalPrice));
	    floatLabel.setText(String.format("Float: %.10f", finalFloat));
	    conditionLabel.setText("Wear: " + finalCondition);
	    patternId.setText("Pattern: " + finalPatternID);
	    String unboxColName = getCollectionName(finalSkinName);
	    collectionLabel.setText(unboxColName != null ? "Collection: " + unboxColName : "");

	    if (lowestFloat > finalFloat) {
	        lowestFloat = finalFloat;
	    }

	    inventoryValue += finalPrice;
	    
	    updateLeaderboard();
	    
	    newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

	    lowFloatLabel.setText(String.format("Lowest Float: %.10f", lowestFloat));
	    totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);

	    writeStats();

	    String cleanItemRarity;

	    if (isStattrak == 1 && !item.contains("Gloves")) {
	        cleanItemRarity = "StatTrak " + item;
	    } else {
	        cleanItemRarity = item;
	    }

	    // Downscale to 130x88 max before storing in InventoryItem to save memory
	    Image storeImg5 = skinImage;
	    if (storeImg5 != null) {
	        int iw5 = storeImg5.getWidth(null), ih5 = storeImg5.getHeight(null);
	        if (iw5 > 130 || ih5 > 88) {
	            double s5 = Math.min(130.0/iw5, 88.0/ih5);
	            storeImg5 = storeImg5.getScaledInstance((int)(iw5*s5),(int)(ih5*s5), Image.SCALE_FAST);
	        }
	    }
	    InventoryItem unboxedItem = new InventoryItem(new ImageIcon(storeImg5), finalSkinName, finalCondition,
	            cleanItemRarity, BigDecimal.valueOf(finalPrice).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	            finalFloat, (isStattrak == 1 && !item.contains("Gloves")), finalPatternID,
	            finalBlueGemTier, finalPrice);
	    unboxedItem.collection = getCollectionName(finalSkinName);
	    inventoryList.add(unboxedItem);
	    
	    currentCase.totalReceived += finalPrice;
	    openingProfit += (finalPrice - currentCase.price);

	    BigDecimal roundedProfit = BigDecimal
	            .valueOf(openingProfit)
	            .setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

	    if (roundedProfit.signum() >= 0) {
	        profitLabel.setForeground(new Color(0, 160, 0));
	        profitLabel.setText("Opening Profit: +$" + roundedProfit);
	    } else {
	        profitLabel.setForeground(Color.RED);
	        profitLabel.setText("Opening Profit: -$" + roundedProfit.abs());
	    }
	    
	    trackOpeningStreak();
	    
	    checkUnboxingAchievements(item, finalSkinName, finalPrice, finalFloat, 
	                             finalBlueGemTier, totMil, totRes, totClass, totCov, totKnife, isStattrak);

	    openCrateButton.setVisible(false);
	    closeCrateButton.setVisible(true);
	    autoOpenButton.setVisible(true);
	    autoOpenButton.setEnabled(true);
	    mainTabs.setEnabled(true);
	    
	    repaint();
	}
	public static class TradeOffer {
	    String npcName;
	    Image npcAvatar;
	    ArrayList<InventoryItem> npcOfferedItems;
	    double npcOfferedMoney;
	    ArrayList<InventoryItem> npcRequestedItems;
	    double npcRequestedMoney;
	    long timestamp;
	    boolean isAccepted;
	    boolean isDeclined;
	    String tradeId;
	    
	    public TradeOffer(String npcName, Image npcAvatar, ArrayList<InventoryItem> offered, 
	                     double offeredMoney, ArrayList<InventoryItem> requested, double requestedMoney) {
	        this.npcName = npcName;
	        this.npcAvatar = npcAvatar;
	        this.npcOfferedItems = new ArrayList<>(offered);
	        this.npcOfferedMoney = offeredMoney;
	        this.npcRequestedItems = new ArrayList<>(requested);
	        this.npcRequestedMoney = requestedMoney;
	        this.timestamp = System.currentTimeMillis();
	        this.isAccepted = false;
	        this.isDeclined = false;
	        this.tradeId = "TRADE_" + System.currentTimeMillis() + "_" + random.nextInt(1000);
	    }
	}
	
	private void startTradeGenerationTimer() {
	    tradeGenerationTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(
	        TRADE_GENERATION_MIN + random.nextInt(TRADE_GENERATION_RANGE), 
	        e -> {
	            SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	                generateRandomTrade();
	                int nextDelay = TRADE_GENERATION_MIN + random.nextInt(TRADE_GENERATION_RANGE);
	                tradeGenerationTimer.setDelay(nextDelay);
	            });
	        }
	    );
	    tradeGenerationTimer.start();
	}
	
	private void generateRandomTrade() {
	    if (inventoryList.isEmpty() && balance <= 0) {
	        return;
	    }

	    final int MAX_ATTEMPTS = 15;

	    for (int attempt = 0; attempt < MAX_ATTEMPTS; attempt++) {

	        String[] npcNames = {
	        		"xX_DarkWolf_Xx", "its_ya_boi_69", "ProGamer2008",
	        		"Shadow_Killerz", "lolNoScopeXD", "urWorstNightmare",
	        		"cooldude_123", "xxsniperxx", "EpicFailGuy",
	        		"ILovePizzaLOL", "DragonSlayer_99", "masterchief_real",
	        		"NotAFurryIPromise", "MrStealYoWin", "TryHard_Mode",
	        		"Owned_U_Once", "BasedGamer", "TooGood4U",
	        		"KidDestroyer420", "ClutchOrKick", "NoobSlayer_XD",
	        		"xXPureSkillXx", "HeadshotMachine", "EZClapsOnly",
	        		"LagMadeMeDie", "MomSaidNoMic", "DefinitelyPro",
	        		"ClickAndPray", "WallbangKing", "TryHardSince09",
	        		"ScopeAndHope", "KeyboardWarrior", "RespawnLegend",
	        		"PingIsTrash", "OneTapOrCry", "RankedAnxiety",
	        		"SilverButMad", "JustBetterBro", "AimAssistPls",
	        		"SkillIssueLOL", "FragDaddy", "SprayAndPray",
	        		"EcoRoundHero", "SmokeDiff", "FlashMeDaddy",
	        		"BombHasBeenPlanted", "FakeDefuse", "KnifeOnlyBTW",
	        		"ShiftWalking", "PreFireGod", "WidePeekEnjoyer",
	        		"CrosshairPlacement", "AngleHolder", "CTSideEnjoyer",
	        		"TSideWarlord", "EntryFragOrDie", "TradeMeBro",
	        		"LastAliveAgain", "ClutchingTime", "SaveRoundPls",
	        		"BuyNextRound", "ForceBuyKing", "DeagleMain",
	        		"AKTapper", "AWPMerchant", "ScopedIn",
	        		"DryPeekLegend", "UtilityDiff", "RetakeMaster",
	        		"PostPlantGod", "AntiEcoVictim", "PeekersAdvantage",
	        		"EcoWarrior", "BottomFragHero", "TopFragNoImpact",
	        		"SoloQueuePain", "MutedTeammate", "AFKForDinner",
	        		"LostToPistols", "JumpShotEnjoyer", "ReloadingNow",
	        		"MissedSprayAgain", "FlickOrFeed", "ShiftKeyBroken",
	        		"RadarBlind", "SoundWhorePro", "SmokeMisplaced",
	        		"PopflashFail", "NadeDamageEnjoyer", "TeamFlashKing",
	        		"AccidentalJump", "NoScopeDreams", "WhiffedAgain",
	        		"RunningHeadshot", "LuckyOneTap", "BuyArmorPls",
	        		"DroppedMyAK", "KnifeOutMid", "BoostGoneWrong",
	        		"MidRushB", "RotateTooLate", "WrongSiteAgain",
	        		"HoldingFlank", "PushedThroughSmoke", "DrySwingOnly",
	        		"UtilitySaving", "DroppedTheBomb", "FakeStratCaller",
	        		"BaitedByTeammate", "LastPlaceAgain", "WarmupLegend",
	        		"ColdHandsIRL", "MousepadTooSmall", "SensitivityCrisis",
	        		"CrosshairTooBig", "CrosshairTooSmall", "FPSDropEnjoyer",
	        		"AltTabbedMidRound", "DiscordMutedMe", "CalloutsConfused",
	        		"LostTheClutch", "AlmostAce", "EcoAceDreamer",
	        		"KnifeKillSeeker", "JumpThrowFail", "ForgotToReload",
	        		"AFKAtSpawn", "WrongBuyAgain", "HelmetForgotten",
	        		"ScopedTooLong", "WideSwingOnly", "TimingHatesMe",
	        		"OneBulletLeft", "LagSpikeNow", "DisconnectedAgain"

	        };

	        String npcName = npcNames[random.nextInt(npcNames.length)];
	        Image npcAvatar = npcAvatars[random.nextInt(npcAvatars.length)];

	        ArrayList<InventoryItem> offered = new ArrayList<>();
	        ArrayList<InventoryItem> requested = new ArrayList<>();
	        double offeredMoney = 0;
	        double requestedMoney = 0;

	        boolean canUseMoneyTrades = balance > 0;
	        boolean shouldOfferBlueGem = random.nextDouble() < 0.10;

	        int tradeType;
	        if (inventoryList.isEmpty()) {
	            tradeType = canUseMoneyTrades ? 4 : 1;
	        } else {
	        	tradeType = random.nextInt(shouldOfferBlueGem ? 5 : 4) + 1;
	        }

	        if (tradeType == 1) {
	            int count = 1 + random.nextInt(Math.min(2, inventoryList.size()));
	            double requestedValue = 0;

	            while (requested.size() < count) {
	                InventoryItem item = inventoryList.get(random.nextInt(inventoryList.size()));
	                if (!requested.contains(item)) {
	                    requested.add(item);
	                    requestedValue += item.price.doubleValue();
	                }
	            }

	            double targetValue = requestedValue * (0.85 + random.nextDouble() * 0.20);
	            double currentValue = 0;

	            for (int i = 0; i < 15 && currentValue < targetValue * 0.90; i++) {
	                InventoryItem item = generateRandomNPCItem();
	                double price = item.price.doubleValue();
	                if (currentValue + price > targetValue * 1.15) break;
	                offered.add(item);
	                currentValue += price;
	            }

	        } else if (tradeType == 2) {
	            int count = 1 + random.nextInt(Math.min(2, inventoryList.size()));
	            double totalValue = 0;

	            while (requested.size() < count) {
	                InventoryItem item = inventoryList.get(random.nextInt(inventoryList.size()));
	                if (!requested.contains(item)) {
	                    requested.add(item);
	                    totalValue += item.price.doubleValue();
	                }
	            }

	            offeredMoney = totalValue * (0.85 + random.nextDouble() * 0.15);

	        } else if (tradeType == 3) {
	            InventoryItem yourItem = inventoryList.get(random.nextInt(inventoryList.size()));
	            requested.add(yourItem);

	            double targetValue = yourItem.price.doubleValue() * (0.90 + random.nextDouble() * 0.20);
	            double currentValue = 0;

	            for (int i = 0; i < 15 && currentValue < targetValue * 0.90; i++) {
	                InventoryItem item = generateRandomNPCItem();
	                double price = item.price.doubleValue();
	                if (currentValue + price > targetValue * 1.15) break;
	                offered.add(item);
	                currentValue += price;
	            }

	        } else if (tradeType == 4 && canUseMoneyTrades) {
	            InventoryItem item = generateRandomNPCItem();
	            offered.add(item);
	            double value = item.price.doubleValue();

	            if (random.nextDouble() < 0.3) {
	                InventoryItem extra = generateRandomNPCItem();
	                offered.add(extra);
	                value += extra.price.doubleValue();
	            }

	            requestedMoney = Math.min(
	                balance,
	                value * (0.95 + random.nextDouble() * 0.10)
	            );

	        } else if (tradeType == 5 && canUseMoneyTrades) {
	            InventoryItem blueGem = generateRandomBlueGemItem();
	            offered.add(blueGem);
	            double gemValue = blueGem.price.doubleValue();

	            if (random.nextDouble() < 0.5 || inventoryList.isEmpty()) {
	                requestedMoney = Math.min(
	                    balance,
	                    gemValue * (0.90 + random.nextDouble() * 0.05)
	                );
	            } else {
	                double targetValue = gemValue * (0.95 + random.nextDouble() * 0.10);
	                double currentValue = 0;

	                for (int i = 0; i < 20 && currentValue < targetValue * 0.85; i++) {
	                    InventoryItem item = inventoryList.get(random.nextInt(inventoryList.size()));
	                    if (!requested.contains(item)) {
	                        requested.add(item);
	                        currentValue += item.price.doubleValue();
	                    }
	                }

	                if (currentValue < targetValue * 0.70) {
	                    requested.clear();
	                    requestedMoney = Math.min(
	                        balance,
	                        gemValue * (0.90 + random.nextDouble() * 0.05)
	                    );
	                }
	            }
	        }

	        if ((offered.isEmpty() && offeredMoney == 0) ||
	            (requested.isEmpty() && requestedMoney == 0)) {
	            continue;
	        }

	        if (requestedMoney > balance) continue;
	        if (balance <= 0 && requestedMoney > 0) continue;

	        double offeredTotal = offeredMoney +
	            offered.stream().mapToDouble(i -> i.price.doubleValue()).sum();

	        double requestedTotal = requestedMoney +
	            requested.stream().mapToDouble(i -> i.price.doubleValue()).sum();

	        if (offeredTotal <= 0 || requestedTotal <= 0) continue;

	        double ratio = offeredTotal / requestedTotal;
	        if (ratio < 0.60 || ratio > 1.40) continue;

	        TradeOffer trade = new TradeOffer(
	            npcName, npcAvatar, offered, offeredMoney, requested, requestedMoney
	        );
	        synchronized (pendingTrades) {
	            pendingTrades.add(trade);
	        }
	        unreadTradesCount++;
	        updateTradeNotification();
	        return;
	    }
	}
	
	private InventoryItem generateRandomBlueGemItem() {
	    String[] blueGemSkins = {
	        "AK-47 | Case Hardened",
	        "Flip Knife | Case Hardened",
	        "M9 Bayonet | Case Hardened",
	        "Butterfly Knife | Case Hardened"
	    };
	    
	    String skinName = blueGemSkins[random.nextInt(blueGemSkins.length)];
	    String rarity = getSkinRarity(skinName);
	    boolean isKnife = rarity.equals("Knife");
	    double basePrice = getBasePrice(skinName);
	    
	    String tier;
	    double tierRoll = random.nextDouble();
	    if (tierRoll < 0.05) {
	        tier = "T1";
	    } else if (tierRoll < 0.20) {
	        tier = "T2";
	    } else if (tierRoll < 0.50) {
	        tier = "T3";
	    } else {
	        tier = "T4";
	    }
	    
	    int patternID = 0;
	    if (skinName.contains("Flip Knife")) {
	        List<Integer> patterns = FLIP_KNIFE_BG.get(tier);
	        if (patterns != null && !patterns.isEmpty()) {
	            patternID = patterns.get(random.nextInt(patterns.size()));
	        }
	    } else if (skinName.contains("M9 Bayonet")) {
	        List<Integer> patterns = M9_BG.get(tier);
	        if (patterns != null && !patterns.isEmpty()) {
	            patternID = patterns.get(random.nextInt(patterns.size()));
	        }
	    } else if (skinName.contains("AK-47")) {
	        List<Integer> patterns = AK_BG.get(tier);
	        if (patterns != null && !patterns.isEmpty()) {
	            patternID = patterns.get(random.nextInt(patterns.size()));
	        }
	    } else if (skinName.contains("Butterfly Knife")) {
	        List<Integer> patterns = BUTTERFLY_BG.get(tier);
	        if (patterns != null && !patterns.isEmpty()) {
	            patternID = patterns.get(random.nextInt(patterns.size()));
	        }
	    }
	    
	    String[] availableConditions = getAvailableConditions(skinName);
	    String condition = availableConditions[random.nextInt(availableConditions.length)];
	    double itemFloat = generateFloatForCondition(skinName, condition);
	    
	    double price = basePrice;
	    if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	        price *= 2.5;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	        price *= 1.7;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	        price *= 1.0;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	        price *= 0.7;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
	        price *= 0.3;
	    }
	    
	    String blueGemTier = "Blue Gem " + tier;
	    price = applyBlueGemMultiplier(skinName, patternID, blueGemTier, price);
	    
	    boolean isStattrak = random.nextDouble() < 0.10;
	    if (isStattrak) {
	        if (isKnife) {
	            price *= 1.15;
	        } else {
	            price *= 3.0;
	        }
	    }
	    
	    double marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarity, 1.0);
	    price *= marketMulti;
	    
	    double trueBasePrice = price / marketMulti;
	    
	    Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(skinName);
	    
	    String displayRarity = isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + rarity : rarity;
	    String fullSkinName = skinName + " (" + blueGemTier + ")";
	    
	    return new InventoryItem(
	        skinImg != null ? new ImageIcon(skinImg) : null,
	        fullSkinName,
	        condition,
	        displayRarity,
	        BigDecimal.valueOf(price).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	        itemFloat,
	        isStattrak,
	        patternID,
	        blueGemTier,
	        trueBasePrice
	    );
	}

	        "P90 | Asiimov", "M4A1-S | Cyrex", "AK-47 | Bloodsport", "USP-S | Neo Noir",
	        
	        "Desert Eagle | Hypnotic", "P90 | Emerald Dragon", "AK-47 | Case Hardened",
	        "P2000 | Ocean Foam", "AWP | Graphite", "Five-SeveN | Fowl Play",
	        "Desert Eagle | Conspiracy", "Glock-18 | Water Elemental",
	        "CZ75-Auto | Xiangliu", "AWP | Fever Dream", "M4A1-S | Decimator",
	        
	        "Glock-18 | Dragon Tattoo", "MAC-10 | Graven", "M4A1-S | Dark Water",
	        "M4A1-S | Bright Water", "USP-S | Dark Water", "M4A4 | Zirka",
	        "USP-S | Overgrowth", "Nova | Koi", "PP-Bizon | Osiris",
	        "CZ75-Auto | Tigris", "P250 | Supernova",
	        "M249 | Emerald Poison Dart", "MAC-10 | Last Dive", "UMP-45 | Scaffold",
	        "XM1014 | Seasons", "Galil AR | Crimson Tsunami",
	        
	        "MP7 | Skulls", "AUG | Wings", "Galil AR | Shattered",
	        "SG 553 | Ultraviolet", "SG 553 | Wave Spray", "G3SG1 | Demeter",
	        "Nova | Tempest", "Dual Berettas | Black Limba", "Negev | Desert-Strike",
	        "UMP-45 | Labyrinth", "P2000 | Ivory", "MP7 | Urban Hazard", "SSG 08 | Abyss",
	        "PP-Bizon | Jungle Slipstream", "Sawed-Off | Zander", "MP7 | Akoben",
	        "P250 | Ripple", "SCAR-20 | Blueprint", "Five-SeveN | Capillary",
	        "Desert Eagle | Oxide Blaze"
	    };

	    String skinName = allSkins[random.nextInt(allSkins.length)];
	    String rarity = getSkinRarity(skinName);
	    double basePrice = getBasePrice(skinName);
	    
	    String[] availableConditions = getAvailableConditions(skinName);
	    String condition = availableConditions[random.nextInt(availableConditions.length)];
	    double itemFloat = generateFloatForCondition(skinName, condition);
	    
	    double price = basePrice;
	    
	    boolean isGloves = rarity.equals("Gloves");
	    boolean isKnife = rarity.equals("Knife");
	    
	    if (isGloves) {
	        double gloveBasePrice = getGloveBasePrice(skinName);
	        price = calculateGlovePrice(skinName, condition, gloveBasePrice);
	        double gloveVariance = 0.90 + (random.nextDouble() * 0.20);
	        price *= gloveVariance;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	        price *= 2.5;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) {
	        price *= 1.7;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Field-Tested")) {
	        price *= 1.0;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Well-Worn")) {
	        price *= 0.7;
	    } else if (condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) {
	        price *= 0.3;
	    }
	    
	    if (!isGloves) {
	        boolean isSpecialKnife = skinName.contains("Doppler") || skinName.contains("Fade");
	        
	        if (!isKnife) {
	            if (itemFloat <= 0.0005) {
	                price *= 3.0;
	            } else if (itemFloat <= 0.001) {
	                price *= 2.0;
	            } else if (itemFloat <= 0.005) {
	                price *= 1.5;
	            } else if (itemFloat <= 0.02) {
	                price *= 1.25;
	            }
	        } else if (!isSpecialKnife) {
	            double rel = getRelativeFloat(skinName, itemFloat);
	            if (!isCappedKnife(skinName)) {
	                if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                    price *= 2.5;
	                } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                    price *= 1.5;
	                } else if (rel <= 0.20) {
	                    price *= 1.1;
	                }
	            } else {
	                if (rel <= 0.01) {
	                    price *= 1.15;
	                } else if (rel <= 0.05) {
	                    price *= 1.05;
	                }
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    
	    boolean isStattrak = !isGloves && random.nextDouble() < 0.10;
	    if (isStattrak) {
	        if (isKnife) {
	            price *= 1.15;
	        } else {
	            price *= 2.0;
	        }
	    }
	    
	    double marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarity, 1.0);
	    price *= marketMulti;
	    
	    Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(skinName);
	    String displayRarity = isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + rarity : rarity;
	    
	    return new InventoryItem(
	        skinImg != null ? new ImageIcon(skinImg) : null,
	        skinName,
	        condition,
	        displayRarity,
	        BigDecimal.valueOf(price).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	        itemFloat,
	        isStattrak,
	        random.nextInt(1000),
	        null,
	        price
	    );
	}

	private void updateTradeNotification() {
	    if (unreadTradesCount > 0) {
	        tradeNotificationLabel.setText(unreadTradesCount + " New Trade" + (unreadTradesCount > 1 ? "s" : ""));
	        tradeNotificationLabel.setVisible(true);
	    } else {
	        tradeNotificationLabel.setText("");
	        tradeNotificationLabel.setVisible(false);
	    }
	}

	private void showTradesWindow() {
	    unreadTradesCount = 0;
	    updateTradeNotification();
	    
	    JFrame tradesFrame = new JFrame("Trade Offers");
	    tradesFrame.setSize(900, 700);
	    tradesFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    tradesFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    tradesFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(true);
	    
	    JTabbedPane tabbedPane = new JTabbedPane();
	    
	    JPanel pendingPanel = createPendingTradesPanel(tradesFrame);
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Pending (" + pendingTrades.size() + ")", pendingPanel);
	    
	    JPanel historyPanel = createTradeHistoryPanel();
	    tabbedPane.addTab("History (" + completedTrades.size() + ")", historyPanel);
	    
	    tradesFrame.add(tabbedPane, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    tradesFrame.setVisible(true);
	    
	    javax.swing.Timer timer = new javax.swing.Timer(100, e -> {
	        tradesFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(false);
	        tradesFrame.toFront();
	        tradesFrame.requestFocus();
	    });
	    timer.setRepeats(false);
	    timer.start();
	}

	private JPanel createPendingTradesPanel(JFrame parent) {
	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    if (pendingTrades.isEmpty()) {
	        JLabel emptyLabel = new JLabel("No pending trade offers", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        emptyLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 24));
	        panel.add(emptyLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        return panel;
	    }
	    
	    JPanel container = new JPanel();
	    container.setLayout(new BoxLayout(container, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    container.setBackground(Color.DARK_GRAY);
	    container.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    List<TradeOffer> tradeSnapshot;
	    synchronized (pendingTrades) {
	        tradeSnapshot = new ArrayList<>(pendingTrades);
	    }
	    for (TradeOffer trade : tradeSnapshot) {
	        JPanel tradeCard = createTradeCard(trade, parent, true);
	        tradeCard.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 350));
	        container.add(tradeCard);
	        container.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 10)));
	    }
	    
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(container);
	    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    panel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    return panel;
	}

	private JPanel createTradeCard(TradeOffer trade, JFrame parent, boolean isPending) {
	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    card.setBackground(new Color(45, 45, 50));
	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(isPending ? Color.ORANGE : 
	            (trade.isAccepted ? new Color(50, 200, 50) : new Color(200, 50, 50)), 3),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10)
	    ));
	    card.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(850, 400));
	    card.setMinimumSize(new Dimension(850, 400));

	    JPanel topPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    topPanel.setBackground(new Color(45, 45, 50));
	    
	    JPanel npcInfoPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));
	    npcInfoPanel.setBackground(new Color(45, 45, 50));
	    
	    JLabel npcAvatarLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(trade.npcAvatar));
	    npcInfoPanel.add(npcAvatarLabel);
	    
	    JLabel npcNameLabel = new JLabel(trade.npcName);
	    npcNameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 18));
	    npcNameLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    npcInfoPanel.add(npcNameLabel);
	    
	    long secondsAgo = (System.currentTimeMillis() - trade.timestamp) / 1000;
	    String timeStr = secondsAgo < 60 ? secondsAgo + "s ago" : (secondsAgo / 60) + "m ago";
	    JLabel timeLabel = new JLabel(" - " + timeStr);
	    timeLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	    npcInfoPanel.add(timeLabel);
	    
	    topPanel.add(npcInfoPanel, BorderLayout.WEST);
	    
	    JPanel tradeTypePanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.RIGHT));
	    tradeTypePanel.setBackground(new Color(45, 45, 50));

	    Color tradeTypeColor = Color.WHITE;
	    
	    boolean npcOffersItems = !trade.npcOfferedItems.isEmpty();
	    boolean npcOffersMoney = trade.npcOfferedMoney > 0;
	    boolean npcRequestsItems = !trade.npcRequestedItems.isEmpty();
	    boolean npcRequestsMoney = trade.npcRequestedMoney > 0;
	    
	    String tradeKey;

	    if (npcOffersItems && npcRequestsMoney && !npcOffersMoney && !npcRequestsItems) {
	        tradeKey = "SELLING";
	        tradeTypeColor = new Color(100, 200, 100);
	    } else if (npcOffersMoney && npcRequestsItems && !npcOffersItems && !npcRequestsMoney) {
	        tradeKey = "BUYING";
	        tradeTypeColor = new Color(255, 200, 50);
	    } else if (npcOffersItems && npcRequestsItems && !npcOffersMoney && !npcRequestsMoney) {
	        tradeKey = "TRADING";
	        tradeTypeColor = new Color(100, 150, 255);
	    } else {
	        tradeKey = "MIXED";
	        tradeTypeColor = new Color(200, 100, 255);
	    }

	    String tradeText = tradeType(tradeKey);

	    JLabel tradeTypeLabel = new JLabel(tradeText);
	    tradeTypeLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    tradeTypeLabel.setForeground(tradeTypeColor);
	    tradeTypeLabel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(tradeTypeColor, 2),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(5, 10, 5, 10)
	    ));
	    tradeTypePanel.add(tradeTypeLabel);
	    
	    topPanel.add(tradeTypePanel, BorderLayout.EAST);
	    
	    card.add(topPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JPanel tradePanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(1, 2, 10, 0));
	    tradePanel.setBackground(new Color(45, 45, 50));
	    tradePanel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(850, 260));

	    JPanel npcSide = createTradeSidePanel(trade.npcOfferedItems, trade.npcOfferedMoney, 
	        trade.npcAvatar, "NPC Offers", true);
	    tradePanel.add(npcSide);

	    JPanel yourSide = createTradeSidePanel(trade.npcRequestedItems, trade.npcRequestedMoney,
	        playerAvatar, "You Give", false);
	    tradePanel.add(yourSide);
	    
	    card.add(tradePanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JPanel bottomPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout());
	    bottomPanel.setBackground(new Color(45, 45, 50));
	    
	    if (isPending) {
	        JButton acceptBtn = new JButton("ACCEPT TRADE");
	        acceptBtn.setBackground(new Color(50, 200, 50));
	        acceptBtn.setForeground(Color.GREEN);
	        acceptBtn.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        acceptBtn.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(200, 40));
	        
	        acceptBtn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	            @Override
	            public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) {
	                playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
	            }
	        });
	        
	        JButton declineBtn = new JButton("DECLINE TRADE");
	        declineBtn.setBackground(new Color(200, 50, 50));
	        declineBtn.setForeground(Color.RED);
	        declineBtn.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        declineBtn.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(200, 40));
	        
	        declineBtn.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	            @Override
	            public void mousePressed(MouseEvent e) {
	                playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
	            }
	        });
	        
	        acceptBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	            handleTradeAccept(trade, parent);
	        });
	        
	        declineBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	            handleTradeDecline(trade, parent);
	        });
	        
	        bottomPanel.add(acceptBtn);
	        bottomPanel.add(declineBtn);
	    } else {
	        JLabel statusLabel = new JLabel(trade.isAccepted ? "ACCEPTED" : "DECLINED");
	        statusLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 20));
	        statusLabel.setForeground(trade.isAccepted ? new Color(50, 200, 50) : new Color(200, 50, 50));
	        bottomPanel.add(statusLabel);
	    }
	    
	    card.add(bottomPanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    
	    return card;
	}
	
	private String tradeType(String type) {
	    String[] lines;

	    if (type.equals("BUYING")) {
	        lines = new String[] {
	            "Hey! I’ve been eyeing that skin - how about some cash for it?",
	            "I like your taste in skins. Want to sell one for this price?",

	            "I’ll give you a clean offer, no lowballing.",
	            "That piece is underrated. I’ll take it off your hands.",

	            "You won’t find a better buyer today.",

	            "Fresh pulls, solid floats. Take a look.",
	            "Market’s dry - I’ve got the good stuff.",

	            "Clean skins, fair price. Simple deal.",
	            "Hard to find skins, easy decision.",
	            "These won’t last long at this price.",
	            "I could list them, but I’d rather deal direct.",
	            "Solid value if you know the market.",
	            "Perfect pickup if you’re upgrading your loadout."

	        lines = new String[] {

	            "You trade smart, I trade smart. Fair exchange?",
	            "Skin for skin. Clean and simple.",
	            "Let’s trade items - win-win.",

	            "Equal value, different style.",

	        };

	    } else {
	        lines = new String[] {
	            "Let’s make a deal - items and cash involved.",
	            "A bit of money, a bit of skins. Sound fair?",
	            "This one’s a mixed offer, but I think it’s solid.",
	            "Not a simple trade, but a profitable one.",

	            "Balances out nicely if you do the math.",
	            "A little creativity makes this work.",

	            "Mixed trades separate good traders from great ones."

	    }

	    return lines[random.nextInt(lines.length)];
	}

	private JPanel createTradeSidePanel(ArrayList<InventoryItem> items, double money, 
            Image avatar, String title, boolean isNPC) {
    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
    panel.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
    panel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(Color.GRAY, 2));
    
    JPanel titlePanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));
    titlePanel.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
    titlePanel.add(new JLabel(new ImageIcon(avatar.getScaledInstance(32, 32, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH))));
    JLabel titleLabel = new JLabel(title);
    titleLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
    titleLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
    titlePanel.add(titleLabel);
    panel.add(titlePanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
    
    JPanel itemsPanel = new JPanel();
    itemsPanel.setLayout(new BoxLayout(itemsPanel, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
    itemsPanel.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
    itemsPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
    
    if (money > 0) {
        JPanel moneyPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));
        moneyPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
        moneyPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(Color.YELLOW, 2));
        moneyPanel.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 80));
        
        JLabel moneyIcon = new JLabel("💵");
        moneyIcon.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 48));
        moneyIcon.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
        moneyPanel.add(moneyIcon);
        
        JLabel moneyLabel = new JLabel("$" + String.format("%.2f", money));
        moneyLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 24));
        moneyLabel.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
        moneyPanel.add(moneyLabel);
        
        itemsPanel.add(moneyPanel);
        itemsPanel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 5)));
    }
    
    for (InventoryItem item : items) {
        JPanel itemCard = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
        itemCard.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
        
        if (item.blueGemTier != null) {
            itemCard.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(Color.CYAN, 3));
        } else {
            itemCard.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(getRarityColor(item.rarity), 2));
        }
        
        itemCard.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 100));
        itemCard.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(350, 100));
        
        if (item.image != null) {
            Image scaled = item.image.getImage().getScaledInstance(100, 75, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH);
            JLabel imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
            imgLabel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(100, 75));
            itemCard.add(imgLabel, BorderLayout.WEST);
        }
        
        JPanel infoPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(4, 1));
        infoPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
        infoPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(5, 10, 5, 10));
        
        JLabel nameLabel;
        if (item.isStattrak) {
            nameLabel = new JLabel("<html> StatTrak " + item.name + "</html>");
            nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 11));
            nameLabel.setForeground(new Color(255, 153, 51));
        } else {
            nameLabel = new JLabel("<html>" + item.name + "</html>");
            nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 11));
            nameLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
        }
        
        JLabel condLabel = new JLabel(item.condition + " | Float: " + String.format("%.4f", item.itemFloat));
        condLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 10));
        condLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
        
        JLabel priceLabel = new JLabel("$" + item.price);
        priceLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 12));
        priceLabel.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
        
        JLabel specialLabel;
        if (item.blueGemTier != null) {
            specialLabel = new JLabel("💎 " + item.blueGemTier + " (Fixed Price)");
            specialLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 10));
            specialLabel.setForeground(Color.CYAN);
        } else {
            specialLabel = new JLabel("Pattern: #" + item.patternID);
            specialLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 10));
            specialLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
        }
        
        infoPanel.add(nameLabel);
        infoPanel.add(condLabel);
        infoPanel.add(priceLabel);
        infoPanel.add(specialLabel);
        
        itemCard.add(infoPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
        itemsPanel.add(itemCard);
        itemsPanel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 5)));
    }

    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(itemsPanel);
    scroll.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
    scroll.setBorder(null);
    panel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);

    if (money == 0 && !items.isEmpty()) {
        double totalValue = items.stream().mapToDouble(it -> it.price.doubleValue()).sum();
        JPanel valuePanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.CENTER));
        valuePanel.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
        JLabel valueLabel = new JLabel("Total: $" + String.format("%.2f", totalValue));
        valueLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
        valueLabel.setForeground(Color.CYAN);
        valuePanel.add(valueLabel);
        panel.add(valuePanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
    }
    return panel;
}
	
	private void optimizeScrollPane(JScrollPane scroll) {
	    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(20);
	    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setBlockIncrement(100);
	    
	    scroll.getViewport().setScrollMode(JViewport.SIMPLE_SCROLL_MODE);
	}

	private void handleTradeAccept(TradeOffer trade, JFrame parent) {
	    for (InventoryItem requestedItem : trade.npcRequestedItems) {
	        if (!inventoryList.contains(requestedItem)) {
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(parent, 
	                "You no longer have " + requestedItem.name + "!",
	                "Trade Failed", JOptionPane.ERROR_MESSAGE);
	            return;
	        }
	    }

	    if (trade.npcRequestedMoney > balance) {
	        JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(parent, 
	            "Insufficient funds! Need $" + String.format("%.2f", trade.npcRequestedMoney),
	            "Trade Failed", JOptionPane.ERROR_MESSAGE);
	        return;
	    }

	    double offeredValue = trade.npcOfferedMoney + 
	        trade.npcOfferedItems.stream().mapToDouble(i -> i.price.doubleValue()).sum();
	    double requestedValue = trade.npcRequestedMoney + 
	        trade.npcRequestedItems.stream().mapToDouble(i -> i.price.doubleValue()).sum();
	    
	    boolean isProfitable = offeredValue > requestedValue;
	    
	    playSound(purchaseSound); 

	    for (InventoryItem item : trade.npcRequestedItems) {
	        inventoryList.remove(item);
	        inventoryValue = Math.max(0.0, inventoryValue - item.price.doubleValue());
	    }
	    
	    balance -= trade.npcRequestedMoney;
	    balance += trade.npcOfferedMoney;
	    
	    for (InventoryItem item : trade.npcOfferedItems) {
	        inventoryList.add(item);
	        inventoryValue += item.price.doubleValue();
	    }
	    
	    trade.isAccepted = true;
	    synchronized (pendingTrades) { pendingTrades.remove(trade); }
	    completedTrades.add(trade);
	    
	    updateBalanceLabel();
	    writeStats();
	    newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	    totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	    
	    crateImage = new ImageIcon("crate.png").getImage();
	    skinImage = null;
	    
	    updateLeaderboard();
	    refreshMainUI();
	    
	    JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(parent, 
	        "Trade completed successfully!",
	        "Success", JOptionPane.INFORMATION_MESSAGE);
	    
	    parent.dispose();
	    
	    if (!achievements.get("first_trade").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("first_trade");
	    }
	    
	    if (isProfitable && !achievements.get("profitable_trade").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("profitable_trade");
	    }
	    
	    long acceptedTrades = completedTrades.stream().filter(t -> t.isAccepted).count();
	    achievements.get("trade_10").progress = (int)acceptedTrades;
	    achievements.get("trade_50").progress = (int)acceptedTrades;
	    if (acceptedTrades == 10 && !achievements.get("trade_10").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("trade_10");
	    }
	    if (acceptedTrades == 50 && !achievements.get("trade_50").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("trade_50");
	    }
	}

	private void handleTradeDecline(TradeOffer trade, JFrame parent) {
	    trade.isDeclined = true;
	    synchronized (pendingTrades) { pendingTrades.remove(trade); }
	    completedTrades.add(trade);
	    
	    JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(parent, 
	        "Trade declined.",
	        "Declined", JOptionPane.INFORMATION_MESSAGE);
	    
	    parent.dispose();
	}
	
	private JPanel createTradeHistoryPanel() {
	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    if (completedTrades.isEmpty()) {
	        JLabel emptyLabel = new JLabel("No trade history", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        emptyLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 24));
	        panel.add(emptyLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        return panel;
	    }
	    
	    JPanel container = new JPanel();
	    container.setLayout(new BoxLayout(container, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    container.setBackground(Color.DARK_GRAY);
	    container.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));

	    for (int i = completedTrades.size() - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
	        TradeOffer trade = completedTrades.get(i);
	        JPanel tradeCard = createTradeCard(trade, null, false);
	        tradeCard.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 350));
	        container.add(tradeCard);
	        container.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 10)));
	    }
	    
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(container);
	    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    panel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    return panel;
	}
	
	private void simulateMarketActivity() {
	    if (marketProcessQueue.isEmpty()) {
	        initializeMarketQueue();
	        return;
	    }
	    
	    int processed = 0;
	    int maxPerCycle = 10;
	    
	    while (processed < maxPerCycle && !marketProcessQueue.isEmpty()) {
	        String skinName = marketProcessQueue.poll();
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = globalMarketListings.get(skinName);
	        
	        if (listings == null || listings.isEmpty()) {
	            processed++;
	            continue;
	        }
	        
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> toRemove = new ArrayList<>();
	        synchronized (listings) {
	            int checkLimit = Math.min(3, listings.size());
	            for (int i = 0; i < checkLimit; i++) {
	                MarketListing listing = listings.get(i);
	                if (listing.isPlayerListing) continue;
	                
	                String rarity = getSkinRarity(listing.item.name.replace("StatTrak ", ""));
	                double marketMulti = marketPriceMultipliers.getOrDefault(rarity, 1.0);
	                double basePrice = getBasePrice(listing.item.name.replace("StatTrak ", ""));
	                double expectedPrice = basePrice * marketMulti;
	                
	                if (listing.item.condition.equals("Factory New")) expectedPrice *= 2.5;
	                else if (listing.item.condition.equals("Minimal Wear")) expectedPrice *= 1.7;
	                else if (listing.item.condition.equals("Well-Worn")) expectedPrice *= 0.7;
	                else if (listing.item.condition.equals("Battle-Scarred")) expectedPrice *= 0.3;
	                
	                if (rarity.equals("Knife") && listing.item.condition.equals("Factory New")) {
	                    FloatRange efr = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(listing.item.name);
	                    if (efr == null) for (Map.Entry<String,FloatRange> e2 : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet())
	                        if (listing.item.name.startsWith(e2.getKey())) { efr = e2.getValue(); break; }
	                    double eMin = (efr != null && efr.min != null) ? efr.min : 0.0;
	                    if (eMin >= 0.06) expectedPrice *= 2.87;
	                }
	                
	                if (listing.item.isStattrak) {
	                    boolean isCW10 = listing.item.name.contains("Crimson Web");
	                    boolean isD10  = listing.item.name.contains("Doppler");
	                    if (isCW10)                            expectedPrice *= 2.0;
	                    else if (isD10)                        expectedPrice *= 0.80;
	                    else if (rarity.equals("Knife"))       expectedPrice *= 0.90;
	                    else                                   expectedPrice *= 1.85;
	                }
	                
	                double priceRatio = listing.listPrice / expectedPrice;
	                double sellChance = priceRatio < 0.85 ? 0.05 : 
	                                   priceRatio < 0.95 ? 0.03 :
	                                   priceRatio < 1.05 ? 0.02 : 0.01;
	                
	                if (random.nextDouble() < sellChance) {
	                    toRemove.add(listing);
	                    String displayName = listing.item.isStattrak ? "StatTrak " + listing.item.name : listing.item.name;
	                    addSaleRecord(new SaleRecord(displayName, listing.listPrice, 
	                        listing.item.condition, listing.item.itemFloat, listing.item.blueGemTier));
	                }
	            }
	            listings.removeAll(toRemove);
	        }
	        processed++;
	    }
	}
	
	private String cleanStatTrakEncoding(String text) {
	    if (text == null) return text;
	    
	    
	    
	    boolean hasStatTrak = text.toLowerCase().contains("stattrak");
	    
	    text = text.replaceAll("(?i)stattrak\\s*", "").trim();
	    
	    if (hasStatTrak) {
	        return "StatTrak " + text;
	    }
	    
	    return text;
	}
	
	private void addSaleRecord(SaleRecord sale) {
	    boolean isSpecial = sale.specialVariant != null || 
	                       sale.skinName.toLowerCase().contains("knife") ||
	                       sale.skinName.toLowerCase().contains("doppler");
	    
	    if (isSpecial) {
	        rareSales.add(sale);
	        // Trim front instead of copying via subList to avoid creating a new ArrayList
	        while (rareSales.size() > MAX_RARE_SALES) rareSales.remove(0);
	    }
	    
	    recentSales.add(sale);
	    // Trim front instead of copying via subList
	    while (recentSales.size() > MAX_SALES_HISTORY) recentSales.remove(0);
	}
	private void addUnboxedSkin(String skinName) {
	    if (skinName == null) return;
	    String cleanName = skinName.replace("StatTrak ", "").trim();
	    
	    if (cleanName.contains("(Blue Gem")) {
	        if (cleanName.contains("(Blue Gem")) cleanName = cleanName.substring(0, cleanName.indexOf("(Blue Gem")).trim();
	    }
	    
	    if (cleanName.contains("Doppler")) {
	        int dopplerIndex = cleanName.indexOf("Doppler");
	        if (dopplerIndex != -1) {
	            cleanName = cleanName.substring(0, dopplerIndex + 7).trim();
	        }
	    }
	    
	    boolean wasNew = !unboxedSkins.contains(cleanName);
	    unboxedSkins.add(cleanName);
	    
	    if (wasNew) {
	        int collectionSize = unboxedSkins.size();
	        
	        achievements.get("collect_10").progress = collectionSize;
	        achievements.get("collect_25").progress = collectionSize;
	        achievements.get("collect_50").progress = collectionSize;
	        achievements.get("collect_all").progress = collectionSize;
	        
	        if (collectionSize == 10 && !achievements.get("collect_10").isUnlocked) {
	            unlockAchievement("collect_10");
	        }
	        if (collectionSize == 25 && !achievements.get("collect_25").isUnlocked) {
	            unlockAchievement("collect_25");
	        }
	        if (collectionSize == 50 && !achievements.get("collect_50").isUnlocked) {
	            unlockAchievement("collect_50");
	        }
	        if (collectionSize == getAllPossibleSkins().size() && !achievements.get("collect_all").isUnlocked) {
	            unlockAchievement("collect_all");
	        }
	    }
	}

	private void showCollectionWindow() {
	    JFrame collectionFrame = new JFrame("Skin Collection");
	    collectionFrame.setSize(1000, 800);
	    collectionFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    collectionFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    collectionFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(true);
	    
	    JPanel headerPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1));
	    headerPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    headerPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    JLabel titleLabel = new JLabel("Skin Collection", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    titleLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 24));
	    titleLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    
	    int totalSkins = getAllPossibleSkins().size();
	    int unlockedCount = unboxedSkins.size();
	    double completionPercent = (unlockedCount * 100.0) / totalSkins;
	    
	    JLabel statsLabel = new JLabel(String.format("Unlocked: %d / %d (%.1f%%)", 
	        unlockedCount, totalSkins, completionPercent), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    statsLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 18));
	    statsLabel.setForeground(Color.CYAN);
	    
	    headerPanel.add(titleLabel);
	    headerPanel.add(statsLabel);
	    collectionFrame.add(headerPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JTabbedPane tabbedPane = new JTabbedPane();
	    
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Knives", createRarityCollectionPanel("Knife"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Gloves", createRarityCollectionPanel("Gloves"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Covert", createRarityCollectionPanel("Covert"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Classified", createRarityCollectionPanel("Classified"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Restricted", createRarityCollectionPanel("Restricted"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Milspec", createRarityCollectionPanel("Milspec"));
	    
	    collectionFrame.add(tabbedPane, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    collectionFrame.setVisible(true);
	    
	    javax.swing.Timer timer = new javax.swing.Timer(100, e -> {
	        collectionFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(false);
	        collectionFrame.toFront();
	        collectionFrame.requestFocus();
	    });
	    timer.setRepeats(false);
	    timer.start();
	}

	private List<String> getSkinsByRarity(String rarity) {
	    List<String> skins = new ArrayList<>();
	    
	    for (String skin : getAllPossibleSkins()) {
	        if (getSkinRarity(skin).equals(rarity)) {
	            skins.add(skin);
	        }
	    }
	    
	    return skins;
	}
	private JPanel createRarityCollectionPanel(String rarity) {
	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    panel.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    
	    List<String> skinsInRarity = getSkinsByRarity(rarity);
	    int unlockedInRarity = 0;
	    for (String skin : skinsInRarity) {
	        if (unboxedSkins.contains(skin)) {
	            unlockedInRarity++;
	        }
	    }
	    
	    JLabel rarityStatsLabel = new JLabel(String.format("%s: %d / %d unlocked", 
	        rarity, unlockedInRarity, skinsInRarity.size()), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    rarityStatsLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    rarityStatsLabel.setForeground(getRarityColor(rarity));
	    rarityStatsLabel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    panel.add(rarityStatsLabel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 3, 10, 10));
	    grid.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    for (String skinName : skinsInRarity) {
	        JPanel skinCard = createCollectionSkinCard(skinName, rarity);
	        grid.add(skinCard);
	    }
	    
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    scroll.setBorder(null);
	    scroll.getViewport().setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    panel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    return panel;
	}
	private JPanel createCollectionSkinCard(String skinName, String rarity) {
	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    card.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(getRarityColor(rarity), 3));
	    card.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(200, 180));
	    
	    boolean isUnlocked = unboxedSkins.contains(skinName);
	    
	    if (isUnlocked) {
	        Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(skinName);
	        if (skinImg != null) {
	            Image scaled = skinImg.getScaledInstance(180, 120, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH);
	            JLabel imgLabel = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled));
	            imgLabel.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.CENTER);
	            card.add(imgLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        } else {
	            JLabel placeholderLabel = new JLabel("Image Missing", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	            placeholderLabel.setForeground(Color.GRAY);
	            placeholderLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.ITALIC, 12));
	            card.add(placeholderLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        }
	        
	        JLabel nameLabel = new JLabel("<html><center>" + skinName + "</center></html>", 
	            SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 11));
	        nameLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	        nameLabel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(5, 5, 5, 5));
	        card.add(nameLabel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    } else {
	        JPanel lockedPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	        lockedPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	        
	        JLabel mysteryLabel = new JLabel("???", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        mysteryLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 72));
	        mysteryLabel.setForeground(new Color(80, 80, 85));
	        lockedPanel.add(mysteryLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        
	        JLabel lockedLabel = new JLabel("LOCKED", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        lockedLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        lockedLabel.setForeground(new Color(100, 100, 105));
	        lockedLabel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(5, 5, 5, 5));
	        lockedPanel.add(lockedLabel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	        
	        card.add(lockedPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    }
	    
	    return card;
	}
	public static class Achievement {
	    String id;
	    String name;
	    String description;
	    double reward;
	    boolean isUnlocked;
	    String category;
	    int progress;
	    int requirement;
	    
	    public Achievement(String id, String name, String description, double reward, String category, int requirement) {
	        this.id = id;
	        this.name = name;
	        this.description = description;
	        this.reward = reward;
	        this.category = category;
	        this.requirement = requirement;
	        this.isUnlocked = false;
	        this.progress = 0;
	    }
	}
