	private void unlockAchievement(String achievementId) {
	    Achievement achievement = achievements.get(achievementId);
	    if (achievement != null && !achievement.isUnlocked) {
	        achievement.isUnlocked = true;
	        unlockedAchievements.add(achievementId);
	        balance += achievement.reward;
	        updateBalanceLabel();
	        
	        showAchievementNotification(achievement);
	    }
	}

	private void showAchievementNotification(Achievement achievement) {

	    JPanel notif = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(6, 0));
	    notif.setBackground(new Color(28, 28, 38));
	    notif.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(255, 210, 30), 2),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 10, 8, 10)
	    ));
	    notif.setCursor(new Cursor(Cursor.HAND_CURSOR));
	    notif.setToolTipText("Click to dismiss");

	    JLabel icon = new JLabel("🏆", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    icon.setFont(new Font("Segoe UI Emoji", Font.PLAIN, 22));
	    notif.add(icon, BorderLayout.WEST);

	    JPanel textPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(3, 1, 0, 1));
	    textPanel.setBackground(new Color(28, 28, 38));

	    JLabel titleLbl = new JLabel("ACHIEVEMENT UNLOCKED");
	    titleLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));
	    titleLbl.setForeground(new Color(255, 210, 30));

	    JLabel nameLbl = new JLabel(achievement.name);
	    nameLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    nameLbl.setForeground(Color.WHITE);

	    JLabel rewardLbl = new JLabel("+" + String.format("$%.0f", achievement.reward) + "  -  " + achievement.description);
	    rewardLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 10));
	    rewardLbl.setForeground(new Color(100, 220, 100));

	    textPanel.add(titleLbl);
	    textPanel.add(nameLbl);
	    textPanel.add(rewardLbl);
	    notif.add(textPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    int w = 320, h = 72;
	    JLayeredPane layered = getLayeredPane();
	    int x = 12;
	    int y = layered.getHeight() - h - 12;
	    notif.setBounds(x, y, w, h);
	    layered.add(notif, JLayeredPane.POPUP_LAYER);
	    layered.revalidate();
	    layered.repaint();

	    MouseAdapter dismiss = new MouseAdapter() {
	        @Override public void mouseClicked(MouseEvent e) {
	            layered.remove(notif);
	            layered.repaint();
	        }
	    };
	    notif.addMouseListener(dismiss);
	    for (Component c : notif.getComponents()) c.addMouseListener(dismiss);
	    for (Component c : textPanel.getComponents()) c.addMouseListener(dismiss);

	    javax.swing.Timer timer = new javax.swing.Timer(4000, e -> {
	        layered.remove(notif);
	        layered.repaint();
	    });
	    timer.setRepeats(false);
	    timer.start();
	}

	private void showAchievementsWindow() {
	    JFrame achievementsFrame = new JFrame("Achievements");
	    achievementsFrame.setSize(1000, 800);
	    achievementsFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    achievementsFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    achievementsFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(true);
	    
	    JPanel headerPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1));
	    headerPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    headerPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    JLabel titleLabel = new JLabel("Achievements", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    titleLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 24));
	    titleLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    
	    int unlockedCount = unlockedAchievements.size();
	    int totalCount = achievements.size();
	    double completionPercent = (unlockedCount * 100.0) / totalCount;
	    
	    JLabel statsLabel = new JLabel(String.format("Unlocked: %d / %d (%.1f%%)", 
	        unlockedCount, totalCount, completionPercent), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    statsLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 18));
	    statsLabel.setForeground(Color.CYAN);
	    
	    headerPanel.add(titleLabel);
	    headerPanel.add(statsLabel);
	    achievementsFrame.add(headerPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JTabbedPane tabbedPane = new JTabbedPane();
	    
	    tabbedPane.addTab("All", createAchievementCategoryPanel("All"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Unboxing", createAchievementCategoryPanel("Unboxing"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Value", createAchievementCategoryPanel("Value"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Market", createAchievementCategoryPanel("Market"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Trading", createAchievementCategoryPanel("Trading"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Special", createAchievementCategoryPanel("Special"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Collection", createAchievementCategoryPanel("Collection"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Float", createAchievementCategoryPanel("Float"));
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Streak", createAchievementCategoryPanel("Streak"));
	    
	    achievementsFrame.add(tabbedPane, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    achievementsFrame.setVisible(true);
	    
	    javax.swing.Timer timer = new javax.swing.Timer(100, e -> {
	        achievementsFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(false);
	        achievementsFrame.toFront();
	        achievementsFrame.requestFocus();
	    });
	    timer.setRepeats(false);
	    timer.start();
	}

	private JPanel createAchievementCategoryPanel(String category) {
	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    panel.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    
	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(0, 2, 10, 10));
	    grid.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    for (Achievement achievement : achievements.values()) {
	        if (category.equals("All") || achievement.category.equals(category)) {
	            JPanel achievementCard = createAchievementCard(achievement);
	            grid.add(achievementCard);
	        }
	    }
	    
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    scroll.setBorder(null);
	    scroll.getViewport().setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    panel.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    return panel;
	}

	private JPanel createAchievementCard(Achievement achievement) {
	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    card.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    card.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(450, 150));
	    
	    Color borderColor = achievement.isUnlocked ? Color.YELLOW : Color.GRAY;
	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(borderColor, 3),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10)
	    ));
	    
	    JPanel leftPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    leftPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    leftPanel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(80, 130));
	    
	    JLabel iconLabel;
	    if (achievement.isUnlocked) {
	        iconLabel = new JLabel("", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        iconLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 60));
	        iconLabel.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
	    } else {
	        iconLabel = new JLabel("?", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        iconLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 60));
	        iconLabel.setForeground(Color.GRAY);
	    }
	    leftPanel.add(iconLabel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    card.add(leftPanel, BorderLayout.WEST);
	    
	    JPanel infoPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(5, 1));
	    infoPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    infoPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(5, 10, 5, 10));
	    
	    JLabel nameLabel = new JLabel(achievement.isUnlocked ? achievement.name : "???");
	    nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    nameLabel.setForeground(achievement.isUnlocked ? Color.WHITE : Color.GRAY);
	    
	    JLabel descLabel = new JLabel(achievement.isUnlocked ? achievement.description : "Locked");
	    descLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    descLabel.setForeground(achievement.isUnlocked ? Color.LIGHT_GRAY : Color.DARK_GRAY);
	    
	    JLabel categoryLabel = new JLabel("Category: " + achievement.category);
	    categoryLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.ITALIC, 11));
	    categoryLabel.setForeground(Color.CYAN);
	    
	    JLabel progressLabel;
	    if (achievement.requirement > 1) {
	        progressLabel = new JLabel(String.format("Progress: %d / %d", 
	            achievement.progress, achievement.requirement));
	        progressLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	        progressLabel.setForeground(achievement.isUnlocked ? Color.GREEN : Color.ORANGE);
	    } else {
	        progressLabel = new JLabel("");
	    }
	    
	    JLabel rewardLabel = new JLabel(achievement.isUnlocked ? 
	        "Reward: $" + String.format("%.2f", achievement.reward) : "Reward: ???");
	    rewardLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	    rewardLabel.setForeground(achievement.isUnlocked ? Color.GREEN : Color.GRAY);
	    
	    infoPanel.add(nameLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(descLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(categoryLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(progressLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(rewardLabel);
	    
	    card.add(infoPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    return card;
	}

	private void showStatsWindow() {
	    JFrame statsFrame = new JFrame("Opening Statistics");
	    statsFrame.setSize(600, 500);
	    statsFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    statsFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    statsFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(true);
	    
	    JPanel headerPanel = new JPanel();
	    headerPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    headerPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(15, 15, 15, 15));
	    
	    JLabel titleLabel = new JLabel("Opening Statistics", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    titleLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 24));
	    titleLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    headerPanel.add(titleLabel);
	    
	    statsFrame.add(headerPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JPanel statsPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(8, 2, 10, 10));
	    statsPanel.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    statsPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(20, 20, 20, 20));
	    
	    addStatRow(statsPanel, "Total Milspecs:", String.valueOf(totMil), Color.BLUE);
	    addStatRow(statsPanel, "Total Restricteds:", String.valueOf(totRes), new Color(128, 0, 128));
	    addStatRow(statsPanel, "Total Classifieds:", String.valueOf(totClass), Color.MAGENTA);
	    addStatRow(statsPanel, "Total Coverts:", String.valueOf(totCov), Color.RED);
	    addStatRow(statsPanel, "Total Knives:", String.valueOf(totKnife), Color.YELLOW);
	    addStatRow(statsPanel, "Total Gloves:", String.valueOf(totGlove), Color.YELLOW);
	    addStatRow(statsPanel, "Total Crates Opened:", String.valueOf(totalCrates), Color.CYAN);
	    addStatRow(statsPanel, "Lowest Float:", String.format("%.10f", lowestFloat), new Color(100, 220, 255));
	    
	    statsFrame.add(statsPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    JPanel percentagesPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(6, 1, 5, 5));
	    percentagesPanel.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    percentagesPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createTitledBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(Color.GRAY), 
	            "Drop Rates", 0, 0, new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14), Color.WHITE),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10)
	    ));
	    
	    if (totalCrates > 0) {
	        addPercentageRow(percentagesPanel, "Milspec:", totMil, totalCrates, Color.BLUE);
	        addPercentageRow(percentagesPanel, "Restricted:", totRes, totalCrates, new Color(128, 0, 128));
	        addPercentageRow(percentagesPanel, "Classified:", totClass, totalCrates, Color.MAGENTA);
	        addPercentageRow(percentagesPanel, "Covert:", totCov, totalCrates, Color.RED);
	        addPercentageRow(percentagesPanel, "Knifes", totKnife, totalCrates, Color.YELLOW);
	        addPercentageRow(percentagesPanel, "Gloves:", totGlove, totalCrates, Color.YELLOW);
	    } else {
	        JLabel noDataLabel = new JLabel("No data yet - open some crates!", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        noDataLabel.setForeground(Color.GRAY);
	        percentagesPanel.add(noDataLabel);
	    }
	    
	    statsFrame.add(percentagesPanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    statsFrame.setVisible(true);
	    
	    javax.swing.Timer timer = new javax.swing.Timer(100, e -> {
	        statsFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(false);
	        statsFrame.toFront();
	        statsFrame.requestFocus();
	    });
	    timer.setRepeats(false);
	    timer.start();
	}

	private void addStatRow(JPanel panel, String label, String value, Color color) {
	    JLabel labelComp = new JLabel(label);
	    labelComp.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    labelComp.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    
	    JLabel valueComp = new JLabel(value);
	    valueComp.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    valueComp.setForeground(color);
	    valueComp.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.RIGHT);
	    
	    panel.add(labelComp);
	    panel.add(valueComp);
	}

	private void addPercentageRow(JPanel panel, String label, int count, int total, Color color) {
	    double percentage = (count * 100.0) / total;
	    JLabel row = new JLabel(String.format("%s %d (%.2f%%)", label, count, percentage));
	    row.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 13));
	    row.setForeground(color);
	    panel.add(row);
	}

	private void checkUnboxingAchievements(String item, String selectedSkinName, double bonusPrice, 
            double itemFloat, String blueGemTier, int totMil, int totRes, 
            int totClass, int totCov, int totKnife, int isStattrak) {
		achievements.get("open_100").progress = totalCrates;
		achievements.get("open_500").progress = totalCrates;
		achievements.get("open_1000").progress = totalCrates;
		achievements.get("glove_collector").progress = totGlove;
		achievements.get("glove_master").progress = totGlove;

		if (totalCrates == 100 && !achievements.get("open_100").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("open_100");
		}
		if (totalCrates == 500 && !achievements.get("open_500").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("open_500");
		}
		if (totalCrates == 1000 && !achievements.get("open_1000").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("open_1000");
		}

		if (item.contains("Milspec") && totMil == 1 && !achievements.get("first_blue").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("first_blue");
		}	
		if (item.contains("Restricted") && totRes == 1 && !achievements.get("first_purple").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("first_purple");
		}
		if (item.contains("Classified") && totClass == 1 && !achievements.get("first_pink").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("first_pink");
		}
		if (item.contains("Covert") && totCov == 1 && !achievements.get("first_red").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("first_red");
		}
		if (item.contains("Knife") && !item.contains("Gloves") && totKnife == 1 && !achievements.get("first_knife").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("first_knife");
	    }
	    if (item.contains("Gloves") && totGlove == 1 && !achievements.get("first_glove").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("first_glove");
	    }	    
	    if (totGlove == 10 && !achievements.get("glove_collector").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("glove_collector");
	    }
	    if (totGlove == 25 && !achievements.get("glove_master").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("glove_master");
	    
	    if (item.contains("Gloves") && bonusPrice >= 2000 && !achievements.get("rare_gloves").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("rare_gloves");
	    }	    
	    if (selectedSkinName.equals("Sport Gloves | Hedge Maze") && !achievements.get("hedge_maze").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("hedge_maze");
	    }	    
	    if (selectedSkinName.equals("Sport Gloves | Pandora's Box") && !achievements.get("pandoras_box").isUnlocked) {
	        unlockAchievement("pandoras_box");
	    }
		if (bonusPrice >= 1000 && !achievements.get("unbox_1000").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("unbox_1000");
		}
		if (bonusPrice >= 5000 && !achievements.get("unbox_5000").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("unbox_5000");
		}
		if (bonusPrice >= 10000 && !achievements.get("unbox_10000").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("unbox_10000");
		}

		if (inventoryValue >= 50000 && !achievements.get("inventory_50k").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("inventory_50k");
		}
		if (inventoryValue >= 100000 && !achievements.get("inventory_100k").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("inventory_100k");
		}
		if (inventoryValue >= 500000 && !achievements.get("inventory_500k").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("inventory_500k");
		}

		if (itemFloat < 0.001 && !achievements.get("float_0001").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("float_0001");
		}
		if (itemFloat < 0.0001 && !achievements.get("float_00001").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("float_00001");
		}
		if (itemFloat < 0.00001 && !achievements.get("float_000001").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("float_000001");
		}

		if (blueGemTier != null && !achievements.get("blue_gem").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("blue_gem");
		}
		if (blueGemTier != null && blueGemTier.contains("T1") && !achievements.get("blue_gem_t1").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("blue_gem_t1");	
		}

		if (selectedSkinName.contains("Doppler") && !achievements.get("doppler").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("doppler");
		}
		if (selectedSkinName.contains("Sapphire") && !achievements.get("sapphire").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("sapphire");
		}
		if (selectedSkinName.contains("Ruby") && !achievements.get("ruby").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("ruby");
		}
		if (selectedSkinName.contains("Black Pearl") && !achievements.get("black_pearl").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("black_pearl");
		}

		if (isStattrak == 1 && item.contains("Knife") && !achievements.get("stattrak_knife").isUnlocked) {
			unlockAchievement("stattrak_knife");
		}
	    }
	}
	
	private String normalizeSkinName(String name) {
	    if (name == null || name.isEmpty()) return "";
	    String clean = name.replaceAll("[\\p{Cc}&&[^\\t\\n\\r]]", "");
	    clean = clean.replaceAll("\\s+", " ").trim();
	    return clean;
	}
	
	private void generateLeaderboard() {
	    globalLeaderboard.clear();
	    
	    if (npcAvatars == null || playerAvatar == null) {
	        System.err.println("Avatars not loaded yet, skipping leaderboard generation");
	        return;
	    }
	    
	    if (inventoryValue > 0) {
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry("YOU", inventoryValue, playerAvatar, true));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 5000000 + (random.nextDouble() * 5000000);
	        Image avatar = npcAvatars[random.nextInt(npcAvatars.length)];
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 90; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 1000000 + (random.nextDouble() * 4000000);
	        Image avatar = npcAvatars[random.nextInt(npcAvatars.length)];
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 400; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 200000 + (random.nextDouble() * 800000);
	        Image avatar = npcAvatars[random.nextInt(npcAvatars.length)];
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 500; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 100000 + (random.nextDouble() * 100000);
	        Image avatar = npcAvatars[random.nextInt(npcAvatars.length)];
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 4000; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 20000 + (random.nextDouble() * 80000);
	        Image avatar = npcAvatars[random.nextInt(npcAvatars.length)];
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 5000; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 5000 + (random.nextDouble() * 15000);
	        Image avatar = npcAvatars[random.nextInt(npcAvatars.length)];
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 15000; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 1000 + (random.nextDouble() * 4000);
	        Image avatar = npcAvatars[random.nextInt(npcAvatars.length)];
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 25000; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 200 + (random.nextDouble() * 800);
	        Image avatar = npcAvatars[random.nextInt(npcAvatars.length)];
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 25000; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 50 + (random.nextDouble() * 150);
	        Image avatar = npcAvatars[random.nextInt(npcAvatars.length)];
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 24999; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 1 + (random.nextDouble() * 49);
	        Image avatar = npcAvatars[random.nextInt(npcAvatars.length)];
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    globalLeaderboard.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.inventoryValue, a.inventoryValue));
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < globalLeaderboard.size(); i++) {
	        globalLeaderboard.get(i).rank = i + 1;
	    }
	}
	
	private void showInventoryLeaderboard() {
	    
	    
	    List<LeaderboardEntry> top100 = new ArrayList<>();
	    
	    
	    String[] topNames = {
	        "KnifeKingElite", "AWPGodTier", "DiamondHandsXX", "InvictusPlayer",
	        "MarketWhaleXX", "CryptoSkinGod", "LegendaryTrader", "UltraRichCS",
	        "SkinBillionaire", "VaultHunter99", "TheProfitMaker", "NightHawkPro"
	    };
	    
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 5_000_000 + random.nextDouble() * 45_000_000;
	        Image avatar = NPC_AVATAR_POOL[random.nextInt(NPC_AVATAR_POOL.length)];
	        top100.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 40; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 500_000 + random.nextDouble() * 4_500_000;
	        Image avatar = NPC_AVATAR_POOL[random.nextInt(NPC_AVATAR_POOL.length)];
	        top100.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
	        String name = NPC_USERNAMES[random.nextInt(NPC_USERNAMES.length)];
	        double value = 100_000 + random.nextDouble() * 400_000;
	        Image avatar = NPC_AVATAR_POOL[random.nextInt(NPC_AVATAR_POOL.length)];
	        top100.add(new LeaderboardEntry(name, value, avatar, false));
	    }
	    
	    
	    top100.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.inventoryValue, a.inventoryValue));
	    for (int i = 0; i < top100.size(); i++) top100.get(i).rank = i + 1;
	    
	    
	    boolean playerInTop100 = false;
	    int playerSimRank = -1;
	    if (inventoryValue > 0) {
	        
	        for (LeaderboardEntry e : globalLeaderboard) {
	            if (e.isPlayer) { playerSimRank = e.rank; break; }
	        }
	        
	        if (!top100.isEmpty() && inventoryValue >= top100.get(top100.size() - 1).inventoryValue) {
	            playerInTop100 = true;
	            
	            top100.add(new LeaderboardEntry("YOU", inventoryValue, playerAvatar, true));
	            top100.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.inventoryValue, a.inventoryValue));
	            
	            while (top100.size() > 100) top100.remove(top100.size() - 1);
	            for (int i = 0; i < top100.size(); i++) top100.get(i).rank = i + 1;
	        }
	    }
	    
	    final boolean finalPlayerInTop100 = playerInTop100;
	    final int finalPlayerSimRank = playerSimRank;
	    
	    
	    JFrame frame = new JFrame("Inventory Leaderboard - Top 100");
	    frame.setSize(720, 860);
	    frame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    frame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    frame.getContentPane().setBackground(new Color(10, 10, 16));
	    
	    
	    JPanel header = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    header.setBackground(new Color(18, 18, 28));
	    header.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 2, 0, new Color(255, 215, 0)),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(14, 20, 14, 20)));
	    
	    JLabel titleLbl = new JLabel("\uD83C\uDFC6  INVENTORY LEADERBOARD  \uD83C\uDFC6", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    titleLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 22));
	    titleLbl.setForeground(new Color(255, 215, 0));
	    
	    String subtitleText;
	    if (inventoryValue <= 0) {
	        subtitleText = "Build your inventory to earn a rank!";
	    } else if (finalPlayerInTop100) {
	        
	        int prank = -1;
	        for (LeaderboardEntry e : top100) { if (e.isPlayer) { prank = e.rank; break; } }
	        subtitleText = String.format("\uD83D\uDD25 YOU ARE RANKED #%d IN THE TOP 100!", prank);
	    } else {
	        subtitleText = String.format("Your estimated rank: #%,d  |  Inv Value: $%,.0f  |  Top 100 threshold: $%,.0f",
	            finalPlayerSimRank > 0 ? finalPlayerSimRank : 999999,
	            inventoryValue,
	            top100.isEmpty() ? 100000 : top100.get(top100.size()-1).inventoryValue);
	    }
	    JLabel subtitleLbl = new JLabel(subtitleText, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    subtitleLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	    subtitleLbl.setForeground(finalPlayerInTop100 ? new Color(80, 220, 120) :
	                              inventoryValue > 0 ? new Color(150, 180, 255) : new Color(130, 130, 155));
	    
	    header.add(titleLbl, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    header.add(subtitleLbl, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    frame.add(header, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    
	    JPanel listPanel = new JPanel();
	    listPanel.setLayout(new BoxLayout(listPanel, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    listPanel.setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 20));
	    
	    
	    JPanel colHeader = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    colHeader.setBackground(new Color(20, 20, 32));
	    colHeader.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(6, 10, 6, 10));
	    colHeader.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 30));
	    JLabel colRank = new JLabel("  RANK", SwingConstants.LEFT);
	    colRank.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    colRank.setForeground(new Color(180, 180, 200));
	    JLabel colVal = new JLabel("INVENTORY VALUE  ", SwingConstants.RIGHT);
	    colVal.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	    colVal.setForeground(new Color(180, 180, 200));
	    colHeader.add(colRank, BorderLayout.WEST);
	    colHeader.add(colVal, BorderLayout.EAST);
	    listPanel.add(colHeader);
	    
	    for (int i = 0; i < top100.size(); i++) {
	        LeaderboardEntry entry = top100.get(i);
	        JPanel row = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(8, 0));
	        row.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 54));
	        row.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(600, 54));
	        
	        Color rowBg;
	        if (entry.isPlayer) {
	            rowBg = new Color(30, 80, 30);
	        } else if (i == 0) {
	            rowBg = new Color(60, 50, 10);
	        } else if (i == 1) {
	            rowBg = new Color(40, 40, 50);
	        } else if (i == 2) {
	            rowBg = new Color(45, 30, 15);
	        } else {
	            rowBg = (i % 2 == 0) ? new Color(16, 16, 26) : new Color(20, 20, 32);
	        }
	        row.setBackground(rowBg);
	        row.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 1, 0, new Color(28, 28, 44)),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 10, 4, 10)));
	        if (entry.isPlayer) {
	            row.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	                BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(80, 220, 80), 2),
	                BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(3, 9, 3, 9)));
	        }
	        
	        
	        String rankStr;
	        Color rankColor;
	        if (i == 0)      { rankStr = "\uD83E\uDD47 #1";  rankColor = new Color(255, 215, 0); }
	        else if (i == 1) { rankStr = "\uD83E\uDD48 #2";  rankColor = new Color(192, 192, 192); }
	        else if (i == 2) { rankStr = "\uD83E\uDD49 #3";  rankColor = new Color(205, 127, 50); }
	        else             { rankStr = " #" + (i + 1);      rankColor = i < 10 ? new Color(255, 160, 60) : new Color(160, 160, 180); }
	        JLabel rankLbl = new JLabel(rankStr, SwingConstants.LEFT);
	        rankLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, i < 3 ? 16 : 13));
	        rankLbl.setForeground(entry.isPlayer ? new Color(80, 255, 80) : rankColor);
	        rankLbl.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(70, 44));
	        
	        
	        JPanel namePanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 6, 6));
	        namePanel.setBackground(rowBg);
	        JLabel avatarLbl = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(entry.avatar.getScaledInstance(36, 36, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH)));
	        JLabel nameLbl = new JLabel(entry.isPlayer ? "YOU" : entry.username);
	        nameLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));
	        nameLbl.setForeground(entry.isPlayer ? new Color(80, 255, 80) : new Color(220, 220, 235));
	        namePanel.add(avatarLbl);
	        namePanel.add(nameLbl);
	        
	        
	        JLabel valueLbl = new JLabel(String.format("$%,.0f", entry.inventoryValue), SwingConstants.RIGHT);
	        valueLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        Color valueColor;
	        if (entry.inventoryValue >= 10_000_000) valueColor = new Color(255, 80, 80);
	        else if (entry.inventoryValue >= 1_000_000) valueColor = new Color(255, 215, 0);
	        else if (entry.inventoryValue >= 500_000)  valueColor = new Color(255, 165, 0);
	        else valueColor = new Color(100, 220, 255);
	        valueLbl.setForeground(entry.isPlayer ? new Color(80, 255, 80) : valueColor);
	        valueLbl.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(0, 0, 0, 6));
	        
	        row.add(rankLbl, BorderLayout.WEST);
	        row.add(namePanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        row.add(valueLbl, BorderLayout.EAST);
	        listPanel.add(row);
	    }
	    
	    
	    if (!finalPlayerInTop100 && inventoryValue > 0) {
	        
	        JPanel sep = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	        sep.setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 20));
	        sep.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 36));
	        JLabel sepLbl = new JLabel("\u2219\u2219\u2219  Your Ranking  \u2219\u2219\u2219", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        sepLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 12));
	        sepLbl.setForeground(new Color(100, 100, 130));
	        sep.add(sepLbl, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        sep.setBorder(BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(1, 0, 1, 0, new Color(40, 40, 60)));
	        listPanel.add(sep);
	        
	        
	        JPanel playerRow = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(8, 0));
	        playerRow.setBackground(new Color(25, 70, 25));
	        playerRow.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 60));
	        playerRow.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(80, 220, 80), 2),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 9, 4, 9)));
	        
	        int displayRank = finalPlayerSimRank > 0 ? finalPlayerSimRank : 999999;
	        JLabel playerRankLbl = new JLabel(" #" + String.format("%,d", displayRank), SwingConstants.LEFT);
	        playerRankLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));
	        playerRankLbl.setForeground(new Color(80, 255, 80));
	        playerRankLbl.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(90, 50));
	        
	        JPanel playerNamePanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 6, 8));
	        playerNamePanel.setBackground(new Color(25, 70, 25));
	        playerNamePanel.add(new JLabel(new ImageIcon(playerAvatar.getScaledInstance(36, 36, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH))));
	        JLabel playerNameLbl = new JLabel("YOU");
	        playerNameLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        playerNameLbl.setForeground(new Color(80, 255, 80));
	        playerNamePanel.add(playerNameLbl);
	        
	        JLabel playerValLbl = new JLabel(String.format("$%,.0f", inventoryValue), SwingConstants.RIGHT);
	        playerValLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 15));
	        playerValLbl.setForeground(new Color(80, 255, 80));
	        playerValLbl.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(0, 0, 0, 6));
	        
	        playerRow.add(playerRankLbl, BorderLayout.WEST);
	        playerRow.add(playerNamePanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        playerRow.add(playerValLbl, BorderLayout.EAST);
	        listPanel.add(playerRow);
	    }
	    
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(listPanel);
	    scroll.setBorder(null);
	    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    scroll.setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 20));
	    frame.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    
	    JPanel footer = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.CENTER, 20, 8));
	    footer.setBackground(new Color(18, 18, 28));
	    footer.setBorder(BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(2, 0, 0, 0, new Color(40, 40, 60)));
	    JLabel footerLbl = new JLabel(String.format("Simulated global pool: %,d players  |  Updated on open",
	        globalLeaderboard.size()));
	    footerLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	    footerLbl.setForeground(new Color(100, 100, 130));
	    footer.add(footerLbl);
	    frame.add(footer, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    
	    frame.setVisible(true);
	    
	    
	    if (finalPlayerInTop100) {
	        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	            for (int i = 0; i < top100.size(); i++) {
	                if (top100.get(i).isPlayer) {
	                    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setValue(Math.max(0, (i - 3) * 55));
	                    break;
	                }
	            }
	        });
	    }
	}
	
	private void showLeaderboard() {

	    boolean playerInLeaderboard = false;
	    for (LeaderboardEntry entry : globalLeaderboard) {
	        if (entry.isPlayer) {
	            entry.inventoryValue = inventoryValue;
	            playerInLeaderboard = true;
	            break;
	        }
	    }
	    
	    if (!playerInLeaderboard && inventoryValue > 0) {
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry("YOU", inventoryValue, playerAvatar, true));
	    }
	    
	    globalLeaderboard.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.inventoryValue, a.inventoryValue));
	    for (int i = 0; i < globalLeaderboard.size(); i++) {
	        globalLeaderboard.get(i).rank = i + 1;
	    }
	    
	    int playerRank = -1;
	    boolean hasInventoryValue = inventoryValue > 0;
	    
	    for (LeaderboardEntry entry : globalLeaderboard) {
	        if (entry.isPlayer) {
	            playerRank = entry.rank;
	            break;
	        }
	    }
	    
	    final int finalPlayerRank = playerRank;
	    final boolean finalHasInventoryValue = hasInventoryValue;
	    
	    JFrame leaderboardFrame = new JFrame("Global Leaderboard");
	    leaderboardFrame.setSize(700, 800);
	    leaderboardFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    leaderboardFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    JPanel headerPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1));
	    headerPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    headerPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    JLabel titleLabel = new JLabel("GLOBAL LEADERBOARD", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    titleLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 24));
	    titleLabel.setForeground(new Color(255, 215, 0));
	    
	    String rankText = finalHasInventoryValue && finalPlayerRank != -1 ? 
	        String.format("Your Rank: #%d / %d", finalPlayerRank, globalLeaderboard.size()) :
	        "Your Rank: N/A (Build inventory to rank)";
	    
	    JLabel yourRankLabel = new JLabel(rankText, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    yourRankLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 18));
	    yourRankLabel.setForeground(finalHasInventoryValue && finalPlayerRank != -1 ? 
	        (finalPlayerRank <= 100 ? Color.GREEN : 
	         finalPlayerRank <= 1000 ? Color.CYAN : Color.WHITE) : Color.GRAY);
	    
	    headerPanel.add(titleLabel);
	    headerPanel.add(yourRankLabel);
	    leaderboardFrame.add(headerPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JPanel listPanel = new JPanel();
	    listPanel.setLayout(new BoxLayout(listPanel, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    listPanel.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    
	    int startIdx = 0;
	    int endIdx = 0;
	    boolean showTopSeparately = false;
	    
	    if (finalHasInventoryValue && finalPlayerRank != -1) {

	        startIdx = Math.max(0, finalPlayerRank - 26);
	        endIdx = Math.min(globalLeaderboard.size(), finalPlayerRank + 24);
	        
	        showTopSeparately = finalPlayerRank > 35;
	    } else {

	        startIdx = 0;
	        endIdx = Math.min(50, globalLeaderboard.size());
	    }
	    
	    final int finalStartIdx = startIdx;
	    
	    if (showTopSeparately) {
	        for (int i = 0; i < Math.min(10, globalLeaderboard.size()); i++) {
	            LeaderboardEntry entry = globalLeaderboard.get(i);
	            JPanel entryPanel = createLeaderboardEntryPanel(entry);
	            listPanel.add(entryPanel);
	            listPanel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 2)));
	        }
	        
	        JPanel separator = new JPanel();
	        separator.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 30));
	        separator.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	        JLabel sepLabel = new JLabel("...", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        sepLabel.setForeground(Color.GRAY);
	        sepLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 20));
	        separator.add(sepLabel);
	        listPanel.add(separator);
	    }
	    
	    for (int i = startIdx; i < endIdx; i++) {
	        LeaderboardEntry entry = globalLeaderboard.get(i);
	        JPanel entryPanel = createLeaderboardEntryPanel(entry);
	        listPanel.add(entryPanel);
	        listPanel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 2)));
	    }
	    
	    JScrollPane scrollPane = new JScrollPane(listPanel);
	    scrollPane.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    scrollPane.setBorder(null);
	    leaderboardFrame.add(scrollPane, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    if (finalHasInventoryValue && finalPlayerRank != -1) {
	        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	            int scrollPosition = Math.max(0, (finalPlayerRank - finalStartIdx - 10) * 62);
	            scrollPane.getVerticalScrollBar().setValue(scrollPosition);
	        });
	    }
	    leaderboardFrame.setVisible(true);
	}
	
	private JPanel createLeaderboardEntryPanel(LeaderboardEntry entry) {
	    JPanel entryPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    entryPanel.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 60));
	    entryPanel.setBackground(entry.isPlayer ? new Color(50, 100, 50) : new Color(45, 45, 50));
	    entryPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(
	        entry.isPlayer ? Color.GREEN : Color.GRAY, entry.isPlayer ? 3 : 1));
	    
	    JLabel rankLabel = new JLabel("#" + entry.rank);
	    rankLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 20));
	    rankLabel.setForeground(entry.rank <= 3 ? new Color(255, 215, 0) : 
	                           entry.rank <= 10 ? new Color(192, 192, 192) :
	                           entry.rank <= 100 ? new Color(205, 127, 50) : Color.WHITE);
	    rankLabel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(0, 15, 0, 15));
	    
	    JPanel infoPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));
	    infoPanel.setBackground(entryPanel.getBackground());
	    infoPanel.add(new JLabel(new ImageIcon(entry.avatar.getScaledInstance(40, 40, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH))));
	    JLabel nameLabel = new JLabel(entry.username);
	    nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    nameLabel.setForeground(entry.isPlayer ? Color.GREEN : Color.WHITE);
	    infoPanel.add(nameLabel);
	    
	    JPanel rightPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.RIGHT, 10, 10));
	    rightPanel.setBackground(entryPanel.getBackground());
	    
	    JLabel valueLabel = new JLabel("$" + String.format("%,.2f", entry.inventoryValue));
	    valueLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    valueLabel.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
	    rightPanel.add(valueLabel);
	    
	    entryPanel.add(rankLabel, BorderLayout.WEST);
	    entryPanel.add(infoPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    entryPanel.add(rightPanel, BorderLayout.EAST);
	    
	    return entryPanel;
	}
	
	private void showCaseSelection() {
	    JFrame caseFrame = new JFrame("Select Case Type");
	    caseFrame.setSize(600, 500);
	    caseFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    caseFrame.setLayout(new GridLayout(2, 2, 20, 20));
	    caseFrame.getContentPane().setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    ((JPanel)caseFrame.getContentPane()).setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(20, 20, 20, 20));
	    
	    for (CaseType caseType : CaseType.values()) {
	        JPanel casePanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	        casePanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	        casePanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(currentCase == caseType ? Color.GREEN : Color.GRAY, 3),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(15, 15, 15, 15)
	        ));
	        
	        JLabel nameLabel = new JLabel(caseType.name, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 20));
	        nameLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	        
	        JLabel priceLabel = new JLabel("$" + String.format("%.2f", caseType.price), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        priceLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 18));
	        priceLabel.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
	        
	        String description = "";
	        if (caseType == CaseType.WEAPON_CASE_ONE) description = "Knives only | $75.00";
	        else if (caseType == CaseType.BRAVO)      description = "Knives only | $50.00";
	        else if (caseType == CaseType.BREAKOUT)   description = "Gloves only | $10.00";
	        else if (caseType == CaseType.SPECTRUM)   description = "Gloves only | $5.00";
	        
	        JLabel descLabel = new JLabel(description, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        descLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.ITALIC, 14));
	        descLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	        
	        JButton selectBtn = new JButton("SELECT");
	        selectBtn.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        selectBtn.setBackground(new Color(50, 150, 50));
	        selectBtn.addActionListener(e -> {
	            currentCase = caseType;
	            currentCaseLabel.setText(currentCase.name);
	            openCrateButton.setText(String.format("OPEN ($%.2f)", currentCase.price));
	            caseFrame.dispose();
	        });
	        
	        JPanel infoPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(4, 1));
	        infoPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	        infoPanel.add(nameLabel);
	        infoPanel.add(priceLabel);
	        infoPanel.add(descLabel);
	        infoPanel.add(selectBtn);
	        
	        casePanel.add(infoPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        caseFrame.add(casePanel);
	    }
	    
	    caseFrame.setVisible(true);
	}
	
	private void addToSearchHistory(String query) {
	    query = query.trim().toLowerCase();
	    if (query.isEmpty()) return;
	    
	    searchHistory.remove(query);
	    searchHistory.addFirst(query);
	    
	    if (searchHistory.size() > MAX_SEARCH_HISTORY) {
	        searchHistory.removeLast();
	    }
	}

	private JComboBox<String> createSearchFieldWithHistory() {
	    JComboBox<String> searchBox = new JComboBox<>();
	    searchBox.setEditable(true);
	    styleComboBox(searchBox);
	    searchBox.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 13));
	    
	    for (String query : searchHistory) {
	        searchBox.addItem(query);
	    }
	    
	    return searchBox;
	}
	
	private void updateLeaderboard() {
	    globalLeaderboard.removeIf(entry -> entry.isPlayer);
	    
	    if (inventoryValue > 0) {
	        globalLeaderboard.add(new LeaderboardEntry("YOU", inventoryValue, playerAvatar, true));
	    }
	    
	    globalLeaderboard.sort((a, b) -> Double.compare(b.inventoryValue, a.inventoryValue));
	    for (int i = 0; i < globalLeaderboard.size(); i++) {
	        globalLeaderboard.get(i).rank = i + 1;
	    }
	}
	
	private void showROIWindow() {
	    JFrame roiFrame = new JFrame("Case Type ROI Statistics");
	    roiFrame.setSize(900, 800);
	    roiFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    roiFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    roiFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(true);
	    
	    JPanel headerPanel = new JPanel();
	    headerPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    headerPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(20, 20, 20, 20));
	    
	    JLabel titleLabel = new JLabel("Case Type ROI Analysis", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    titleLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 28));
	    titleLabel.setForeground(Color.WHITE);
	    headerPanel.add(titleLabel);
	    
	    roiFrame.add(headerPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JPanel statsContainer = new JPanel();
	    statsContainer.setLayout(new BoxLayout(statsContainer, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    statsContainer.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    statsContainer.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(30, 40, 30, 40));
	    
	    for (CaseType caseType : CaseType.values()) {
	        JPanel casePanel = createCaseROIPanel(caseType);
	        statsContainer.add(casePanel);
	        statsContainer.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 25)));
	    }
	    
	    JScrollPane scrollPane = new JScrollPane(statsContainer);
	    scrollPane.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    scrollPane.setBorder(null);
	    scrollPane.getViewport().setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    
	    roiFrame.add(scrollPane, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    JPanel footerPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.CENTER));
	    footerPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    footerPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(15, 15, 15, 15));
	    
	    JLabel infoLabel = new JLabel("ROI = (Total Received - Total Spent) / Total Spent × 100%");
	    infoLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.ITALIC, 14));
	    infoLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	    footerPanel.add(infoLabel);
	    
	    roiFrame.add(footerPanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    
	    roiFrame.setVisible(true);
	    
	    javax.swing.Timer timer = new javax.swing.Timer(100, e -> {
	        roiFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(false);
	        roiFrame.toFront();
	        roiFrame.requestFocus();
	    });
	    timer.setRepeats(false);
	    timer.start();
	}
	
	private JPanel createCaseROIPanel(CaseType caseType) {
	    JPanel panel = new JPanel();
	    panel.setLayout(new BoxLayout(panel, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    panel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    panel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(Color.GRAY, 2),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(20, 20, 20, 20)
	    ));
	    panel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(700, 280));
	    panel.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(800, 280));
	    
	    JPanel headerPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT));
	    headerPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    headerPanel.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 40));
	    
	    JLabel nameLabel = new JLabel(caseType.name + " - $" + String.format("%.2f", caseType.price));
	    nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 20));
	    nameLabel.setForeground(Color.YELLOW);
	    headerPanel.add(nameLabel);
	    
	    panel.add(headerPanel);
	    panel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 10)));
	    
	    JPanel statsPanel = new JPanel();
	    statsPanel.setLayout(new BoxLayout(statsPanel, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    statsPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    
	    addROIStatRow(statsPanel, "Times Opened:", String.valueOf(caseType.timesOpened));
	    addROIStatRow(statsPanel, "Total Spent:", "$" + String.format("%,.2f", caseType.totalSpent));
	    addROIStatRow(statsPanel, "Total Received:", "$" + String.format("%,.2f", caseType.totalReceived));
	    
	    double roi = caseType.getROI();
	    Color roiColor = roi >= 0 ? new Color(50, 200, 50) : Color.RED;
	    String roiSign = roi >= 0 ? "+" : "";
	    addROIStatRow(statsPanel, "ROI:", roiSign + String.format("%.2f%%", roi), roiColor);
	    
	    double avgProfit = caseType.getAverageProfit();
	    Color profitColor = avgProfit >= 0 ? new Color(50, 200, 50) : Color.RED;
	    String profitSign = avgProfit >= 0 ? "+" : "";
	    addROIStatRow(statsPanel, "Avg Profit/Case:", profitSign + "$" + String.format("%.2f", avgProfit), profitColor);
	    
	    panel.add(statsPanel);
	    
	    return panel;
	}
	
	private void addROIStatRow(JPanel panel, String label, String value) {
	    addROIStatRow(panel, label, value, Color.WHITE);
	}

	private void addROIStatRow(JPanel panel, String label, String value, Color valueColor) {
	    JPanel rowPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    rowPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    rowPanel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(650, 40));
	    rowPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(5, 10, 5, 10));
	    
	    JLabel labelComp = new JLabel(label);
	    labelComp.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    labelComp.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	    
	    JLabel valueComp = new JLabel(value);
	    valueComp.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    valueComp.setForeground(valueColor);
	    valueComp.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.RIGHT);
	    
	    rowPanel.add(labelComp, BorderLayout.WEST);
	    rowPanel.add(valueComp, BorderLayout.EAST);
	    
	    panel.add(rowPanel);
	}
	
	private void showMarketAnalytics() {
	    JFrame analyticsFrame = new JFrame("Market Analytics");
	    analyticsFrame.setSize(1400, 900);
	    analyticsFrame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    analyticsFrame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    
	    analyticsFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(true);
	    
	    JPanel headerPanel = new JPanel();
	    headerPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    headerPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(15, 15, 15, 15));
	    
	    JLabel titleLabel = new JLabel("MARKET ANALYTICS", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    titleLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 28));
	    titleLabel.setForeground(new Color(255, 215, 0));
	    headerPanel.add(titleLabel);
	    
	    analyticsFrame.add(headerPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JTabbedPane tabbedPane = new JTabbedPane();
	    
	    tabbedPane.addTab("Price Movers", createPriceMoversPanel());
	    
	    analyticsFrame.add(tabbedPane, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    analyticsFrame.setVisible(true);
	    
	    javax.swing.Timer timer = new javax.swing.Timer(100, e -> {
	        analyticsFrame.setAlwaysOnTop(false);
	        analyticsFrame.toFront();
	        analyticsFrame.requestFocus();
	    });
	    timer.setRepeats(false);
	    timer.start();
	}
	
	private JPanel createPriceMoversPanel() {
		JPanel mainPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    mainPanel.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    
	    JPanel controlPanel = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.CENTER));
	    controlPanel.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 35));
	    controlPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 10, 10, 10));
	    
	    JButton refreshButton = new JButton("REFRESH DATA");
	    refreshButton.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    refreshButton.setBackground(new Color(70, 130, 180));
	    refreshButton.setForeground(Color.BLACK);
	    refreshButton.setFocusPainted(false);
	    refreshButton.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(200, 40));
	    	    
	    JLabel lastUpdateLabel = new JLabel("Click refresh to update price movers");
	    lastUpdateLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.ITALIC, 12));
	    lastUpdateLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
	    
	    controlPanel.add(refreshButton);
	    controlPanel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(10, 0)));
	    controlPanel.add(lastUpdateLabel);
	    
	    mainPanel.add(controlPanel, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JPanel panel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(1, 2, 20, 0));
	    panel.setBackground(new Color(35, 35, 40));
	    panel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(20, 20, 20, 20));
	    
	    JPanel gainersPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    gainersPanel.setBackground(new Color(40, 40, 45));
	    gainersPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(50, 200, 50), 3),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(15, 15, 15, 15)
	    ));
	    
	    JLabel gainersTitle = new JLabel("TOP 10 GAINERS", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    gainersTitle.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 22));
	    gainersTitle.setForeground(new Color(50, 255, 50));
	    gainersTitle.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(0, 0, 15, 0));
	    gainersPanel.add(gainersTitle, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JPanel gainersListPanel = new JPanel();
	    gainersListPanel.setLayout(new BoxLayout(gainersListPanel, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    gainersListPanel.setBackground(new Color(40, 40, 45));
	    
	    List<PriceMover> gainers = getTopPriceMovers(true);
	    for (int i = 0; i < gainers.size(); i++) {
	        PriceMover mover = gainers.get(i);
	        JPanel moverCard = createPriceMoverCard(mover, i + 1, true);
	        gainersListPanel.add(moverCard);
	        gainersListPanel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 8)));
	    }
	    
	    JScrollPane gainersScroll = new JScrollPane(gainersListPanel);
	    gainersScroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    gainersScroll.setBorder(null);
	    gainersScroll.getViewport().setBackground(new Color(40, 40, 45));
	    gainersPanel.add(gainersScroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    JPanel losersPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    losersPanel.setBackground(new Color(40, 40, 45));
	    losersPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(200, 50, 50), 3),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(15, 15, 15, 15)
	    ));
	    
	    JLabel losersTitle = new JLabel("TOP 10 LOSERS", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    losersTitle.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 22));
	    losersTitle.setForeground(new Color(255, 50, 50));
	    losersTitle.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(0, 0, 15, 0));
	    losersPanel.add(losersTitle, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    JPanel losersListPanel = new JPanel();
	    losersListPanel.setLayout(new BoxLayout(losersListPanel, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    losersListPanel.setBackground(new Color(40, 40, 45));
	    
	    List<PriceMover> losers = getTopPriceMovers(false);
	    for (int i = 0; i < losers.size(); i++) {
	        PriceMover mover = losers.get(i);
	        JPanel moverCard = createPriceMoverCard(mover, i + 1, false);
	        losersListPanel.add(moverCard);
	        losersListPanel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 8)));
	    }
	    
	    JScrollPane losersScroll = new JScrollPane(losersListPanel);
	    losersScroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    losersScroll.setBorder(null);
	    losersScroll.getViewport().setBackground(new Color(40, 40, 45));
	    losersPanel.add(losersScroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    panel.add(gainersPanel);
	    panel.add(losersPanel);
	    
	    mainPanel.add(panel, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    refreshButton.addActionListener(e -> {
	        refreshButton.setEnabled(false);
	        refreshButton.setText("Refreshing...");
	        
	        SwingWorker<Void, Void> worker = new SwingWorker<Void, Void>() {
	            @Override
	            protected Void doInBackground() throws Exception {
	                Thread.sleep(500);
	                return null;
	            }
	            
	            @Override
	            protected void done() {
	                refreshPriceMoversPanel(gainersListPanel, losersListPanel);
	                
	                java.text.SimpleDateFormat sdf = new java.text.SimpleDateFormat("HH:mm:ss");
	                lastUpdateLabel.setText("Last updated: " + sdf.format(new java.util.Date()));
	                
	                refreshButton.setText("REFRESH DATA");
	                refreshButton.setEnabled(true);
	            }
	        };
	        worker.execute();
	    });
	    
	    return mainPanel;
	}
	
	private static class PriceMover {
	    String baseName;
	    boolean isStatTrak;
	    String condition;
	    String rarity;
	    double currentPrice;
	    double initialPrice;
	    double changePercent;
	    Image skinImage;

	    PriceMover(String marketKey,
	               String baseName,
	               boolean isStatTrak,
	               String condition,
	               String rarity,
	               double currentPrice,
	               double initialPrice,
	               Image skinImage) {

	        this.baseName = baseName;
	        this.isStatTrak = isStatTrak;
	        this.condition = condition;
	        this.rarity = rarity;
	        this.currentPrice = currentPrice;
	        this.initialPrice = initialPrice;
	        this.changePercent =
	                initialPrice > 0
	                        ? ((currentPrice - initialPrice) / initialPrice) * 100.0
	                        : 0;
	        this.skinImage = skinImage;
	    }
	}
	
	private List<PriceMover> getTopPriceMovers(boolean topGainers) {
	    List<PriceMover> movers = new ArrayList<>();

	    if (priceTrackingStartTime == 0) {
	        priceTrackingStartTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
	        captureInitialConditionPrices();
	    }

	    for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> entry : globalMarketListings.entrySet()) {
	        String marketKey = entry.getKey();
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = entry.getValue();
	        if (listings == null || listings.isEmpty()) continue;

	        MarketListing sample = listings.get(0);

	        boolean isStatTrak = sample.item.isStattrak;
	        String baseName = normalizeSkinName(sample.item.name);
	        String rarity = getSkinRarity(baseName);
	        Image skinImg = getSkinImageFromName(baseName);

	        Map<String, List<MarketListing>> byCondition =
	                listings.stream().collect(Collectors.groupingBy(l -> l.item.condition));

	        for (Map.Entry<String, List<MarketListing>> condEntry : byCondition.entrySet()) {
	            String condition = condEntry.getKey();

	            double currentLowest = condEntry.getValue().stream()
	                    .mapToDouble(l -> l.listPrice)
	                    .min()
	                    .orElse(0);

	            if (currentLowest <= 0) continue;

	            Map<String, Double> condMap =
	                    initialConditionPrices.computeIfAbsent(
	                            marketKey, k -> new HashMap<>());

	            double initial = condMap.computeIfAbsent(condition, k -> currentLowest);

	            movers.add(new PriceMover(
	                    marketKey,
	                    baseName,
	                    isStatTrak,
	                    condition,
	                    rarity,
	                    currentLowest,
	                    initial,
	                    skinImg
	            ));
	        }
	    }

	    movers.sort((a, b) ->
	            topGainers
	                    ? Double.compare(b.changePercent, a.changePercent)
	                    : Double.compare(a.changePercent, b.changePercent)
	    );

	    return movers.subList(0, Math.min(10, movers.size()));
	}
	
	private void refreshPriceMoversPanel(JPanel gainersListPanel, JPanel losersListPanel) {

	    gainersListPanel.removeAll();
	    losersListPanel.removeAll();
	    
	    List<PriceMover> gainers = getTopPriceMovers(true);
	    for (int i = 0; i < gainers.size(); i++) {
	        PriceMover mover = gainers.get(i);
	        JPanel moverCard = createPriceMoverCard(mover, i + 1, true);
	        gainersListPanel.add(moverCard);
	        gainersListPanel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 8)));
	    }
	    
	    List<PriceMover> losers = getTopPriceMovers(false);
	    for (int i = 0; i < losers.size(); i++) {
	        PriceMover mover = losers.get(i);
	        JPanel moverCard = createPriceMoverCard(mover, i + 1, false);
	        losersListPanel.add(moverCard);
	        losersListPanel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 8)));
	    }
	    
	    gainersListPanel.revalidate();
	    gainersListPanel.repaint();
	    losersListPanel.revalidate();
	    losersListPanel.repaint();
	}
	
	private JPanel createPriceMoverCard(PriceMover mover, int rank, boolean isGainer) {
	    JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    card.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 110));
	    card.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(
	                    isGainer ? new Color(50, 200, 50) : new Color(200, 50, 50), 2),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 10, 8, 10)
	    ));

	    JLabel rankLabel = new JLabel("#" + rank);
	    rankLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 20));
	    rankLabel.setForeground(rank <= 3 ? Color.YELLOW : Color.WHITE);
	    rankLabel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(0, 5, 0, 15));
	    card.add(rankLabel, BorderLayout.WEST);

	    JPanel imagePanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    imagePanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    imagePanel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(100, 70));
	    if (mover.skinImage != null) {
	        Image scaled = mover.skinImage.getScaledInstance(100, 70, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH);
	        imagePanel.add(new JLabel(new ImageIcon(scaled)), BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    }
	    card.add(imagePanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JPanel infoPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(4, 1));
	    infoPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));

	    String displayName = mover.isStatTrak
	            ? "StatTrak " + mover.baseName
	            : mover.baseName;

	    JLabel nameLabel = new JLabel(displayName + " (" + mover.condition + ")");
	    nameLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 13));
	    nameLabel.setForeground(
	            mover.isStatTrak ? new Color(255, 153, 51) : Color.WHITE
	    );

	    JLabel rarityLabel = new JLabel(mover.rarity);
	    rarityLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	    rarityLabel.setForeground(getRarityColor(mover.rarity));

	    JLabel priceLabel = new JLabel(
	            String.format("$%.2f -> $%.2f", mover.initialPrice, mover.currentPrice)
	    );
	    priceLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    priceLabel.setForeground(Color.LIGHT_GRAY);

	    JLabel changeLabel = new JLabel(String.format("%+.2f%%", mover.changePercent));
	    changeLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    changeLabel.setForeground(
	            isGainer ? new Color(50, 255, 50) : new Color(255, 50, 50)
	    );

	    infoPanel.add(nameLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(rarityLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(priceLabel);
	    infoPanel.add(changeLabel);

	    JPanel rightPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(5, 0));
	    rightPanel.setBackground(new Color(50, 50, 55));
	    rightPanel.add(infoPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    card.add(rightPanel, BorderLayout.EAST);

	    return card;
	}
	
	

	private void updateLegendAndChart(JList<String> skinList, JPanel legendPanel, 
            JPanel chartPanel, JComboBox<String> conditionSelector) {

		Component[] components = legendPanel.getComponents();
		for (int i = components.length - 1; i > 1; i--) {
			legendPanel.remove(i);
		}

		Color[] colors = {
				Color.RED, Color.BLUE, new Color(255, 0, 255), 
				new Color(0, 150, 0), new Color(255, 140, 0), 
				new Color(0, 200, 200), new Color(139, 69, 19),
				new Color(255, 20, 147), new Color(0, 255, 127),
				new Color(255, 215, 0)
		};

		String selectedCondition = (String) conditionSelector.getSelectedItem();
		List<String> selected = skinList.getSelectedValuesList();
		int colorIndex = 0;

		for (String skinName : selected) {
			JPanel legendItem = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.LEFT, 3, 3));
			legendItem.setBackground(new Color(250, 250, 255));
			legendItem.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(200, 50));

			JPanel colorBox = new JPanel();
			colorBox.setBackground(colors[colorIndex % colors.length]);
			colorBox.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(15, 15));
			colorBox.setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(Color.BLACK, 1));

			String displayName = skinName.length() > 20 ? 
					skinName.substring(0, 17) + "..." : skinName;
			JLabel skinLabel = new JLabel("<html>" + displayName + 
					"<br><small>" + selectedCondition + "</small></html>");
			skinLabel.setFont(new Font("Arial", Font.PLAIN, 9));
			skinLabel.setForeground(new Color(50, 50, 50));
			skinLabel.setToolTipText(skinName + " (" + selectedCondition + ")");

			legendItem.add(colorBox);
			legendItem.add(skinLabel);
			legendPanel.add(legendItem);
			legendPanel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 3)));

			colorIndex++;
		}

		legendPanel.revalidate();
		legendPanel.repaint();
		chartPanel.repaint();
	}
	
	private void captureInitialConditionPrices() {
	    initialConditionPrices.clear();
	    
	    for (Map.Entry<String, ArrayList<MarketListing>> entry : globalMarketListings.entrySet()) {
	        String skinName = entry.getKey();
	        ArrayList<MarketListing> listings = entry.getValue();
	        
	        if (listings != null && !listings.isEmpty()) {
	            Map<String, Double> conditionPrices = new HashMap<>();
	            
	            Map<String, List<MarketListing>> byCondition = listings.stream()
	                .collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.groupingBy(l -> l.item.condition));
	            
	            for (Map.Entry<String, List<MarketListing>> condEntry : byCondition.entrySet()) {
	                String condition = condEntry.getKey();
	                double lowestPrice = condEntry.getValue().stream()
	                    .mapToDouble(l -> l.listPrice)
	                    .min()
	                    .orElse(0);
	                
	                if (lowestPrice > 0) {
	                    conditionPrices.put(condition, lowestPrice);
	                }
	            }
	            
	            if (!conditionPrices.isEmpty()) {
	                initialConditionPrices.put(skinName, conditionPrices);
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    for (Map.Entry<String, Map<String, Double>> entry : initialConditionPrices.entrySet()) {
	        String skinName = entry.getKey();
	        Map<String, Double> conditions = entry.getValue();
	        
	        for (Map.Entry<String, Double> condEntry : conditions.entrySet()) {
	            String condition = condEntry.getKey();
	            double price = condEntry.getValue();
	            
	            String historyKey = skinName + ":" + condition;
	            skinConditionPriceHistory
	                .computeIfAbsent(historyKey, k -> new ArrayList<>())
	                .add(price);
	        }
	    }
	}
	

	
	
	
	public static class Mission {
	    String id;
	    String name;
	    String description;
	    String type; 
	    int goal;
	    int current;
	    int starReward;
	    boolean completed;
	    
	    Mission(String id, String name, String description, String type, int goal, int starReward) {
	        this.id = id; this.name = name; this.description = description;
	        this.type = type; this.goal = goal; this.starReward = starReward;
	        this.current = 0; this.completed = false;
	    }
	    double progressPct() { return Math.min(1.0, (double)current / goal); }
	}
