	private void generateNewMissions() {
	    activeMissions.clear();
	    java.util.List<Object[]> pool = new java.util.ArrayList<>(java.util.Arrays.asList(ALL_MISSION_TEMPLATES));
	    java.util.Collections.shuffle(pool, random);
	    // Pick 4 missions, at most one per mission TYPE to prevent overlapping goals
	    java.util.Set<String> usedTypes = new java.util.HashSet<>();
	    int count = 0;
	    for (Object[] tpl : pool) {
	        if (count >= 4) break;
	        String type = (String)tpl[3];
	        if (usedTypes.contains(type)) continue;
	        usedTypes.add(type);
	        String id = (String)tpl[0] + "_" + System.currentTimeMillis();
	        activeMissions.add(new Mission(id, (String)tpl[1], (String)tpl[2],
	            (String)tpl[3], (int)tpl[4], (int)tpl[5]));
	        count++;
	    }
	    missionCasesOpened = 0; missionTradeUps = 0;
	    missionMarketSpent = 0; missionKnivesUnboxed = 0;
	    missionGlovesUnboxed = 0; missionMarketSales = 0;
	    missionArmouryRedeems = 0; missionCovertsUnboxed = 0;
	    missionClassifiedsUnboxed = 0;
	}
	
	private void checkMissionProgress() {
	    if (activeMissions.isEmpty()) return;
	    boolean anyCompleted = false;
	    for (Mission m : activeMissions) {
	        if (m.completed) continue;
	        int prev = m.current;
	        switch (m.type) {
	            case "CASES":        m.current = missionCasesOpened; break;
	            case "TRADEUP":      m.current = missionTradeUps; break;
	            case "MARKET_SPEND": m.current = (int)(missionMarketSpent / 100.0); break;
	            case "MARKET_SELL":  m.current = missionMarketSellCount; break;
	            case "KNIFE":        m.current = missionKnivesUnboxed; break;
	            case "GLOVES":       m.current = missionGlovesUnboxed; break;
	            case "ARMOURY":      m.current = missionArmouryRedeems; break;
	            case "INVENTORY":    m.current = inventoryList.size(); break;
	            case "COVERT":       m.current = missionCovertsUnboxed; break;
	            case "CLASSIFIED":   m.current = missionClassifiedsUnboxed; break;
	            case "BALANCE":      m.current = (int)Math.min(balance, m.goal); break;
	        }
	        if (m.current >= m.goal && !m.completed) {
	            m.completed = true;
	            m.current = m.goal;
	            awardStars(m.starReward, m.name);
	            anyCompleted = true;
	        }
	    }
	}
	
	private void awardStars(int amount, String source) {
	    playerStars += amount;
	    updateStarsLabel();
	    
	    javax.swing.SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
	        JPanel notif = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(6, 0));
	        notif.setBackground(new Color(20, 20, 32));
	        notif.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(255, 215, 0), 2),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 12, 8, 12)));
	        JLabel icon = new JLabel("*", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        icon.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 26));
	        icon.setForeground(new Color(255, 215, 0));
	        JLabel msg = new JLabel("<html><b>Mission Complete!</b><br>" + source + "<br>+" + amount + " Star" + (amount > 1 ? "s" : "") + " awarded</html>");
	        msg.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	        msg.setForeground(new Color(230, 230, 235));
	        notif.add(icon, BorderLayout.WEST);
	        notif.add(msg, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        notif.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(280, 70));
	        JLayeredPane lp2 = getLayeredPane();
	        notif.setBounds(lp2.getWidth() - 292, lp2.getHeight() - 82, 280, 70);
	        JLayeredPane lp = getLayeredPane();
	        lp.add(notif, JLayeredPane.POPUP_LAYER);
	        lp.revalidate(); lp.repaint();
	        javax.swing.Timer t = new javax.swing.Timer(3500, ev -> {
	            lp.remove(notif); lp.revalidate(); lp.repaint();
	        });
	        t.setRepeats(false); t.start();
	    });
	}
	
	private void updateStarsLabel() {
	    if (starsLabel != null)
	        starsLabel.setText("* " + playerStars + " Star" + (playerStars == 1 ? "" : "s"));
	    if (armouryStarsDisp != null)
	        armouryStarsDisp.setText("* " + playerStars + " Stars");
	}
	
	private void showMissionsWindow() {
	    if (activeMissions.isEmpty()) generateNewMissions();
	    
	    JFrame frame = new JFrame("Missions");
	    frame.setSize(620, 520);
	    frame.setLocationRelativeTo(this);
	    frame.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    frame.getContentPane().setBackground(new Color(10, 10, 18));
	    
	    
	    JPanel header = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    header.setBackground(new Color(18, 18, 30));
	    header.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 2, 0, new Color(100, 180, 255)),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(14, 20, 14, 20)));
	    JLabel titleLbl = new JLabel("*  MISSIONS  *", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    titleLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 22));
	    titleLbl.setForeground(new Color(255, 215, 0));
	    JLabel subLbl = new JLabel("Complete missions to earn Stars. Stars are spent in the Armoury.", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    subLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	    subLbl.setForeground(new Color(140, 160, 200));
	    JLabel starsLbl = new JLabel("Your Stars: " + playerStars + " *", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    starsLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 14));
	    starsLbl.setForeground(new Color(255, 215, 0));
	    JPanel headerSub = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2,1,0,4));
	    headerSub.setBackground(new Color(18, 18, 30));
	    headerSub.add(subLbl);
	    headerSub.add(starsLbl);
	    header.add(titleLbl, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    header.add(headerSub, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    frame.add(header, BorderLayout.NORTH);
	    
	    
	    JPanel missionPanel = new JPanel();
	    missionPanel.setLayout(new BoxLayout(missionPanel, BoxLayout.Y_AXIS));
	    missionPanel.setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 20));
	    missionPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(16, 20, 16, 20));
	    
	    checkMissionProgress();
	    
	    for (Mission m : activeMissions) {
	        JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(12, 6));
	        card.setBackground(m.completed ? new Color(20, 50, 20) : new Color(22, 22, 36));
	        card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	            BorderFactory.createLineBorder(m.completed ? new Color(80, 200, 80) : new Color(50, 55, 80), 2),
	            BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(14, 16, 14, 16)));
	        card.setMaximumSize(new Dimension(Integer.MAX_VALUE, 100));
	        
	        
	        JPanel badge = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	        badge.setBackground(card.getBackground());
	        badge.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(70, 60));
	        JLabel badgeNumLbl = new JLabel("+" + m.starReward, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        badgeNumLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 20));
	        badgeNumLbl.setForeground(new Color(255, 215, 0));
	        JLabel badgeStarLbl = new JLabel("Stars", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        badgeStarLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));
	        badgeStarLbl.setForeground(new Color(255, 215, 0));
	        badge.setLayout(new java.awt.GridLayout(2, 1, 0, 0));
	        badge.add(badgeNumLbl);
	        badge.add(badgeStarLbl);
	        
	        
	        JPanel info = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1, 0, 4));
	        info.setBackground(card.getBackground());
	        JLabel nameLbl = new JLabel(m.completed ? "\u2713 " + m.name + " (COMPLETED)" : m.name);
	        nameLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 14));
	        nameLbl.setForeground(m.completed ? new Color(80, 220, 80) : new Color(220, 220, 240));
	        JLabel descLbl = new JLabel(m.description);
	        descLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 11));
	        descLbl.setForeground(new Color(130, 140, 170));
	        info.add(nameLbl); info.add(descLbl);
	        
	        
	        JPanel progressPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(4, 4));
	        progressPanel.setBackground(card.getBackground());
	        progressPanel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(130, 50));
	        JProgressBar bar = new JProgressBar(0, m.goal);
	        bar.setValue(Math.min(m.current, m.goal));
	        bar.setStringPainted(true);
	        bar.setString(m.completed ? "DONE!" : m.current + " / " + m.goal);
	        bar.setForeground(m.completed ? new Color(80, 200, 80) : new Color(100, 160, 255));
	        bar.setBackground(new Color(30, 30, 45));
	        bar.setBorderPainted(false);
	        JLabel progLbl = new JLabel(String.format("%.0f%%", m.progressPct()*100), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	        progLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 11));
	        progLbl.setForeground(new Color(160, 160, 190));
	        progressPanel.add(bar, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        progressPanel.add(progLbl, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	        
	        card.add(badge, BorderLayout.WEST);
	        card.add(info, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	        card.add(progressPanel, BorderLayout.EAST);
	        missionPanel.add(card);
	        missionPanel.add(Box.createRigidArea(new Dimension(0, 10)));
	    }
	    
	    JScrollPane scroll = new JScrollPane(missionPanel);
	    scroll.setBorder(null);
	    scroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(16);
	    frame.add(scroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    
	    
	    JPanel footer = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.CENTER, 12, 10));
	    footer.setBackground(new Color(18, 18, 30));
	    footer.setBorder(BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(2, 0, 0, 0, new Color(40, 45, 70)));
	    
	    boolean allDone = activeMissions.stream().allMatch(m2 -> m2.completed);
	    JButton refreshBtn = new JButton(allDone ? "GET NEW MISSIONS" : "REFRESH MISSIONS");
	    styleButton(refreshBtn, allDone ? new Color(30, 80, 30) : new Color(30, 30, 50),
	               allDone ? new Color(80, 220, 80) : new Color(130, 140, 170),
	               allDone ? new Color(80, 200, 80) : new Color(50, 55, 80));
	    refreshBtn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));
	    refreshBtn.addActionListener(ev -> {
	        generateNewMissions();
	        frame.dispose();
	        showMissionsWindow();
	    });
	    JLabel footerNote = new JLabel("New missions reset your progress counters.");
	    footerNote.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 10));
	    footerNote.setForeground(new Color(100, 100, 130));
	    footer.add(refreshBtn);
	    footer.add(footerNote);
	    frame.add(footer, BorderLayout.SOUTH);
	    
	    frame.setVisible(true);
	}
	
	
	
	
	public static class ArmouryCollection {
	    String name;
	    String[] industrial; 
	    String[] industrialNames;
	    double[] industrialPrices;
	    String[] milspec;
	    String[] milspecNames;
	    double[] milspecPrices;
	    String[] restricted;
	    String[] restrictedNames;
	    double[] restrictedPrices;
	    String[] classified;
	    String[] classifiedNames;
	    double[] classifiedPrices;
	    String[] covert;
	    String[] covertNames;
	    double[] covertPrices;
	    String thumbnailFile; 
	    
	    ArmouryCollection(String name,
	        String[] industrial, String[] industrialNames, double[] industrialPrices,
	        String[] milspec,    String[] milspecNames,    double[] milspecPrices,
	        String[] restricted, String[] restrictedNames, double[] restrictedPrices,
	        String[] classified, String[] classifiedNames, double[] classifiedPrices,
	        String[] covert,     String[] covertNames,     double[] covertPrices) {
	        this.name = name;
	        this.industrial = industrial; this.industrialNames = industrialNames; this.industrialPrices = industrialPrices;
	        this.milspec = milspec; this.milspecNames = milspecNames; this.milspecPrices = milspecPrices;
	        this.restricted = restricted; this.restrictedNames = restrictedNames; this.restrictedPrices = restrictedPrices;
	        this.classified = classified; this.classifiedNames = classifiedNames; this.classifiedPrices = classifiedPrices;
	        this.covert = covert; this.covertNames = covertNames; this.covertPrices = covertPrices;
	        this.thumbnailFile = covert != null && covert.length > 0 ? covert[0] + ".png" : null;
	    }
	}

	private void refreshArmouryTab() {
	    armouryTabPanel.removeAll();
	    Color BG_DARK   = new Color(15, 15, 20);
	    Color BG_PANEL  = new Color(22, 22, 30);
	    Color BG_CARD   = new Color(28, 28, 38);
	    Color ACCENT    = new Color(247, 147, 30);
	    Color TEXT_MAIN = new Color(230, 230, 235);
	    Color TEXT_DIM  = new Color(140, 140, 155);
	    Color GOLD      = new Color(255, 215, 0);

	    armouryTabPanel.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    armouryTabPanel.setLayout(new BorderLayout());

	    JPanel topBar = new JPanel(new BorderLayout());
	    topBar.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    topBar.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(0, 0, 2, 0, ACCENT),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(10, 16, 10, 16)));

	    JLabel titleLbl = new JLabel("ARMOURY", SwingConstants.LEFT);
	    titleLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 20));
	    titleLbl.setForeground(ACCENT);

	    JPanel rightBar = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.RIGHT, 14, 0));
	    rightBar.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    armouryStarsDisp = new JLabel("* " + playerStars + " Stars", SwingConstants.RIGHT);
	    JLabel starsDisp = armouryStarsDisp;
	    starsDisp.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    starsDisp.setForeground(GOLD);
	    rightBar.add(starsDisp);

	    topBar.add(titleLbl, BorderLayout.WEST);
	    topBar.add(rightBar, BorderLayout.EAST);
	    armouryTabPanel.add(topBar, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    JTabbedPane collectionTabs = new JTabbedPane();
	    collectionTabs.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    collectionTabs.setForeground(TEXT_MAIN);
	    collectionTabs.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));

	    for (ArmouryCollection col : ARMOURY_COLLECTIONS) {
	        JPanel colPage = buildCollectionPage(col, starsDisp, BG_DARK, BG_CARD, BG_PANEL, ACCENT, TEXT_MAIN, TEXT_DIM, GOLD);
	        collectionTabs.addTab(col.name, colPage);
	    }

	    if (lastArmouryTabIndex < collectionTabs.getTabCount())
	        collectionTabs.setSelectedIndex(lastArmouryTabIndex);
	    collectionTabs.addChangeListener(e -> lastArmouryTabIndex = collectionTabs.getSelectedIndex());

	    armouryTabPanel.add(collectionTabs, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    armouryTabPanel.revalidate();
	    armouryTabPanel.repaint();
	}

	private JPanel buildCollectionPage(ArmouryCollection col, JLabel starsDisplay,
	        Color BG_DARK, Color BG_CARD, Color BG_PANEL, Color ACCENT,
	        Color TEXT_MAIN, Color TEXT_DIM, Color GOLD) {

	    JPanel page = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(0, 0));
	    page.setBackground(BG_DARK);

	    Object[][] tiers = {
	        {"Covert",     col.covert,     col.covertNames,     col.covertPrices,     new Color(235,75,75)},
	        {"Classified", col.classified, col.classifiedNames, col.classifiedPrices, new Color(211,44,230)},
	        {"Restricted", col.restricted, col.restrictedNames, col.restrictedPrices, new Color(136,71,255)},
	        {"Milspec",    col.milspec,    col.milspecNames,    col.milspecPrices,    new Color(75,105,255)},
	        {"Industrial", col.industrial, col.industrialNames, col.industrialPrices, new Color(110,190,110)},
	    };

	    int totalSkins = 0;
	    for (Object[] t : tiers) {
	        String[] files = (String[]) t[1];
	        if (files != null) totalSkins += files.length;
	    }

	    int cols = 3;
	    int rows = (int) Math.ceil((double) totalSkins / cols);
	    JPanel grid = new JPanel(new GridLayout(rows, cols, 10, 10));
	    grid.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    grid.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(14, 14, 14, 14));

	    for (Object[] tier : tiers) {
	        String tierKey  = (String)   tier[0];
	        String[] files  = (String[]) tier[1];
	        String[] names  = (String[]) tier[2];
	        double[] prices = (double[]) tier[3];
	        Color tierColor = (Color)    tier[4];

	        if (files == null || files.length == 0) continue;

	        for (int si = 0; si < files.length; si++) {
	            final String file      = files[si] + ".png";
	            final String skinName  = names[si];
	            final double skinPrice = prices[si];
	            final Color  tColor    = tierColor;
	            final String tierKeyF  = tierKey;

	            JPanel card = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(0, 0));
	            card.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	            card.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	                BorderFactory.createLineBorder(tColor, 2),
	                BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(6, 6, 6, 6)));

	            Image skinImg = new ImageIcon(file).getImage();
	            JLabel imgLbl = new JLabel(new ImageIcon(skinImg.getScaledInstance(180, 125, Image.SCALE_SMOOTH)));
	            imgLbl.setHorizontalAlignment(SwingConstants.CENTER);
	            card.add(imgLbl, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	            JPanel infoPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1, 0, 2));
	            infoPanel.setBackground(BG_CARD);
	            infoPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(4, 0, 0, 0));

	            JLabel nameLbl = new JLabel(skinName.length() > 28 ? skinName.substring(0, 25) + "..." : skinName, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	            nameLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 10));
	            nameLbl.setForeground(TEXT_MAIN);
	            nameLbl.setToolTipText(skinName);

	            JLabel rarLbl = new JLabel(tierKey, SwingConstants.CENTER);
	            rarLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 9));
	            rarLbl.setForeground(tColor);

	            infoPanel.add(nameLbl);
	            infoPanel.add(rarLbl);
	            card.add(infoPanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	            card.addMouseListener(new MouseAdapter() {
	                public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) { card.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 56)); infoPanel.setBackground(new Color(38, 38, 56)); }
	                public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e)  { card.setBackground(BG_CARD); infoPanel.setBackground(BG_CARD); }
	            });

	            grid.add(card);
	        }
	    }

	    int remainder = totalSkins % cols;
	    if (remainder != 0) {
	        for (int i = 0; i < (cols - remainder); i++) {
	            JPanel blank = new JPanel();
	            blank.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	            grid.add(blank);
	        }
	    }

	    JScrollPane gridScroll = new JScrollPane(grid);
	    gridScroll.setBorder(null);
	    gridScroll.getVerticalScrollBar().setUnitIncrement(20);
	    gridScroll.setHorizontalScrollBarPolicy(ScrollPaneConstants.HORIZONTAL_SCROLLBAR_NEVER);
	    gridScroll.setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    gridScroll.getViewport().setBackground(BG_DARK);
	    page.add(gridScroll, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JPanel bottomBar = new JPanel(new FlowLayout(FlowLayout.CENTER, 0, 10));
	    bottomBar.setBackground(BG_PANEL);
	    bottomBar.setBorder(BorderFactory.createMatteBorder(2, 0, 0, 0, ACCENT));

	    JButton redeemBtn = new JButton("REDEEM - 3 Stars");
	    redeemBtn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 14));
	    redeemBtn.setBackground(new Color(30, 60, 30));
	    redeemBtn.setForeground(GOLD);
	    redeemBtn.setFocusPainted(false);
	    redeemBtn.setOpaque(true);
	    redeemBtn.setCursor(new Cursor(Cursor.HAND_CURSOR));
	    redeemBtn.setBorder(BorderFactory.createCompoundBorder(
	        BorderFactory.createLineBorder(GOLD, 2),
	        BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 24, 8, 24)));
	    redeemBtn.addActionListener(ev -> {
	        if (playerStars < 3) {
	            JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null,
	                "You need 3 Stars to redeem! Complete missions to earn Stars.",
	                "Not Enough Stars", JOptionPane.WARNING_MESSAGE);
	            return;
	        }
	        playerStars -= 3;
	        updateStarsLabel();
	        starsDisplay.setText("* " + playerStars + " Stars");
	        missionArmouryRedeems++;
	        checkMissionProgress();

	        double[] rarityWeights = {0.0025, 0.01, 0.032, 0.125, 0.79};
	        String[][] tierFiles   = {col.covert,      col.classified,      col.restricted,      col.milspec,      col.industrial};
	        String[][] tierNames   = {col.covertNames,  col.classifiedNames,  col.restrictedNames,  col.milspecNames,  col.industrialNames};
	        double[][] tierPrices  = {col.covertPrices, col.classifiedPrices, col.restrictedPrices, col.milspecPrices, col.industrialPrices};
	        String[] tierRarities  = {"Covert", "Classified", "Restricted", "Milspec", "Industrial"};
	        double roll = random.nextDouble();
	        double cumulative = 0.0;
	        int chosenTier = 4;
	        for (int ti = 0; ti < rarityWeights.length; ti++) {
	            cumulative += rarityWeights[ti];
	            if (roll < cumulative && tierFiles[ti] != null && tierFiles[ti].length > 0) {
	                chosenTier = ti;
	                break;
	            }
	        }
	        while (chosenTier < 4 && (tierFiles[chosenTier] == null || tierFiles[chosenTier].length == 0))
	            chosenTier++;
	        int skinIdx         = random.nextInt(tierFiles[chosenTier].length);
	        String chosenFile   = tierFiles[chosenTier][skinIdx] + ".png";
	        String chosenName   = tierNames[chosenTier][skinIdx];
	        double chosenPrice  = tierPrices[chosenTier][skinIdx];
	        String chosenRarity = tierRarities[chosenTier];
	        redeemBtn.setEnabled(false);
	        performArmouryRedeem(col, chosenName, chosenRarity, chosenPrice, chosenFile, redeemBtn);
	    });

	    bottomBar.add(redeemBtn);
	    page.add(bottomBar, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    return page;
	}

	private void performArmouryRedeem(ArmouryCollection col, String skinName, String skinRarity, double basePrice, String imageFile, JButton redeemBtn) {
	    playSoundFile("case_open.wav");


	    final Image finalSkinImg = new ImageIcon(imageFile).getImage();
	    FloatRange fr2 = FLOAT_LIMITS.get(skinName);
	    if (fr2 == null) for (Map.Entry<String, FloatRange> e2 : FLOAT_LIMITS.entrySet())
	        if (skinName.startsWith(e2.getKey())) { fr2 = e2.getValue(); break; }
	    double floatMin2 = (fr2 != null && fr2.min != null) ? fr2.min : 0.0;
	    double floatMax2 = (fr2 != null && fr2.max != null) ? fr2.max : 0.80;
	    final double itemFloat2 = floatMin2 + random.nextDouble() * (floatMax2 - floatMin2);
	    String condition2;
	    if      (itemFloat2 <= 0.07) condition2 = "Factory New";
	    else if (itemFloat2 <= 0.15) condition2 = "Minimal Wear";
	    else if (itemFloat2 <= 0.38) condition2 = "Field-Tested";
	    else if (itemFloat2 <= 0.45) condition2 = "Well-Worn";
	    else                         condition2 = "Battle-Scarred";

	    double condMult = condition2.equals("Factory New") ? 2.2 : condition2.equals("Minimal Wear") ? 1.5 :
	                      condition2.equals("Field-Tested") ? 1.0 : condition2.equals("Well-Worn") ? 0.65 : 0.3;
	    final double finalPrice2 = basePrice * condMult * (0.88 + random.nextDouble() * 0.24);
	    final String finalCondStr = condition2;

	    final int FINAL_IDX = 50;
	    final int SKIN_W = 210, SKIN_H = 155, CARD_GAP = 6;
	    final int SPACING = SKIN_W + CARD_GAP;

	    Color rarCol = skinRarity.equals("Covert")     ? new Color(235,75,75)  :
	                   skinRarity.equals("Classified")  ? new Color(211,44,230) :
	                   skinRarity.equals("Restricted")  ? new Color(136,71,255) :
	                   skinRarity.equals("Industrial")  ? new Color(110,190,110) : new Color(75,105,255);

	    // Build rarity-weighted pool for the strip animation
	    String[][] wFiles = {col.industrial, col.milspec, col.restricted, col.classified, col.covert};
	    Color[] wColors  = {new Color(110,190,110), new Color(75,105,255), new Color(136,71,255), new Color(211,44,230), new Color(235,75,75)};
	    int[] wCounts   = {79, 13, 5, 2, 1};
	    java.util.List<Image> wPool = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	    java.util.List<Color> wPoolColors = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	    for (int wi = 0; wi < wFiles.length; wi++) {
	        if (wFiles[wi] == null || wFiles[wi].length == 0) continue;
	        for (int wc = 0; wc < wCounts[wi]; wc++) {
	            int pick = random.nextInt(wFiles[wi].length);
	            wPool.add(new ImageIcon(wFiles[wi][pick] + ".png").getImage());
	            wPoolColors.add(wColors[wi]);
	        }
	    }
	    if (wPool.isEmpty()) {
	        for (Image img : blueSkins) { wPool.add(img); wPoolColors.add(new Color(75,105,255)); }
	    }

	    java.util.List<Image> strip = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	    java.util.List<Color> stripColors = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
	    for (int i = 0; i < 65; i++) {
	        if (i == FINAL_IDX) { strip.add(finalSkinImg); stripColors.add(rarCol); }
	        else { int pick = random.nextInt(wPool.size()); strip.add(wPool.get(pick)); stripColors.add(wPoolColors.get(pick)); }
	    }

	    JDialog animDialog = new JDialog(hGui.this, "Opening - " + col.name, false);
	    animDialog.setUndecorated(true);
	    animDialog.getRootPane().setBorder(BorderFactory.createLineBorder(new Color(247, 147, 30), 2));
	    animDialog.setSize(800, 340);
	    animDialog.setLocationRelativeTo(hGui.this);
	    animDialog.setLayout(new BorderLayout());
	    animDialog.getContentPane().setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 20));

	    JLabel topLbl = new JLabel("Opening " + col.name + "...", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    topLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 15));
	    topLbl.setForeground(new Color(95, 200, 255));
	    topLbl.setOpaque(true);
	    topLbl.setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 20));
	    topLbl.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 0, 8, 0));
	    animDialog.add(topLbl, BorderLayout.NORTH);

	    final int[] scrollPos = {0};
	    final double randomBias = (random.nextDouble() - 0.5) * 100.0;
	    final int targetPos = (int)(FINAL_IDX * SPACING - (800 / 2) + (SKIN_W / 2) + randomBias);

	    JPanel animPanel = new JPanel() {
	        @Override protected void paintComponent(Graphics g) {
	            super.paintComponent(g);
	            Graphics2D g2 = (Graphics2D) g;
	            g2.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_ANTIALIASING, RenderingHints.VALUE_ANTIALIAS_ON);
	            g2.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_RENDERING, RenderingHints.VALUE_RENDER_QUALITY);
	            java.awt.GradientPaint bgGrad = new java.awt.GradientPaint(0, 0, new Color(18,18,28), 0, getHeight(), new Color(28,28,42));
	            g2.setPaint(bgGrad);
	            g2.fillRect(0, 0, getWidth(), getHeight());
	            int cx = getWidth() / 2;
	            int cy = getHeight() / 2;
	            int startX = -scrollPos[0];
	            for (int si = 0; si < strip.size(); si++) {
	                int x = startX + si * SPACING;
	                int y = cy - SKIN_H / 2;
	                if (x + SKIN_W < 0 || x > getWidth()) continue;
	                Image img = strip.get(si);
	                g2.setColor(new Color(40, 40, 55));
	                g2.fillRoundRect(x, y, SKIN_W, SKIN_H, 8, 8);
	                int ip = 10;
	                g2.drawImage(img, x + ip, y + ip, SKIN_W - ip*2, SKIN_H - ip*2 - 8, null);
	                int barH = 8;
	                Color rc = (si < stripColors.size()) ? stripColors.get(si) : new Color(75, 105, 255);
	                java.awt.GradientPaint barGrad = new java.awt.GradientPaint(x, 0, rc.darker(), x + SKIN_W, 0, rc.brighter());
	                g2.setPaint(barGrad);
	                g2.fillRoundRect(x, y + SKIN_H - barH, SKIN_W, barH, 4, 4);
	                g2.fillRect(x, y + SKIN_H - barH, SKIN_W, barH / 2);
	                g2.setPaint(null);
	            }
	            g2.setColor(new Color(255, 215, 0));
	            g2.setStroke(new BasicStroke(2.5f));
	            g2.drawLine(cx, 0, cx, getHeight());
	        }
	    };
	    animPanel.setBackground(new Color(18, 18, 28));
	    animPanel.setPreferredSize(new Dimension(800, 240));
	    animDialog.add(animPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

	    JPanel resultPanel = new JPanel(new BorderLayout(10, 6));
	    resultPanel.setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 20));
	    resultPanel.setBorder(BorderFactory.createEmptyBorder(8, 14, 8, 14));
	    resultPanel.setVisible(false);

	    JLabel resNameLbl = new JLabel(skinName + "  (" + finalCondStr + ")", SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    resNameLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 16));
	    resNameLbl.setForeground(rarCol);
	    JLabel resPriceLbl = new JLabel(String.format("Value: $%.2f  |  %s  |  Float: %.4f", finalPrice2, skinRarity, itemFloat2), SwingConstants.CENTER);
	    resPriceLbl.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.PLAIN, 12));
	    resPriceLbl.setForeground(new Color(200, 200, 220));

	    JButton closeBtn = new JButton("CLOSE");
	    styleButton(closeBtn, new Color(30, 80, 30), new Color(80, 220, 80), new Color(80, 200, 80));
	    closeBtn.setFont(new Font("Consolas", Font.BOLD, 13));
	    closeBtn.addActionListener(evv -> {
	        double scl2 = Math.min(130.0 / Math.max(1, finalSkinImg.getWidth(null)), 88.0 / Math.max(1, finalSkinImg.getHeight(null)));
	        Image scaledSkinImg = finalSkinImg.getScaledInstance(
	            (int)(finalSkinImg.getWidth(null) * scl2), (int)(finalSkinImg.getHeight(null) * scl2), Image.SCALE_SMOOTH);
	        InventoryItem item2 = new InventoryItem(new ImageIcon(scaledSkinImg), skinName, finalCondStr,
	            skinRarity, BigDecimal.valueOf(finalPrice2).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP),
	            itemFloat2, false, random.nextInt(1000), null, finalPrice2);
	        item2.collection = col.name;
	        inventoryList.add(item2);
	        inventoryValue += finalPrice2;
	        newInventoryValue = BigDecimal.valueOf(inventoryValue).setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
	        if (totalInventoryValueLabel != null) totalInventoryValueLabel.setText("Inventory Value: $" + newInventoryValue);
	        playSoundFile("button_click.wav");
	        animDialog.dispose();
	        refreshArmouryTab();
	    });

	    JPanel resCenter = new JPanel(new GridLayout(2, 1, 0, 4));
	    resCenter.setBackground(new Color(12, 12, 20));
	    resCenter.add(resNameLbl);
	    resCenter.add(resPriceLbl);
	    resultPanel.add(resCenter, BorderLayout.CENTER);
	    resultPanel.add(closeBtn, BorderLayout.EAST);
	    animDialog.add(resultPanel, BorderLayout.SOUTH);

	    animDialog.addWindowFocusListener(new java.awt.event.WindowFocusListener() {
	        public void windowGainedFocus(java.awt.event.WindowEvent e) {}
	        public void windowLostFocus(java.awt.event.WindowEvent e) { if (animDialog.isVisible()) animDialog.toFront(); }
	    });
	    animDialog.addWindowListener(new java.awt.event.WindowAdapter() {
	        @Override public void windowClosed(java.awt.event.WindowEvent e) {
	            if (redeemBtn != null) redeemBtn.setEnabled(true);
	        }
	    });
	    animDialog.setVisible(true);

	    final double maxSpeed  = 58.0;
	    final double accel     = 2.4;
	    final double decelZone = 1800.0;
	    final double stopVel   = 0.15;
	    javax.swing.Timer scrollTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(16, null);
	    scrollTimer.addActionListener(new ActionListener() {
	        private double currentOffset = 0.0;
	        private double velocity = 0.0;
	        private int prevCenterIdx = -1;

	        @Override
	        public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
	            double distance = targetPos - currentOffset;
	            if (distance > decelZone) {
	                velocity = Math.min(velocity + accel, maxSpeed);
	            } else {
	                double factor = distance / decelZone;
	                velocity = maxSpeed * factor;
	            }
	            if (distance < 260) velocity *= 0.96;
	            velocity = Math.min(velocity, distance);
	            currentOffset += velocity;
	            scrollPos[0] = (int) currentOffset;
	            int centerIdx = (scrollPos[0] + 400) / SPACING;
	            if (centerIdx != prevCenterIdx && centerIdx >= 0 && centerIdx < strip.size()) {
	                playSoundFile("case_open.wav");
	                prevCenterIdx = centerIdx;
	            }
	            animPanel.repaint();

	            if (velocity < stopVel) {
	                scrollTimer.stop();
	                javax.swing.Timer delayTimer = new javax.swing.Timer(800, evt -> {
	                    playSoundFile("unbox.wav");
	                    resultPanel.setVisible(true);
	                    animDialog.revalidate();
	                    animDialog.repaint();
	                });
	                delayTimer.setRepeats(false);
	                delayTimer.start();
	            }
	        }
	    });
	    scrollTimer.start();
	}
}
